### [1] [Random neural networks match observed dimensionality of neural population recordings and motivate stronger experimental tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26551)
*Zehui Zhao,Michael J Pasek,Ilya M Nemenman*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文通过将有限测量时间和行为上下文变异性纳入动力平均场理论（Dynamical Mean-Field Theory），证明最小随机神经网络模型预测的维度与大规模神经记录实验数据定量一致，但当前记录时长难以通过维度区分不同连接结构；此外，神经流形在不同行为上下文间的方向相似性比维度对网络结构更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机连接神经网络（randomly connected neural networks）长期以来作为研究神经群体集体动力学的理论工具，但与实验的定量比较仍然有限。尽管最小模型预测了群体相关性的一般结构，两者是否定量一致尚未经过检验。

Method: 基于动力平均场理论（Dynamical Mean-Field Theory）的最新进展，在最小随机神经网络模型中引入两个额外实验相关特征：有限测量时间（finite measurement time）和行为上下文变异性（variability across behavioral contexts）。

Result: 当纳入有限测量时间和行为上下文变异性后，大规模神经记录中测量的维度（dimensionality）与随机模型预测值一致；但现有记录时长不足以通过维度区分不同连接结构。维度随外部输入强度（external input strength）呈非单调变化；神经流形（neural manifolds）在不同行为上下文间的方向相似性（orientation similarity）比维度对网络结构更敏感。

Conclusion: 这些结果为实验设计提供了定量指导，以推断群体活动背后的连接结构（connectivity structure）。

Abstract: Randomly connected neural networks have long served as a theoretical tool for studying collective dynamics in neural populations, yet quantitative comparisons to experiments remain limited. Recent technological advances have made it possible to resolve population-wide correlations across neurons, and minimal models such as random neural networks predict their generic structure. Whether the two agree quantitatively remains untested. In this work, we examine whether a minimally structured random neural network can account for the low dimensionality of activity in neural population recordings by building on recent developments in Dynamical Mean-Field Theory and incorporating two additional experimentally relevant features into the model: finite measurement time and variability across behavioral contexts. We show that, when these factors are included, the dimensionality measured from large-scale recordings is consistent with the values predicted by random models. However, current recording durations make it difficult to use dimensionality to discriminate among connectivity structures. We further show that analytically predicted dimensionality varies non-monotonically with external input strength, and that the orientation similarity between neural manifolds recorded under different behavioral contexts can be more sensitive to network structure than dimensionality is. Together, these results provide quantitative guidance for experimental design to infer the connectivity structure underlying population activity.

</details>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Critical Inter-Horizon Thermal Dynamics on the Lukewarm Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter Manifold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26122)
*J. Khalloufi,H. El Moumni,K. Masmar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将四维Reissner–Nordström–de Sitter黑洞的微温分支重新诠释为一个有效双视界非平衡系统的精确零耗散热流形。通过固定电荷扇区中视界间热亲和力控制熵产生并在微温分支上精确消失，结合精确弛豫系数\(K_L(ρ)\)及其在临界比率\(ρ_*≈0.4354\)处的稳定性转变（弛豫时间发散），最终将微温分支从几何等温提升为临界热流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在重新理解Reissner–Nordström–de Sitter黑洞中“微温分支”（lukewarm branch）的物理本质，将其从传统的等温几何描述提升为一个精确的临界热流形，并揭示其作为非平衡系统中零耗散热流形的角色。

Method: 论文将四维Reissner–Nordström–de Sitter黑洞的微温分支重新解释为有效双视界非平衡系统的精确零耗散热流形。在固定电荷扇区中，通过视界间热亲和力（inter-horizon thermal affinity）控制熵产生，并在微温分支上精确消失。线性化的热模态由精确弛豫系数\(K_L(ρ)\)（其中\(ρ=r_+/r_c\)）描述，稳定性在临界比率\(ρ_*=\frac{1+\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}\,3^{1/4}}{2}\approx 0.4354\)处改变，弛豫时间在临界点发散为\(τ\sim |ρ-ρ_*|^{-1}\)。该临界结构被编码为最小Bragg–Williams泛函和Onsager–Machlup作用量，用于热模态的有效轨迹描述。

Result: 发现了精确弛豫系数\(K_L(ρ)\)，确定了稳定性转变的临界比率\(ρ_*\approx 0.4354\)，在该点弛豫时间以\(τ\sim |ρ-ρ_*|^{-1}\)的形式发散。建立了描述该临界结构的Bragg–Williams泛函和Onsager–Machlup作用量。

Conclusion: 微温分支被提升为物理意义更为丰富的临界热流形（critical inter-horizon thermal manifold），而不仅仅是几何上的等温线，为理解黑洞热力学与非平衡统计力学的联系提供了新视角。

Abstract: We reinterpret the lukewarm sector of four-dimensional Reissner--Nordström--de Sitter black holes as the exact zero-dissipation thermal manifold of an effective two-horizon nonequilibrium system. In the fixed-charge sector, the inter-horizon thermal affinity controls the entropy production and vanishes precisely on the lukewarm branch. The corresponding linearized thermal mode is governed by an exact relaxation coefficient \(K_L(ρ)\), with \(ρ=r_+/r_c\), and changes stability at the critical ratio \[ ρ_*=\frac{1+\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}\,3^{1/4}}{2}\approx 0.4354, \] where the relaxation time diverges as \(τ\sim |ρ-ρ_*|^{-1}\). We then encode this critical structure in a minimal Bragg--Williams functional and an Onsager--Machlup action for the effective trajectories of the thermal mode. In this way, the lukewarm branch is promoted from a geometric equal-temperature locus to a critical inter-horizon thermal manifold.

</details>


### [3] [Astrophysical environment around a black hole in the braneworld and its optical signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26124)
*M. F. Fauzi,A. O. Latief,A. Sulaksono*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了膜世界理论（braneworld theory）对黑洞周围天体物理环境的影响，发现有限膜张力（finite brane tension）通过二次和非局域修正削弱引力，阻止视界形成，并分析了黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）与爱因斯坦环半径（Einstein ring radius）作为联合约束膜张力的光学可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究膜世界理论中有限膜张力对黑洞周围天体物理环境的引力修正效应，并寻找可行的光学观测约束手段。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦簇（Einstein cluster）描述环境，分析来自体空间（bulk）局域化物质所源出的黑洞（包括规则黑洞和Schwarzschild黑洞），结合中子星观测对膜张力的现有约束进行讨论。

Result: 各向异性簇与有限膜张力耦合导致的二次和非局域修正削弱了引力，阻止视界形成；该效应在亚恒星质量黑洞嵌入致密环境时尤为显著。爱因斯坦环半径随膜张力减小而减小，黑洞阴影半径反而增大，与引力弱化效应看似矛盾。

Conclusion: 黑洞阴影与爱因斯坦环半径可共同用于在特定天体物理场景中约束膜张力的数值。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of braneworld theory on the astrophysical environment surrounding a black hole. The black hole is sourced by localized matter from the bulk, which could describe both regular and singular (Schwarzschild) black hole. Employing an Einstein cluster description for the environment, we find that the anisotropic nature of the cluster, coupled with finite brane tension, leads to a weakening of gravity due to the quadratic and nonlocal corrections to the effective four-dimensional field equations. Consequently, this effect prevents horizon formation within the environment. Applying current constraints on the brane tension derived from neutron star observations, we demonstrate that this effect is particularly relevant for sub-stellar mass black holes embedded in compact environments. Furthermore, we investigate the optical signatures of finite brane tension in this scenario, specifically focusing on the black hole shadow and Einstein ring radii. We show that the Einstein ring radius decreases with a smaller brane tension, whereas the black hole shadow radius increases--somewhat contradicts the weakening gravity effects. Ultimately, these two observables may jointly serve to constrain the value of the brane tension in a very specific astrophysical scenarios.

</details>


### [4] [Symmetries of tensionless strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26185)
*Ulf Lindström*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文反驳了 arXiv:2605.12414 中声称的某尺度变换在无张力弦（tensionless string）讨论中被“系统性忽略”的观点，指出该对称性在经典与量子理论中已有广泛讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对 arXiv:2605.12414 提出的“某尺度变换被系统性忽略”这一论断，作者旨在澄清该对称性在无张力弦理论中并非被忽略，而是已有多处研究涉及。

Method: 作者通过文献回顾与理论分析，指出该尺度变换对称性在无张力弦的经典理论与量子理论中均有讨论，以此反驳原论断。

Result: 作者发现该尺度变换对称性在无张力弦的经典理论与量子理论中已有多处文献涉及，并非如 arXiv:2605.12414 所声称的那样被“系统性忽略”。

Conclusion: 该尺度变换对称性在无张力弦理论中并非被忽略，相关讨论在经典与量子层面均已有记载。

Abstract: In a recent article, arXiv:2605.12414, it is stated that a certain scale transformation has been "systematically overlooked" in discussions of the tensionless string. Here we point out that this kind of symmetry is treated in numerous places, in the classical as well as the quantum theory.

</details>


### [5] [Fermion Families and Pontryagin Class: Topological Field Theory via Colour Symmetry Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26202)
*Zheyan Wan,Juven Wang,Shing-Tung Yau*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从拓扑异常（topological anomaly）约束出发，证明了标准模型（Standard Model）中恰好存在3代夸克和轻子（3 families of quarks and leptons）的必然性。通过分析离散$Z_n$对称性下的4维费米子异常及其5维自旋配边群（5d spin bordism group）分类，研究指出仅群上同调（group-cohomology）子类可通过拓扑量子场论（TQFT）消除，并证明在最小颜色扩展下，$N_c=N_f=3$是唯一能使标准模型重子为费米子的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 家族谜题（Family puzzle）询问为何标准模型恰好包含3代（3 families）夸克和轻子。本文旨在从拓扑约束（topological constraints）和反常消除（anomaly cancellation）机制出发，为这一观测事实提供理论解释。

Method: 利用5维自旋配边群（5d spin bordism group）分类离散$Z_n$对称性下的4维费米子异常（4d fermionic anomalies），区分群上同调子类（group-cohomology subclass）H$^5(Z_n,U(1))$与超出群上同调的$A_{Z_n} p_1$类（涉及庞特里亚金类 Pontryagin class $p_1$）。构建对称性扩展（symmetry extension）构造，并分析$N_c$色（colors）与$N_f$代（families）广义标准模型的反常消除条件。

Result: 仅群上同调子类H$^5(Z_n,U(1))\cong Z_n$可由反常$Z_n$对称的4维$Z_n$规范拓扑量子场论（TQFT）消除，而$A_{Z_n} p_1$类除$n=2,3$外均不可消除。对于$d=5, n=3$，构建了消除标准模型混合$({\bf B+L})$-规范-引力反常（mixed discrete $({\bf B+L})$-gauge-gravitational anomaly）的TQFT，替代3个“惰性”右手中微子$\nu_R$。最小颜色扩展解为：$N_c=3, N_f\ge 3$；$N_c=4, N_f\ge 2$；$N_c=12, N_f\ge 6$。要求标准模型重子为费米子（fermion）且$N_c$为奇数时，$N_c=N_f=3$是唯一解。

Conclusion: 标准模型中3代夸克和轻子以及3种颜色（3 colors）$N_c=N_f=3$是满足拓扑异常消除和重子费米子统计的唯一情况。缺失的$ν_R$可由特定的4维反常TQFT自然替代。

Abstract: Family puzzle asks why the Standard Model (SM) features exactly 3 families of quarks and leptons. Motivated by topological constraints, we study 4-dimensional fermionic anomalies with discrete $Z_n$ symmetry, classified by the 5d spin bordism group. We show that only the group-cohomology subclass H$^5(Z_n,U(1))\cong Z_n$ can be canceled by an anomalous $Z_n$-symmetric 4d $Z_n$-gauge topological quantum field theory (TQFT), while beyond-group-cohomology $A_{Z_n} p_1$ involving the Pontryagin class $p_1$ cannot (except $n=2,3$). More generally, we prove that any cocycle $α_d\in$H$^d(Z_n,U(1))$ in odd spacetime dimension $d\ge3$ is trivialised by the symmetry extension $1\to Z_n\to Z_{n^2}\to Z_n\to 1,$ and we construct the corresponding symmetric anomalous boundary TQFT. For $d=5$ and $n=3$, this yields a Spin$\times Z_3$-symmetric 4d $Z_3$-gauge TQFT that cancels the mixed discrete $(\bf B+L)$-gauge-gravitational anomaly of the SM in the absence of 3 "sterile" right-handed neutrinos $ν_R$. We further analyze a generalized SM with $N_c$ colors and $N_f$ families and argue that missing $N_f$ copies of the $ν_R$ can be naturally replaced by that 4d anomalous $Spin\times_{Z_2^F} Z_{2 N_f,{{\bf B} + {\bf L}}}$ symmetric $Z_{N_c}$-gauge TQFT under the anomaly cancellation, via an appropriate $Z_{N_c}$-color symmetry extension construction $1\to Z_{N_c}\to Spin\times Z_{N_cN_f}\to Spin\times_{Z_2^F} Z_{2N_f}\to1$ of anomalous topological order. For minimal nonzero positive integers $N_c$ and $N_f$, we find the minimal color extensions: $N_c=3, N_f \ge 3$; $N_c=4, N_f \ge 2$; and $N_c=12, N_f \ge 6$. If we further require that an SM baryon is a fermion so $N_c$ is odd, then $Z_{N_c}=Z($SU$(N_c))$ color center, we prove 3 families and 3 colors, $N_c=N_f=3$, is the unique case that stands out. We also prove that $A_{Z_3}p_1= 0\mod3$ for the mod 3 cohomology class in an appropriate context.

</details>


### [6] [EFTs with Symmetric Moduli Spaces: the Landscape and the Swampland](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26212)
*Stephanie Baines,Veronica Collazuol,Bernardo Fraiman,Mariana Graña,Daniel Waldram*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于前期关于对称模空间（symmetric moduli spaces）中沼泽地距离猜想（Swampland Distance Conjecture, SDC）的研究成果，分析了质量衰减率如何由粒子态表示的权多面体（weight polytope）编码，进而确定了具有这些衰减率的对称空间有效场论（EFT）及表示。研究发现，若粒子态处于不可约表示（irreducible representation）中，可能的权多面体和模空间数量是有限的；不同EFT之间通过模空间嵌入或解紧化极限（decompactification limit）相互关联。除三个理论无法从M-理论或弦理论紧化（compactification）得到外，其余均可基于E_{8(8)}的EFT推导，分析还识别了谱中应存在的弦与膜表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统性地确定哪些对称空间有效场论（EFT）及其表示能够实现由权多面体编码的质量衰减率，并检验这些理论是否均能从M-理论或弦理论紧化中获得。

Method: 利用arXiv:2508.18401中关于对称模空间SDC的结果，通过权多面体编码质量衰减率；假定粒子态在不可约表示下变换，列举可能的权多面体和模空间；通过嵌入或解紧化极限关联不同EFT，并在分支（branching）过程中要求粒子表示保持兼容性。

Result: 在有限的可能性中，大部分理论可从基于E_{8(8)}的EFT出发得到，但有三个理论无法由M-理论或弦理论紧化导出；此外，通过嵌入过程识别了谱中应有的弦与膜表示。

Conclusion: 对称空间EFT在SDC框架下存在有限分类，且多数可通过E_{8(8)}统一导出，但存在三个例外，暗示这些理论可能落在弦理论所能实现的景观之外。

Abstract: The Swampland Distance Conjecture (SDC) states that, for any infinite-distance limit in the moduli space of a quantum gravity effective field theory (EFT), there should exist an infinite tower of states that become exponentially light. According to the Emergent String Conjecture, such a tower should consist either of tensionless strings or of Kaluza-Klein modes, each with a mass-decay rate that depends in a precise way on the dimension of the effective field theory.
  In this paper, we use the results obtained in arXiv:2508.18401 on the SDC for symmetric moduli spaces and how these rates are encoded in the weight polytope of the corresponding particle-state representations to determine the symmetric space EFTs and representations that have these decay rates. Remarkably, assuming that the particle states transform in an irreducible representation, the list of possible polytopes and moduli spaces is finite. Different EFTs are related by embedding one moduli space in another or by taking a decompactification limit. Requiring compatibility of the particle representations under such branching, we find that, while most of the theories can be obtained from an EFT based on $E_{8(8)}$, there remain three in our list that appear to be impossible to get from M- or string-theory compactifications. Using the same embedding procedure, we also identify the string and brane representations that should be present in the spectrum.

</details>


### [7] [$S$-duality, boundary states, and higher-form symmetries on ALE spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26224)
*Mohamed M. Anber*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell theory）在A型渐近局部欧几里得（ALE）空间上的阿贝尔S-对偶性（Abelian S-duality），发现ALE空间上的路径积分并非标量配分函数，而是由平坦U(1)和乐扇区标记的theta函数块构成。这些块被解释为希尔伯特空间边界态的分量，在模群作用下呈矢量值模协变（vector-valued modular covariance）。通过将Eguchi-Hanson空间与其定向反转体粘合得到S^2×S^2，并验证了配对结果与标准配分函数一致。引入1-形式对称性背景后，ALE theta块成为Cartan环面上的线丛截面，反映了电磁混合1-形式反常。ALE空间可视为四维麦克斯韦理论的手征性积木块，其边界态配对类似于二维CFT中左右手征共形块的配对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解麦克斯韦理论在ALE空间上的S-对偶性行为。不同于闭四流形，ALE空间上路径积分不是标量配分函数，需要建立适当的协变框架来处理模群作用。

Method: 将ALE路径积分分解为按平坦U(1)和乐扇区标记的theta函数块，并解释为希尔伯特空间边界态的分量。通过粘合Eguchi-Hanson空间与其定向反转体构造闭流形S^2×S^2，验证配对机制。进一步引入电场和磁场的1-形式对称性背景，分析theta块的线丛截面性质及离散子群规范理论。

Result: ALE theta块在模群作用下呈矢量值模协变，而非普通模性。Eguchi-Hanson边界态的自然配对精确再现了S^2×S^2上的标准麦克斯韦配分函数。引入1-形式对称性背景后，theta块成为与A_{N-1}根格关联的Cartan环面上的线丛截面，反映了电磁混合1-形式反常。

Conclusion: ALE空间充当四维麦克斯韦理论的手征性积木块：单个ALE块携带扇区分辨的边界数据，粘合操作配对扇区产生闭流形配分函数，与二维CFT中左右手征共形块的配对机制在结构上平行。矢量值边界态框架在规范离散子群后依然保持协变性。

Abstract: We study Abelian $S$-duality of Maxwell theory on $A$-type asymptotically locally Euclidean (ALE) spaces. Unlike on closed four-manifolds, the Maxwell path integral on an ALE space is not naturally a scalar partition function. Rather, it decomposes into theta-function blocks labeled by flat $U(1)$ holonomy sectors on the asymptotic lens-space boundary. We interpret these blocks as components of the Hilbert-space boundary state prepared by the ALE path integral. With this interpretation, the apparent failure of ordinary modularity is replaced by vector-valued modular covariance under the action of the modular group. We test this picture explicitly for Eguchi-Hanson space by gluing it to its orientation reversal. The resulting closed four-manifold is diffeomorphic to $S^2\times S^2$, and the natural pairing of the two ALE boundary states reproduces the standard Maxwell partition function on $S^2\times S^2$. We then refine the construction by turning on electric and magnetic $1$-form symmetry backgrounds. In their presence, the ALE theta blocks are not ordinary functions, but sections of a line bundle over the Cartan torus associated with the $A_{N-1}$ root lattice, reflecting the mixed electric-magnetic $1$-form anomaly. We also discuss gauging discrete $\mathbb Z_k$ subgroups of the $1$-form symmetries and show that the vector-valued boundary-state structure remains the natural covariant framework after gauging. In this sense, ALE spaces behave as chiral building blocks for four-dimensional Maxwell theory: individual ALE blocks carry sector-resolved boundary data, while gluing pairs these sectors to produce an ordinary closed-manifold partition function, much like the pairing of left- and right-moving conformal blocks in two-dimensional CFT.

</details>


### [8] [Krylov Complexity in Periodically Driven CFTs and Critical Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26250)
*Ankit Gill,Anurag Sarkar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过Krylov构造研究了周期驱动共形场论及其通过临界费米子实现的晶格模型，发现方波与正弦波驱动在共形场论侧表现出相似的Krylov增长，但在晶格实现中展现出截然不同的谱与图结构特征，表明加热与非加热相变涉及不同的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在周期驱动系统中，加热相（heating phase）与非加热相（non-heating phase）之间的转变是核心问题。本文旨在通过Krylov构造这一工具，深入比较不同驱动形式（方波与正弦波）下共形场论及其晶格实现中Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）的演化行为，揭示驱动形式对相变机制的影响。

Method: 采用Arnoldi构造（Arnoldi construction）计算Arnoldi系数（Arnoldi coefficients）与返回振幅（return amplitudes）。针对周期驱动共形场论，研究加热相与非加热相中的行为；在晶格实现中，进一步分析关联矩阵的Krylov复杂度、准能级统计（quasi energy level statistics）以及由Floquet算符（Floquet operator）诱导的图结构（graph structure）。

Result: 在加热相中，Arnoldi系数呈指数趋近于1；在非加热相中，Arnoldi系数呈现振荡行为。在共形场论侧，两种驱动方式的Krylov增长行为相似；但在晶格实现中，方波驱动与正弦波驱动在谱特征和图结构上表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: 两种驱动虽然在共形场论层面表现类似，但晶格实现中的差异表明，加热相与非加热相之间的转变由不同的物理机制主导。Krylov构造及其在晶格模型中的扩展分析有助于区分这些机制。

Abstract: We study Krylov construction in periodically driven conformal field theories and their lattice realisations via critical fermions. Two types of driving are considered: a square-wave drive and a continuous sinusoidal drive. Using the Arnoldi construction, we examine Arnoldi coefficients and return amplitudes in periodically driven conformal field theories in the heating and non-heating phases. In the heating phase, the Arnoldi coefficients approach unity exponentially; in contrast, in the non-heating phase, they exhibit oscillatory behaviour. For the lattice realisations, we further analyse the Krylov complexity of the correlation matrix, quasi energy level statistics, and the graph structure induced by the Floquet operator. Although the two drives exhibit similar Krylov growth on the CFT side, their lattice realisations exhibit markedly different spectral and graph signatures, indicating distinct mechanisms governing the transition between the heating and non-heating phases.

### [9] [Torsional black holes and wormholes in Einstein-Cartan-Maxwell gravity with a conformal scalar field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26360)
*Luis Avilés,Omar Valdivia,Rodolfo Véliz,Carlos Vera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种含单参数推广的Weyl变换（Weyl transformation），将其引入一阶引力（first-order gravity）并定义了一个具有动态挠率（dynamical torsion）的共形耦合标量场（conformally coupled scalar）扇区。该构造在参数 λ→1 时退化至标准无挠共形耦合情形。在相应的 Einstein-Cartan-Maxwell 理论中，论文导出了渐近平直与渐近局部 AdS 时空中的精确静态解，这些解分别描述了标量着衣黑洞（scalar-dressed black hole）、规则黑洞（regular black hole）以及可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）。研究表明，挠率可以正则化标量场，并在适当分支下改善几何奇点结构。在 AdS 扇区中，拓扑黑洞（topological black hole）的存在需要非零电荷。这些结果为四维引力中规则构型与挠性构型提供了新的精确例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典引力理论中，挠率（torsion）与共形对称性（conformal symmetry）的相互作用尚未被充分探索，特别是挠率能否在精确解层面改善奇点结构并产生规则构型尚不明确。本文旨在构造一阶引力中一种含单参数的推广Weyl变换，从而定义包含动态挠率的共形耦合标量扇区，并研究其经典精确解的性质，探索挠率在正则化标量场与几何奇点方面的潜力。

Method: 论文基于一阶引力（first-order gravity）框架，提出一个含单参数 λ 的推广Weyl变换，将无挠共形耦合理论推广至包含动态挠率的一般情形。该构造在 λ→1 极限下恢复标准的无挠共形耦合（standard torsionless conformal coupling）。随后在 Einstein-Cartan-Maxwell 理论中，通过求解场方程获得精确静态解，并分析参数空间（积分常数与变形参数 λ）对解的性质的影响。

Result: 获得了三类精确静态解：标量着衣黑洞、规则黑洞以及可穿越虫洞，其性质取决于积分常数与变形参数 λ 的取值。挠率能够正则化标量场，并在适当分支下改善几何奇点结构。在渐近局部 AdS 扇区中，拓扑黑洞的存在要求非零电电荷（electric charge）。这些结果为四维引力中同时包含挠率与规则构型的精确解提供了新的范例。

Conclusion: 本文通过一个单参数推广的Weyl变换成功地将动态挠率引入共形耦合标量扇区，并在 Einstein-Cartan-Maxwell 理论中获得了包括规则黑洞与可穿越虫洞在内的丰富精确解家族。挠率被证明具有正则化标量场与部分平滑奇点的能力，这为利用挠率改善经典引力奇点问题提供了新的理论支撑。此外，AdS 扇区中拓扑黑洞对电荷的依赖关系进一步揭示了挠率与电磁场耦合下的独特约束条件。

Abstract: We formulate a one-parameter extension of Weyl transformations in first-order gravity and show that it defines a conformally coupled scalar sector with dynamical torsion. The construction reduces to the standard torsionless conformal coupling in the limit $λ\to 1$. In the corresponding Einstein-Cartan-Maxwell theory, we derive exact static solutions in asymptotically flat and asymptotically locally AdS spacetimes. These solutions describe scalar-dressed black holes, regular black holes, and traversable wormholes, depending on the values of the integration constants and of the deformation parameter. We show that torsion can regularize the scalar field and, for suitable branches, also improve the geometric singularity structure. In the AdS sector, the existence of topological black holes requires a nonvanishing electric charge. These results provide new exact examples of regular and torsional configurations in four-dimensional gravity.

### [11] [Nonlinear Breit-Wheeler Process Driven by Intense Squeezed Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26706)
*Xin Ge,Kai-Hong Zhuang,Pei-Lun He,Yue-Yue Chen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛框架研究了压缩相干驱动场（squeezed coherent driving field）的统计特性如何改变非线性Breit-Wheeler过程的电子-正电子对产生，发现即使在固定平均电场振幅下，压缩相干态的统计涨落也显著影响粒子对的能谱、角分布和自旋极化等可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偏振分辨的蒙特卡洛框架（polarization-resolved Monte Carlo framework），结合基于Husimi Q函数（Husimi Q-function）推导的场振幅分布进行随机平均，模拟伽马光子与压缩光（squeezed light）的碰撞过程。

Result: 研究发现三个显著效应：谐波结构平滑化、高阶多光子通道增强、以及由于强场实现提升有效质量阈值（dressed-mass threshold）导致的单激光光子吸收通道抑制；正电子极化度随压缩参数（squeezing parameter）单调增加，角分布随大场振幅统计权重增大而展宽。

Conclusion: 压缩相干态固有的统计涨落可以在固定平均电场振幅下显著改变强场对产生过程中的能谱、角分布和自旋分辨可观测量，揭示了源态相关的场统计特性与强场对产生可观测量之间的直接联系，为研究驱动场的压缩态制备如何影响高能QED过程提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The nonlinear Breit-Wheeler process is a fundamental phenomenon of strong-field quantum electrodynamics and is usually studied for classically prescribed laser backgrounds. Here we examine how the statistical properties of a squeezed coherent driving field modify nonlinear Breit-Wheeler pair production. Using a polarization-resolved Monte Carlo framework with stochastic averaging over the field-amplitude distribution derived from the Husimi Q-function, we simulate collisions of gamma photons with squeezed light and identify clear source-state-dependent modifications of the pair production signal. These effects include the smoothing of harmonic structure, the enhancement of higher-order multiphoton channels, and the suppression of the single-laser-photon absorption channel when stronger-field realizations raise the dressed-mass threshold. Within the selected spectral window, the degree of positron polarization increases monotonically with the squeezing parameter, while the angular distributions broaden as the statistical weight of larger field amplitudes increases. Our results show that, even at fixed mean electric-field amplitude, the statistical fluctuations inherent to the squeezed coherent state can substantially reshape spectral, angular, and spin-resolved observables in strong-field pair production. These findings illustrate a direct link between source-state-dependent field statistics and strong-field pair production observables, and provide a theoretical framework for studying how squeezed-state preparation of the driving field can influence high-energy QED processes.

### [12] [Thermal Casimir Effect in A Schwarzschild-like Wormhole Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26743)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the finite-temperature Casimir effect for a massless scalar field confined between two parallel plates in a Schwarzschild-like wormhole spacetime. Thermodynamic quantities derived from the Casimir free energy, namely, the renormalized Casimir entropy, internal energy, and heat capacity at constant volume, exhibit distinct temperature dependence. ### [13] [Null Strings Gauged and Reloaded, II: Consistent Classical Treatment of the Null Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26822)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示零弦（null strings）相较于拉伸弦（tensile strings）在规范对称性结构上的本质差异，特别是探索Carroll-Weyl规范对称性是否以及为何必须在零弦理论中出现。

Method: 采用哈密顿分析（Hamiltonian analysis）方法对约束/规范系统（constrained/gauged systems）进行详细处理；通过比较超相对论Carroll极限（ultra-relativistic Carrollian limit）下的对称性代数，论证Carroll-Weyl规范对称性的必然性。

Result: 零弦展现出一种无法从拉伸弦的Carroll极限导出的额外规范对称性——Carroll-Weyl规范对称性；约束代数的结构因此从标准BMS₃代数扩展为由一个权重一算符（weight one operator）扩展的BMS₃代数。

Conclusion: Carroll-Weyl规范对称性是零弦理论内在且必要的对称性，这一发现修正了关于零弦约束代数结构的已有认识，即必须采用扩展BMS₃代数而非其Carroll极限形式。

Abstract: We observed that the null strings, tensionless strings with Carrollian worldsheets, exhibit an extra gauge symmetry, \textit{Carroll-Weyl} gauge symmetry, which cannot be obtained from ultra-relativistic Carrollian limit of tensile strings. Due to the existence of this symmetry, the BMS$_3$ algebra of constraints, which is obtained as the Carrollian limit of two Virasoro algebras of the standard tensile strings, should be replaced with an BMS$_3$ algebra extended by a weight one operator. To establish further the existence and necessity of the Carroll-Weyl gauge symmetry, we carefully work through Hamiltonian analyses of constrained/gauged systems. We also discuss the extended BMS$_3$ algebra of constraints.

### [14] [A universal geometric mechanism for chaos-bound violations in black hole spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26829)
*Terkaa Victor Targema,Kazuharu Bamba,Usman Zafar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了爱因斯坦引力、标量-张量引力及高阶曲率引力中广泛黑洞解的类圆测地线不稳定性，发现Maldacena-Shenker-Stanford（MSS）混沌界限的违反由不稳定圆轨道与近极端视界结构的相对行为决定，并据此提出一个直接从光子球（photon-sphere）和视界结构判断MSS界限适用性的几何猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多种黑洞时空中已观察到MSS混沌界限的违反，但其物理起源尚不明确，尤其不清楚这些违反源于广义相对论的修正，还是反映了黑洞时空的更基本特征。

Method: 在爱因斯坦引力、标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）和高阶曲率引力（higher-curvature gravity）中，系统研究了一类广泛黑洞解的圆类测地线不稳定性（instability of circular geodesics），分析不稳定圆轨道与近极端（near-extremal）视界结构的相对关系。

Result: 当相关轨道在表面引力（surface gravity）趋于零时仍保持在视界之外，不稳定性尺度持续存在，可违反混沌界限；当轨道趋近退化视界（degenerate horizon）时，不稳定性因发散的重力时间膨胀（gravitational time dilation）而被压制，最终导致界限饱和。据此提出一个直接从光子球与视界结构判断MSS界限适用性的几何猜想。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一个决定MSS界限在黑洞时空中适用性的普遍几何判据（universal geometric criterion），表明将量子混沌界限推广到经典引力环境存在一个基本约束。

Abstract: Violation of the Maldacena-Shenker-Stanford (MSS) chaos bound has been observed in various black hole spacetimes, but its physical origin remains unclear. In particular, it is uncertain whether these violations arise from modifications of general relativity or reflect a more fundamental feature of black hole spacetimes. In this work, we systematically investigate the instability of circular geodesics across a broad class of black hole solutions in Einstein, scalar-tensor, and higher-curvature gravity. We show that the violations are governed by the relative behavior of unstable circular orbits and the horizon structure in near-extremal regimes. When the relevant orbit remains outside the horizon as the surface gravity vanishes, the instability scale persists, and the chaos bound can be violated. On the other hand, as the orbit approaches the degenerate horizon, the instability becomes suppressed by the associated divergent gravitational time dilation, ultimately leading to saturation of the bound. Motivated by these results, we propose a geometric conjecture that determines the applicability of the MSS bound directly from the photon-sphere and horizon structure of the spacetime. Our findings identify a universal geometric criterion that governs the applicability of the MSS bound in black hole spacetimes, revealing a fundamental constraint on extending the quantum chaos bound to classical gravitational settings.

### [15] [A reparametrization invariant nonabelian surface holonomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26853)
*Dongsu Bak,Andreas Gustavsson*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于 $U(N)$ 群环代数的单形式规范势构造的非阿贝尔曲面和乐（nonabelian surface holonomy），用于平行输运非阿贝尔弦（nonabelian string），并证明该曲面和乐具有曲面重参数化不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统规范理论中的和乐（holonomy）概念局限于线（loop）层面，而弦理论或高维扩展规范场论需要曲面上的平行输运。本文旨在构造一种非阿贝尔的曲面和乐，以推广平行输运到弦（string）对象，同时保持对曲面重参数化的不变性。

Method: 采用取值于 $U(N)$ 规范群环代数（loop algebra）的单形式规范势（one-form gauge potential），基于该代数结构定义曲面上的非阿贝尔平行输运，并分析其变换性质。

Result: 成功构造了一种非阿贝尔曲面和乐，能够平行输运非阿贝尔弦。尽管在构造过程中该不变性并非显式，但最终证明了该曲面和乐在曲面的重参数化（reparametrization）下保持不变。

Conclusion: 该构造为非阿贝尔弦的平行输运提供了严格的曲面和乐框架，并保证了重参数化不变性，为进一步研究高维规范理论与弦理论中的非阿贝尔结构奠定了基础。

Abstract: We introduce a nonabelian surface holonomy that is constructed from a one-form gauge potential that takes values in a loop algebra of the $U(N)$ gauge group. The surface holonomy parallel transports a nonabelian string. Although it is not manifest in our formulation, we will see that our nonabelian surface holonomy is invariant under reparametrizations of the surface.

</details>


### [16] [Constrained Symplectic Quantization II: The Free Scalar Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26892)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将有约束辛量化（constrained symplectic quantization）从量子力学框架推广到闵可夫斯基时空中的相对论标量量子场论，通过解析延拓与约束条件定义稳定的内蕴时间轨迹和收敛的微正则泛函积分，证明在连续极限下微正则生成泛函可还原为费曼生成泛函（Feynman generating functional），并在1+1维自由标量场中通过数值模拟验证了实时间两点关联函数、等时对易关系及Dyson-Schwinger方程。

Method: 通过将场和作用量从实轴 $\mathbb{R}$ 解析延拓至复数域 $\mathbb{C}$，并引入约束条件来选择稳定的内蕴时间（intrinsic time）轨迹，同时定义对应的微正则泛函（microcanonical functional）的收敛积分环路。在1+1维自由标量场情形下，推导有约束运动方程并执行数值模拟。

Result: 在连续极限下，微正则生成泛函可还原为费曼生成泛函。数值验证了实时间两点关联函数（real-time two-point correlators）、等时对易关系（equal-time commutator relations）以及包含接触项（contact terms）的Dyson-Schwinger方程。

Conclusion: 有约束辛量化框架能够成功推广至闵可夫斯基时空的标量场论，并在数值上复现了量子场论的关键时序关联与代数结构。

Abstract: Constrained symplectic quantization is a functional formulation of quantum field theory in which quantum fluctuations are sampled through a deterministic Hamiltonian flow in an auxiliary intrinsic time $τ$. In this paper we extend the quantum-mechanical framework introduced in [1] to a relativistic scalar quantum field theory in Minkowski space-time. The construction is based on the analytic continuation of fields and action from $\mathbb{R}$ to $\mathbb{C}$ together with constraints that select stable intrinsic-time trajectories and, at the same time, define convergent integration cycles for the corresponding microcanonical functional. We show that, in the continuum limit, the microcanonical generating functional reproduces the Feynman generating functional. For the free scalar field in $1+1$ dimensions we derive the constrained equations of motion, implement the resulting dynamics numerically, and verify real-time two-point correlators, equal-time commutator relations, and Dyson--Schwinger equations including the expected contact terms.

Method: 将标量耦合直接引入能量泛函的动能（kinetic）和梯度（gradient）贡献中，构造广义场论模型，并在可分离（separable）情形下将其解释为具有杂质的几何约束有效单场理论（geometrically-constrained effective one-field theories with impurities）。

Abstract: This short communication investigates impurity coupling in generalized field theories where scalar coupling is introduced directly at the level of the kinetic and gradient contributions of the energy. We show that the fundamental aspects of the original theory, which has been previously investigated in the impurity-free setting, can be extended to the inhomogeneous scenario. In particular, an interpretation in terms of geometrically-constrained effective one-field theories with impurities is possible in the separable case. We show that BPS multi-kink configurations are possible in the model, as well as in the usual half-BPS scalar theories.

We derive the analytic form of the abelian vertices and identify the corresponding analytic higher-spin $\mathcal{N}=2$ supercurrents. We show that the vertex structure is fully determined by the analytic supercurrents $J^{++}_{α(s-1)\dotα(s-1)}$, $J^+_{α(s-1)\dotα(s-2)}$, and $\bar{J}^+_{α(s-2)\dotα(s-1)}$. The analytic form of the vertices provides a simple framework for analyzing their component structure. As an example, we explore the component content of such interactions on the Bel--Robinson diagonal. Using the superfield inverse Noether procedure, we study higher-spin gauge transformations for the $\mathcal{N}=2$ vector multiplet associated with the $(\mathbf{s}, \mathbf{1}, \mathbf{1})$ interaction. *K. B. Alkalaev,Semyon Mandrygin,Vladimir Samsonov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用影子形式（shadow formalism），建立了平直时空、热场和缺陷背景下的共形分波（conformal partial waves）之间的对应关系，展示了热一块（thermal one-point）块可通过特定算子配置从平直四点和缺陷两点块导出，并给出了热Casimir方程与平直Casimir系统的约化关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）中的共形分波在不同背景（平直、热场、缺陷）下缺乏系统的对应关系，限制了跨背景下关联函数的统一理解与计算。

Method: 采用影子形式（shadow formalism）建立映射；通过考虑特定算子配置，将热场下一标量单点块（thermal one-point block）系统地从平直空间四点块（four-point flat-space block）和缺陷两点块（defect two-point block）导出；利用该框架，将热Casimir方程（thermal Casimir equation）推导为平直空间Casimir系统（flat-space Casimir system）的对角约化（diagonal reduction）。

Result: 热场中标量单点块可由平直空间四点块和缺陷两点块通过算子配置得到；热Casimir方程是平直Casimir系统的对角约化形式，无需引入化学势；自旋为l的交换算子对应的缺陷两点块等价于外场为自旋l算子的热场单点块。

Conclusion: 不同背景下的共形分波之间存在系统的对应关系，该框架为统一处理平直、热场和缺陷CFT中的关联函数提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between conformal partial waves on flat, thermal, and defect backgrounds using the shadow formalism. We demonstrate that scalar one-point thermal blocks can be systematically obtained from their four-point flat-space and two-point defect counterparts by considering specific operator configurations. This framework allows us to derive the thermal Casimir equation as a diagonal reduction of the flat-space Casimir system without introducing chemical potentials. We further show that defect two-point blocks with a spin-$l$ exchange operator correspond to thermal one-point blocks for an external spin-$l$ operator.

### [20] [Wilson coefficients from a non-renormalization theorem in 2D SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27359)
*Kabir Bajaj*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过非重整化（non-renormalization）论证，从紫外（UV）规范理论出发，确定了矩阵弦论（matrix string theory）中红外（IR）固定点附近主导不可约微扰——Dijkgraaf-Verlinde-Verlinde 算符——的未知 Wilson 系数，结果与矩阵弦论猜想一致，并为杨-米尔斯耦合常数与弦耦合常数之间的关系提供了第一性原理的检验。

Method: 利用来自紫外规范理论的非重整化（non-renormalization）论证来推导红外固定点处 Dijkgraaf-Verlinde-Verlinde 算符的 Wilson 系数。该方法避免了对未知高阶修正的直接计算，仅基于理论中不受量子修正的保护性质来提取系数。

Result: 成功确定了 Dijkgraaf-Verlinde-Verlinde 算符的 Wilson 系数，结果与矩阵弦论猜想一致，从而为杨-米尔斯耦合常数（g_YM）与弦耦合常数之间的关系提供了来自第一性原理（first-principles）的检验。

Conclusion: 该结果验证了矩阵弦论对偶性，并表明非重整化论证可以有效地用于确定红外有效理论中的 Wilson 系数。文中还讨论了利用类似方法进一步确定其他 Wilson 系数的前景。

Abstract: Matrix string theory (arXiv:hep-th/9703030, arXiv:hep-th/9701025, arXiv:hep-th/9710009) is a conjectured duality between two-dimensional maximally supersymmetric $U(N)$ Yang-Mills theory and type-IIA string theory in ten-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. The IR description of this gauge theory is governed by the symmetric product orbifold $(\mathbb{R}^8)^N/S_N$ CFT. The leading irrelevant deformation from this IR fixed point is the Dijkgraaf-Verlinde-Verlinde operator, which comes with an unknown Wilson coefficient. We determine this coefficient using non-renormalization arguments from the UV gauge theory. The result is consistent with the matrix string theory conjecture and gives a first-principles check of the relation between $g_{\rm YM}$ and the string coupling. We also comment on the prospects for fixing further Wilson coefficients using similar methods.

### [21] [Spectral Cut-off Oscillatory Integrals for Non-Autonomous Hamiltonian Evolution Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26899)
*Jean-Pierre Magnot*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于谱截断（spectral cut-off）的构造方法，用于处理与非自治哈密顿量演化方程相关的实时振荡积分，证明了截断振幅收敛到原始强解，并在周期情形下联系到Floquet-Magnus展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非自治哈密顿量演化方程对应的实时振荡积分缺乏直接的泛函积分构造，尤其是当哈密顿量无界时，标准的有限维逼近与收敛性分析面临困难。

Method: 选取一个正自伴参考算子H_0，利用其谱投影P_N构造有限维截断哈密顿量H_N(t)=P_N H(t)P_N，对应传播子由时间分片（time-sliced）的有限维振荡积分表示；在适当的H_0-相对正则性与稳定性假设下，证明截断振幅收敛到原方程的强解。

Result: 证明了谱截断后的有限维振荡振幅在合适的假设下收敛到原非自治哈密顿量演化方程的强解；在周期情形下，该构造给出了有限维有效哈密顿量，为无界算子的Floquet-Magnus展开提供了自然桥梁。

Conclusion: 谱截断构造为实时振荡积分提供了一种系统的有限维逼近方案，未来可用于定义实时振幅的重整化迹（renormalized trace）。

Abstract: We develop a spectral cut-off construction of real-time oscillatory integrals associated with non-autonomous Hamiltonian evolution equations. Let \(H_0\) be a positive self-adjoint reference operator on a Hilbert space \(\Hilb\), and let \(P_N=\mathbf 1_{[0,N]}(H_0)\) be its spectral projections. For a time-dependent family of generally unbounded Hamiltonians \(H(t)\), we consider the finite-dimensional cut-off Hamiltonians \[
  H_N(t)=P_NH(t)P_N . \] The corresponding propagators are represented by time-sliced finite dimensional oscillatory integrals. Under suitable \(H_0\)-relative regularity and stability assumptions, we prove convergence of these cut-off oscillatory amplitudes to the strong solution of the original Hamiltonian evolution equation \[
  \ii \partial_t u(t)=H(t)u(t). \] In the periodic case, the same construction yields finite-dimensional effective Hamiltonians and provides a natural bridge with the Floquet--Magnus expansion for unbounded operators. We also discuss how spectral cut-offs may later be used to define renormalized traces of real-time amplitudes.

### [22] [MARUT: An Exascale-Ready, GPU-Accelerated High-Order CFD Framework with AMR for High-Speed Flows and Finite-Rate Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26388)
*Trishit Mondal,Ameya D. Jagtap*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 MARUT，一个可扩展的多 GPU 计算流体动力学（computational fluid dynamics, CFD）框架，用于高保真模拟从亚音速到高超声速的可压缩流动，涵盖具有有限速率化学反应的化学非平衡流与自适应网格细化（adaptive mesh refinement, AMR）。该框架采用基于 MPI 的分布式内存并行架构并在 NVIDIA GPU 上原生实现，结合高阶谱间断伽辽金离散化（spectral discontinuous Galerkin discretisation）与强稳定性保持龙格-库塔时间积分（strong-stability-preserving Runge–Kutta time integration），实现了低耗散、高分辨率的激波、涡结构及反应界面捕捉。动态 AMR 将计算资源高效集中于局部物理复杂区域，大幅降低计算成本同时保持求解精度。MARUT 通过 GPU 驻留计算与可扩展 MPI 通信策略维持强并行效率，在多个 GPU 上实现近线性强扩展。求解器在包含无粘与反应可压缩流动的多个典型基准问题上得到验证，数值预测与已知参考解高度吻合。该框架还反映了计算科学向模块化、自适应及 AI 兼容仿真生态系统的更广泛转型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发能够在新兴异构超级计算架构上解析强非线性、多尺度流动物理的数值精确且计算可扩展的算法，是当代科学计算中的核心挑战。

Method: 基于分布式内存 MPI 并行基础设施并在 NVIDIA GPU 上原生实现；采用高阶谱间断伽辽金离散化与强稳定性保持龙格-库塔时间积分相结合的方法；引入动态自适应网格细化（AMR）以集中计算资源于局部复杂区域；通过 GPU 驻留计算与可扩展 MPI 通信策略维持并行效率。

Result: 在多个 GPU 上实现了近线性强扩展（near-linear strong scaling）；在涉及无粘与反应可压缩流动的典型基准问题（涵盖亚音速、跨音速、超音速及高超声速构型，包含多物种非平衡化学）上，数值预测与已知参考解高度吻合。

Conclusion: MARUT 框架不仅展现了优异的性能特征，还反映了计算科学向模块化、自适应及 AI 兼容仿真生态系统的更广泛转型。

Abstract: We present \texttt{MARUT}, a scalable multi-GPU computational fluid dynamics (CFD) framework designed for high-fidelity simulations of compressible flows spanning subsonic to hypersonic regimes, including chemically reacting nonequilibrium flows with finite-rate chemistry and adaptive mesh refinement (AMR). The framework addresses a central challenge in contemporary scientific computing: the development of numerically accurate and computationally scalable algorithms capable of resolving strongly nonlinear, multiscale flow physics on emerging heterogeneous supercomputing architectures. Built around a distributed-memory MPI-parallel infrastructure and implemented natively on NVIDIA GPUs, \texttt{MARUT} combines high-order spectral discontinuous Galerkin discretisations with strong-stability-preserving Runge--Kutta time integration to achieve low-dissipation and high-resolution representation of shocks, vortical structures and reactive interfaces. Dynamic AMR further enables efficient concentration of computational resources in localized regions of physical complexity, thereby substantially reducing computational cost while preserving solution fidelity. \texttt{MARUT} is designed to maintain strong parallel efficiency through GPU-resident computations and scalable MPI communication strategies, achieving near-linear strong scaling across multiple GPUs. The solver is validated against a broad suite of canonical benchmark problems involving inviscid and reactive compressible flows, including subsonic, transonic, supersonic and hypersonic configurations with multi-species nonequilibrium chemistry, where the numerical predictions show close agreement with established reference solutions. Beyond its immediate performance characteristics, the framework reflects the broader transition of computational science towards modular, adaptive and AI-compatible simulation ecosystems.

</details>

### [23] [GWTC-5.0: Population Properties of Merging Compact Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27226)

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 基于引力波瞬变目录5.0（GWTC-5.0）中267个致密双星并合事件，推断双黑洞（binary black hole）并合的总体性质、子群体特征、质量谱结构、自旋分布及并合通道限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用当前最大的引力波事件样本（267个并合事件）系统性地推断致密双星并合的群体性质（population properties），特别是双黑洞并合的率、质量分布、自旋分布及天体物理起源通道。

Method: 对GWTC-5.0中的267个并合事件进行分层贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference），构建并拟合质量分布、自旋分布和质量比分布等群体模型。

Result: 双黑洞并合率在红移z=0.2处为27.5–49.4 Gpc⁻³ yr⁻¹（90%置信水平）；发现存在一个包含快速自旋黑洞（无量纲自旋χ~0.7）的子群体，出现在~10–20 M⊙和~45 M⊙以上两个质量区间，总并合率为0.2–3.11 Gpc⁻³ yr⁻¹；质量谱在~10 M⊙处存在峰值，在~35 M⊙处斜率变化；~35 M⊙的黑洞倾向于与相近质量伴星配对；有效旋进自旋（effective inspiral spin）分布不对称于零，至少9%的并合来自存在自旋-轨道对齐（spin-orbit alignment）偏好

Conclusion: 双黑洞并合群体存在层次并合（hierarchical merger）等不同形成通道的特征信号，质量谱结构暗示黑洞形成过程存在特征质量标度，自旋分布的不对称性表明部分并合通道具有自旋-轨道对齐偏好。

Abstract: We present the population properties of merging compact binaries inferred using 267 mergers from the cumulative Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog 5.0. As this data set contains no new sources with a neutron star, we primarily focus on the properties of the binary black hole mergers. We infer the merger rate of binary black holes with component masses between $2.5\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $ and $200\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $ to be $27.5\text{--} 49.4 \, \mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\,\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (all intervals at $90\%$ credible levels) at redshift $z = 0.2$. We find evidence for a subpopulation of binary black hole mergers that host a rapidly spinning black hole (dimensionless spins $χ\sim 0.7$), consistent with signatures of hierarchical mergers. We find that these occur at two mass scales, the first at primary masses $\sim 10$--$20\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $ and the second above $\sim 45\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $, and we estimate their total rate at $z=0.2$ to be $0.2\text{--} 3.11 \, {\rm Gpc}^{-3} {\rm yr}^{-1}$. We infer that, above $40\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $, the mass distribution of the less massive (secondary) black hole declines more steeply than that of the more massive (primary) one. This is consistent with a flatter mass-ratio distribution and indicates the prevalence of unequal-mass binaries with large primary masses. We find evidence for two features in the black hole mass spectrum: a peak around $10\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $ and a change of slope at around $35\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $. Black holes of $\sim 35\,\mathrm{M}_\odot $ pair preferentially with companions of similar mass. Additionally, we find that the effective inspiral spin distribution of binary black holes is asymmetric about zero, based on which we infer that at least $9 \%$ of mergers occur in channels with some preference for spin-orbit alignment. We find evidence that...

### [24] [Selective Biexciton Generation Under Energy-Time Entangled Quantum Light in Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26466)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量-时间纠缠光子有望突破经典极限控制多光子吸收，但如何利用其量子关联特性在量子受限体系中实现双激子的选择性高效生成尚待探索。

Method: 采用三能级模型（three-level model）分析纠缠光场驱动下双激子生成对光子到达时间纠缠（arrival-time entanglement）和泵浦带宽（pump bandwidth）的非平凡依赖关系，并进一步扩展到包含多激子态的CdSe/CdS核壳量子点（core-shell quantum dots）真实体系。

Result: 增大双光子到达时间纠缠（更接近的到达时间）可增强相长路径干涉（constructive pathway interference）并扩展可访问的激发通道，同时较经典光具有更好的能量守恒激发特性；调整时间关联性质可实现紧邻双激子态的选择性激发。

Conclusion: 纠缠量子光是实现量子受限体系中非线性光学过程选择性激发和调控的有力工具。

Abstract: Energy-time entangled photons provide new opportunities for controlling multiphoton absorption beyond classical limits. Here, we investigate biexciton generation in nanocrystal quantum dots driven by energy-time-entangled quantum light generated via a spontaneous parametric down-conversion process. We show that quantum correlations can enhance biexciton production while suppressing excitonic populations. By employing a three-level model, we demonstrate that biexciton generation depends nontrivially on the photon arrival-time entanglement and the pump bandwidth. Consequently, we find that maximizing efficiency requires an optimally shaped entangled photon field rather than simply scaling parameters for a monotonic improvement. Extending to a realistic CdSe/CdS core-shell quantum dots containing many excitonic states coupled to the quantum field, we demonstrate that increasing the bi-photon arrival time entanglement (closer arrival time) enhances constructive pathway interference and expands accessible excitation channels while preserving a better energy conservation excitation than classical light when generating biexciton. Furthermore, tuning the time correlation properties enables selective excitation of closely spaced biexciton states. These results establish entangled quantum light as a powerful tool for selective excitation and control of nonlinear optical processes in quantum-confined systems.

### [25] [Slave-boson Formalism for Superconducting Pairing at Strong Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26233)
*Sarbajit Mazumdar,Jonas Issing,Jannis Seufert,David Riegler,Peter Wölfle,Ronny Thomale,Michael Klett*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联体系（strongly correlated systems）中超导配对机制尚未完全清楚，特别是在强耦合区域如何将重整化平均场描述与配对透明性统一起来仍是一个挑战。作者受Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子方法本身具有的內禀重整化平均场基态启发，希望建立一种既能捕捉强关联重整化效应、又具备RPA型配对透明性的理论框架。

Method: 采用自旋旋转不变的Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子（slave-boson, SB）方法研究单带Hubbard模型。从鞍点（saddle point）附近的动力学涨落（dynamical fluctuations）构建有效的配对顶点（pairing vertex），并在正方晶格（square lattice）上求解各向异性、频率依赖的能隙方程（anisotropic, frequency-dependent gap equation）。

Result: 该方法在掺杂（doping）、相互作用强度（interaction）、温度（temperature）和实频率能隙结构（real-frequency gap structure）等维度上映射出配对不稳定性（pairing instabilities），其结果与铜氧化物（cuprate）超导体的实验观测定性一致。

Conclusion: 该框架将强关联领域的奴隶玻色子重整化与RPA型配对的透明性有机融合，为在强耦合（strong coupling）下建模多轨道（multi-orbital）超导电性提供了一条可扩展的路径。

Abstract: We study the emergence of superconductivity in the one-band Hubbard model using the spin-rotation-invariant Kotliar-Ruckenstein slave-boson (SB) approach. Motivated by its intrinsically renormalized mean-field ground state, we construct an effective pairing vertex from dynamical fluctuations about the saddle point. Solving the anisotropic, frequency-dependent gap equation on the square lattice, we map the pairing instabilities across doping, interaction, temperature and real-frequency gap structure that qualitatively match experimental cuprate observations. This framework merges strong-correlation SB-type renormalizations with RPA-type pairing transparency, providing a scalable route to modeling multi-orbital superconductivity at strong coupling.

### [26] [Superconductivity-enhanced phonon angular momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26794)
*Natsuki Okada,Philipp Werner,Shintaro Hoshino*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过理论计算研究了超导态中声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）的性质，以外部磁场中的富勒烯（fulleride）化合物为模型系统。研究发现，进入超导态后，磁场诱导的声子角动量显著增强并发生符号反转，其机制可归因于电子带宽与声子能标之间的竞争，以及费米面对费米体积贡献的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超导态中声子角动量的行为，特别是外部磁场下电子-声子耦合如何影响声子角动量的增强与符号反转，从而揭示超导态中电子与晶格自由度之间新的相互作用机制。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，以富勒烯化合物在外加磁场中为模型体系，研究电子轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）通过电子-声子耦合（electron–phonon coupling）转移至声子子系统的过程，并对正常态与超导态的响应函数进行对比。

Result: 在超导态中，磁场诱导的声子角动量显著增强，增强量级约为电子带宽 $D$ 与声子能标 $\omega_1$ 之比 $D/\omega_1$，并且发生符号反转。正常态中主导响应函数的能标是电子带宽 $D$，而超导态中声子能标 $\omega_1$ 进入分母，导致上述增强。符号反转可归因于费米面（Fermi surface）与费米体积（Fermi volume）贡献之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 超导态显著改变了声子角动量的响应特性，包括数量级的增强与符号反转，这为理解超导体系中电子-声子耦合的动力学效应提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the properties of phonon angular momentum in the superconducting state, using fulleride compounds in an external magnetic field as a model system. The electron orbital angular momentum injected by an external field is transferred to the phonon subsystem via electron--phonon coupling. We show that this field-induced phonon angular momentum is significantly enhanced and undergoes a sign reversal upon entering the superconducting state. In the normal state, the dominant energy scale governing the response function is the electronic bandwidth $D$. In the superconducting state, the phonon energy scale $ω_1$ enters the denominator, leading to an enhancement of order $D/ω_1$. The observed sign change in the response can be explained by the competition between Fermi surface and Fermi volume contributions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 测量不同化学计量比MoSi薄膜的临界温度Tc、方块电阻Rs和厚度d，观察其标度行为；通过改变纳米线宽度及入射波长（780–1550 nm）测量偏置依赖计数率曲线，并利用回复电流（return current）测定界面热边界电导β。

Conclusion: MoSi薄膜的化学计量比通过调控Tc、Rs及β等参数显著影响SNSPD性能，低Tc高Rs的富Mo组分有利于实现高灵敏度探测。

Abstract: We report on the impact of the stoichiometry of superconducting MoSi thin films on the performance of superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors (SNSPDs). Specifically, we investigate the relation between the film parameters critical temperature Tc , sheet resistance Rs and superconductor thickness d and observe a universal scaling behavior. To benchmark the performance of SNSPDs fabricated from films having different stoichiometry, we measure the bias dependent count rate curves, while the detector is illuminated with wavelengths between 780 nm and 1550 nm. The detector performance as a function photon energy for different nanowire widths reveals a linear relation between the detection current and the photon energy. Furthermore, we determine the interfacial thermal boundary conductance $β$ between the superconducting thin film and the substrate, by measuring the return current of the SNSPD and find an increase of $β$ with increasing Mo concentration. The highest sensitivity amongst all compared devices is achieved for Mo$_{0.53}$Si$_{0.47}$, with low Tc (4.1 K) and high Rs (397$Ω$/sq) at a film thickness of 5.4 nm.

*Jiance Sun,Ting Zhong,Shoutao Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳可与主族金属在高压下反应生成超导化合物，但高压钾碳化物（potassium carbides）的研究尚不系统且不充分，亟需全面探索。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合先进的群体智能结构预测（swarm intelligence structure prediction）技术，系统研究K-C二元体系在压缩下的结构、电子及超导性质。

Result: 电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）计算表明，高钾浓度的单斜K7C（空间群C2/m）是零维电子化合物超导体（zero-dimensional electride superconductor），在25 GPa下Tc为0.6 K；正交KC（空间群Imma）的Tc随减压升高，归因于声学支和光学支的声子软化（phonon softening），在25 GPa下达到最大Tc为21.4 K。

Conclusion: 该工作为K-C化合物提供了有价值的见解，并拓宽了金属碳化物超导体（metal carbide superconductors）的多样性，尤其Imma KC在低压下实现高Tc的特性具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Carbon possesses remarkable physicochemical properties, enabling main group metals to react with it under high pressure and produce superconducting compounds. However, the research on high-pressure potassium carbides remains still unsystematic and inadequate. Using first-principles calculations and state-of-the-art swarm intelligence structure prediction techniques, we comprehensively explore the binary novel potassium-carbon system and characterize their structural, electronic, and superconducting properties under compression. Calculations of electron-phonon coupling show that monoclinic K7C (space group C2/m) with high K concentration is a zero-dimensional electride superconductor with a transition temperature Tc of 0.6 K at 25 GPa. By contrast, the Tc of orthorhombic KC with symmetry Imma increases upon decompression owing to the phonon softening of both acoustic and optical branches. Impressively, Imma KC reaches a maximum Tc of 21.4 K at 25 GPa, which is highly desirable for low-pressure metallic carbide superconductors. This work provides valuable insights into K-C compounds and broadens the diversity of metal carbide superconductors.

### [29] [Kubo-Ando Means and Rigidity of Quantum Positivity Cones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26272)
*Mohsen Kian*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子正性锥（quantum positivity cones）在非线性算子均值下的稳定性，发现加权算术均值是唯一在所有维度下保持可分锥（separable cone）的Kubo-Ando均值；非算术均值的严格正曲率会违反PPT条件并增加施密特数（Schmidt number），通过Choi-Jamiołkowski对应，进一步指出凸混合是唯一允许的保持纠缠破坏量子信道（entanglement-breaking quantum channels）的Kubo-Ando操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非线性算子均值（尤其是Kubo-Ando均值）如何影响量子正性锥（如可分锥、PPT锥和施密特数锥）的稳定性，以理解量子纠缠与量子信道之间结构的几何与代数约束。

Method: 通过分析算符单调函数（operator monotone functions）在单位元处的曲率，研究Kubo-Ando均值对各类量子正性锥的保持性质；利用Choi-Jamiołkowski对应将几何障碍转换到映射（map-theoretic）框架中。

Result: 加权算术均值是唯一在所有维度下保持可分锥的Kubo-Ando均值；任何非算术均值都会因严格正曲率而在两比特体系中破坏PPT条件，并严格增加施密特数；凸混合是唯一允许的保持纠缠破坏量子信道的Kubo-Ando操作。

Conclusion: Kubo-Ando均值与量子正性锥的相容性存在严格的刚性（rigidity）现象，加权算术均值在保持可分性与纠缠破坏性方面具有独特地位。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of quantum positivity cones under nonlinear operator means. Specifically, we examine how Kubo--Ando means interact with the separable, positive partial transpose (PPT), and Schmidt-number cones. By analyzing the curvature of operator monotone functions at the identity, we give a strict rigidity phenomenon: weighted arithmetic means are the only Kubo--Ando means that preserve the separable cone in all dimensions. We show that the strictly positive curvature of any non-arithmetic mean explicitly forces a violation of the PPT condition, even in the foundational two-qubit setting, and can strictly increase the Schmidt number of the resulting operator. Finally, using the Choi--Jamiołkowski correspondence, we translate these geometric obstructions to the map-theoretic setting, concluding that convex mixing is the uniquely permissible Kubo--Ando operation for preserving entanglement-breaking quantum channels.

</details>


### [30] [Uncertainty Relation for a Single Observable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26331)
*Haruki Yamashita,Aina Mayumi,Gen Kimura*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明单个可观测量（observable）的方差存在一个由可观测量与量子态之间非对易性（noncommutativity）导出的非平凡下界。通过引入经典不确定性概念进一步锐化该下界，并给出了最优系数的显式表达式。工作包括对 Luo 的 Wigner-Yanase 型关系的最优态依赖改进，以及对相干性（coherence）或不对称性（asymmetry）不可消除贡献的直接刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性关系通常被表述为两个或多个可观测量之间的权衡关系，而单个可观测量的不确定性是否具有非平凡的下界尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示单个可观测量的方差同样存在由非对易性导致的固有下界。

Method: 证明单个可观测量的方差存在锐利下界，并通过引入固定态下该可观测量的经典不确定性（classical uncertainty）概念进一步锐化该下界。最优系数由态的最小和最大本征值（eigenvalues）唯一确定。对于量子比特（qubits），锐化后的边界退化为精确恒等式，将方差完全分解为经典部分和非对易部分。

Result: 得到了单个可观测量的最优态依赖下界；包含对 Luo 的 Wigner-Yanase 型关系的最优改进；证明了态相对于可观测量的相干性或不对称性对不确定性存在不可消除的贡献；对于量子比特，方差可精确分解为经典部分与非对易部分；这些单可观测量关系进一步改进了可观测量对（pairs of observables）的乘积形式不确定性关系。

Conclusion: 单个可观测量的不确定性本身即具有非平凡的结构，其下界由可观测量与量子态之间的非对易性决定，且该结构可通过经典与非对易部分的分解得到完整刻画。这些结果不仅深化了对不确定性原理（uncertainty principle）的理解，也为改进多可观测量不确定性关系提供了新途径。

Abstract: Uncertainty relations are usually formulated as trade-off relations between two or more observables. Here we show that the uncertainty of a single observable already has a nontrivial lower bound originating from the noncommutativity between the observable and the quantum state. We prove sharp lower bounds on the variance of a single observable and then sharpen them further by introducing the classical uncertainty of the observable under a fixed state. The optimal coefficient is determined solely by the smallest and largest eigenvalues of the state. Our results include an optimal state-dependent improvement of Luo's Wigner--Yanase-type relation and a direct bound showing that coherence or asymmetry of the state with respect to the observable gives an unavoidable contribution to its uncertainty. For qubits, the sharpened bounds become exact identities, giving a complete decomposition of the variance into classical and noncommutative parts. These single-observable relations also yield improved product-form uncertainty relations for pairs of observables.

</details>


### [31] [Exact Solution for Non-Hermitian Free Fermions: A Case Study of the XY Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26813)
*Yuguan Li,D. C. Liu,Murray T. Batchelor*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究具有开放边界条件的非厄米XY自旋链，通过将各向异性参数延拓至复数值，揭示了其准能谱的自由费米子结构、边界多项式表示的切比雪夫多项式形式、例外点（EP）处的若尔当标准型与广义本征向量的构造，以及EP作为复数各向异性平面中的支点所导致的本征态交换现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非厄米（non-Hermitian）多体系统中例外点（exceptional points, EPs）的解析可控模型，弥补当前对EP物理和非厄米拓扑的研究大多局限于动量空间（momentum-space）描述、缺乏多体可解模型的不足。

Method: 将各向异性参数延拓至复数值，在开放边界条件下分析准哈密顿量（quasi-Hamiltonian）矩阵；利用切比雪夫多项式（Chebyshev polynomial）显式表示开放边界本征向量，以准能量（quasi-energy）$\varepsilon$作为自然谱变量；在EP处通过$\varepsilon$微分构造广义本征向量，导出若尔当标准型（Jordan normal form）。

Result: 非厄米模型的准能谱（quasi-energy spectrum）与厄米模型具有相同的自由费米子结构；在EP处构造了若尔当标准型和广义本征向量，给出了独立多体本征态的正确计数；EP在复数各向异性平面中充当支点（branch point），绕EP一周导致本征能量和本征态的置换。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个可解析控制的多体平台（many-body platform），用于研究EP物理和非厄米拓扑，尤其适用于超越动量空间描述的场景。

Abstract: We consider the non-Hermitian XY spin chain with open boundary conditions when the anisotropy parameter is extended to complex values. By analyzing the quasi-Hamiltonian matrix, we demonstrate that the free-fermion structure of the quasi-energy spectrum coincides with that of the Hermitian model and construct the corresponding biorthogonal fermionic basis away from exceptional points (EPs). We make use of an explicit Chebyshev-polynomial representation of the open-boundary eigenvectors in which the quasi-energy $\varepsilon$ is the natural spectral variable. This quasi-energy polynomial form is particularly useful at EPs, because EPs correspond to repeated roots of the same boundary polynomial, making the construction of generalized eigenvectors by $\varepsilon$-differentiation transparent. At EPs, where the quasi-Hamiltonian becomes defective, we derive the Jordan normal form and construct the associated generalized eigenvectors, which yields the correct counting of independent many-body eigenstates. We further show that EPs act as branch points in the complex anisotropy plane, leading to the characteristic permutation of eigenenergies and eigenstates upon encirclement. The branch-cut structure of the biorthogonal eigenstates provides direct evidence for the exchange of eigenstates when an EP is encircled. These results provide an analytically controlled many-body platform for studying EP physics and non-Hermitian topology beyond momentum-space descriptions.

### [32] [Extremal Marginal States of Maximal Rank in $(d, d+m)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26920)
*Indu Bala,Swapan Rana*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文在(d, d+m)维Hilbert空间中构造了秩为d+m的极值点，参数范围为d≥3、m > (d²-2d-2)/2（d=2时m≥1）。进一步通过分析证明，研究一般𝒞(ρ₁,ρ₂)的极值点可归结为研究约化密度矩阵为对角矩阵（diagonal marginals）的特殊情形𝒞(𝒟₁,𝒟₂)，并假设d₁≤d₂而无失一般性。

Result: 构造出的极值点秩达到可能的最大值d+m，覆盖了所有已知的极值点例子。结果表明，对于每个d₁，除了可能少数有限情形外，几乎在所有情况下极值点的最大秩都能达到。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了大秩极值态在双粒子量子态凸集中普遍存在，并提供了系统性的简化分析框架，将一般约化密度矩阵问题约化到对角矩阵情形，推进了对凸集边界结构的理解。

Abstract: We study the extreme points of the convex set $\mathcal{C}(ρ_1,ρ_2)$ of bipartite quantum states with fixed marginals $ρ_1$ and $ρ_2$. We construct extreme points in $(d,\,d+m)$ dimension, of rank $d+m$, matching the highest possible value, for all $d\geq 3$, $m > \frac{d^2-2d-2}{2}$ (when $d=2$, $m\geq 1$). This proves the existence of extremal states with relatively large rank and also covers all the known examples. We further show that, in order to analyze the extreme points of $\mathcal{C}(ρ_1,ρ_2)$, it is sufficient to study the special case $\mathcal{C}(\mathcal{D}_1,\mathcal{D}_2)$, where the marginals are diagonal. Additionally, we observe that it is sufficient to consider $d_1\leq d_2$. Thus, our results show that apart from possibly a few finite cases, for each $d_1$, the maximal rank is achieved almost all times.

### [33] [Bose-Einstein thermal operators for semidefinite optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27228)
*Michele Minervini,Nana Liu,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了无界正半定锥上的半定规划（SDP）与独立玻色子（bosonic）模式热力学系统之间的数学等价性，将SDP重新表述为玻色子自由能最小化问题，并基于此发展了新的对偶间隙上界、量子相对熵以及混合量子-经典算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半定规划（SDP）求解器的运行时间依赖于原始迹（primal trace）的先验上界，且内点法的对偶间隙（duality gap）在最坏情况下随问题维度线性增长；此外，标准Umegaki相对熵在无界正定锥上可能取负值，缺乏合适的散度（divergence）度量。

Method: 将无界正半定锥上的SDP重新解释为统计力学（statistical mechanics）中独立玻色子模式的热力学系统，优化变量的特征值对应期望占据数（expected occupation numbers），线性目标对应总期望能量，线性等式约束对应守恒的非对易荷（conserved non-commuting charges）。最优原始变量取为由对偶变量参数化的玻色-爱因斯坦热算符（Bose-Einstein thermal operator）形式。基于此，引入玻色-爱因斯坦量子相对熵（Bose-Einstein quantum relative entropy）作为无界正定锥上的Bregman散度。

Result: 证明了依赖于对偶松弛算子（dual slack operator）的基态简并度与谱隙（spectral gap）的近似误差界，改进了一般的线性维度最坏情况对偶间隙。证明了玻色-爱因斯坦量子相对熵在模拟玻色子高斯信道的仿射映射下具有受限单调性（restricted monotonicity）。给出了混合量子-经典算法的运行时间闭式上界，该上界不依赖于原始迹的先验上界，转而依赖于对偶松弛算子的谱结构。

Conclusion: 该工作将SDP理论与量子热力学深刻联系，为正定锥上的优化问题提供了新的正则化视角和算法框架，特别适用于无需迹约束的量子SDP求解场景。

Abstract: We establish that semidefinite programs (SDPs) over the unbounded positive semidefinite cone are mathematically equivalent to thermodynamic systems of independent bosonic modes: the eigenvalues of the optimization variable play the role of expected occupation numbers, the linear objective plays the role of total expected energy, and the linear equality constraints play the role of conserved non-commuting charges. Building on this perspective, we recast general SDPs as bosonic free-energy minimization problems at strictly positive temperature, regularized by the Bose-Einstein entropy; the original SDP is recovered in the zero-temperature limit. The optimal primal variable takes the form of a Bose-Einstein thermal operator parametrized by the dual variables. We prove an approximation-error bound that depends on the ground-space degeneracy and the spectral gap of the dual slack operator, improving on the linear-in-dimension worst-case duality gap of interior-point methods. We also introduce the Bose-Einstein quantum relative entropy as a Bregman divergence on the unbounded positive semidefinite cone, generated by the negative Bose-Einstein entropy. We propose it as a natural divergence for unnormalized positive operators, for which the standard Umegaki relative entropy can become negative, and we show that it satisfies a restricted monotonicity property under affine maps modeling bosonic Gaussian channels. Finally, we develop hybrid quantum-classical algorithms for the regularized SDP using only Hamiltonian simulation, Hadamard tests, and classical sampling, and bound their runtime in closed form. Unlike existing quantum SDP solvers, whose runtimes scale polynomially with an a priori upper bound on the primal trace, our framework operates directly on the unbounded cone, replacing this bound with a dependence on the spectral structure of the dual slack operator.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者在矩阵乘积态框架下构造了显式的局域算子，其期望值能够再现扭场的作用。该构造在可注入性极限下精确成立，且要求张量选在正交中心（center of orthogonality）。数值测试在横场伊辛模型上进行，验证了方法随着可注入性尺度的逼近而快速收敛到精确纠缠熵。

Result: 数值结果表明，在横场伊辛模型中，该方法在达到可注入性尺度后迅速收敛至精确纠缠熵。此外，由较小参考系统确定的扭算子（twist operators），当参考尺寸超过关联长度（correlation length）所表征的特征尺度后，可 reliably 迁移至更大系统。

Conclusion: 由于所构造的算子可分解为有限数量的局域可观测量（local observables），该研究为在量子模拟器中探测纠缠提供了一种可扩展且实验可行的框架。

Abstract: Twist fields are a powerful formal tool to compute Rényi entropies in quantum many-body systems, but their conventional formulation in tensor network states involves operations acting on virtual degrees of freedom, which are not directly accessible in experiments. In this work, we construct explicit local operators acting on the physical Hilbert space whose expectation values reproduce the action of twist fields in matrix product states. Our construction is exact in the injectivity limit and when the tensor is chosen at the center of orthogonality, and provides a direct operational method to evaluate Rényi entropies without accessing auxiliary tensor indices. We test our formulation numerically in the transverse-field Ising model, demonstrating rapid convergence to the exact entanglement entropy as the injectivity scale is reached. Furthermore, we show that twist operators determined from relatively small reference systems can be reliably transferred to larger systems, once the reference size exceeds a characteristic scale set by the correlation length. Since the resulting operators admit a decomposition in terms of a finite number of local observables, our results provide a scalable and experimentally accessible framework to probe entanglement in quantum simulators.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) 方程描述，分析了通用多模系统（multimode systems），推导了白色热噪声下双线性相互作用的保可分性条件（separability-preserving condition）。

Result: (1) 推导出白色热噪声下双线性相互作用的纠缠产生普适条件；(2) 对于引力诱导纠缠，引力相互作用必须主导热噪声才能产生纠缠；(3) 该界限无法通过改变初始态或引入中介系统来放宽，尽管这些手段可以增强已产生纠缠的纠缠量。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了热环境中纠缠产生协议（entanglement-generation protocols）的一般限制，表明在热噪声环境下存在不可放松的纠缠产生阈值。

Abstract: We derive a universal condition for entanglement generation under general bilinear interactions in the presence of white thermal noise. While various protocols have been proposed to enhance the amount of generated entanglement, it remains unclear whether they can also relax the threshold for entanglement generation itself. Using a Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad description, we analyze general multimode systems and derive a separability-preserving condition for bilinear interactions under white thermal noise. As an application to gravity-induced entanglement, we show that the gravitational interaction must dominate over thermal noise for entanglement to arise. In particular, this bound cannot be relaxed by changing the initial state or by introducing mediator systems, although such ingredients may enhance the amount of entanglement once it is generated. These results establish a general limitation on entanglement-generation protocols in thermal environments.

### [36] [Amplification and generation bounds of gravity-induced entanglement in pulsed optomechanical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26240)
*Daisuke Miki,Alfred Li,Yanbei Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了两个脉冲光机械系统（pulsed optomechanical systems）之间由引力诱导的纠缠（gravity-induced entanglement），分析了输入态的压缩或Fock态如何放大纠缠，并建立了纠缠生成的阈值条件$g_G > 2γ_m N_{\rm th}$，该阈值不受输入态选择影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两个红失谐（red-detuned）脉冲光机械系统，其质量通过相互引力耦合；每个系统使用两个矩形脉冲，第一个脉冲将非经典态（nonclassical state）印刻到机械模式（mechanical modes）上，第二个脉冲将引力生成的纠缠读取到出射光上。

Result: 压缩态或Fock态输入可以放大纠缠量，但纠缠生成的阈值由引力耦合强度与热退相干（thermal decoherence）之间的竞争决定，即$g_G > 2γ_m N_{\rm th}$，该阈值不受输入态选择影响；该阈值对双模高斯输入（two-mode Gaussian inputs）和Fock态输入均成立；非完美探测会改变阈值，并确定了纠缠湮灭（entanglement-annihilating）和纠缠破坏（entanglement-breaking）区域，这些区域由相互作用时间内累积的热退相干决定，与引力耦合无关。

Conclusion: 引力诱导的光机械纠缠可以通过输入非经典态来放大，但纠缠生成的本质阈值由热退相干主导，无法通过改变输入态来降低；非完美探测进一步影响这一阈值，并揭示了纠缠存在的参数边界。

Abstract: We investigate gravity-induced entanglement between the output optical fields of two red-detuned pulsed optomechanical systems with their masses coupled by mutual gravitational interaction. For each individual system, the optomechanical interaction realizes a beam-splitter state swap between an incident optical pulse and its mechanical mode. Using two rectangular pulses for each system -- the first to imprint a nonclassical state on the mechanical modes and the second to read the gravitationally generated entanglement back onto the outgoing light -- we show that the amount of entanglement can be amplified by preparing the input in a squeezed or Fock state. However, the threshold for entanglement generation is set by the competition between the gravitational coupling and thermal decoherence, $g_G>2γ_m N_{\rm th}$, and cannot be lowered by any choice of input state. We prove this bound for two-mode Gaussian inputs and show that it continues to hold for Fock-state inputs. We further analyze how imperfect detection modifies the threshold and identify the entanglement-annihilating and entanglement-breaking regimes, which are set by the thermal decoherence accumulated over the interaction time, independent of the gravitational coupling.

### [37] [AI-Enabled Decoding of Qubit Loss for Quantum Error-Correcting Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14269)

Abstract: Qubit loss is a major source of error in quantum computation, as it invalidates the algebraic structure of the standard stabilizer formalism for quantum error-correcting codes. On the one hand, it complicates decoding; on the other hand, it introduces stochastic flicker patterns in stabilizers as a hallmark of qubit loss. Here, we develop an artificial-intelligence-enabled decoder based on a spatiotemporal Graph Neural Network (STGNN) architecture to extract spatial and temporal correlations from syndrome histories. Our decoder performs a dual-head task, simultaneously correcting standard Pauli errors and identifying the locations of qubit loss. Our decoder achieves significantly higher logical accuracy than both the traditional minimum-weight perfect matching (MWPM) algorithm and even delayed-erasure MWPM decoders that use qubit loss information from the final round as input. Our decoder can also identify more than 90% of loss locations after accumulating stabilizer measurements over the subsequent ten rounds, thereby facilitating qubit reinitialization, for instance, via the continuous loading technique on the atom array platform. For both tasks, our STGNN performs nearly identically to a modified version of AlphaQubit, but it employs a parallel input structure, giving it an advantage in inference time over modified AlphaQubit's recurrent input structure. This work provides a robust and scalable framework for correcting qubit loss errors, paving the way for more efficient fault-tolerant quantum computation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在受控模型中，反馈驱动下边界杂质与体态杂质均发生相变；在幺正粒子与算子模型中，边界杂质导致了从饱和（saturation）到持续增长与加扰（sustained growth and scrambling）的类似相变。

Abstract: We study impurity-induced particle growth and scrambling in clean one-dimensional free-fermion systems. We show that a single local impurity can act as a branching source: particle or operator weight propagates coherently into the free bulk, returns to the impurity, and is locally converted into additional degrees of freedom. We develop this branching picture in three complementary settings: a monitored free-fermion model with feedback, a fully unitary interacting particle model, and Heisenberg operator dynamics with an interacting impurity. In the monitored model, we find a feedback-driven transition for both boundary and bulk impurities. In the unitary particle and operator models, a boundary impurity gives rise to an analogous transition from saturation to sustained growth and scrambling. These results reveal how a single impurity can generate complex many-body dynamics in an otherwise clean and free quantum system.

### [39] [Exact strong zero modes are generic in integrable spin systems with large anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26205)
*Sascha Gehrmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现，在一大类具有各向异性相互作用的可积自旋模型中，精确强零模（exact strong zero modes, ESZMs）普遍存在，其产生机制可追溯至底层R-矩阵和K-矩阵的两个代数性质——谱参数的准周期性（quasi-periodicity）和无迹性（tracelessness），从而建立了一个统一的、与模型无关的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于可积系统中精确强零模（ESZM）的构造采用逐模型（model-by-model）的方式，缺乏一个统一的共同框架，因此需要建立更具普适性的理论机制来解释ESZM的起源。

Method: 论文通过分析可积自旋模型底层R-矩阵和K-矩阵的代数结构，识别出两个关键性质——谱参数的准周期性和无迹性——并证明这两个性质足以导出ESZM的存在性，从而构建了一个模型无关（model-independent）的统一框架。

Result: 该框架不仅将已知的XXZ链及其更高自旋推广中的ESZM作为特例加以涵盖，还成功预测了在以往未被识别的模型中同样存在ESZM。

Conclusion: ESZM的生成机制可以被归结为可积结构中R-矩阵与K-矩阵的代数性质，这为理解边界局域化算符的长时相干行为提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: Strong zero modes (SZMs) are edge-localized operators that commute with the Hamiltonian up to corrections exponentially small in system size, yielding anomalously long edge coherence times. In some settings, notably certain integrable models, this commutator can be made to vanish exactly at finite size, defining an exact SZM (ESZM). Existing ESZM constructions in the integrable setting, however, have proceeded model by model and have not been unified into a common framework. Here, I show that ESZMs arise generically in a broad family of integrable spin models with anisotropic interactions. Their existence follows from two algebraic properties of the underlying R- and K-matrices -- quasi-periodicity in the spectral parameter and tracelessness, respectively -- providing a uniform, model-independent mechanism. The framework recovers the known ESZM in XXZ chain and its higher-spin generalizations as special cases and predicts ESZMs in previously unrecognized models.

</details>


### [40] [Practical Tests and Witnesses of Fermionic non-Gaussianity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26218)
*Tobias Haug,Xhek Turkeshi,Piotr Sierant*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了基于费米子反平坦度（FAF）的量子非高斯性检测与见证工具，提出了两种互补的测量协议，改进了现有方法的样本复杂度，并在量子计算机上验证了其噪声鲁棒性，同时揭示了伪随机态生成需要大量费米子非高斯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检测量子态何时离开可高效模拟的费米子高斯（fermionic Gaussian）区域，是基准测试量子设备与认证费米子魔法资源（fermionic magic resources）的核心任务。

Method: 基于费米子反平坦度（FAF）——一种依赖于协方差矩阵的非高斯性度量——开发了实用的测试与见证工具。对于n量子比特态，提出两种互补协议：两拷贝贝尔测量（two-copy Bell measurements）方案和基于马约拉纳双线性算符（Majorana bilinears）可交换匹配的单拷贝（single-copy）方案。对于混合态，引入经纯度修正的FAF见证（purity-corrected FAF witness）。

Result: 两种协议可在$O(n^2/ε^2)$次两拷贝贝尔测量或$O(n^3/ε^4)$次单拷贝测量内，区分纯高斯态与距离高斯集$ε$-远的态，在$n$和$ε$的依赖关系上均优于现有方法。纯度修正的FAF见证对噪声高度鲁棒，在IQM量子计算机上的实验表明噪声既可降低亦可增强非高斯性。伪非高斯性（pseudo non-Gaussianity）分析显示，伪随机态生成（pseudorandom-state generation）需要大量费米子非高斯性。

Conclusion: 这些结果为检测、见证和量化非高斯费米子资源提供了实验上可行的工具。

Abstract: Detecting when a quantum state leaves the efficiently simulable fermionic Gaussian regime is a central task for benchmarking quantum devices and certifying fermionic magic resources. We develop practical tests and witnesses based on fermionic antiflatness (FAF), a covariance-matrix-based measure of non-Gaussianity. For $n$-qubit states, we estimate FAF using two complementary protocols: two-copy Bell measurements and a single-copy scheme based on commuting matchings of Majorana bilinears. These yield testers that distinguish pure Gaussian states from states $ε$-far from the Gaussian set, using $O(n^2/ε^2)$ two-copy Bell measurements or $O(n^3/ε^4)$ single-copy measurements, improving the state of the art in the dependence on both $n$ and $ε$. For mixed states, we introduce a purity-corrected FAF witness that certifies non-Gaussianity and is highly robust to noise. With our witness, we demonstrate on the IQM quantum computer that noise can both reduce and enhance non-Gaussianity. Finally, by examining pseudo non-Gaussianity, we show that the cryptographic task of pseudorandom-state generation requires extensive fermionic non-Gaussianity. Together, these results provide experimentally accessible tools for detecting, witnessing, and quantifying non-Gaussian fermionic resources.

</details>


### [41] [Entanglement Pattern Transition of Quantum States from Directed Percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26219)
*Julian Boesl,Frank Pollmann,Michael Knap*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用随机自动机与等距张量网络态（isometric Tensor Network States, isoTNS）之间的映射，从Domany-Kinzel自动机构造二维量子态，发现其在临界点具有各向同性代数关联，且其父哈密顿量基态流形中存在从W态类纠缠到平庸纠缠的转变，从而揭示了超越稳定平衡相框架的纠缠结构与临界现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相变（quantum phase transition）的核心特征包括纠缠结构的变化和临界现象，但现有研究多局限于物质的稳定平衡相（stable equilibrium phases）范式。本文旨在探索具有不同纠缠模式的状态类之间的相变，以理解超越该范式的希尔伯特空间结构。

Method: 利用随机自动机（stochastic automata）与等距张量网络态（isometric Tensor Network States, isoTNS）之间的映射，从属于有向渗流（directed percolation, DP）类、具有吸收相变（absorbing phase transition）的 (1+1)维 Domany-Kinzel 自动机构造了一个二维量子态，并研究了其父哈密顿量的性质。

Result: 在自动机临界点处，对应的 isoTNS 在所有空间方向上均呈现代数关联（algebraic correlations）。该量子态的连续父哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）具有简并的基态流形，包含一个乘积态（即吸收态）和另一个态；后者经历从远距离区域间的两体纠缠（类似于 W 态，W state）到平庸纠缠（trivial entanglement）的转变。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，isoTNS 与经典随机演化之间的对应关系可用于探测超越稳定基态流形之外的希尔伯特空间结构，为理解纠缠态类之间的相变提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Changes in the entanglement structure and critical phenomena are hallmarks of quantum phase transitions. Here, we discuss how they appear in transitions between classes of states with distinct entanglement patterns beyond the paradigm of stable equilibrium phases of matter. Using a mapping between stochastic automata and isometric Tensor Network States (isoTNS), we construct a two-dimensional quantum state from the Domany-Kinzel automaton, which is a (1+1)D process with an absorbing phase transition in the directed percolation class. At the critical point of the automaton, the corresponding isoTNS hosts algebraic correlations in all spatial directions. The continuous parent Hamiltonian of this state has a degenerate ground state manifold. It consists of a product state (the absorbing state) and a second state that undergoes a transition from pairwise entanglement between distant regions, similarly to the W state, to a state with trivial entanglement. Our results demonstrate how the correspondence between isoTNS and classical stochastic evolution can be used to probe the Hilbert space structure beyond stable ground state manifolds.
