### [42] [Preparing thermal states of frustrated quantum spin systems using 139 qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26245)
*Roland C. Farrell,Yongtao Zhan,Lucas Katschke,Lode Pollet,Ilan T. Rosen,Jad C. Halimeh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用数字量子计算机上的耗散热态制备（dissipative thermal state preparation）方法，研究了阻挫自旋系统的有限温度性质。在kagome晶格上，针对反铁磁海森堡模型（AFHM）和反铁磁伊辛模型（AFIM），通过IBM量子处理器和经典态矢量模拟，展示了系统尺寸无关的平衡电路深度，证实了工程化耗散是有限温度量子模拟的有前景途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子物质（strongly correlated quantum matter）的有限温度性质对凝聚态物理、化学和高能物理至关重要，但经典方法（如量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC））因符号问题（sign problem）难以处理阻挫系统。本文旨在探索利用数字量子计算机上的耗散热态制备来克服这一困难。

Method: 在kagome晶格上研究两个模型：反铁磁海森堡模型（antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model, AFHM，存在严重符号问题）和反铁磁伊辛模型（antiferromagnetic Ising model, AFIM，无符号问题基准）。使用IBM量子处理器制备AFIM的近似热态，并辅以经典态矢量模拟（classical statevector simulation）研究AFIM和AFHM的可扩展性。

Result: 在IBM量子处理器上，实现了多达79个自旋耦合60个环境量子比特的AFIM热态制备，观察到鲁棒的稳态（robust steady state）和可调有效温度，稳态在超过1000层两量子比特门的电路中持续存在。经典模拟显示，在最多24个格点的晶格上，达到热平衡所需的电路深度（circuit depth）与系统尺寸无关，且随逆温度（inverse temperature）最多线性增长。

Conclusion: 工程化耗散（engineered dissipation）是实现阻挫物质有限温度量子模拟的一种有前景的方法，并指出了量子设备可能超越经典方法的参数区间。

Abstract: Finite-temperature properties of strongly correlated quantum matter are central to condensed matter, chemistry, and high-energy physics, yet are often inaccessible to classical methods such as quantum Monte Carlo (QMC). Here, we investigate dissipative thermal state preparation of frustrated spin systems using digital quantum computers. We focus on two paradigmatic models on the kagome lattice: the antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model (AFHM), whose finite-temperature properties are inaccessible to QMC due to a severe sign problem, and the antiferromagnetic Ising model (AFIM), which serves as a sign-problem-free benchmark. Using IBM quantum processors, we prepare approximate thermal states of the AFIM on kagome lattices with up to $79$ spins coupled to $60$ environment qubits. We observe the emergence of a robust steady state with an adjustable effective temperature that persists in circuits with over 1000 layers of two-qubit gates. We further study the scalability of the dissipative protocol through classical statevector simulations of the AFIM and AFHM. On lattices with up to 24 sites, we find that the circuit depth to reach thermal equilibrium is independent of system size and grows at most linearly with inverse temperature. These results establish engineered dissipation as a promising approach to finite-temperature quantum simulation of frustrated matter, and point toward regimes where quantum devices may outperform classical methods.

</details>


### [43] [Scar Full Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26389)
*Ning Sun,Yanting Cheng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“疤痕完全本征态热化假说”（scar full ETH），将标准ETH框架扩展到存在量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）的系统，系统描述了疤痕态矩阵元间的关联特性，并通过PXP模型验证了该理论的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准本征态热化假说（eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, ETH）描述孤立混沌量子系统中涌现统计力学（statistical mechanics）的机制，但该描述在存在量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）的系统中失效，因为这些系统包含具有广延能量的非热本征态（non-thermal eigenstates）。因此需要发展一个更普适的理论框架来刻画这类系统中的关联特性。

Method: 通过典型性论证（typicality arguments）建立疤痕完整ETH的标度形式（scaling forms）和因子化性质（factorization properties），并将多时间关联函数（multi-time correlation functions）分解为热累积量（thermal cumulants）和疤痕累积量（scar cumulants），实现对高阶关联的重组。

Result: 在量子疤痕的范例模型PXP模型中，通过数值计算验证了所提出的疤痕完整ETH框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作为系统理解存在量子多体疤痕的系统中的关联性质奠定了基础，推动了ETH理论向更广泛量子系统的推广。

Abstract: The eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH) provides a fundamental mechanism for emergent statistical mechanics in isolated chaotic quantum systems, asserting that individual energy eigenstates behave as pseudorandom vectors within an energy window. This enables a complete characterization of nontrivial correlations among matrix elements in the energy eigenbasis, as described by the full ETH ansatz. Nevertheless, this description breaks down in systems exhibiting quantum many-body scars, which host non-thermal eigenstates with extensive energy. In this Letter, we address this problem by formulating the \textit{scar full ETH}, which captures correlations among matrix elements involving scar states. The corresponding scaling forms and factorization properties are established using typicality arguments. Multi-time correlation functions for scar states are then organized in terms of both thermal and scar cumulants, providing a nontrivial reorganization of higher-order correlations. We numerically demonstrate the validity of this framework in the paradigmatic model of quantum scars, the PXP model. Our results pave the way for a systematic understanding of intriguing correlations in systems with quantum many-body scars.

</details>


### [44] [Analytical Singular-Value Structure of Analytic-Continuation Kernels from Slepian Information Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26586)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将热核（thermal kernel）的动力学部分与统计权重分离，揭示了从虚时格林函数（imaginary-time Green's function）到实频谱（real-frequency spectra）的解析延拓（analytic continuation）问题具有解析广义奇异值结构，并证明了该问题的信息容量由香农数（Shannon number）N_c = βω_max/π 决定，同时给出了无需迭代的最优采样点方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从虚时格林函数到实频谱的解析延拓是量子多体物理（quantum many-body physics）中的一个核心病态反问题（ill-posed inverse problem），现有方法高度依赖数值正则化，缺乏对问题内在结构的深刻理解。本文旨在揭示该问题的解析结构，从而为信息容量和最优采样提供理论依据。

Method: 将热核的纯动力学部分与热浴（heat bath）施加的统计权重分离，证明动力学核等价于Slepian有限傅里叶变换（finite Fourier transform）的虚频带延拓，受同一Sturm-Liouville代数支配，产生长椭球波函数（prolate spheroidal wave functions）。费米子和玻色子统计以规范变换（gauge transformation）形式进入频域内积，产生自伴有效势（self-adjoint effective potentials）但无需数值核对角化。最优采样点通过Legendre伴随矩阵（Legendre colleague matrix）的特征值获得。

Result: 香农数 N_c = βω_max/π 确定了该纯拉普拉斯通道（pure Laplace channel）的上限信息容量。最优采样点可由Legendre伴随矩阵的特征值直接给出，形成确定性压缩感知网格（deterministic compressed-sensing grid），无需迭代求根。

Conclusion: 虚时格林函数解析延拓问题具有可解析求解的广义奇异值结构，其信息容量由香农数严格界定，且最优采样可通过代数方法高效获得，为量子多体系统中的谱函数重建提供了理论框架和实用工具。

Abstract: Analytic continuation from imaginary-time Green's functions to real-frequency spectra is a central ill-posed inverse problem in quantum many-body physics. We show that the thermal kernel admits an analytical generalized singular-value structure once its purely dynamical part is separated from the statistical weight imposed by the heat bath. The dynamical kernel is the imaginary-bandwidth continuation of Slepian's finite Fourier transform and is governed by the same Sturm-Liouville algebra that yields prolate spheroidal wave functions. Fermionic and bosonic statistics then enter as gauge transformations of the frequency-space inner product, producing self-adjoint effective potentials but no numerical kernel diagonalization. The Shannon number, $N_c=β\wmax/π$, fixes the upper information capacity of this pure Laplace channel. Finally, the optimal sampling points are obtained as eigenvalues of a Legendre colleague matrix, giving a deterministic compressed-sensing grid without iterative root searches.

</details>


### [45] [Nonclassical energy-change distribution as a witness of non-Markovian quantum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26818)
*Marco Pezzutto,Anton Corr,Gabriele De Chiara,Salvatore Lorenzo,Stefano Gherardini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出仅通过测量开放量子系统的能量来识别非马尔可夫量子时间演化，证明CP-可分割性（CP-divisibility）的违反总是由系统哈密顿量在连续时刻的能量变化Kirkwood-Dirac准概率分布（Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobability distribution）的非正值所见证，且该证实在能量守恒的体系-环境相互作用下更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决仅通过系统能量测量来识别开放量子系统中非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）量子时间演化的问题，探索一种更直接且实验上可行的非马尔可夫性检测方案。

Method: 基于系统哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）在连续时刻的能量变化，构建Kirkwood-Dirac准概率分布，通过该分布的非正值来检测CP-可分割性的违反。同时利用量子互信息（quantum mutual information）构造非马尔可夫性度量以检测异常能流（anomalous energy fluxes）。

Result: CP-可分割性的违反总是由能量变化Kirkwood-Dirac准概率分布的非正值所见证；当系统-环境相互作用为能量守恒（energy-preserving）时，这种关联更强；非马尔可夫性导致的反常能流可被上述分布的非正值和基于量子互信息的度量所检测。

Conclusion: 系统的能量测量足以作为非马尔可夫量子演化的探针，且能量变化分布的非正性为检测非马尔可夫性提供了一种原则性工具。

Abstract: We address the problem of identifying non-Markovian quantum time evolutions of an open quantum system by only performing measurements of the system's energy. We demonstrate that violations of CP-divisibility are always witnessed by non-positive values of the energy-change Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobability distribution associated with the system's Hamiltonian, evaluated at consecutive times. The link between non CP-divisibility and non-positivity of the system's energy-change distribution is stronger when the system-environment interactions are energy-preserving. The witness works whenever anomalous energy fluxes, due to non-Markovianity, are realized. Anomalous fluxes are also detected by the non-Markovianity measure built over the quantum mutual information between the states of the open system and of a quantum correlated reference.

</details>

### [46] [Closed-Form Analytical Charge Response Model for Silicon Photomultipliers with Recursive Correlated Avalanches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27340)
*Yiqi Liu,Xuewei Liu,Benda Xu*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一闭式解析模型，利用特征函数（characteristic-function）框架描述硅光电倍增管（SiPM）的完整电荷响应谱，将基底噪声、单电子响应（SER）、内部光学串扰和后脉冲效应整合为三个独立物理分量，并通过Lambert W函数和负二项分布等解析工具实现无需数值卷积的闭式表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅光电倍增管（SiPM）已成为下一代中微子实验中的首选光电探测器，但其完整电荷响应谱至今缺乏一个无截断（truncation）和无数值卷积（numerical convolution）的统一闭式解析表达式，且必须同时捕捉传统光电倍增管（PMT）中不存在的关联串扰（cross-talk）和后脉冲（afterpulsing）效应。

Method: 在特征函数框架下，将完整电荷谱分解为三个独立物理分量：基底噪声（pedestal）、单电子响应（SER）和雪崩计数统计（avalanche count statistics）。内部光学串扰建模为带有泊松后代的Galton-Watson分支过程，利用Lagrange-Bürmann反演推导出总后裔概率生成函数（PGF）的Lambert W闭式。后脉冲建模为每雪崩几何链（geometric chain），从最大熵泊松-伽马混合分布导出，其N雪崩总和服从负二项分布（Negative Binomial）。

Result: 得到一个八参数（eight-parameter）闭式表达式，并进一步推导出每个通道的电荷-时间似然（charge-time likelihood），用于事件级能量重建，且在推理时无需数值卷积。

Conclusion: 该模型从理论上统一了SiPM电荷响应谱中的多个关键物理效应，提供了完全解析的闭式表达，可显著提升事件级能量重建的计算效率。

Abstract: Silicon photomultipliers (SiPMs) have become the preferred photodetectors in next-generation neutrino experiments, yet no unified closed-form analytical expression free of truncation and numerical convolution has been established for their full charge response spectrum, which must simultaneously capture correlated cross-talk and afterpulsing effects absent in conventional photomultiplier tubes (PMTs). We present a unified closed-form model for the SiPM charge response within the characteristic-function framework, treating pedestal noise, single-electron-response (SER) charge, internal optical cross-talk, and afterpulsing on equal footing. The characteristic-function representation factorises the full charge spectrum into three independent physical components: pedestal, single-electron response (SER), and avalanche count statistics. Prompt internal optical cross-talk is modelled as a Galton-Watson branching process with Poisson offspring; building on the Generalised Poisson count statistics identified by Vinogradov, we derive a Lambert $W$ closed form for the total-progeny PGF via Lagrange-Bürmann inversion, providing the analytical handle needed for efficient event-level reconstruction. Afterpulsing is modelled as a per-avalanche geometric chain, derived as the maximum-entropy Poisson-Gamma mixture: the exponential prior-maximum-entropy for a positive continuous yield with fixed mean-marginalised over a Poisson count yields the geometric per-avalanche distribution, whose $N$-avalanche total is Negative Binomial. This naturally encompasses the Poisson afterpulsing limit and recursive afterpulse chains while preserving analytical closure. The resulting eight-parameter expression is further applied to derive an explicit per-channel charge-time likelihood for event-level energy reconstruction without numerical convolution at inference time.

</details>

### [47] [Field-level multi-tracers simulation-based inference of cosmological parameters from 3D maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26210)
*Giulio Scelfo,Satvik Mishra,Mauro Rigo,Roberto Trotta,Matteo Viel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究构建了一个基于模拟的推断（Simulation-Based Inference, SBI）流水线，利用神经网络仿真器（neural emulator）结合流体动力学模拟，从星系计数、中性氢（HI）强度映射及其组合中约束宇宙学参数{Ωₘ, σ₈}。相比传统功率谱摘要统计，场级（field-level）推断可将约束能力提升约3倍，多示踪剂（multi-tracer）组合可进一步将联合精度提升2–7倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前和未来的大尺度结构（large-scale structure）数据需要超越传统基于似然推断的摘要统计（summary statistics），以充分提取宇宙学信息。模拟推断有望利用场级信息（field-level information）和现代流体动力学模拟的丰富物理内容，但尚缺乏端到端的实证验证。

Method: 开发了一个概念验证（proof-of-concept）SBI流水线：使用神经网络仿真器在全流体动力学模拟上训练，将快速近似暗物质模拟映射为星系和HI地图；结合神经后验估计（neural posterior estimation），在边缘化天体物理效应（astrophysical effects）的同时估计宇宙学参数；分别在功率谱和场级表示（2D/3D地图）上进行推断，比较单示踪剂与多示踪剂组合的效果。

Result: 多示踪剂（星系+HI）组合相比单示踪剂，在描述宇宙学参数联合精度的品质因子（Figure of Merit）上提升了2–7倍。从摘要统计转向场级推断，约束能力稳定提升约3倍，其中3D地图给出最精确且标定良好的后验分布（posteriors）。

Conclusion: SBI结合神经网络仿真器与场级信息能够显著提升宇宙学参数约束精度，且在天体物理参数被边缘化时增益仍然稳健。未来需纳入真实巡天效应（realistic survey effects）并提升仿真器保真度（faithfulness），以将该方法应用于实际巡天数据。

Abstract: Extracting maximum cosmological information from current and upcoming large-scale structure data requires going beyond summary statistics as currently used in likelihood-based inference. Simulation-Based Inference (SBI) promises to enable the exploitation of field-level information and the rich physics of modern hydrodynamical simulations. We develop a proof-of-concept SBI pipeline to explore its potential to constrain the cosmological parameters $\{Ω_{\rm m}, σ_8\}$ from galaxy number counts, neutral hydrogen (HI) intensity mapping and their combination. We use neural emulators trained on full hydrodynamical simulations to generate galaxy and HI maps from fast, approximate dark matter simulations. Combined with neural posterior estimation, this enables the estimation of cosmological parameters while marginalizing over astrophysical effects. We perform inference both on the power spectrum and on representations derived from field-level 2D or 3D maps, comparing results from each probe and the combination of both tracers, and assessing the impact of data compression and multi-tracers information on cosmological constraints. Combining galaxy and HI fields improves constraints with respect to single-tracer cases by a factor 2 to 7 in terms of a Figure of Merit describing the joint precision on cosmological parameters, depending on the tracer/configuration. Moving from summary statistics to field-level inference leads to a consistent gain in constraining power of about a factor 3, with 3D maps providing the most precise and well-calibrated posteriors. This gain in precision is robust even when astrophysical parameters are marginalized over. Further developments (including realistic survey effects and improvements in emulators' faithfulness) will enable the application of this analysis pipeline to upcoming surveys.

</details>


### [48] [Constraining Early Dark Energy cosmological models with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26749)
*Teodora M. Matei,Cristian Croitoru,Tiberiu Harko*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用嵌套采样算法构建模拟器（eden程序），研究早期暗能量（Early Dark Energy）模型对太初核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis）的影响，给出了不同状态方程下暗能量密度的上限约束，并识别出温度依赖的状态方程作为最物理自洽的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学图像中存在显著张力（tension），表明标准ΛCDM模型可能不完备。早期暗能量（Early Dark Energy）模型可通过假设早期加速膨胀来缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），但其对太初核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis）过程的影响尚需系统研究。

Method: 考虑多种宇宙学模型，包括简单宇宙常数模型以及具有可变状态方程（equation of state）的暗能量模型。通过嵌套采样算法（nested sampling algorithm）构建模拟器（eden程序），估算模型参数的上限并确定辐射主导时期（radiation-dominated era）中暗能量密度的最大允许贡献。

Result: 对于线性状态方程，暗能量密度在95%置信水平下被限制在$10^{-13}$ MeV$^4$以下；对于多方状态方程（polytropic equation of state），上限为$10^{-5}$ MeV$^4$。温度依赖的状态方程是最物理自洽的框架，耦合参数$\lesssim 10^{-2}$时与原初丰度（primordial abundances）保持一致，允许高温下偏离标准ΛCDM膨胀历史，并在弱冻结期（weak freeze-out era）迅速稀释至标准广义相对论结果。

Conclusion: 温度依赖的状态方程暗能量模型能够在高温阶段偏离ΛCDM膨胀历史以缓解哈勃张力，同时在核合成时期迅速稀释以保持与原初丰度观测一致，是最具物理吸引力的框架。

Abstract: The recent cosmological picture contains a significant tension indicating that our standard $Λ$CDM picture may be incomplete. Early Dark Energy models can alleviate the Hubble tension, by assuming an early acceleration that could explain the divergence between the early and late-time cosmological data. We investigate the implications of Early Dark Energy models on the Big Bang Nucleosynthesis processes by considering several cosmological models, including a model assuming a simple cosmological constant, alongside with varying equations of state dark energy models. We construct a simulator through a nested sampling algorithm, with the help of which we estimate the upper bounds for model parameters, and determine the maximum allowable dark energy density contribution during the radiation-dominated era. Our results are obtained through the \href{https://github.com/croi900/eden}{eden} program. We show that for a linear or polytropic equation of state, the dark energy density is constrained to less than $10^{-13}$ MeV$^4$ and $10^{-5}$ MeV$^4$, respectively, at the 95\% confidence level. Furthermore, we identify a temperature-dependent equation of state of dark energy as the most physically compelling framework, which remains consistent with primordial abundances for coupling parameters $\lesssim 10^{-2}$. This model successfully allows for high-temperature deviations from the standard $Λ$CDM expansion history, while rapidly diluting to obtain standard general relativistic results in the weak freeze-out era.

</details>


### [49] [GWTC-5.0: Constraints on the Cosmic Expansion Rate and Modified Gravitational-wave Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27227)
*The LIGO Scientific Collaboration,the Virgo Collaboration,the KAGRA Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 利用LIGO–Virgo–KAGRA第五次引力波瞬变目录（GWTC-5.0）中的236个引力波源，结合质量谱特征与统计宿主星系关联两种红移推断方法，估计哈勃常数H0 = 71.0_{-7.1}^{+9.0} km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，并检验了引力波传播中广义相对论的偏离，未发现异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）数据独立估计哈勃常数（Hubble constant, H0），以解决宇宙学中不同观测手段对H0测量值的争议，并进一步检验广义相对论（general relativity, GR）在宇宙尺度上的有效性。

Method: 采用GWTC-5.0目录中的236个引力波源，通过两种方法推断红移：一是利用质量谱（mass spectrum）特征获取红移信息，二是利用统计宿主星系关联（statistical host galaxy association）。结合源坐标系质量分布（source-frame mass distribution）、GW170817及其电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart）的H0测量，以及暗能量巡天第六年（Dark Energy Survey Year 6, DES-Y6）的星系目录信息，对光源光度距离（luminosity distance）与红移关系进行约束，并引入参数化检验来探测引力波传播中广义相对论的偏离。

Result: 估计得到H0 = 71.0_{-7.1}^{+9.0} km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹（中位数，68%对称可信区间）。相比GWTC-4.0的测量，由于使用了更多引力波源（部分天区定位体积显著更小），H0不确定度降低25.7%，且重建的质量分布具有更低的不确定度。在引力波传播的参数化检验中未发现偏离广义相对论的信号。

Conclusion: 基于GWTC-5.0的大样本引力波数据，结合多种红移推断方法，能够有效提升哈勃常数的测量精度，并验证广义相对论在引力波传播层面的正确性。

Abstract: We employ 236 gravitational-wave (GW) sources in the fifth LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA Collaboration (LVK) Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-5.0) to estimate the Hubble constant $H_0$. We compare the luminosity distance measured from GWs to the redshift inferred i) using features in the mass spectrum, and ii) using statistical host galaxy association. Probing the relationship between source luminosity distances and redshifts obtained in this way yields constraints on cosmological parameters. We estimate $H_0 = {71.0}_{-7.1}^{+9.0}\,{\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}}$ (median with $68\%$ symmetric credible interval). This combines information from the source-frame mass distribution with the $H_0$ measurement from GW170817 and its electromagnetic counterpart as well as galaxy catalog information from Dark Energy Survey Year 6 (DES-Y6). We improve over the GWTC-4.0 measurement by using more GW sources, some with significantly smaller sky localization volumes, which leads to a reduction by $25.7\%$ of the $H_0$ uncertainty and a reconstructed mass distribution with lower uncertainties. We also constrain deviations from general relativity (GR) which affect GW propagation, specifically that modify the luminosity distance inferred from the GW signal. We find no departures from GR in parameterized tests of GW propagation.

</details>


### [50] [$w_0$-probe: A new diagnostic of dark energy based on $Om$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27230)
*Satadru Bag,Ryan E. Keeley,Varun Sahni,Arman Shafieloo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对DESI数据暗示暗能量可能演化的观测背景，提出了一种名为$w_0$-probe的新诊断量。该诊断量基于$Om(z)$构建，无需对膨胀历史$h(z)$进行额外微分即可直接确定当前暗能量状态方程参数$w_0$，同时保留了$Om(z)$对$Λ$CDM模型的零检验（null-test）能力。通过对现有超新星（SNe Ia）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据的高斯过程（GP）重建，$w_0$-probe以95%置信水平排除$Λ$CDM，并给出$w_0\simeq-0.62\pm0.03$的估计。经$\chi^2$限制重建的稳健性检验，结果同样支持$w_0\in(-0.8,-0.5)$，表明该诊断量是一种简单、模型无关且稳健的当前暗能量状态方程诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期DESI数据暗示暗能量（dark energy）可能正在演化，这促使研究者采用模型无关的诊断方法，如$Om(z)$以及暗能量状态方程（equation of state, EoS）$w(z)$的探针。然而，传统的$w(z)$重建方法依赖于对膨胀历史（expansion history）$h(z)=H(z)/H_0$的微分，这一过程会放大噪声和系统不确定性。

Method: 本文引入了一种新的诊断量——$w_0$-probe，它基于$Om(z)$构建，能够直接从$h(z)$确定当前暗能量状态方程参数$w_0$，而无需进行额外的微分操作。该方法保留了$Om(z)$对$Λ$CDM的零检验能力，同时直接提供$w_0$的估计，且对于任何光滑的底层$w(z)$均保持稳健。作者将其应用于超新星（SNe Ia）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据的高斯过程（Gaussian process, GP）重建。为缓解GP先验可能导致的过约束，还额外分析了超过95%置信水平阈值的高似然$\chi^2$限制重建样本。

Result: 基于高斯过程（GP）重建的分析中，$Om(z)$和$w_0$-probe均在95%置信水平下排除了$Λ$CDM模型，后者倾向于$w_0\simeq-0.62\pm0.03$（95% C.L.）。$\chi^2$限制重建的高似然样本也主要排除$Λ$CDM，并在$z\to 0$时给出$w_0\in(-0.8,-0.5)$，验证了结果的稳健性。

Conclusion: $w_0$-probe提供了一种简单、模型无关且稳健的当前暗能量状态方程诊断工具，能够有效避免传统微分方法带来的噪声放大问题，并在当前数据中给出对$Λ$CDM模型的显著排除结果。

Abstract: Recent DESI data suggest that dark energy may be evolving and motivate the use of model-independent diagnostics such as $Om(z)$ and probes of the equation of state (EoS) of dark energy, $w(z)$. Traditional reconstructions of $w(z)$ rely on differentiating the expansion history, $h(z)=H(z)/H_0$, which amplifies noise and systematic uncertainties. In this work, we introduce a new diagnostic, the $w_0$-probe, which is constructed from $Om(z)$, and which enables a direct determination of the current EoS from $h(z)$ without any additional differentiation. While retaining the null-test capability of $Om(z)$ for $Λ$CDM, the $w_0$-probe also provides a direct estimate of $w_0$ -- the current EoS of dark energy. We demonstrate that this reconstruction of $w_0$ is robust for any smooth underlying $w(z)$. We apply this method to Gaussian-process (GP) reconstructions of $h(z)$ using current SNe Ia+BAO+CMB data. Both $Om(z)$ and the $w_0$-probe exclude $Λ$CDM at the $95\%$ confidence level (C.L.), with the latter favouring $w_0\simeq-0.62 \pm 0.03$ at $95\%$ C.L. To mitigate potential over-constraining from GP priors, we additionally analyze $χ^2$-limited reconstructions with likelihoods exceeding the $95\%$ CPL threshold. The $w_0$-probe obtained from these high-likelihood samples again predominantly excludes $Λ$CDM and yields $w_0\in(-0.8,-0.5)$ at $z\to 0$, demonstrating the robustness of our results. The $w_0$-probe therefore provides a simple, model-independent, and robust diagnostic of the current EoS of dark energy.

</details>


### [51] [Effective Phantom Dark Energy: What Cosmological Reconstruction Does and Does Not Imply](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27301)
*Swagat S. Mishra*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文系统澄清了有效暗能量重构中幻影行为（phantom behaviour）的含义，指出观测到的幻影或穿越幻影（phantom-crossing）行为并不必然意味着存在基本幻影场、微观鬼影不稳定性（ghost instabilities）、零能量条件（null energy condition）破坏或灾难性的宇宙未来。文章旨在为暗能量重构的物理诠释提供明确、系统的区分框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期DESI重子声学振荡（BAO）测量结合宇宙微波背景（CMB）和超新星数据，显示出对具有幻影或穿越幻影行为的动力学暗能量的温和偏好。然而这些趋势的统计显著性有限，且未解决的系统误差或建模不确定性仍可能重要。由此引发的讨论凸显了需要对有效暗能量重构给予更清晰的诠释。

Method: 本文通过概念分析和物理机制讨论，系统阐述有效暗能量（effective dark energy）的定义、幻影及穿越幻影行为的诠释，以及有效幻影行为在无基本病态（fundamental pathologies）情况下可能产生的物理机制。

Result: 有效幻影行为并不必然意味着存在基本幻影场、微观鬼影不稳定性、基本应力张量（stress tensor）对零能量条件的破坏，或灾难性的宇宙未来。

Conclusion: 许多区分在暗能量重构社区内虽已熟悉，但在更广泛的动力学暗能量讨论中常被隐式处理。本文希望为观测重构的暗能量究竟蕴含什么和不蕴含什么提供清晰的说明，并对当前观测情形之外的未来讨论保持有用。

Abstract: In observational cosmology, the dark energy density and equation of state are effective quantities reconstructed at the background level under a set of assumptions. These include the FLRW framework, the standard Friedmann equation of General Relativity, and separately conserved non-relativistic matter at late times. Recent analyses involving DESI BAO measurements combined with CMB and supernova data have shown mild preference for dynamical dark energy featuring phantom or phantom-crossing behaviour. While the statistical significance of these trends remains limited, and unresolved systematics or modelling uncertainties may still be important, the resulting discussions have highlighted the need for a clearer interpretation of effective dark energy reconstruction. In particular, effective phantom behaviour does not necessarily imply the existence of a fundamental phantom field, microscopic ghost instabilities, violation of the null energy condition by the fundamental stress tensor, or a catastrophic cosmic future. The purpose of this work is to clarify these distinctions explicitly and systematically, independently of whether the current observational preference for dynamical dark energy survives future data. We discuss the definition of effective dark energy in cosmology, the interpretation of phantom and phantom-crossing behaviour, and physical mechanisms through which effective phantom behaviour may arise without fundamental pathologies. While many of these distinctions are familiar within the dark energy reconstruction community, they are often left implicit in broader discussions of dynamical dark energy. We hope that this work will remain useful beyond the present observational situation as a clarification of what observationally reconstructed dark energy does and does not imply.

</details>


### [52] [A Fast Method to Compute Scalar Induced Gravitational Waves on a Lattice with Primordial Non-Gaussianities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27231)
*Giovanni Piccoli*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于晶格模拟与GPU加速的方法（FLAN-SIGW）来高效计算包含任意非高斯性的标量诱导引力波（SIGW）功率谱，将原本无法直接求解的傅里叶空间积分转化为约50个可用快速傅里叶变换（FFT）计算的卷积，在秒级时间内达到10%以内的误差，并在标准辐射主导背景（w=1/3）下验证了方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量诱导引力波（SIGW）在二阶扰动理论中产生，其观测显著性要求暴胀动力学在小尺度上偏离标准慢滚场景，产生具有强非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）的大曲率扰动。现有方法难以高效处理任意非高斯性下的SIGW功率谱计算。

Method: 首先采用半解析方法求解波动方程，得到包含傅里叶空间积分的表达式；然后将这些无法在晶格上直接求解的积分重新表述为约50个卷积之和，每个卷积可通过快速傅里叶变换（FFT）高效计算；最后从晶格实现中直接测量功率谱。该方法在GPU加速代码FLAN-SIGW中实现，采用标准辐射主导背景（w=1/3）进行性能评估。

Result: FLAN-SIGW能够在数秒内计算出完全非微扰、非高斯的SIGW功率谱，误差控制在10%以内，且仅需适度的计算资源。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法显著提升了含任意非高斯性的SIGW功率谱计算效率，为未来引力波观测与早期宇宙物理之间的联系提供了可行的计算工具。代码已在GitHub上公开。

Abstract: Scalar Induced Gravitational Waves (SIGW) are generated at second order in perturbation theory and to achieve observational relevance, inflationary dynamics must evade the standard slow-roll scenario at small scales, generating large curvature perturbations following strongly non-Gaussian statistics. We propose a method to efficiently compute the SIGW spectrum including arbitrary non-Gaussianities. First, we solve the wave equation adopting semi-analytic methods; this results in an expression involving integrals in Fourier space which are impossible to solve directly on a lattice. We overcome this bottleneck by recasting these integrals as a sum of about 50 convolutions, each of which can be computed efficiently with FFT methods. Finally, the power spectrum is measured directly from the lattice realization. We implement this in FLAN-SIGW, a GPU-accelerated code capable of computing fully non-perturbative, non-Gaussian SIGW spectra in seconds with an error within 10% with modest computational resources. The code is made public at https://github.com/giovannipiccoli99/FLAN-SIGW. In this first implementation, in order to assess the performance of the method, we adopt a standard radiation-dominated background with $w = 1/3$.

</details>


### [53] [Gaussian Process Reconstruction of Cosmological Parameters with Gravitational Wave Sirens using Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27357)
*Gourab Nandi,Anish Ghoshal,David F. Mota*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于高斯过程回归（Gaussian Process Regression, GPR）的模型无关重建框架，利用未来引力波标准汽笛（standard siren）目录（如LISA和Einstein Telescope），在多种暗能量和暗物质模型背景下重建共动距离及其导数，并通过全协方差传播稳健计算哈勃参数等诊断量；结果表明背景距离测量本身无法有效区分不同宇宙学模型，但导数敏感的诊断量可锁定具有最大区分能力的红移窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来引力波标准汽笛目录将提供传统电磁观测难以触及的红移范围内的晚期宇宙膨胀历史，迫切需要评估这些背景距离信息在多大程度上能够区分可行的宇宙学模型。

Method: 构建基于高斯过程回归（Gaussian Process Regression, GPR）的模型无关重建框架，分析六种基准宇宙学背景（ΛCDM、CPL、CPL+Λ、相互作用暗物质、相互作用暗能量、轴子启发早期暗能量）下的模拟LISA和爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）目录，重建共动距离及其导数，并利用全高斯过程协方差（包括导数交叉协方差）传播计算哈勃参数$H(z)$及其他诊断量（如$q(z)$、$\mathcal{O}_{m}(z)$、$w_{\rm total}(z)$和$\kappa(z)$），最后采用逐点边缘Hellinger距离评估模型间的统计可区分性。

Result: 引力波亮标准汽笛能够忠实恢复基准膨胀历史；但背景测量本身无法提供模型间决定性的统计分离；导数敏感的诊断量可定位特定红移窗口（例如ET在$z\simeq1.6-1.8$，LISA在$z\simeq2.6-2.9$），其中未来目录的区分能力最大。

Conclusion: 该贝叶斯高斯过程回归（Bayesian GPR）流水线提供了一种非参数化且原则性的方法，可精确定位未来引力波数据中蕴含的最有价值的宇宙学信息所在红移区间。

Abstract: Future gravitational wave (GW) standard siren catalogues will probe the late-time expansion history of the Universe across redshift ranges largely inaccessible to traditional electromagnetic observations. To determine how effectively this background distance information can distinguish between viable cosmological models, we introduce a model-independent reconstruction framework utilizing Gaussian Process Regression (GPR). Analyzing mock LISA and Einstein Telescope (ET) catalogues across six fiducial cosmological backgrounds-$Λ$CDM, CPL, CPL+$Λ$, interacting dark matter, interacting dark energy and axion inspired early dark energy. We reconstruct the comoving distance and its derivatives. Crucially, we propagated the full GP covariance, including derivative cross-covariances, to robustly evaluate the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ and other diagnostics such as $q(z)$, $\mathcal{O}_{m}(z)$ $w_{\rm total}(z)$ and $κ(z)$. While our analysis demonstrates that GW bright standard sirens faithfully recover fiducial expansion histories, applying pointwise marginal Hellinger distance reveals that background measurements alone do not provide decisive statistical separation among models. Instead, derivative sensitive diagnostics pinpoint specific redshift windows (e.g., $z\simeq1.6-1.8$ for ET and $z\simeq2.6-2.9$ for LISA) where future catalogues will maximize their discriminatory power. As machine learning methodologies become increasingly integral to astrophysics and cosmology, this Bayesian GPR pipeline offers a principled, nonparametric approach to precisely identifying where the most valuable cosmological information lies.

</details>


<div id='math.RA'></div>

# math.RA [[Back]](#toc)

### [54] [Explicit class of finite-dimensional polynomial algebras with Wronskians over $\mathbb{R}^d$ as $N$-ary Lie brackets: beyond $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27305)
*Markuss G. Ķēniņš,Arthemy V. Kiselev*

Main category: math.RA

TL;DR: 本文证明了由完全广义Wronskian行列式（complete generalised Wronskian determinant）定义的$N$元括号（$N$-ary bracket）可将多项式空间构造为有限维强同伦李代数（strong homotopy Lie algebra, SH-Lie algebra），并给出了其结构常数中出现的广义Vandermonde行列式的因式分解公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在$\mathfrak{sl}(2)$李代数（Lie algebra）可由多项式系数的向量场及其Wronskian行列式实现这一事实的启发下，作者希望将这一构造推广到更高维度和更高阶的多元括号（multiple brackets），以建立更一般的有限维多项式强同伦李代数（polynomial SH-Lie algebras）框架。

Method: 作者利用完全广义Wronskian $W^{d\geqslant 1}_{k\geqslant 1}$（阶数为$k$、维数为$d$）作为$N$元括号（其中$N=\binom{d+k}{d}$），在多项式环$\Bbbk[x^1,\ldots,x^d]$（$\Bbbk=\mathbb{R}$或$\mathbb{C}$）中筛选出有限维子空间$\mathcal{A}$，使其在该括号下封闭并构成强同伦李代数（SH-Lie algebra）。具体地，对于$d=2$且$k=1$的情形，三元括号（ternary bracket）$W^{d=2}_{k=1}=\mathbf{1}\wedge \partial_x \wedge \partial_y$定义了由$\langle 1, x, y, p\rangle$（$p\in\{x^2, xy, y^2\}$）张成的有限维SH-Lie代数。

Result: 作者明确描述了所有由完全广义Wronskian $W^{d\geqslant 1}_{k\geqslant 1}$作为$N$元括号的有限维多项式SH-Lie代数$\Bbbk_k[{\boldsymbol{x}}]\subseteq \mathcal{A} \subseteq \Bbbk[x^1,\ldots,x^d]$；并获得了出现在这些多项式代数结构常数中的广义Vandermonde行列式（generalised Vandermonde determinant）的因式分解公式（factorisation formula）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了通过完全广义Wronskian构造有限维多项式SH-Lie代数的完整分类框架，并揭示了结构常数与广义Vandermonde行列式之间的因式分解关系，为高维微分算子实现同伦代数（homotopy algebra）提供了系统性方法。

Abstract: Lie algebra $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$ can be realised by vector fields on $\mathbb{R}^1\ni x$ with polynomial coefficients $1$, $-2x$, $-x^2$; their Wronskian determinants yield the Lie bracket. Likewise, the monomials $1$, $\ldots$, $x^k/k!$, $\ldots$, $x^N/N!$ span finite-dimensional strong homotopy (SH) Lie algebras with the Wronskians $\mathbf{1} \wedge \partial_x \wedge \ldots \wedge \partial_x^{N-1}$ as the $N$-ary brackets. Over dimension $d=2$ with $\mathbb{R}^2\ni(x,y)$ and for the generalised complete Wronskian $W^{d=2}_{k=1}=\mathbf{1}\wedge \partial_x \wedge \partial_y$ of differential order $k=1$ as the ternary bracket, the finite-dimensional polynomial SH-Lie algebras are spanned by $\langle 1$, $x$, $y$, $p\rangle$ with $p\in\{x^2$, $xy$, $y^2\}$. We explicitly describe all finite-dimensional polynomial SH-Lie algebras $\Bbbk_k[{\boldsymbol{x}}]\subseteq \mathcal{A} \subseteq \Bbbk[x^1,\ldots,x^d]$ (over $\Bbbk=\mathbb{R}$ or $\mathbb{C}$) with the complete generalised Wronskians $W^{d\geqslant 1}_{k\geqslant 1}$ of order $k$ as $N$-ary bracket: $N=\binom{d+k}{d}$. We obtain a factorisation formula for the generalised Vandermonde determinants which show up in the structure constants of the polynomial algebras $\mathcal{A}$.

</details>

Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 通过测量LHCb探测器记录的中心质系能量每核子对5.36 TeV的NeNe与OO碰撞中D^0介子产额比，研究轻离子碰撞中核效应的出现。该产额比随横动量（p_T）的变化与仅基于核子结构核修正的预期不一致，表明随着核尺寸增大，夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的产生开始出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在轻离子碰撞体系中研究核效应的起始特征，并检验仅由核子部分子分布函数（parton distribution function）的核修正能否解释观测到的D^0介子产额比变化，或是否需要引入夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）等新物理机制。

Method: 利用LHCb探测器记录的中心质系能量每核子对5.36 TeV的NeNe和OO碰撞数据。在横动量（transverse momentum, p_T）区间0.5<p_T<20 GeV以及快度（rapidity, y）区间2.0<y<4.5内测量D^0介子产额，并将其归一化至各数据样本中记录的非弹性核-核碰撞总数，从而得到NeNe与OO碰撞的产额比。

Result: NeNe与OO碰撞的D^0介子产额比显示出随p_T变化的证据，该变化趋势与仅基于核子结构的核修正（nuclear modification of nucleon structure）所作的预测不一致。

Conclusion: 该测量结果与以下图像一致：在高能核碰撞中，随着核尺寸增大，夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的产生开始出现。

Abstract: The onset of nuclear effects in light-ion collisions is studied by measuring the ratio of $D^0$ meson production between NeNe and OO collisions at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of $5.36\,{\rm TeV}$ recorded by the LHCb detector. The $D^0$ meson yields are measured differentially in transverse momentum ($p_{\rm T}$) for $0.5<p_{\rm T}<20\,{\rm GeV}$ in the rapidity ($y$) region $2.0<y<4.5$, and are normalized to the total number of recorded inelastic nucleus-nucleus collisions in each data sample. The resulting production ratio shows evidence of variation as a function of $p_{\rm T}$, which is inconsistent with predictions based on nuclear modification of nucleon structure alone. This measurement is consistent with the onset of quark-gluon plasma production with increasing nucleus size in high-energy nuclear collisions.

</details>

### [56] [Phase behavior of solvent-nematogen mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26338)
*Sullivan Bailey-Darland,Takumi Matsuzawa,Eric R. Dufresne*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和平均场模型研究了含向列相物质（nematogen）的液体混合物的相行为，发现了两种二元相图类型（存在/不存在各向同性-各向同性共存区），并通过调节溶剂比例连续调变相边界、揭示三相共存区。所提出的平均场模型定量描述了二元和三元相行为，并可推广至多组分系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 含向列相物质的液体混合物可同时发生流体相分离和各向同性-向列相转变，这两种相变相互耦合导致不同于简单液体混合物或纯液晶的复杂相行为，因此需要系统研究其相图特征及调控规律。

Method: 实验上测量了向列相物质5CB与简单液体溶剂（角鲨烷和/或角鲨烯）混合物的相行为；理论上采用结合经典液体混合模型与向列相有序模型（classical models of liquid mixing and nematic ordering）的平均场模型（mean-field model）进行定量描述。

Result: 观测到两种二元相图类型：存在和不存在各向同性-各向同性共存区（isotropic-isotropic coexistence）。通过改变角鲨烯与角鲨烷的比例，连续调变了表观二元系统的相边界，并揭示了三相共存区（three-phase coexistence）。

Conclusion: 所提出的平均场模型能够定量描述二元和三元相行为，预测了一系列拓扑复杂的三元相图，并可自然推广至更多组分的系统。

Abstract: Liquid mixtures with a nematogen can undergo both fluid phase separation and a transition from an isotropic to a nematic state. These phase transitions can couple and lead to phase behavior distinct from simple liquid mixtures or pure liquid crystals. We measured the phase behavior of mixtures of a nematogen (5CB) with simple liquid solvents (squalane and/or squalene). We observed two distinct kinds of binary phase diagrams: with and without a region of isotropic-isotropic coexistence. Varying the ratio of squalene to squalane, we continuously tuned the phase boundaries of the apparent binary system and revealed a region of three-phase coexistence. A mean-field model combining classical models of liquid mixing and nematic ordering quantitatively describes both binary and ternary phase behavior. This simple model predicts a range of topologically complex ternary phase diagrams and extends naturally to systems with more components.

</details>


### [57] [Directional Symmetry Breaking of Spherical Active Colloids by Magnetoviscous Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26458)
*Ziyang Zhou,Takuya Kobayashi,Keita Saito,Masato Ito,Kohei Yoshinaga,Yasutaka Iwashita,Kazusa Beppu,Yusuke T. Maeda*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过铁磁流体（ferrofluid）在均匀磁场下的各向异性黏性响应，实现了对磁性惰性活性胶体（active colloids）的转向控制，并揭示了由游动者产生流场与各向异性旋转黏度耦合所导致的涌现重定向力矩（emergent reorientation torque），为基于各向异性流变学（anisotropic rheology）将黏性耗散转化为方向对称性破缺提供了流体力学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用活性物质（active matter）需要在不改变自驱推进机制本身的前提下打破自驱运动的方向对称性。现有方法往往直接操控粒子或其推进速度，而本研究旨在探索一种不依赖直接磁场操控的转向策略。

Method: 实验上，将磁性惰性的自驱动Janus胶体（Janus colloids）置于均匀磁场下的铁磁流体中，通过铁磁流体的各向异性黏性响应诱导胶体产生垂直于磁场方向的稳健横向运动（cross-field motion）。理论上，采用磁黏性介质中的squirmer模型（squirmer model）进行定量描述，揭示重定向力矩来源于游动者产生流场与各向异性旋转黏度的耦合。

Result: 定性结果表明，自驱动Janus胶体在均匀磁场下表现出稳健的横向运动，而磁场既不直接控制粒子也不控制其推进速度。定量测量显示，涌现出的重定向力矩随推进速度和磁场强度增大而增大。squirmer模型成功捕捉了这些实验观测。

Conclusion: 本研究表明可以通过各向异性流变学将黏性耗散转化为方向对称性破缺，为通过磁场控制活性物质实现材料输运提供了一条新途径，建立了基于各向异性流变学的活性物质流体力学控制基础。

Abstract: Harnessing active matter requires strategies that break the directional symmetry of self-propelled motion without altering the propulsion mechanism itself. Here, we show that magnetically inert spherical active colloids can be steered through the anisotropic viscous response of a ferrofluid under a uniform magnetic field. Self-propelled Janus colloids exhibit robust cross-field motion transverse to the magnetic field, although the applied magnetic field directly controls neither the particles nor their propulsion speed. Quantitative measurements reveal an emergent reorientation torque that grows with propulsion speed and magnetic field strength. A squirmer model in a magnetoviscous medium captures these observations and shows that the torque arises from the coupling between swimmer-generated flow and anisotropic rotational viscosity. Our findings establish a hydrodynamic foundation for converting viscous dissipation into directional symmetry breaking through anisotropic rheology, providing a route to field-controlled material transport by active matter.

</details>


### [58] [Super-Arrhenius Dynamic Slowdown Revealed by Slow Variable Modulation in the Fragile Supercooled Liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26541)
*Zhiye Tang,Shubham Kumar,Shinji Saito*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过分析Kob-Andersen Lennard-Jones (KALJ)模型中粒子跳跃动力学，揭示了超过冷液体中超阿伦尼乌斯（super-Arrhenius）动态减缓的微观机制：第一配位壳层外区域的分布偏移导致跳跃速率涨落增强，且该行为随温度降低扩展至更远的配位壳层，其空间增长与静态关联长度的增加密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脆弱过冷液体（fragile supercooled liquids）中的超阿伦尼乌斯动态减缓是凝聚态物理学（condensed matter physics）尚未解决的核心问题之一，需要揭示其微观机制。

Method: 以跳跃粒子的位移作为反应坐标（reaction coordinate），分析KALJ模型中的粒子跳跃动力学；通过将存活概率（survival probability）与使用分布作为慢变量（slow variable）的慢涨落极限（slow-fluctuation limit）进行比较，验证该变量对跳跃动力学的调制作用。

Result: 低温下非泊松动力学（non-Poissonian dynamics）显现；轻度过冷时，跳跃粒子第一配位壳层的外区域在跳跃过程中出现显著分布偏移；该区域的粒子调制跳跃动力学、增强跳跃速率涨落，从而诱导动态减缓；随温度降低，该行为扩展至第二配位壳层及更远区域，加剧减缓；慢变量的空间增长与静态关联长度（static correlation length）的增加存在紧密对应关系。

Conclusion: 该结果首次为KALJ模型中的超阿伦尼乌斯动态减缓提供了微观机制解释。

Abstract: The super-Arrhenius dynamic slowdown in fragile supercooled liquids remains one of the central unresolved questions in condensed matter physics. In this study, we analyze particle jump dynamics in a prototypical fragile glass-forming liquid, the Kob-Andersen Lennard-Jones (KALJ) model. Using the displacement of jumping particles as the reaction coordinate, we demonstrate the emergence of non-Poissonian dynamics as the temperature decreases. In the mildly supercooled regime, the outer region of the first coordination shell of a jumping particle exhibits a significant distribution shift during the jump motion. By comparing the survival probability with its slow-fluctuation limit using this distribution as a slow variable, we confirm that particles in this region modulate the jump dynamics, enhance the jump rate fluctuations, and thereby induce the dynamic slowdown as supercooling proceeds. As the temperature decreases, this behavior extends to the outer regions of the second coordination shell and beyond, intensifying the dynamic slowdown. This spatial growth of the slow variables responsible for dynamic disorder exhibits close correspondence with an increase in the static correlation length. These results provide a microscopic mechanism for the super-Arrhenius dynamic slowdown in the KALJ model.

</details>


### [59] [Chirality-Driven Hierarchical Morphologies in Self-Assembled Biaxial Amphiphiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26716)
*Sayantan Mondal,Jayashree Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究了分子尺度手性（chirality）如何驱动两亲分子（amphiphiles）自组装形成多种扭曲液晶相（liquid crystalline phases），并揭示了从微观手性到介观结构（mesoscale structure）形成的层级有序演化及其与疏水相互作用（hydrophobic interaction）竞争的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管生物和合成材料中普遍存在由自组装（self-assembly）导致的扭曲或螺旋聚集体，但分子尺度手性如何引发两亲分子复杂扭曲形态的微观机制尚不清楚，现有理论和实验研究均未充分揭示这一过程。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟，系统改变分子相对浓度和固有手性（intrinsic chirality），并通过取向关联函数（orientational correlation functions）表征自发生成的平衡态扭曲液晶结构。

Result: 手性变化驱动了层状（lamellar）、柱状（cylindrical）和囊泡状（vesicular）等多种扭曲液晶相的序列出现；手性增加诱导系统内层级手性有序（hierarchical chiral order）的演化；进一步提高手性会与疏水相互作用竞争，导致形态不稳定性（morphological instabilities）。

Conclusion: 研究建立了微观手性与介观结构形成及其不稳定性之间的直接联系，并对观察到的相形态的流动性（liquidity）和螺距（pitch）与手性量之间的关系进行了定性比较。

Abstract: Chirality plays a crucial role in determining the structure of many systems in nature. Twisted or helical aggregates as a consequence of self-assembly can be seen in many biological and synthetic materials. Despite extensive theoretical and experimental efforts, how molecular-scale chirality gives rise to complex twisted morphologies in amphiphiles still remains unexplored. Here we study the interplay between molecular hydrophobicity, shape anisotropy and chirality using molecular dynamics simulation. Variation of relative molecular concentration and intrinsic chirality of molecules drive a sequence of twisted liquid crystalline variants of lamellar, cylindrical and vesicular phases. These structures emerge spontaneously under equilibrium conditions and are characterized by orientational correlation functions. We demonstrate that variation in molecular chirality gives rise to the development of hierarchical chiral order within the system. Further increment of chirality competes with hydrophobic interactions, leading to morphological instabilities. Our findings establish a direct link between microscopic chirality and mesoscale structure formation and their instabilities. Qualitative comparison of liquidity and pitch of the observed phase morphologies with the amount of chirality has been reported.

</details>


### [60] [Dynamics of ring polymer melts: Memory function approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26905)
*Nail Fatkullin,Carlos Mattea,Kevin Lindt,Siegfried Stapf,Margarita Kruteva*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过引入有效吸引势（effective attractive potential）和记忆函数（memory function），采用重整化Rouse形式体系（renormalized Rouse formalism）研究环状聚合物（ring polymer）的静态与动态性质，提出了描述自扩散系数随分子量指数衰减的自洽近似方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有环状聚合物的理论模型难以同时解释静态构象与动态缠结效应，尤其是大分子量下自扩散行为的异常衰减，需要一种改进的解析框架来统一描述这些现象。

Method: 在标准Rouse环模型基础上引入一个有效球对称吸引势（描述熵性质）和一个记忆函数（描述动态缠结效应）。采用重整化Rouse形式体系近似记忆矩阵的时间依赖性，并为大分子量情形提出一种改进的自洽近似（self-consistent approximation）。

Result: 所得结果与现有实验数据和计算机模拟结果吻合良好。对于大分子量环，自洽近似成功描述了自扩散系数随分子量指数衰减的行为，即动态局域化（dynamic localization）效应。

Conclusion: 所提出的理论框架能够有效捕捉环状聚合物的静态与动态性质，尤其是大分子量下的动态局域化现象，为理解环状聚合物的缠结动力学提供了新的解析途径。

Abstract: We investigated the static and dynamic properties of a Rouse ring polymer modified by introducing an effective, spherically symmetric, attractive potential of entropic nature and a memory function describing the effect of dynamic entanglement. Renormalized Rouse formalism is used to approximate the time dependence of the memory matrix. The results obtained are in good agreement with existing experimental data and the results of computer simulations of ring polymer ring with , , where N_e is the number of Kuhn segments in linear polymer melts between neighboring entanglements and , the number of Kuhn segments. For large molecular weights, a refined self-consistent approximation is proposed to describe the time dependence of the memory function. It is shown that this approximation allows us to describe an exponential decrease in the self-diffusion coefficient with molecular weight of the rings, i.e., the effect of dynamic localization.

</details>


### [61] [Structure and energetics of grain boundaries in self-assembled double-gyroid block copolymer networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26927)
*Jing Chen,Aiping Zhu,Dan Wei,An-Chang Shi,Kai Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）框架系统研究了双螺旋（double-gyroid, DG）嵌段共聚物网络中的晶界（grain boundary, GB）结构与能量学，发现了一种能量最低的未识别不对称倾斜网络切换晶界（ATNS），并揭示了DG网络中晶界稳定性主要由熵驱动，而非焓主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶界（grain boundaries, GBs）是晶体材料中普遍存在的缺陷，但在嵌段共聚物有序相中研究较少。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统探索DG嵌段共聚物网络中的GB结构及其能量学特征。

Method: 采用自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）框架，计算DG嵌段共聚物网络中晶界能量随晶界取向的变化，并对代表性低能和高能晶界进行对比分析。

Result: GB能量景观呈现多个局部极小值，对应不同的网络切换晶界（network-switching GBs）。全局最小值为此前未识别的非对称倾斜网络切换晶界（asymmetric-tilt network-switching GB, ATNS），其能量低于实验观测到的(422)孪晶界（twin boundary, TB）。

Conclusion: 与焓主导的硬物质不同，DG网络中晶界稳定性主要由熵驱动。扭转晶界（twist-type GBs）产生新节点并破坏节点共面性，导致链堆积受阻和较大的熵惩罚；而ATNS保留了有利的网络连通性，最小化了对聚合物链构象的限制，因而成为能量上最优先的晶界。

Abstract: Grain boundaries (GBs) are ubiquitous defects in crystalline materials. However, they remain less explored in block copolymer ordered phases. Here, we develop a self-consistent field theory framework to investigate GB structure and energetics in double-gyroid (DG) diblock copolymer networks. The GB energy landscape is obtained as a function of GB orientation, which reveals multiple local minima representing distinct network-switching GBs. Remarkably, the global minimum is a previously unidentified asymmetric-tilt network-switching GB (ATNS), exhibiting a lower energy than the experimentally observed $(422)$ twin boundary (TB). Comparative analyses of representative low- (ATNS, $(422)$ TB) and high-energy twist ($(0\bar{1}\bar{1})$, $(100)$ TNSs) GBs reveal that, unlike enthalpy-dominated hard matter, GB stability in DG networks is predominantly entropy-driven. Twist-type GBs generate new nodes and disrupt nodal coplanarity, causing chain packing frustration and large entropy penalties. Conversely, the ATNS preserves favorable network connectivity and minimizes conformational constraints on polymer chains, making it the energetically preferred GB.

</details>


### [62] [Kinetic Superselectivity in Multivalent Binding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27019)
*Vid Ravnik,Baptiste Chabaud,Urban Bren,Galina V. Dubacheva,Tine Curk*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文结合透明质酸聚合物实验、随机化学动力学模型（stochastic chemical kinetics）与分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），系统研究多价结合（multivalent binding）的动力学行为。研究发现，结合与解离动力学均能比平衡结合（equilibrium binding）更具选择性，并基于快弱与慢强相互作用的两步结合模型（two-step binding model）解释该现象，提出了一种基于结合速率（association rate）而非平衡态的超选择性靶向（superselective targeting）新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多价结合利用多个同时发生的超分子相互作用，相比单价结合具有更高的亲和力（avidity）和选择性。然而，尽管多价结合的平衡性质已被充分表征，其非平衡动力学行为仍未被充分理解。

Method: 采用透明质酸聚合物（hyaluronic acid polymer）实验、基于随机化学动力学（stochastic chemical kinetics）的动力学建模以及分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），对多价结合的动力学进行系统研究。

Result: 发现多价结合的结合和解离动力学均可比其平衡结合更具选择性。通过包含快弱相互作用与慢强相互作用的两步结合模型（two-step binding model）解释了这一行为。

Conclusion: 提出一种基于结合速率而非平衡态（equilibrium state）的超选择性靶向（superselective targeting）新方法。本文的动力学理论与实验为多价动力学（multivalent kinetics）提供了基础理解，并为非平衡系统（out-of-equilibrium systems）中的超选择性靶向建立了设计规则。

Abstract: Multivalent binding employs multiple simultaneous supramolecular interactions, increasing avidity and selectivity compared with monovalent binding. While equilibrium aspects of multivalency are well characterized, non-equilibrium behavior remains poorly understood. By combining experiments on hyaluronic acid polymers with kinetic modeling based on stochastic chemical kinetics and molecular dynamics simulations, we systematically investigate the kinetics of multivalent binding. Notably, we find that both association and dissociation kinetics can be more selective than equilibrium binding. We explain this behavior using a two-step binding model featuring a combination of fast, weak and slow, strong interactions. These findings demonstrate a new approach: superselective targeting based on the association rate instead of the equilibrium state. The kinetic theory and experiments presented here provide a fundamental understanding of multivalent kinetics and establish design rules for superselective targeting in out-of-equilibrium systems.

</details>


### [63] [Designing Multivalent Copolymers for Selective Targeting of Multicomponent Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27040)
*Vid Ravnik,Urban Bren,Tine Curk*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过巨正则蒙特卡洛模拟（grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations）发现，通过设计共聚物（copolymer）上的配体分布，可以高选择性地靶向具有特定受体密度谱（receptor density profile）的膜表面。最佳选择性要求配体谱与受体谱匹配，且配体-受体亲和力与配体谱成反比；相较于纳米颗粒，聚合物构象带来的熵效应显著增强了结合选择性。随机共聚物（random copolymer）对整体受体浓度选择性最优，而规则共聚物（regular copolymer）对特定受体谱选择性最强，但若同种配体形成均匀嵌段则可能出现反选择性（anti-selective）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 选择性靶向具有特定受体谱（receptor profile）的膜是靶向药物递送中的一个持续挑战，本工作旨在探索如何通过设计聚合物配体分布来实现对特定受体密度谱的高选择性靶向。

Method: 采用巨正则蒙特卡洛模拟（grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations），研究共聚物（copolymer）在多组分受体覆盖表面上的吸附行为。

Result: 聚合物的配体分布与靶向受体谱匹配且配体-受体亲和力与配体谱成反比时可实现靶向；聚合物相比纳米颗粒因构象熵效应具有更高选择性；随机共聚物（random copolymer）对整体受体浓度选择性最优，规则共聚物（regular copolymer）对特定受体谱选择性最强，但同种配体形成均匀嵌段时会出现反选择性（anti-selective）；配体分布关键而持续长度（persistence length）不显著影响选择性。

Conclusion: 序列控制（sequence control）是线性共聚物选择性靶向特定膜受体密度谱的必要条件。

Abstract: Selective targeting of membranes with a specific receptor profile is an ongoing challenge in targeted drug delivery. We investigate the adsorption of copolymers on a multicomponent receptor-covered surface using grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations and demonstrate that polymers can be designed to target a particular receptor density profile. To achieve this, the ligand profile on the polymers should match the targeted receptor profile, and the ligand--receptor affinity should be inversely proportional to the ligand profile. While the same can be obtained using multivalent nanoparticles, the entropic effects due to polymer conformations significantly enhance the binding selectivity of multivalent polymers compared to nanoparticles. Surprisingly, the ligand distribution on the polymer plays a crucial role, whereas the persistence length does not. The optimal selectivity to the overall receptor concentration is obtained by the Poisson distribution of ligands (random copolymer), whereas the maximal selectivity to a specific receptor profile is obtained by a defined sequence of grouped alternating ligands (regular copolymer). Interestingly, the regular copolymer can become anti-selective when ligands of the same type are in homogenous blocks, showing that specific ligand distribution qualitatively affects the targeting ability. These findings suggest that sequence control is necessary to selectively target a specific density profile of membrane receptors using linear copolymers.

</details>


### [64] [Resolving Capillary Mode Transitions in Microparticles at Fluid Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27251)
*Sungwan Park,Justin Jeongwoo Choi,Albert Tianxiang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与理论结合，揭示了流体界面处微粒自组装中从单极毛细作用到四极毛细作用的转变机制，发现传统邦德数（Bond number）不足以预测该转变，进而提出一个新的无量纲参数作为通用设计规则，用于预测引力诱导的单极吸引与表面钉扎诱导的四极吸引之间的主导关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微尺度高纵横比（高宽比）颗粒是构筑形状导向自组装材料的有前景的基元，但控制其组装的毛细作用规则尚不完全清晰，特别是单极（monopolar）与四极（quadrupolar）两种毛细作用 regime 之间的转变机制未被充分理解。

Method: 结合实验观测与理论分析，系统研究颗粒在流体界面处的毛细相互作用，识别并引入了一个新的无量纲参数，该参数综合了颗粒尺寸、密度、表面粗糙度（surface roughness）、接触角（contact angle）和四极强度等关键因素。

Result: 传统邦德数因忽略了材料和表面形貌效应而无法预测单极与四极毛细作用之间的转变；新提出的无量纲参数能够准确预测何种吸引机制（重力诱导的单极吸引或表面钉扎诱导的四极吸引）占主导地位。

Conclusion: 所建立的模型解释了颗粒在多个长度尺度上的自组织行为，为工程化设计基于微型颗粒构建块（particulate building blocks）的下一代界面材料提供了指导性原则。

Abstract: Capillarity-driven self-assembly at fluidic interfaces offers a scalable route to large, reconfigurable materials. Microscale particles with high horizontal-to-vertical aspect ratios become attractive building blocks for shape-directed organization, but the capillary rules governing their assembly remain incompletely understood. Here, we combine experiments and theory to explain the transition between two capillary regimes: monopolar interactions arising from millimeter-scale curved interfaces, and quadrupolar interactions arising from local contact-line distortions. We show that the conventional Bond number is insufficient to predict this transition because it omits key material and surface-topography effects. Instead, we identify a new dimensionless parameter that captures the coupled roles of particle size, density, surface roughness, contact angle, and quadrupolar strength. This criterion correctly predicts when gravitationally induced monopolar attraction or surface-pinning-induced quadrupolar attraction dominates, providing a general design rule for interfacial particle assembly. The resulting model explains how particles self-organize across length scales and offers guiding principles for engineering next-generation interfacial materials from miniaturized particulate building blocks.

### [65] [Geometry and relaxation dynamics of nematic loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27297)
*F. Aprile,A. J. H. Houston,G. Gonnella,D. Marenduzzo,T. N. Shendruk,G. Negro*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对三维向列相液晶中向错环（disclination loops）的几何描述提出了一种基于克利福德代数 Cl(3,0) 的方法，将局部缺陷剖面的几何信息编码为 SU(2) 和乐（holonomy），并发现该几何结构直接决定了缺陷环的动力学演化，包括拓扑液滴的成核、自扭转导致的附加链接环产生以及不同剖面过渡模式下的拓扑行为差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的同伦论（homotopy theory）分类仅能捕捉向错环的全局拓扑特征，但无法编码沿环的缺陷剖面（defect profile）几何结构，而这一几何信息强烈影响缺陷动力学。因此，需要一种能够自然描述局部几何及其沿环变化的几何描述框架。

Method: 采用克利福德代数 Cl(3,0) 对向错环进行几何描述，将局部缺陷剖面的几何信息及其沿环的变化编码为 SU(2) 和乐（holonomy）。通过数值模拟研究嵌入向列相液晶中具有特定几何结构的缺陷环的动力学演化行为。

Result: 数值模拟发现，向错环会成核出被称为“拓扑液滴（topological blobs）”的缺陷结构，随后这些液滴耗散并留下均匀的向列织构（uniform nematic textures）。缺陷剖面的自扭转（self-twist）会引发附加的链接向错线（linking disclination lines）的成核，且总自扭转与链接数（linking number）之间存在简单的算术关系。具有偶数个离散剖面转变的环则产生环间穿线程但无链接的结构。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了向错环的几何和乐与其后续动力学演化之间的直接联系，为理解缺陷环的演化机制提供了几何框架。该描述方法有望推广至更复杂的有序参量流形（order parameter manifolds），如胆甾相（cholesterics）或近晶相（smectics）液晶。

Abstract: Disclination lines in three-dimensional nematic liquid crystals generically form closed loops whose topology is classified by homotopy theory. While this classification successfully captures global topological features, it does not encode the geometry of the defect profile along the loop, which can strongly influence defect dynamics. Here, we propose a geometric description of nematic disclination loops using the Clifford algebra Cl(3,0). This approach naturally captures the geometry of the local defect profile, as well as changes along the loop, which is mathematically a SU(2) holonomy. Simulations of the dynamics of defect loops with specified geometries embedded in nematic liquid crystals demonstrate that loops nucleate the growth of "topological blobs" of defects, which later dissipate leaving uniform nematic textures. Self-twist of the defect profile leads to nucleation of additional linking disclination lines, with a simple arithmetic relation between total self-twist and linking number. In contrast, loops with an even number of discrete profile transitions generate patterns with threading between loops, but no linking. These results establish a direct connection between the geometric holonomy of a disclination loop and its subsequent evolution, and may be extendable to more complex order parameter manifolds, such as cholesterics or smectics.

</details>

### [66] [ModMax black hole surrounded by perfect-fluid dark matter in Lorentz-violating Kalb-Ramond gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26131)
*Fernando M. Belchior,Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在洛伦兹破缺的Kalb-Ramond引力框架下，研究了被完美流体暗物质包围的ModMax黑洞，分析了非线性电动力学、洛伦兹对称性破缺和暗物质环境对黑洞几何、热力学及稳定性的联合影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验超出标准带电黑洞热力学的偏离，探索非线性电动力学与洛伦兹破缺在暗物质环境中的耦合效应。

Method: 在洛伦兹破缺的Kalb-Ramond引力框架下，融合ModMax非线性电动力学、背景Kalb-Ramond场导致的洛伦兹对称性破缺以及完美流体暗物质环境，求解静态球对称黑洞几何，并计算霍金温度、熵、热容和亥姆霍兹自由能等热力学量。

Result: ModMax电动力学可有效屏蔽电扇区；Kalb-Ramond参数放大几何变形并改变热力学响应；暗物质贡献额外的对数修正，在中等径向尺度尤为显著；三者联合效应会移动极端构型、改变热稳定区域并产生非平凡相行为。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹破缺背景下的暗物质环绕黑洞为探测标准带电黑洞热力学的偏离提供了一个有用的检验平台。

Abstract: We investigate a ModMax black hole surrounded by perfect-fluid dark matter within the framework of Lorentz-violating Kalb-Ramond gravity. The model combines three physically distinct contributions: nonlinear electrodynamic corrections from the ModMax sector, Lorentz-symmetry-breaking effects induced by the background Kalb-Ramond field, and environmental modifications associated with the surrounding dark matter fluid. We obtain the corresponding static and spherically symmetric black hole geometry and analyze how the charge, ModMax parameter, Kalb-Ramond coupling, and dark matter parameter affect the horizon structure and thermodynamic behavior. In particular, we study the Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity, and Helmholtz free energy, showing that the combined effects of nonlinear electrodynamics and Lorentz violation may shift the extremal configuration, modify the thermal stability regions, and generate nontrivial phase behavior. The perfect fluid dark matter contribution introduces an additional logarithmic correction to the geometry, becoming especially relevant at intermediate radial scales. Our results indicate that ModMax electrodynamics can effectively screen the electric sector, while the Kalb-Ramond parameter amplifies the geometric deformation and changes the thermodynamic response of the system. These features suggest that black holes in Lorentz-violating backgrounds surrounded by dark matter provide a useful arena for probing deviations from standard charged black-hole thermodynamics.

*Antonio Capolupo,Salvatore Capozziello,Gabriele Pisacane,Aniello Quaranta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文回顾了弯曲时空量子场论框架下的新近结果：中微子味真空的半经典能量-动量张量满足尘埃和冷暗物质的状态方程，且在弱场近似下贡献出对牛顿势的汤川修正，从而为解释螺旋星系平坦旋转曲线提供了可能机制，表明中微子混合可作为暗物质的一个可行贡献因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索中微子混合（neutrino mixing）在弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）框架下是否能够解释暗物质（dark matter）现象，特别是螺旋星系（spiral galaxy）的平坦旋转曲线（flat rotation curve）。

Method: 在弯曲时空量子场论框架内，计算中微子味真空（neutrino flavor vacuum）的半经典能量-动量张量（semiclassical energy-momentum tensor），并在弱场近似（weak field approximation）下考虑球对称时空（spherically symmetric spacetimes），分析其对牛顿势（Newtonian potential）的修正。

Result: 中微子味真空的能量-动量张量满足尘埃（dust）和冷暗物质（cold dark matter）的状态方程（equation of state）；该真空在弱场近似下产生对牛顿势的汤川修正（Yukawa correction），可解释螺旋星系的平坦旋转曲线。

Conclusion: 中微子混合（neutrino mixing）可能是宇宙暗物质（dark matter）的一个可行贡献因素。

Abstract: We review recent results showing that, within the framework of quantum field theory in curved spacetime, the semiclassical energy-momentum tensor of the neutrino flavor vacuum fulfills the equation of state of dust and cold dark matter. By considering spherically symmetric spacetimes in the weak field approximation, the flavor vacuum is shown to contribute as a Yukawa correction to the Newtonian potential. We discuss how this modified potential provides a mechanism to account for the flat rotation curves of spiral galaxies. In this perspective, neutrino mixing is presented as a viable contributing factor to the dark matter content of the universe.

</details>


### [68] [Covariant Dynamical Systems Formulation of the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26187)
*Eduardo Bittencourt,Mariam Campbell,Peter K. S. Dunsby,Sergio E. Jorás*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论框架下，利用1+1+2半标架形式体系重新审视了静态球对称理想流体恒星模型，将Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff系统转化为协变一阶动力系统，并针对不同物态方程（EoS）分析了其相空间结构，在线性EoS下简化为二维平面动力系统，在多方EoS下表现为三维动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于相对论性恒星模型的研究主要基于度规描述，缺乏一种协变（covariant）且几何意义清晰的动力系统视角。本文旨在通过1+1+2半标架形式体系，将TOV系统重构为低维自治流，从而揭示其相空间结构与稳定性特征的几何解释。

Method: 采用1+1+2半标架形式体系（semi-tetrad formalism）处理局部转动对称（locally rotationally symmetric）静态时空；将TOV系统表达为协变一阶动力系统，通过适当归一化将其重构为三维自治流（autonomous flow）；在线性物态方程情形下进一步降维为二维平面动力系统，分析其有限与渐近平衡点及其稳定性。

Result: 在线性物态方程（EoS）情形下，系统可降为平面动力系统，其有限平衡点与渐近平衡点及其稳定性具有清晰的协变变量几何解释；对于多方物态方程（polytropic EoS）等更一般情形，动力学系统自然呈现真正的三维特征。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种紧凑、协变且物理透明的相对论性恒星问题重构，阐明了标准度规描述如何被编码在一个由几何意义明确的协变变量构造的全局相空间结构之中。

Abstract: We revisit static, spherically symmetric perfect-fluid stellar models in General Relativity within the framework of the $1+1+2$ semi-tetrad formalism. For locally rotationally symmetric static spacetimes, the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff system can be expressed as a covariant first-order dynamical system and, after suitable normalization, reformulated as a three-dimensional autonomous flow for a general equation of state (EoS). In the case of a linear EoS, the system reduces further to a planar dynamical system whose finite and asymptotic equilibrium points, together with their stability properties, admit a clear geometrical interpretation in terms of covariant variables. For more general equations of state, such as the polytropic case, the dynamics naturally acquire a genuinely three-dimensional character. Beyond providing a compact, covariant, and physically transparent reformulation of the relativistic stellar problem, the present analysis clarifies how the standard metric description is encoded within a global phase-space structure constructed from geometrically meaningful covariant variables.

</details>


### [69] [Black string immersed in perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26198)
*L. G. Barbosa,L. C. N. Santos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在反德西特背景下的完美流体暗物质中，精确构造了一个四维黑弦解。通过求解各向异性流体的爱因斯坦场方程，得到了由暗物质参数α通过对数项修正的度规函数。利用朗伯W函数解析确定了事件视界半径，并通过克雷奇曼标量验证了原点处的曲率奇异性与渐近行为。热力学分析表明，在弱能量条件被违反的区间，热容在临界视界半径处发散，暗示存在热力学相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质与黑弦（black string）这类高维引力物体在反德西特（anti-de Sitter, AdS）背景下的相互作用，旨在构建一个包含暗物质效应的精确黑弦解，并分析其几何与热力学性质。

Method: 首先对各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid）假设下的爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）进行求解，得到一个包含由暗物质参数α决定的对数项的度规函数。随后利用朗伯W函数（Lambert W function）解析确定事件视界（event horizon）半径，并通过克雷奇曼标量（Kretschmann scalar）检验曲率奇异性。最后通过热容（heat capacity）分析热力学稳定性及相变行为。

Result: 得到了一个精确的四维AdS黑弦解，其度规在完美流体暗物质（perfect fluid dark matter）的修正下出现对数项。事件视界半径可由朗伯W函数解析表达；原点处存在本征曲率奇异性，渐近行为符合预期。对于α>0的情形，热容在某一临界视界半径处发散，对应于弱能量条件（weak energy condition）被违反区域中的热力学相变（thermodynamic phase transition）。

Conclusion: 成功构建了AdS背景下浸没于完美流体暗物质中的黑弦精确解，揭示了暗物质参数对时空几何与热力学相变的关键调控作用。该结果为研究暗物质与黑洞/黑弦热力学的耦合提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We present an exact four-dimensional black string solution immersed in perfect fluid dark matter within an anti-de Sitter background. By solving the Einstein field equations for an anisotropic fluid, we obtain a metric function that modifies the standard black string geometry through a logarithmic term governed by the dark matter parameter $α$. The event horizon radii are analytically determined using the Lambert $W$ function, and the Kretschmann scalar confirms a genuine curvature singularity at the origin alongside the expected asymptotic behavior. Furthermore, we evaluate the thermodynamic properties of the solution. The heat capacity diverges at a critical horizon radius for $α>0$, a behavior commonly associated with a thermodynamic phase transition in a regime where the weak energy condition is violated.

</details>


### [70] [Trade-off Relation for Black Hole Entropy Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26214)
*Kensuke Gallock-Yoshimura,Yoshihiko Hasegawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在随机半经典引力（stochastic semiclassical gravity）框架内证明，黑洞视界（horizon）无法以任意小的熵涨落记录相关量子信息，并推导出黑洞熵变随机方差与光子数之间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞通过改变其熵来响应落入的量子物质场。由于这些物质本质上是量子的，其熵响应应敏感于量子涨落。本文旨在探究黑洞在记录量子信息时，其熵涨落是否存在基本限制。

Method: 在随机半经典引力（stochastic semiclassical gravity）的理论框架下展开分析，以Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald退相干实验中编码“哪条路径信息（which-path information）”的入射光子为具体对象，推导熵变方差与光子数之间的数学关系。

Result: 推导出一个权衡关系（trade-off relation）：黑洞熵变的随机方差（stochastic variance）与入射光子数之间存在相互制约，即黑洞无法以任意小的熵涨落来记录相关的量子信息。

Conclusion: 黑洞视界在记录量子信息时必然伴随不可忽视的熵涨落，这一结果为黑洞信息处理能力施加了基本限制，可能对理解黑洞信息悖论（black hole information paradox）具有启示意义。

Abstract: Black holes respond to infalling quantum matter fields by changing their entropy. Since such matter is quantum in nature, the entropy response should be sensitive to its quantum fluctuations. We show, within stochastic semiclassical gravity, that a horizon cannot record relevant quantum information with arbitrarily small entropy fluctuations. For the infalling photons encoding which-path information in the Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald decoherence experiment, we derive a trade-off relation between the stochastic variance of the black hole entropy change and the photon number.

</details>


### [71] [Donutization Inside Neutron Stars: Shell-Localized Scalar Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26228)
*Hao-Jui Kuan,Alan Tsz-Lok Lam,Jacquelyn Noronha-Hostler,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 标量-张量引力中的重标量场（$m_φ\gtrsim10^{-9}$ eV，康普顿波长小于中子星尺度）仍可通过壳层定域化（donutization）在中子星内部诱导标量化，改变有效物态方程，使强子星模仿夸克星或混合星的质量-半径行为，并打破转动惯量-四极矩（$I$--$Q$）关系，同时保持对双脉冲星观测不可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有理论认为，标量-张量引力中质量较大的标量场（$m_φ\gtrsim10^{-9}$ eV）因康普顿波长（Compton wavelength）小于中子星尺度，应无法被中子星观测所探测。本文旨在检验这一预期是否成立，并探究中子星在该情形下是否仍能发生标量化（scalarization）现象。

Method: 通过理论分析，证明重标量场可以在中子星内部形成壳层定域化（shell-localized）的轮廓——标量场在星体中心与外部被抑制，而在内部达到峰值。这种构型被称为“donutization”，并以此为基础重新计算有效物态方程（equation of state）及可观测量。

Result: Donutization效应重塑了有效物态方程，使强子星（hadronic star）展现出类似夸克星（quark star）的质量-半径行为，或表现出具有分裂稳定分支（split stable branches）的混合星（hybrid star）特征。同时，该效应打破了转动惯量-四极矩（$I$--$Q$）关系，但保持对双脉冲星（binary pulsar）观测的不可见性。

Conclusion: 重标量场在中子星内部仍可通过donutization机制诱导标量化，从而显著改变恒星的结构与可观测量，却不被现有脉冲星双星观测所排斥。这一发现挑战了此前关于重标量场不可观测的普遍认知，并为区分强子星与夸克星等致密天体提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: Heavy scalar fields ($m_φ\gtrsim10^{-9}$ eV) in scalar-tensor gravity are expected to be hidden from neutron-star observations because their Compton wavelength is sub-stellar. We show that neutron stars can nevertheless scalarize by forming a shell-localized profile, suppressed at their center and exterior but peaked in their interior. This \emph{donutization} reshapes the effective equation of state, making hadronic stars mimic quark-star mass-radius behavior or hybrid-star behavior with split stable branches, and breaks the $I$--$Q$ relation, while remaining hidden from binary pulsar observations.

</details>

*Rodrigo Calderon,Eric V. Linder*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在 Horndeski 引力（Horndeski gravity）框架下，通过引入平移对称项（shift symmetric terms）加上线性势（linear potential）实现有效暗能量（effective dark energy）跨越 $w=-1$ 的宇宙学模型，指出该类模型难以很好地拟合当前观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在修改引力理论中实现有效暗能量状态方程参数 $w$ 跨越 $w=-1$（即从 $w>-1$ 的"精质"区域进入 $w<-1$ 的"幻影"区域）的可能性，并检验此类模型与当前宇宙学观测数据的兼容性。

Method: 基于 Horndeski 引力理论，引入平移对称项与线性势构建模型；利用近乎守恒的标量荷（scalar charge）作为关键约束，推导宇宙演化方程并识别三种穿越 $w=-1$ 的途径；提供在线交互式应用程序求解演化方程组，供读者探索不同场景。

Result: 该理论对早期幻影行为（phantom behavior）具有高度可预测性；识别出的三种穿越 $w=-1$ 的途径均未能很好地重现当前数据所指示的条件；缺乏宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）且仅单次穿越 $w=-1$ 的简化修改引力模型难以拟合当前观测数据。

Conclusion: 仅含势项（不含宇宙学常数）且仅单次穿越 $w=-1$ 的 Horndeski 引力模型与当前观测数据存在显著张力，表明此类简化修改引力模型在解释暗能量观测方面面临困难。

Abstract: Cosmology where the effective dark energy crosses $w=-1$ can be realized in Horndeski gravity with shift symmetric terms plus a linear potential. We highlight the special role of the nearly conserved scalar charge. The theory is highly predictive for the early phantom behavior and we identify three ways to cross $w=-1$. None of them recreate conditions indicated by current data very well. The major lesson is that such modified gravity with a potential lacking a cosmological constant and only crossing $w=-1$ once (hence the less elaborate models) has difficulty fitting current data. We provide an online interactive application solving the system of evolution equations, for the reader to explore various scenarios at will.

### [73] [Superdilations at Schwarzschild null infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26296)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定义了渐近共形 Killing 视界，并在此框架下构造 Schwarzschild 时空未来零无穷远处的渐近共形对称性生成元，分析其所闭合的代数结构，并通过计算相关非平凡荷来检验超伸缩是否为纯规范变换。

Result: 所得代数因超伸缩的存在而成为 BMS 代数（Bondi–van der Burg–Metzner–Sachs algebra）的一种扩展版本；非平凡荷的存在排除了超伸缩是纯规范变换的假设；超伸缩对两个观测者的效应表现为与局域非零荷通量相关联的角度依赖红移。

Conclusion: Schwarzschild 时空中的渐近共形对称代数因超伸缩而得以扩展，且超伸缩对应非平凡荷，具有可观测的物理效应（角度依赖红移），因此不能被视为纯规范变换。

Abstract: Relying on the definition of asymptotic conformal Killing horizons, the generators of asymptotic conformal symmetries at future null infinity in Schwarzschild space-time are considered. The algebra they close is an extended version of the BMS one due to the presence of superdilations. Several features are then studied, such as the related non-trivial charge, excluding the hypothesis that superdilations are pure-gauge transformations. Their effect on two observers can be understood as an angle-dependent redshift, connected to the local nonvanishing flux of the charge.

### [74] [Holographic Thermodynamic Signatures of Simpson--Visser--AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26300)
*Saeed Noori Gashti,Behnam Pourhassan,Izzet Sakalli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对四维 Schwarzschild–anti–de Sitter (AdS) 黑洞的 Simpson–Visser (SV) 正则化版本进行了全息研究，发现当正则化参数 $\tilde{a} < 1/\sqrt{24}$ 时系统呈现范德瓦尔斯型多分支温度结构和三共存平衡态，拓扑荷 $W=+1$ 区别于 Schwarzschild-AdS ($W=0$)，表明 SV-AdS 属于正则 AdS 黑洞的普适类。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用 Simpson–Visser 正则化（Simpson–Visser regularization）替换 Schwarzschild–AdS 度规中的径向坐标 $r \to \sqrt{r^2+a^2}$，使度规在 $r=0$ 处正则；随后利用全息词典（holographic dictionary）解析推导边界熵、能量、温度和化学势，并借助拓扑矢量场（topological vector field）方法分析相变和局部缠绕数（local winding numbers）。

Result: SV 正则化参数 $a$ 以封闭形式形变边界热力学量；当 $\tilde{a} < \tilde{a}_c = 1/\sqrt{24} \approx 0.204$ 时，体温度呈现小/中/大分支的范德瓦尔斯型结构（van der Waals-type structure），离壳自由能支持三个共存平衡态；拓扑分析给出局部缠绕数 $(+1,-1,+1)$，总拓扑荷 $W=+1$。

Conclusion: SV-AdS 黑洞家族的总拓扑荷 $W=+1$ 与 Schwarzschild-AdS ($W=0$) 不同，而与 Bardeen-AdS 和 Hayward-AdS 等正则 AdS 黑洞相同，表明其属于正则 AdS 黑洞的普适类（universality class）。

Abstract: We study a Simpson--Visser regularization of the four-dimensional Schwarzschild--anti--de\,Sitter (SV--AdS) black hole, treated as the bulk dual of a planar conformal field theory (CFT) on the AdS boundary. The bulk lapse $f(r)=1-2M/\sqrt{r^2+a^2}+(r^2+a^2)/\ell^2$ is regular at $r=0$ for any $a>0$, and the holographic dictionary inherits this regularity at the boundary CFT level. We derive in closed form the boundary entropy, energy, temperature, and chemical potentials, and we trace how the SV regularization parameter $a$ deforms each of them as a function of the horizon radius. For $\tila<\tila_c=1/\sqrt{24}\approx 0.204$ the bulk temperature develops a van der Waals--type small/intermediate/large branch structure and the off-shell free energy supports three coexisting equilibria; the topological-vector-field analysis assigns local winding numbers $(+1,-1,+1)$ with total charge $W=+1$, matching the universality class of regular AdS black holes (Bardeen-AdS, Hayward-AdS) and distinguishing the SV-AdS family from Schwarzschild-AdS ($W=0$).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 准正态模/阴影上界与能量提取约束共同在(a/M, g/M)平面上显著缩小了g/M的允许区域，表明即使采用简化的单层赤道模型，这两种互补探针已能为NED变形参数提供信息丰富的约束。

Abstract: We study rotating black holes in general relativity coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED), focusing on an axisymmetric solution with deformation parameter g. On the spherical seed, weak-field lensing via the Gauss-Bonnet method and the shadow radius yield a spin-insensitive bound by enforcing a conservative ~10% tolerance on the Sgr A* ring size, namely g/M \lesssim 1.26. In the eikonal regime we derive analytic quasinormal-mode shifts, even in g, and obtain an independent ceiling consistent with the shadow constraint. For the rotating geometry, we provide closed-form ZAMO scalars, chart horizons and ergoregion, and analyze equatorial geodesics (photon orbits and ISCO). We then formulate in the ZAMO frame the Comisso-Asenjo reconnection channel, identify the negative-energy window, and integrate the extracted power over the allowed radii; from the tolerated fractional departure from the Kerr power we define a spin-dependent extraction bound g_δ(a|σ_0,ξ). Taken together, the QNM/shadow ceiling and the extraction bound appreciably narrow the admissible region for g/M in the (a/M, g/M) plane, so even within our deliberately simplified, single-layer equatorial setup, the two complementary probes already provide informative constraints on NED deformations, testable with present data and upcoming horizon-scale and ringdown campaigns.

### [76] [Thermodynamics and quasinormal modes of the regular Dymnikova-Letelier black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26372)
*L. C. N. Santos,L. G. Barbosa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从含有效各向异性流体（effective anisotropic fluid）的爱因斯坦场方程出发，解析推导黑洞的时空几何与热力学量（Hawking temperature, heat capacity, Gibbs free energy）；采用六阶WKB近似（sixth-order WKB approximation）计算标量扰动的准正则模（quasinormal modes）频谱。

Result: 热容发散揭示了与弦流体参数相关的相变（phase transitions）；所有参数下的准正则频率虚部为负、实部为正，表明黑洞对标量扰动稳定；弦流体参数的系统性变化导致振荡频率与衰减率的偏移。

Conclusion: 弦流体显著影响Dymnikova-Letelier时空的热力学行为与动力学稳定性；研究结果有助于理解含各向异性物质源的黑洞系统的全息性质与动力学响应。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermodynamic properties and quasinormal modes of a regular Dymnikova-Letelier black hole. Starting from the Einstein field equations sourced by an effective anisotropic fluid, we analyze the resulting spacetime geometry and derive the associated thermodynamic quantities, including the Hawking temperature, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy. The thermodynamic analysis reveals the existence of phase transitions characterized by divergences in the heat capacity, whose location depends sensitively on the string fluid parameter. We then study the dynamical response of the system under scalar perturbations by computing the quasinormal mode spectrum using the sixth-order WKB approximation. Our results show that, for all considered values of the parameters, the imaginary part of the quasinormal frequencies remains negative, while the real part stays positive, indicating the stability of the black hole under scalar perturbations. Furthermore, the presence of the string fluid leads to systematic shifts in both the oscillation frequencies and damping rates. These results demonstrate that the string fluid significantly affects both the thermodynamic behavior and the dynamical stability of the Dymnikova-Letelier spacetime.

### [77] [Generalized Entropies and Black Hole Area Quantization from Landauer's Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26386)
*Jorge Ananias Neto,Ronaldo Thibes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将Landauer原理（Landauer's principle）应用于黑洞离散熵变，推导出黑洞面积量子化谱。对于Bekenstein-Hawking熵（Bekenstein--Hawking entropy），得到标准的Bekenstein-Mukhanov面积谱参数；对于Barrow熵、修正Rényi熵和修正Kaniadakis熵等广义熵泛函，则揭示了参数依赖性、大n极限下相对间距的消失行为及奇异性等不同特征，表明Landauer原理为分析广义黑洞面积谱提供了有效框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞面积量子化（black hole area quantization）的谱结构，并将Landauer原理这一信息论约束推广到Barrow、Rényi和Kaniadakis等广义熵泛函上，以检验其面积谱是否仍具有Bekenstein-Mukhanov形式的规则性。

Method: 将Landauer原理施加于相邻面积能级之间的离散熵变上，将基本跃迁识别为擦除一比特信息对应的熵代价（\(ΔS=k_B\ln 2\)）；对Bekenstein-Hawking熵、Barrow熵、修正Rényi熵及修正Kaniadakis熵分别进行相同的离散构造，并分析面积谱参数在大小n极限下的行为。

Result: Bekenstein-Hawking熵恢复了标准Bekenstein-Mukhanov面积谱参数。Barrow熵中参数γ呈现能级依赖性，但相邻面积能级在大n下相对间隔仍趋于零。修正Rényi熵的非奇异分支大n下相对间距消失，奇异分支则出现有限极点。修正Kaniadakis熵在小κ展开下，固定形变参数（deformation parameter）使大n极限下相对间距无法消失。

Conclusion: Landauer原理为分析Bekenstein-Mukhanov面积谱的广义熵延伸提供了一个有用的理论框架，可用于区分不同广义熵模型在黑洞量子化中的行为特征。

Abstract: We investigate black hole area quantization by imposing Landauer's principle on the discrete entropy change between consecutive area levels. The elementary transition is identified with the entropy cost of erasing one bit of information, \(ΔS=k_B\ln 2\). For the Bekenstein--Hawking entropy, this gives the standard Bekenstein--Mukhanov value of the area spectrum parameter, which is used as the reference limit. The same discrete construction is then applied to generalized entropy functionals. For Barrow entropy, the parameter \(γ\) becomes level dependent, while the relative separation between adjacent area levels still vanishes for large \(n\). For the modified Rényi entropy, the nonsingular branch has vanishing relative spacing at large \(n\), whereas the singular branch develops a finite-level pole. For the modified Kaniadakis entropy, the small \(κ\) expansion shows that a fixed deformation parameter prevents the relative area spacing from vanishing in the large \(n\) limit. Overall, the results suggest that Landauer's principle provides a useful framework for analyzing generalized entropic extensions of the Bekenstein--Mukhanov area spectrum.

</details>


### [78] [Equatorial Circular Motion of Charged Test Particles in a Weakly Magnetized Taub--NUT Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26395)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于 Taub–NUT 度规在非零 NUT 参数 l 下不具有赤道反射对称性，带电粒子的轨道通常位于非零余纬的锥面上而非赤道平面，因此需要系统研究约束圆周运动及其稳定条件。

Method: 通过 Wald 方案引入弱外磁场，在赤道切片上对带电检验粒子施加约束条件 x = \dot{x} = 0 以获得约束圆周轨道，并以闭合形式导出残余的角向约束条件，进而推导圆轨道条件（circularity condition）和边缘稳定性条件（marginal-stability condition）。

Result: 磁场强度 B 的增大会单调降低 ISCO 半径；粒子电荷符号导致顺行与逆行分支的 ISCO 半径排序发生反转；Manko–Ruiz 参数 C 仅贡献次主导修正。

Conclusion: 约束圆周轨道的分析揭示了磁场和电荷符号对轨道稳定性的关键影响，下一步的自然拓展方向是研究完全自洽的锥面轨道。

Abstract: We study circular motion of charged test particles on the equatorial slice of a Taub--NUT black hole with Manko--Ruiz parameter $C$, immersed in a weak external magnetic field introduced via Wald's prescription. Because the Taub--NUT metric is not reflection-symmetric about the equator once $l\neq 0$, generic charged orbits lie on cones $x=\cosθ\neq 0$ rather than on the equatorial plane. We therefore analyse \emph{constrained} circular orbits obtained by imposing $x=\dot x=0$, and we exhibit in closed form the residual angular constraint that a fully self-consistent orbit would have to satisfy. Within this scope we derive the circularity and marginal-stability conditions and study how $B$ and $C$ shift the ISCO radius for prograde and retrograde branches. Increasing $B$ monotonically decreases $r_{\mathrm{ISCO}}$; the sign of the particle charge splits the two branches, with the ordering reversed between prograde and retrograde motion; and $C$ contributes only subleading corrections. The extension to self-consistent conical orbits is the natural direction for follow-up work.

</details>


### [79] [Universal Thermodynamic Topological Classes of BTZ Black Holes in Einstein and F(R) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26481)
*Yu-Die Wan,Peng Zhao,Meng-Yao Zhang,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc
