Result: F(R)引力修正改变了黑洞相对于爱因斯坦引力下BTZ黑洞的本征拓扑类（intrinsic topological class）；不同物质场进一步调制了拓扑分类结果；正则系综与巨正则系综下的黑洞拓扑类存在显著差异，且该差异与引力框架和物质场相关。

Conclusion: 引力框架、物质场和系综选择是决定黑洞拓扑分类的关键因素；所有识别出的拓扑类别均属于现有三维时空拓扑分类体系，表明其具有普遍性。该工作深化了对三维BTZ黑洞热力学-拓扑关联的理解，并为将此类拓扑分类推广到修正引力理论和不同物质场背景提供了严格理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we systematically study three classes of three-dimensional Bañados-Teitelboim-Zanelli (BTZ) black holes based on different gravitational frameworks and matter field structures: the Einstein-Maxwell BTZ, the F(R)-Maxwell BTZ, and the F(R)-phantom BTZ.Within the canonical and grand canonical ensemble frameworks, we construct the generalized free energy of these black hole systems and systematically analyze the asymptotic behavior of Hawking thermodynamics.The results indicate that both gravitational modifications and matter fields significantly influence black hole topology: the F(R) gravitational modification alters the intrinsic topological class of the black hole compared to the BTZ black hole under Einsteinian gravity, while different matter fields further modulate the topological classification results. Furthermore, by comparing the two types of ensembles, we find significant differences in black hole topological classes, and these differences are correlated with the gravitational framework and matter fields. In summary, the gravitational framework, matter fields, and ensemble selection are key factors governing the topological classification of black holes; all identified topological categories belong to the existing three-dimensional spacetime topological classification system, highlighting their universality. This work deepens our understanding of the thermodynamic-topological connection in three-dimensional BTZ black holes and provides a rigorous theoretical foundation for extending such topological classifications to modified gravity theories and different matter field backgrounds.

### [80] [Probing Spacetime Topology and Superposition with Accelerated Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26490)

Abstract: We study entanglement harvested by Unruh DeWitt detectors following Rindler trajectories in compactified and superposed Minkowski spacetime. We consider different directions of acceleration (both parallel and antiparallel), separation between detectors and direction of spatial compactification mutually perpendicular to each other. Using the standard entanglement harvesting protocol, we analyze how these features influence the extracted correlations. When detector separation is perpendicular to the direction of acceleration, the harvested entanglement is uniformly suppressed due to increased spacelike separation. Compactification enhances field correlations leading to an increased concurrence and an extended harvesting range at higher accelerations. Additionally, we show that spacetime superposition introduces interference effects that further enlarge the entanglement harvesting region in parameter space, particularly in the high acceleration regime. We also find that the effect of antiparallel acceleration yielding significantly higher entanglement than parallel acceleration prevails in compactified and superposed spacetime.

Method: 本文采用综述方法，系统梳理了闵可夫斯基时空稳定性理论中的主要思想与技术路线，尤其强调了衰减假设、几何叶状结构、能量恒等式以及规范选择在全局分析（global analysis）中的作用，并对外部稳定性结果、最小衰减机制以及边界情形中的阈值现象进行了特别关注。

Result: 文章指出，在边界情形中，非线性相互作用的时空可积性（spacetime integrability）的失效揭示了微妙的阈值现象；同时，论文提供了对该领域演化过程的连贯视角，并明确了已知结果背后的结构机制。

Conclusion: 本文旨在为该领域提供一个整合性视角，澄清已有结果背后的结构机制，并勾勒出在边界机制中仍待解决的核心开放问题。

Abstract: The nonlinear stability of Minkowski spacetime has been one of the central achievements in the mathematical theory of general relativity and, more broadly, in the analysis of nonlinear geometric wave equations. Since the seminal work of Christodoulou-Klainerman, the problem has shaped fundamental advances in our understanding of decay, dispersion, and the intricate interplay between geometry and analysis in the Einstein vacuum equations.
  This survey presents an overview of the main ideas and techniques underlying the stability theory of Minkowski spacetime. We emphasize the role of decay assumptions, geometric foliations, energy identities, and gauge choices in the global analysis. Particular attention is devoted to exterior stability results, minimal decay regimes, and the borderline case, where the failure of spacetime integrability for nonlinear interactions reveals subtle threshold phenomena.
  Our goal is to provide a coherent perspective on the evolution of the field, to clarify the structural mechanisms behind the known results, and to outline some of the central open problems that remain in the borderline regime.

### [82] [Are Petrov type-N and D spacetimes admitting CTCs valid in $f(R,\mathcal{L}_m,Φ,X)$ gravity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26696)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文检验了两种经典时间机器度规——Ori (2005) 的紧致真空核度规和Ahmed (2018) 的Misner空间四维推广——在扩展引力理论 $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m},\Phi,X)$ 中是否仍为精确解。结果表明，在所选模型下，两种度规均满足修正场方程，且时间序破坏区域持续存在，表明标量自由度并未触发时序保护机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为检验新近提出的 $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m},\Phi,X)$ 引力理论中是否会出现时序保护（chronology protection）机制，即额外标量自由度能否消除经典时间机器度规中的闭合类时曲线（closed timelike curves, CTCs），从而维护因果性。

Method: 选取显式模型 $f = R + \mathcal{L}_{m} + (λ/2)\,X$ 并取标量势为零，对Ori度规和Ahmed度规计算曲率不变量（curvature invariants）、修正场方程及有效应力-能量分量，采用调和谐波标量剖面 $\Phi(x,y) = a(x^{2}-y^{2})/2$。

Result: 里奇标量（Ricci scalar）在Ori度规中为零，在Ahmed度规中满足 $R = e^{f}(f_{,xx}+f_{,yy})$；动能不变量（kinetic invariant）$X$ 在两种度规下分别为 $a^{2}(x^{2}+y^{2})$ 和 $a^{2}e^{f}(x^{2}+y^{2})$。两种度规均在各向异性物质源（anisotropic matter sources）下解出修正场方程，且时间序破坏区域 $g_{zz}<0$（Ori）与 $g_{ψψ}<0$（Ahmed）在修改后仍存在。

Conclusion: $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m},\Phi,X)$ 引力中的额外标量自由度在Ori和Ahmed两种时间机器背景下均未强制执行时序保护机制。该结论与Li时间机器的平行结果一致，为非全局双曲（non-globally-hyperbolic）设定中标量扩展修正引力提供了自洽性检验。

Abstract: We ask whether two classical time-machine geometries, the Ori (2005) compact-vacuum-core metric and the Ahmed (2018) four-dimensional generalisation of Misner space, remain admissible exact solutions when the gravitational sector is enlarged to the recently proposed $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m},Φ,X)$ class, an extension of $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m})$ that couples curvature, the matter Lagrangian density, a scalar field $Φ$, and its kinetic invariant $X = g^{μν}\nabla_μΦ\nabla_νΦ$. Working with the explicit model $f = R + \mathcal{L}_{m} + (λ/2)\,X$ and a vanishing scalar potential, we compute the curvature invariants, the modified field equations, and the effective stress-energy components produced by the harmonic scalar profile $Φ(x,y) = a(x^{2}-y^{2})/2$ in both backgrounds. The Ricci scalar vanishes for the Ori metric and obeys $R = e^{f}(f_{,xx}+f_{,yy})$ for the Ahmed metric; the kinetic invariant takes the explicit forms $X = a^{2}(x^{2}+y^{2})$ and $X = a^{2}e^{f}(x^{2}+y^{2})$, respectively. Both metrics solve the field equations of the modified theory with anisotropic matter sources, and the chronology-violating regions $g_{zz}<0$ (Ori) and $g_{ψψ}<0$ (Ahmed) survive the modification. Energy-density profiles measured by a closed-timelike-curve observer match those measured by a static observer outside the chronology horizon, so the additional scalar degree of freedom in $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{m},Φ,X)$ gravity does not enforce a chronology-protection mechanism in either background. The conclusion mirrors the parallel result for the Li time-machine and supplies a consistency test for scalar-extended modified gravity in non-globally-hyperbolic settings.

### [83] [Canonical quantization of massive vector field in Schwarzschild black hole background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27047)
*Chandra Prakash,Rajesh Karmakar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对 Schwarzschild 时空背景下的大质量矢量场（Proca 场）进行了第一性原理正则量子化，通过 Dirac 括号机制处理约束，定义了 Boulware、Unruh 和 Hartle-Hawking 三种真空态，推导了霍金辐射谱，并数值计算了三种真空下的 Proca 凝聚体（condensate），发现其在未来视界边界附近显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 Schwarzschild 背景下，标量场、费米子场和电磁场的量子化已有充分研究，但 Proca 场因纵向极化模（longitudinal polarization mode）的物理性质及场变量的约束动力学（constrained dynamics）需要更精细的处理，目前尚缺乏系统的第一性原理量子化框架。

Method: 采用 Dirac 括号机制（Dirac bracket formalism）处理 Proca 作用量中的约束，构建产生湮灭算符的对易子代数；随后定义 Boulware、Unruh 和 Hartle-Hawking 三种真空态；基于 Unruh 真空推导霍金辐射谱；利用两点关联函数 $\langle A_\mu(x) A_\nu(x') \rangle$ 数值计算三种真空态下的 Proca 凝聚体。

Result: Proca 凝聚体在未来视界（future horizon）边界附近变得显著；不同极化模之间的相互作用以及 Proca 质量对量子可观测量的影响得以揭示。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了 Schwarzschild 背景下 Proca 场量子化的自洽框架，表明 Proca 质量及其纵向模在黑洞量子效应中起重要作用，为未来进一步研究大质量矢量场在弯曲时空中的量子现象奠定了基础。

Abstract: We perform a first-principles canonical quantization of a massive vector field, often referred to as the Proca field, in a Schwarzschild spacetime background. While scalar, fermionic, and electromagnetic fields are well studied in this context, the Proca field requires a more nuanced treatment because of the physical nature of the longitudinal polarization mode and the constrained dynamics of the field variables. By implementing the Dirac bracket formalism to treat the constraints inherent in the Proca action, we derive a consistent framework for the commutator algebra of creation and annihilation operators. Following this construction, we define the usual Boulware, Unruh, and Hartle-Hawking vacua. Using the Unruh vacuum, we derive and analyze the Hawking spectrum of the Proca field. Furthermore, we numerically evaluate the Proca condensate constructed from the two-point correlation function $\langle A_μ(x) A_ν(x') \rangle$, defined on all three vacuum states. We find that the condensate becomes significant near the boundary of the future horizon. Our results highlight the interplay among the different polarization modes and the significance of the Proca mass in quantum observables.

### [85] [Diffeomorphism-Like Symmetry in Gravitoelectromagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27125)
*L. A. S. Evangelista,A. F. Santos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Weyl形式论下研究引力电磁学（gravitoelectromagnetism, GEM），通过受限规范对称性分析张量场A_{μν}，导出并分解了GEM场的传播子（propagator），指出仅自旋-2和标量自旋-0分量贡献物理过程。研究表明，Lorentz型规范条件与受限规范对称性一致，而de Donder规范会引入残余规范依赖的标量贡献。该规范对称性可扩展至费米子和电磁扇区，相应的守恒流与能量-动量张量一致，验证了Ward恒等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于通过Weyl形式论（Weyl formalism）深入分析引力电磁学（GEM）的规范对称结构及其动力学行为，明确不同自旋分量的物理贡献，并检验不同规范固定条件对理论一致性的影响。

Method: 采用受限规范对称性（restricted gauge symmetry）作用于张量场A_{μν}；利用Barnes–Rivers形式论（Barnes–Rivers formalism）显式推导并分解GEM场的传播子；通过耦合到守恒源（conserved sources）分析不同自旋扇区的物理贡献；考虑Lorentz型与de Donder型规范条件进行规范固定分析；将规范对称性扩展至费米子和电磁扇区，导出守恒流并验证Ward恒等式（Ward identities）。

Result: 传播子分解后显示自旋-2、自旋-1和标量自旋-0三个扇区，但耦合守恒源后仅自旋-2和标量扇区贡献物理过程，自旋-1分量退耦（decouple）。有效传播子可写成紧致的度规形式，与线性化广义相对论（linearized General Relativity）的引力子传播子高度相似。Lorentz型规范与受限规范对称性相容且振幅规范无关；de Donder规范则残留规范依赖的标量贡献。扩展至费米子和电磁扇区后，守恒流恰好对应各自的能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor），表明GEM场与物质的耦合方式同线性化引力一致。Ward恒等式得到验证。

Conclusion: Weyl形式论下的GEM理论通过受限规范对称性实现了与线性化广义相对论一致的物理内容，但需注意规范选择对理论自洽性的影响——Lorentz型规范是合适的选择，而de Donder规范因残留标量贡献而不兼容。该理论在与物质耦合方面与线性化引力等价，Ward恒等式进一步确认了其规范结构的一致性。

Abstract: Gravitoelectromagnetism in the Weyl formalism is investigated through an analysis of the consequences of a restricted gauge symmetry acting on the tensor field $A_{μν}$. The propagator associated with the GEM field is explicitly derived and decomposed within the Barnes--Rivers formalism, revealing contributions from the spin-2, spin-1, and scalar spin-0 sectors. By coupling the theory to conserved sources, it is shown that only the spin-2 and scalar sectors contribute to physical processes, while the spin-1 component decouples. The resulting effective propagator can then be written in a compact metric form closely resembling the graviton propagator of linearized General Relativity. The role of gauge fixing is also analyzed by considering both Lorentz-like and de Donder-type gauge conditions. It is shown that the Lorentz-like gauge is consistent with the restricted gauge symmetry of the theory and leads to gauge-independent physical amplitudes, whereas the de Donder gauge introduces residual gauge-dependent scalar contributions, signaling an incompatibility with the underlying symmetry structure. The gauge symmetry is further extended to the fermionic and electromagnetic sectors through diffeomorphism-like transformations. In both cases, conserved currents are derived and shown to coincide with the corresponding energy-momentum tensors, implying that the GEM field couples to matter in the same manner as in linearized gravity. Finally, the associated Ward identities are verified, providing a nontrivial consistency check of the gauge structure and interaction vertices of the theory.

</details>


### [86] [Hybrid Expansion Cosmology in f(T) Gravity: Late-Time Evolution and Observational Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27196)
*Rajalakshmi Jena,Vishal M C,Sankarsan Tarai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在teleparallel引力框架下，采用指数型f(T)函数形式，通过混合尺度因子建模宇宙从早期减速到当前加速膨胀的平滑过渡，并利用31个哈勃数据点约束模型参数。分析表明模型物质-能量密度和压力演化与观测一致，诊断分析确认模型处于quintessence区域并渐近趋近ΛCDM情景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在teleparallel引力（teleparallel gravity）框架下，研究加速膨胀宇宙的宇宙学动力学（cosmological dynamics），探索指数型f(T)泛函形式能否描述宇宙从早期减速到当前加速膨胀的平滑过渡。

Method: 采用混合尺度因子（hybrid scale factor）建模宇宙演化阶段转换；运用指数型f(T)泛函形式在teleparallel引力框架下求解精确宇宙学解；通过经典能量条件（classical energy conditions）和宇宙学参数（cosmographic parameters）分析模型的物理一致性；利用31个哈勃数据点（Hubble data points）对模型参数进行约束。

Result: 约束后的模型给出的物质-能量密度（matter-energy density）和压力演化与观测到的宇宙加速膨胀一致；诊断分析表明模型处于quintessence regime（quintessence区域）并渐近趋近ΛCDM情景（ΛCDM scenario）。

Conclusion: 在teleparallel引力框架下，指数型f(T)模型能够有效描述宇宙从减速到加速膨胀的动力学演化，其行为在quintessence区域且最终趋近于ΛCDM模型，表明该模型在宇宙学上具有物理合理性。

Abstract: This study investigates the cosmological dynamics of an accelerating universe within the framework of teleparallel gravity using an exponential f(T) functional form. To obtain exact cosmological solutions, a hybrid scale factor is employed to model the smooth transition from an early decelerated phase to the present accelerated expansion of the Universe. The physical consistency of the model is analyzed through classical energy conditions and cosmographic parameters. By constraining the model parameters using 31 Hubble data points, we find that the resulting matter-energy density and pressure evolution remain consistent with the observed cosmic acceleration. Diagnostic analysis confirms that the model remains within the quintessence regime and asymptotically approaches the ΛCDM scenario.

</details>

Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,Z. Zhu,D. Z. Zieba,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: GWTC-5.0 是 LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA 合作组发布的第五版引力波瞬变目录，包含了截至 2025 年 1 月 28 日第四次观测运行第二阶段的观测数据，将已探测到的黑洞与中子星并合双星系统数量显著提升至超过 300 个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展已有的引力波瞬变目录（Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog），将第四次 LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA 联合观测运行后半段的数据纳入其中，以持续追踪和记录引力波信号候选体。

Method: 通过 LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA 探测器收集引力波数据，识别短时标（瞬变）引力波信号，并利用观测数据推断信号源的属性（如到达时间、振幅及源的性质）。

Result: GWTC-5.0 将已探测到的黑洞与中子星并合双星系统的数量显著增加至超过 300 个，为后续研究提供了更为丰富的样本。

Conclusion: 该目录及其配套文章为理解引力波宇宙提供了关键数据和方法文档，支持大量后续研究，包括事件目录总结、源总体的观测测量以及特定候选体的详细讨论。

Abstract: The Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC) is a collection of short-duration (transient) gravitational-wave signals identified by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration in gravitational-wave data produced by the eponymous detectors. The catalog provides information about the identified candidates, such as the arrival time and amplitude of the signal and properties of the signal's source as inferred from the observational data. GWTC is the release of this dataset and version 5.0 extends the catalog to include observations made during the second part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run up until 2025 January 28. This paper marks an introduction to a collection of articles related to this version of the catalog, GWTC-5.0. This update significantly increases the number of detected merging binary systems of black holes and neutron stars to over 300, enabling many follow-up studies toward understanding the gravitational-wave universe. The collection of articles accompanying the catalog provides documentation of the methods used to analyze the data, summaries of the catalog of events, observational measurements drawn from the population, and detailed discussions of selected candidates.

</details>


### [88] [GWTC-5.0: Methods for Identifying and Characterizing Gravitational-wave Transients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27224)
*The LIGO Scientific Collaboration,the Virgo Collaboration,the KAGRA Collaboration*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统描述了LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组第五版引力波瞬变源目录（GWTC-5.0）所使用的分析方法，重点涵盖信号建模、瞬变识别、数据质量评估、参数推断、波形模型比较以及大规模结果处理等环节，聚焦于第四次观测运行后半段的数据分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波瞬变源目录（GWTC）的构建需要复杂且多样的分析方法，随着观测运行（observing run）的推进，有必要系统性地记录和更新这些方法，以确保目录的科学可重复性和可靠性。本文旨在为GWTC-5.0所采用的方法提供详尽的技术描述，聚焦第四次观测运行（O4）后半段的处理流程。

Method: 本文所描述的方法涵盖从原始探测器数据到最终目录产出的完整分析管线（analysis pipeline），包括：信号建模（signal modeling）、瞬变识别（transient identification）、数据质量评估与仪器问题缓解、参数推断（parameter inference）、波形模型（waveform model）与数据的比较，以及大规模分析结果的整合与处理。

Result: 本文作为方法学描述性论文，主要输出为对GWTC-5.0分析流程的系统性技术记录，而非新物理结果。其核心贡献在于明确了第五版目录所采用的分析方法与数据处理策略。

Conclusion: 该文为GWTC-5.0目录的使用者提供了必需的方法学基础，确保了目录中候选引力波瞬变信号的分析流程具备透明性和可追溯性，为后续天体物理研究提供了可靠的技术参照。

Abstract: The Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC) is a collection of candidate gravitational-wave transient signals identified and characterized by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration. Producing the contents of the GWTC from detector data requires complex analysis methods. These comprise techniques to model the signal; identify the transients in the data; evaluate the quality of the data and mitigate possible instrumental issues; infer the parameters of each transient; compare the data with the waveform models for compact binary coalescences, and handle the large amount of results associated with all these different analyses. In this paper, we describe the methods employed to produce the catalog's fifth release, GWTC-5.0, focusing on the analysis of the second part of the fourth observing run of LIGO, Virgo and KAGRA.

</details>


### [89] [GWTC-5.0: Observations from the Second Part of the Fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Observing Run and Updates to the Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27225)
*The LIGO Scientific Collaboration,the Virgo Collaboration,the KAGRA Collaboration*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: GWTC-5.0目录新增了LIGO、Virgo和KAGRA在O4b运行期间探测到的150个紧凑双星并合候选体，其中103个具有详细的源属性测量。目录中双黑洞的质量范围从5.14M⊙到70M⊙，首次发现网络信噪比超过70的双黑洞信号，累计GWTC候选体总数达到390个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LIGO、Virgo和KAGRA引力波观测站第四次观测运行后半段（O4b）及前期工程运行数据的积累，为更新引力波瞬变源目录、扩展对引力波宇宙的认知提供了新的数据基础。

Method: 使用至少一种搜索算法筛选出天体物理起源概率p_astro ≥ 0.5且未在事件验证中被拒绝的候选体，并选择误报率（false-alarm rate）< 1yr⁻¹的候选体进行详细的源属性测量。

Result: 新增150个紧凑双星并合候选体，其中103个具有详细源属性测量；双黑洞质量中值范围为5.14M⊙至70M⊙；首次探测到网络信噪比（network signal-to-noise ratio）超过70的双黑洞信号GW250114_082203；累计GWTC瞬变源总数达390个。

Conclusion: 所有新增候选体均与双黑洞（binary black hole）信号一致，未发现双中子星（binary neutron star）或中子星-黑洞双星（neutron star-black hole binary）。高信噪比事件GW250114_082203为高保真度研究天体物理性质及检验广义相对论（general relativity）提供了新机遇，进一步扩展了引力波目录的规模和我们对引力波宇宙的认知。

Abstract: Version 5.0 of the Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-5.0) adds new candidates detected by the LIGO, Virgo, and KAGRA observatories through the second part of the fourth observing run (O4b: 2024 April 10 15:00:00 to 2025 January 28 17:00:00 UTC) and a preceding engineering run. In these new data, we find 150 compact binary coalescence candidates that are identified by at least one of our search algorithms with a probability of astrophysical origin $p_\mathrm{astro} \geq 0.5$ and that are not vetoed during event validation. We also provide detailed source property measurements for 103 of these that have a false-alarm rate < 1yr$^{-1}$. Based on the inferred component masses, these candidates are consistent with signals from binary black holes without binary neutron stars or neutron star-black hole binaries. Median inferred component masses of binary black holes in the catalog now range from 5.14$M_\odot$ (GW241109_115924) to 70$M_\odot$ (GW241116_151753). For the first time, we have discovered binary black hole signals with network signal-to-noise ratio exceeding 70, GW250114_082203, enabling high-fidelity studies of the astrophysical properties of these systems and test of general relativity. Together with updated 139 candidates up to the first part of the fourth observing run, this brings the total number of transients in the cumulative GWTC to 390, which fulfills the criteria of $p_\mathrm{astro} \geq 0.5$, further expanding the size of the catalog and our view of the gravitational-wave Universe.

</details>


### [90] [Strong-lensing degeneracies of black holes embedded in self-interacting scalar field dark matter halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27242)
*Mohsen Fathi,Gabriel Gómez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过爱因斯坦星团（Einstein cluster）形式，数值重建了嵌入自相互作用标量场暗物质晕（self-interacting scalar field dark matter halo）及NFW暗物质晕中的黑洞时空几何，系统分析了强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）观测量的行为。结果表明，相较于纯Schwarzschild黑洞，暗物质晕造成的偏差约为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$量级，导致模型间存在强观测简并（observational degeneracy）；其中相对论图像间的时间延迟（time delay）为最敏感的暗物质探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质晕（dark matter halo）对黑洞周围强引力透镜效应的影响，并比较自相互作用标量场暗物质晕与NFW型暗物质晕两种典型构型。其核心动机在于检验强引力透镜观测是否能够区分黑洞周围不同类型的暗物质分布。

Method: 首先通过爱因斯坦星团（Einstein cluster）形式数值重构嵌入暗物质晕中的黑洞时空几何，进而分析光子轨迹的有效函数，计算光子球半径（photon sphere radius）与临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）。在此基础上，研究多种强透镜观测量，包括相对论爱因斯坦环（relativistic Einstein rings）、有限阶像位置（finite-order image positions）、像间距（image separations）、放大率（magnifications）及时间延迟（time delays），并以超大质量黑洞M87*和Sgr A*为具体案例进行数值分析。

Result: 暗物质晕构型相对于纯Schwarzschild情形产生的偏差约为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$量级或更小，导致不同模型间的强透镜观测量表现出强烈的简并性（degeneracy）。然而，时间延迟（time delay）相对论图像中出现了小但系统性的差异，对于超大质量黑洞，该观测量最为明显地放大了暗物质晕的修正效应。

Conclusion: 标准强引力透镜观测量在暗物质晕环境下具有很高的鲁棒性（robustness），难以区分不同的暗物质分布模型；而时域特征（time-domain signatures），尤其是相对论图像间的时间延迟，可能成为探测黑洞周围暗物质效应的更有前景的途径。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore the strong gravitational lensing properties of black holes embedded in self-interacting scalar field dark matter halos, together with NFW-type configurations for comparison. The corresponding spacetime geometry is reconstructed numerically through the Einstein cluster formalism, allowing us to study how the surrounding dark matter distribution affects the propagation of photons near the black hole. We first analyze the effective function governing photon trajectories and calculate the corresponding photon sphere radius and critical impact parameter. We then investigate different strong-lensing observables, including relativistic Einstein rings, finite-order image positions, image separations, magnifications, and time delays, with particular attention to the supermassive black holes M87* and Sgr A*. Our results show that the considered halo configurations produce only small deviations with respect to the Schwarzschild case, typically at the level of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$ or smaller, leading to a strong observational degeneracy among the models. Nevertheless, small but systematic differences remain present, especially in the time delay between relativistic images, which provides the clearest amplification of the halo-induced corrections for very massive black holes. These results suggest that, although standard strong-lensing observables remain highly robust against the considered halo environments, time-domain signatures may offer a more promising way to probe the effect of dark matter surrounding black holes.

</details>


### [91] [Reconstructing the cosmic expansion in $f(R, L_{m})$ gravity via parametrized Hubble function constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27324)
*Khomesh R. Patle,G. P. Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 $f(R, L_{m})$ 引力框架下，采用具体函数形式 $f(R, L_{m}) = \frac{R}{2} + L_{m}^λ$，构建了三个新的宇宙学模型。通过贝叶斯方法（Bayesian methods）结合 $\chi^{2}$ 最小化技术，利用宇宙时计（CC）数据集和联合数据集（CC+Pantheon）约束模型参数，系统分析了减速参数、能量密度、压强、状态方程参数、能量条件、状态发现诊断以及热力学性质，模型预测的宇宙年龄与晚期天文观测高度一致。

Method: 选用 $f(R, L_{m}) = \frac{R}{2} + L_{m}^λ$ 的函数形式，构造三个以红移相关哈勃参数 $H(z)$ 表达的宇宙学模型；采用基于 $\chi^{2}$ 最小化技术的贝叶斯方法，分别使用宇宙时计（CC）和联合（CC+Pantheon）数据集确定模型参数的中位值。

Result: 确定了模型参数在两类数据约束下的中位值；系统分析了减速参数、能量密度、压强、状态方程参数、能量条件及状态发现诊断（statefinder diagnostic）的行为；验证了模型在温度与熵密度演化方面的热力学可行性（thermodynamic viability）；模型预测的宇宙年龄与晚期天文观测吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所提出的 $f(R, L_{m})$ 宇宙学模型能够较好地描述宇宙膨胀历史，满足热力学自洽性，且与晚期天文观测数据一致，表明该框架在解释当前宇宙演化方面具有潜在有效性。

Abstract: We probe the cosmic expansion scenario within the framework of $f(R, L_{m})$ gravity by employing a well-motivated functional form of $f(R, L_{m}) = \frac{R}{2} + L_{m}^λ$. Specifically, we introduce three novel cosmological models formulated in terms of the redshift-dependent Hubble parameter $H(z)$, offering deeper insights into the underlying cosmic dynamics. The models are further utilized to investigate the expansion history of the universe and the evolution of several cosmological parameters. By using the Bayesian methods based on the $χ^{2}$-minimization technique, the median values of the model parameters are determined for the cosmic chronometer (CC) and joint (CC+Pantheon) datasets. A comprehensive study of the deceleration parameter, energy density, pressure and the equation of state parameter is carried out to understand the universe's evolution. Additionally, the validity of the energy conditions and the behavior of the statefinder diagnostic are thoroughly examined. Finally, the thermodynamic viability of the models is confirmed through the evolution of temperature and entropy density, and the estimated age of the universe further exemplifies good agreement with late-time astronomical observations.

### [92] [Vertex operator algebras, partition functions and Teichmüller modular forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26972)

Method: 论文采用几何化方法，将每个全纯顶点算子代数与任意亏格曲线模空间上的一个霍奇线丛幂次截面——即 Teichmüller 模形式——进行显式关联。该方法基于二维共形场论中已知的几何框架，并将其系统拓展至一般亏格情形。

Result: 论文的主要成果是建立了一个从全纯顶点算子代数到任意亏格 Teichmüller 模形式的标准构造。这一构造将模空间几何与顶点代数分类问题建立了直接联系，并指出可以利用全纯顶点代数理论获得模空间的新结果。

Conclusion: 论文表明，全纯顶点算子代数与曲线模空间上的 Teichmüller 模形式之间存在系统性对应关系。这一关系不仅为顶点代数分类提供了几何工具，也为模空间研究带来了代数方法的潜力。最后部分展示了如何利用这些模形式逆向重建顶点代数。

Abstract: In the spirit of the geometric approach to two-dimensional conformal field theory, we explicitly associate to every holomorphic vertex operator algebra a section of a power of Hodge line bundle on the moduli space of curves of arbitrary genus - or equivalently a Teichmüller modular form in any genus. As a first application, we connect the geometry of the moduli space of curves to the classification program for holomorphic vertex algebras. We then discuss how to use the theory of holomorphic vertex algebras to reach new results about the moduli space of curves. In the last part of the paper we study how the above mentioned forms can be used to reconstruct the vertex algebra.

### [93] [Competition between pair and single-particle superfluidity in bosonic quasi-flat bands: A Gaussian state approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26231)
*Maxime Burgher,Simon Loddo,Laurens Vanderstraeten,Nathan Goldman,Ivan Amelio*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过变分高斯态方法研究了一维准平带模型，揭示了从对超流到单粒子超流的相变，并建立了声速与“量子几何核”之间的普适关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解相互作用与量子几何之间的竞争如何驱动弱色散玻色子进入不同的多体超流相，尤其是在准平带（quasi flat-band）体系中，对超流（pair superfluid）与单粒子超流（single-particle superfluid）之间的转变机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用变分高斯态（variational Gaussian state）方法统一描述单粒子和对超流相的基态波函数（ground state wavefunction）与集体激发谱（collective excitation spectrum）；结合双玻色子问题（two-boson problem）与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）确定完整相图。

Result: 在全平带极限下系统呈现扩展的对超流相；引入单粒子跃迁后，对超流相在有限跃迁强度范围内保持稳定，最终转变为常规单粒子超流相；推导出声速与“量子几何核”（quantum geometric kernel）之间的普适关系，推广了以往基于单粒子平均场理论建立的量子度量（quantum metric）联系。

Conclusion: 高斯态方法是研究多轨道晶格中相互作用玻色子各类超流相的通用工具；所建立的声速-量子几何核关系为理解超流性质与量子几何的深层关联提供了新框架。

Abstract: The interplay between interactions and quantum geometry can drive weakly dispersive bosons into different exotic many-body phases. In this work we study a quasi flat-band model in one dimension that exhibits an extended pair-superfluid phase in the all-flat-band limit. Introducing single-particle hopping leads to an intriguing competition with a more conventional single-particle superfluid: we find that the pair superfluid remains stable for a finite range of the hopping strength until the system eventually transitions into the conventional superfluid phase. In our study, we make use of a variational Gaussian state approach that provides a unified description of the single-particle and pair superfluid phases, regarding both the ground state wavefunction and the collective excitation spectrum. In particular, we derive a general relation between the speed of sound and a ``quantum geometric kernel'', thereby extending earlier connections to the quantum metric, which relied on single-particle mean-field theory. This approach is combined with insights from the two-boson problem and exact diagonalization to map out the full phase diagram of the model. Our results show that the Gaussian approach is a versatile tool for studying a broad range of superfluid phases of interacting bosons in multi-orbital lattices.

### [94] [Extended Bose-Hubbard Model on Small Grids: Exact Diagonalization and Monte Carlo Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26303)
*Gabriele Costa,Matteo Ciardi,Fabio Cinti,Santi Prestipino*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过精确对角化和路径积分蒙特卡洛（path-integral Monte Carlo）模拟，研究了小型截断晶格（truncated lattices）上硬核玻色子的超流-绝缘体相变（superfluid-insulator transition）残余特征，发现有限尺寸系统与热力学极限下的行为既存在显著差异也有相似之处，即使在仅含5个粒子的连续系统中也观察到玻色-哈伯德（Bose-Hubbard）行为的迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超流-绝缘体相变在无限大晶格体系中已被充分研究，但在截断晶格（truncated lattices）中的残余特征（remnants of the transition）受到的关注较少。本文旨在探索在极小尺寸的晶格片段中，该相变是否仍有可辨识的特征。

Method: 在硬核极限（hard-core limit）下，对包含最多13个格点的小型正方形和三角形晶格上的扩展Bose-Hubbard模型进行精确对角化（exact diagonalization），绘制零温相图。接着，对束缚于光学晶格势阱中的少量连续（continuum）相互作用玻色子系统，采用路径积分蒙特卡洛（path-integral Monte Carlo）模拟，计算动能、势能、超流性（superfluidity）和交换环统计量（exchange-cycle statistics）。

Result: 精确对角化表明，有限尺寸系统的基态特征与热力学极限下的结果既有明显差异也有相似之处。蒙特卡洛模拟发现，即使在仅有5个粒子的系统中，也出现了Bose-Hubbard行为的迹象。

Conclusion: 在极小截断晶格和少量连续玻色子系统中，超流-绝缘体相变的残余特征依然可辨，且与无限体系的Bose-Hubbard模型行为存在关联。

Abstract: The superfluid-insulator transition in systems of lattice bosons is usually analyzed in the framework of the Bose-Hubbard model, and has been extensively studied by theory and simulations. Less attention has been paid to the remnants of the transition in truncated lattices, with or without periodic boundary conditions. Here we consider the hard-core limit of the extended Bose-Hubbard model on small square and triangular grids -- i.e., sections of the square and triangular lattices containing up to 13 sites. By mapping out the zero-temperature phase diagram through exact diagonalization, we find ground-state characteristics that are markedly different from those emerging in the thermodynamic limit, together with similarities. The dichotomy between superfluid-like and insulating-like behavior is then investigated in two-dimensional systems of a few interacting bosons in the continuum, subject to confining and optical-lattice potentials mimicking the $3\times 3$ square grid. Using path-integral Monte Carlo simulations, we compute kinetic and potential energies, as well as superfluidity and exchange-cycle statistics, finding hints of Bose-Hubbard behavior even in systems of just five particles.

</details>

Result: 调制不稳定性主要由吸引与排斥平均场相互作用之间的竞争主导；谐振束缚会改变稳定区间，增加凝聚体对SOC诱导不对称性以及组分内与组分间相互作用的敏感性。

A linearized GP equation is used to investigate modulation instability (MI), demonstrating the impact of strong coupling effects and anisotropic confinement on the instability dynamics. It has been shown that the modulation instability in the condensate is predominantly governed by the competition between the attractive and repulsive mean-field interactions. Additionally, stability regimes are altered by the harmonic confinement, enhancing their susceptibility to SOC-induced asymmetry and intra- and intercomponent interactions. ### [97] [Quantum Resistance Paradox of Low-Dimensional Superfluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27356)
*Simon Wili,Meng-Zi Huang,Tommaso Bonaccorsi,Michael Mühlematter,Mohsen Talebi,Yaakov Yudkin,Alex Gómez-Salvador,Filip Marijanovic,Eugene Demler,Tilman Esslinger*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过在无缺陷统一费米气体中利用数字可编程输运几何结构，实验研究了超流耗散从一维（1D）到二维（2D）的维度交叉，发现通道宽度增大时电阻反而出现最小值，揭示了耗散机制从相滑移（phase slip）到涡旋（vortex）的转变，并在超过十个数量级的范围内验证了Langer-Ambegaokar-McCumber-Halperin理论的指数标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解一维到二维维度交叉（dimensional crossover）过程中电阻和耗散如何演化，是凝聚态物理中的一个开放问题，但在固态实验中受无序、杂质和几何缺陷的干扰而难以研究，同时理论上因竞争性耗散过程和显著的有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）而面临挑战。

Method: 采用无缺陷的统一费米气体（unitary Fermi gas）作为清洁体系，结合数字可编程输运几何结构来隔离几何效应对超流耗散的影响，分别在准一维和准二维通道中测量耗散行为，并与Langer-Ambegaokar-McCumber-Halperin相滑移理论及有限尺寸涡旋模型进行对比。

Result: 在从一维到二维的交叉中，电阻达到一个最小值；增加通道宽度反而导致电阻增大。窄的准一维通道中耗散符合Langer-Ambegaokar-McCumber-Halperin相滑移理论，通道宽度变化时活化因子的指数标度在超过十个数量级的范围内得到验证。宽的准二维通道中耗散与有限尺寸涡旋模型一致。维度交叉处的最小耗散反映了主导耗散机制从相滑移向涡旋的转变，两种机制同时被抑制。

Conclusion: 测量结果表明，通过控制几何维度可以有效抑制超流耗散，为最小化超导器件中的耗散提供了一条可能路径，并为描述维度交叉的理论工作提供了基准。

Abstract: Resistance in standard conductors decreases with increasing cross-section. Yet, in low-dimensional superconductors and superfluids residual resistance arises from topological fluctuations of the order parameter manifesting as phase slips in one-dimensional (1D) and vortices in two-dimensional (2D) systems. How resistance and dissipation evolve as geometry interpolates between these regimes remains an open question. This evolution is masked in solid-state experiments by disorder, impurities, and geometric imperfections, and poses theoretical challenges due to competing dissipative processes and pronounced finite-size effects. Here, we use a defect-free unitary Fermi gas in a digitally programmable transport geometry to isolate geometric effects on superfluid dissipation and discover a paradox: in the crossover from 1D to 2D, the resistance reaches a minimum. There, widening a channel increases its resistance. Narrower, quasi-1D channels show dissipation described by Langer-Ambegaokar-McCumber-Halperin theory of phase slips. In this regime, varying the channel width yields the predicted exponential scaling of the activation factor over more than ten orders of magnitude. Wider, quasi-2D channels show dissipation consistent with a finite-size vortex model. The minimal dissipation in the dimensional crossover reflects a transition in the dominant dissipative mechanism, with both phase slips and vortices simultaneously suppressed. Our measurements suggest a route to minimizing dissipation in superconducting devices and provide a benchmark for theoretical efforts aimed at describing the dimensional crossover.

</details>

### [98] [AutoDFT: A Closed-Loop Multi-Agent Framework for Autonomous DFT Calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26179)
*Penghui Yang,Zhonghan Zhang,Yue Li,Xinrun Wag,Yanchen Deng,Yuhao Lu,Bijun Tang,Zheng Liu,Bo An*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出AutoDFT，一种闭环多智能体框架（closed-loop multi-agent framework），将大语言模型（LLM）嵌入密度泛函理论（DFT）计算的每个阶段，通过战略规划、即时步骤规划与监控-恢复-反思循环，替代传统人工调试和仅初始规划的方法，在34项任务的VASPBench上实现94.1%的成功率，并能可靠预测电子、磁性和能量性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体仅自动化DFT计算的初始规划阶段，生成完整执行计划后便依赖人工预设规则处理后续调整，导致工作流程脆弱、泛化能力差，在收敛失败、出现意外物理现象或中间结果改变问题时仍需专家介入。

Method: AutoDFT采用闭环多智能体架构：战略规划器（strategic planner）生成步骤目标骨架计划；步骤规划器（step planner）根据前序结果即时生成数值参数；监控-恢复-反思循环（monitor-recover-reflect cycle）诊断故障、修复问题并在证据充分时修订计划。

Result: 在自建的VASPBench基准（涵盖34项任务、9种DFT计算类型）上，AutoDFT结合GPT-5.2达到94.1%的任务级成功率；在已有材料数据库上，对电子、磁性和能量性质给出定量可靠的预测结果。

Conclusion: 通过闭合规划与执行之间的回路，AutoDFT使不具备深厚计算专业知识的实验研究者也能获得可靠的第一性原理（first-principles）计算结果。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) serves as the basis for computational discovery in materials science and chemistry, yet each calculation demands extensive human effort: adjusting algorithms when convergence stalls, revising plans when unexpected physics emerges, and inserting steps as intermediate results reshape the problem. Existing LLM-based agents automate only the initial planning stage, producing a full execution plan upfront and leaving all subsequent adaptation to hand-crafted rules. As a result, these workflows remain fragile, do not generalize well beyond pre-planned scenarios, and often require expert intervention when failures or unexpected intermediate results require changes to the calculation path. Here, we introduce AutoDFT, a closed-loop multi-agent framework that embeds LLM reasoning into every stage of the DFT lifecycle, where a strategic planner produces a skeletal plan of step objectives; a step planner generates numerical parameters just in time from preceding results; and a monitor-recover-reflect cycle diagnoses failures, repairs them, and revises the plan when the evidence justifies it. We demonstrate both breadth and depth: breadth on VASPBench, a purpose-built benchmark spanning 34 tasks and 9 DFT calculation types, where AutoDFT achieves 94.1% task-level success with GPT-5.2; and depth on established materials databases, where AutoDFT produces quantitatively reliable property predictions across electronic, magnetic, and energetic properties. By closing the loop between planning and execution, AutoDFT enables experimentalists without deep computational expertise to obtain reliable first-principles results.

</details>

Abstract: Compound-refractive lenses (CRL) are a type of x-ray optics that find widespread applications as focusing and imaging lenses. The choice of material is one of the most defining properties of these lenses. In this work, we present a CRL made out of diamond. It provides an advantageous balance between refractivity and absorption, along with good manufacturability. Compared to Be CRLs, it features a higher optical density and thus enables application at higher photon energies without relying on large lens stacks or very small radii of curvature, which are challenging to manufacture. A diamond CRL is characterized for use as an objective for Dark-field X-ray Microscopy (DFXM) at the ID03 beamline of the European Synchrotron Radiation Facility (ESRF) and compared to Al and Be CRLs at 17 keV, 33 keV and 37 keV. Increasing the photon energy in DFXM from 17 keV to 37 keV opens up the possibility to investigate new sample systems, that were previously opaque to low energy x-ray radiation. The capability of the diamond CRL at 33 keV is illustrated through DFXM measurements on two 0.5 mm-thick iron-based samples, which cannot be probed at 17 keV.

Method: 使用60 MeV ³⁵Cl离子束对高度取向热解石墨（HOPG）和多层还原氧化石墨烯（ML-rGO）进行辐照，注量分别为5.11×10⁹和1.3×10¹⁰ ions/cm²。采用X射线衍射（XRD）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）、扫描电子显微镜（SEM）、原子力显微镜（AFM）及电输运测量对样品进行表征。

The results show that the irradiation response is strongly influenced by the initial structural organization of the material. In HOPG, ion exposure leads to a progressive loss of crystalline order, evidenced by XRD peak broadening and an increase in the Raman ID/IG ratio, accompanied by a reduction in electrical transport performance. In contrast, ML-rGO exhibits distinct behavior at higher fluences, suggesting partial structural reorganization. The appearance of more defined graphitic features in XRD and Raman analyses, along with changes in surface morphology and electrical response, suggests the formation of more ordered sp2 domains. These findings indicate that irradiation effects vary with the initial degree of order, providing useful insights for selecting carbon-based materials for devices operating under severe radiation conditions.

### [101] [Finite Temperature Stacking Fault Stability in Random and Locally Ordered CoCrNi beyond the Harmonic Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26364)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用近量子精度的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential）结合完全非简谐的投影平均力积分器（projected average force integrator），分别计算了随机固溶体（RSS）和局部化学有序（LCO）CoCrNi合金随温度变化的广义层错自由能（generalized stacking-fault free energy）。

Result: 非简谐计算显示，RSS的层错能（ISFE）随温度升高而降低，并始终为负，说明RSS层错在高温下无法被热稳定；而LCO在0–1000 K温度范围内保持正层错能。分子动力学模拟进一步证实，RSS CoCrNi中位错解离无界，而LCO状态下则呈现有限层错宽度。

Conclusion: RSS状态下CoCrNi的负层错能无法通过有限温度效应得到稳定，LCO才是维持正层错能并解释实验中有限层错宽度的关键因素。

Abstract: Previous density functional theory (DFT) calculations for random solid solution (RSS) CoCrNi predict negative intrinsic stacking-fault energy (ISFE) at 0 K, contrary to experimental observations of finite stacking-fault widths. Two explanations have been proposed: finite-temperature stabilization of the RSS state, suggested by harmonic approximations showing increasing ISFE with temperature, and local chemical order (LCO), which shifts the ISFE to positive values at 0 K. Here, we compute temperature-dependent generalized stacking-fault free energies for RSS and LCO CoCrNi using a near-quantum-accuracy machine learning interatomic potential and the fully anharmonic projected average force integrator. Unlike harmonic approximations, our anharmonic calculations show that the RSS ISFE decreases with temperature and remains negative, indicating that RSS stacking faults are not thermally stabilized at elevated temperatures. By contrast, LCO maintains positive ISFE over 0-1000 K. Molecular dynamics simulations further confirm unbounded dislocation dissociation in RSS CoCrNi but finite stacking-fault widths in the LCO state.

*Xinlin Xu,Junji Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段拓扑优化框架，通过基于高斯加权的选择函数实现多目标优化，在声子晶体带隙中精确设计缺陷态，同时吸引目标模式并排斥竞争模式，无需人工模式跟踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以系统解决在声子晶体（phononic crystals）带隙中同时吸引目标缺陷模式（defect mode）并排斥竞争模式（competing modes）的冲突目标，导致带隙内出现虚假谐振模式，限制了设计纯度。

Method: 提出两阶段拓扑优化框架（two-stage topology optimization framework）。第一阶段优化原胞（unit cell）拓扑以在目标频率周围形成宽带隙；第二阶段基于选择函数$S(ω)$（selection function with Gaussian weighting）和自适应σ参数设计多目标目标函数，动态平衡模式吸引与排斥，自动识别并吸引最合适的缺陷模式，无需手动模式跟踪。

Result: 数值实验表明，该框架成功生成了具有工程化缺陷态的声子晶体，在宽带隙内于指定频率处产生精确定位的局域谐振模式（localized resonant modes）。

Conclusion: 该工作为频率选择性滤波器和弹性波操控器件（frequency-selective filters and elastic wave manipulation devices）提供了一种系统化的设计方法。

Abstract: Phononic crystals enable precise manipulation of elastic wave propagation through engineered bandgaps; however, designing defect states within these bandgaps for frequency-selective applications remains a significant challenge. Existing design approaches, including prior optimization formulations, struggle to systematically resolve the competing objectives of attracting desired defect modes to target frequencies while simultaneously repelling unwanted modes from the bandgap region. This inability to suppress competing modes often results in spurious, undesired in-gap resonant modes, thereby limiting design purity. This paper presents a novel two-stage topology optimization framework that addresses this challenge through an innovative multi-objective formulation based on a selection function with Gaussian weighting. In the first stage, the unit cell topology is optimized to create a wide bandgap around a target frequency. In the second stage, a supercell containing a defect is optimized using a specially designed objective function that dynamically balances mode attraction and repulsion via a selection function $S(ω)$ with adaptive $σ$ parameters. This selection mechanism enables the optimizer to automatically identify and selectively attract the most suitable defect mode while repelling competing modes from the bandgap region, eliminating the need for manual mode tracking. Numerical examples demonstrate that the proposed framework successfully generates phononic crystals featuring engineered defect states that yield precisely positioned localized resonant modes at prescribed frequencies within wide bandgaps, with potential applications in frequency-selective filters and elastic wave manipulation devices.

### [103] [Structural Alter-Phononics: Sublattice-Momentum Locking in Spinless Lattice Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26453)
*Jing-Yang You,Zhen Zhang,Xianlei Sheng,Gang Su*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过晶体对称性分析，在非磁性晶体中识别出一种无自旋的“交变声子学”（alter-phononics）机制，其中声子本征模在等效子晶格上产生动量依赖的子晶格极化与频率分裂，建立了交变声子学作为交变磁（altermagnetism）的无自旋对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁（altermagnetism）的发现已表明晶格对称性能够在无净磁化条件下产生动量依赖的内部极化，但自旋自由度缺失的晶格振动（phonon）中是否存在类似的对称性组织的动量空间序仍悬而未决。

Method: 作者定义了子晶格分辨的动力学不对称性 $\Delta(\mathbf q)=D_{AA}(\mathbf q)-D_{BB}(\mathbf q)$ 作为核心量，并提出了交变生成器（alter-generator）的对称性规则：该生成器在转动波矢的同时映射等效子晶格，同时要求缺乏反演交换（inversion exchange）和小子群子晶格交换（little-group sublattice-exchange）约束。通过第一性原理计算在代表性非磁性晶体中验证了该机制。

Result: 对称性规则产生了向列型 d 波（nematic d-wave）、四方 d/g 波（tetragonal d/g-wave）和三部分六瓣（tripartite six-lobe）声子纹理。对称保持的结构畸变可通过移除滑移诱导的均分陷阱（equipartition trap）同时保留螺旋轴交变生成器，解锁隐藏的 $d_{x^2-y^2}$ 型纹理。该本征矢量纹理进一步被子晶格投影的电子-声子耦合和非简谐响应函数继承。

Conclusion: 结构交变声子学确立了作为交变磁动量空间序的无自旋对应物的地位，并在有限波矢声子谱和位移模式中提供了可实验检验的特征信号。

Abstract: The discovery of altermagnetism has shown that crystal symmetry can generate momentum-dependent internal polarization without net magnetization. Whether an analogous form of symmetry-organized momentum-space order can exist for spinless lattice vibrations remains unresolved. Here we identify a structural mechanism for $alter$-$phononics$, in which phonon eigenmodes formed from structurally equivalent sublattices acquire momentum-dependent sublattice polarization and frequency splitting in nonmagnetic crystals. The central quantity is the sublattice-resolved dynamical asymmetry $Δ(\mathbf q)=D_{AA}(\mathbf q)-D_{BB}(\mathbf q)$, which controls the associated eigenvector polarization. We show that this effect requires an alter-generator that maps equivalent sublattices onto one another while rotating the wave vector, together with the absence of inversion exchange and little-group sublattice-exchange constraints that would otherwise enforce sublattice equipartition. These symmetry rules generate nematic $d$-wave, tetragonal $d/g$-wave, and tripartite six-lobe phonon textures. First-principles calculations demonstrate the mechanism in representative nonmagnetic crystals and show how a symmetry-preserving structural distortion can unlock a hidden $d_{x^2-y^2}$-type texture by removing glide-induced equipartition traps while retaining the screw-axis alter-generator. We further show that the eigenvector texture is inherited by sublattice-projected electron-phonon coupling and anharmonic response functions. Our results establish structural alter-phononics as a spinless counterpart to altermagnetic momentum-space order and provide experimentally testable signatures in finite-$\mathbf q$ phonon spectra and displacement patterns.

Abstract: Twisted moire superlattices in van-der-Waals heterostructures provide a powerful platform for engineering correlated states through moire-band reconstruction. However, whether globally coherent electronic orders can be continuously manipulated at the nanoscale remains largely unexplored. Reconstructed moire structures in small-angle and near-commensurate regime feature continuously varying local environments, offering new opportunities for nanoscale manipulation of correlated phases. Here, we report the modulation of charge density wave (CDW) states in a twisted vortex moire superlattice formed between monolayer VTe2 and superconducting NbSe2. Scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy reveals that the intrinsic long-range CDW of monolayer VTe2 is reconstructed into inequivalent local phases with distinct stability and coherence within a single moire unit cell, including suppressed CDW order and enhanced short-range CDW correlations persisting to room temperature. First-principles calculations show that the reconstructed CDW landscape originates from strong local strain variation, where compressive strain substantially stabilizes the charge order. Furthermore, the modulated CDW states exhibit competing interplay with proximity-induced superconductivity. Our results establish vortex moire superlattices as a versatile platform for nanoscale manipulation of correlated electronic orders in low-dimensional quantum materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文通过理论分析，针对给定铁电层和介电层厚度，推导出畴壁能参数存在一个临界值（critical value），超过该临界值时系统可稳定在无畴负电容状态。

Conclusion: 为实现理想负电容，应从理论和实验两方面着手，通过高通量设计（high throughput design）、发现（discovery）和工程化（engineering）铁电材料的手段，全面理解并控制畴壁能（domain wall energy）。

Abstract: While negative capacitance has been demonstrated in ferroelectric-dielectric heterostructures in the form of capacitance enhancement, all experimental evidence, to date, suggests the existence of domains therein. Here, we address the question: what are the conditions to achieve ideal, domain-free negative capacitance in ferroelectric-dielectric heterostructures? Our main claim is that for given thicknesses of the ferroelectric and the dielectric layers, there is a critical value of domain wall energy parameter -- above which the system would be stabilized in an ideal and robust domain-free negative capacitance state and would be robust against domain formation. Our analyses suggest that to achieve ideal negative capacitance, efforts should lie in understanding the means to control the domain wall energy on all fronts, both theory and experiments via high throughput design, discovery, and engineering of ferroelectrics.

Abstract: Operando microscopy has unveiled key mechanistic insights in battery materials during early cycling, but long-term characterization to unveil material evolution, degradation, and failure remain limited. We image through-plane, bulk-representative electrodeposition behavior of aqueous tin metal anodes, which are promising due to their high energy density but whose reactivity limits practical cycle life. We show that substrate governs the morphology and stability of plated tin, particularly at high plated capacities. ### [108] [MatFormBench: A Benchmarking Evaluation Framework for Target-Driven Materials Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26741)
*Linhan Wu,Chenxi Wang,Chuhan Yang,Zhengwei Yang,Yuyang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 MatFormBench，一个面向目标驱动材料配方逆设计（inverse design）的统一基准生态系统，包含物理驱动的配方生成方案、五个难度等级以及多维度评价指标 MatFormScore。通过评估 39 种逆设计算法（涵盖代理辅助搜索、深度生成模型和基于大语言模型的策略），发现扩散模型（diffusion-based models）整体表现最优，变分自编码器（VAE）和遗传算法（GA）在特定场景下各具优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 MatFormBench 基准生态系统，包含：(1) 物理驱动的配方生成方案，生成忠实模拟真实材料结构-性能响应关系（materials structure-property response relationships）的合成样本；(2) 五个递增难度等级，量化响应关系的复杂度；(3) 多维度指标 MatFormScore，从目标成功率、搜索效率、探索能力、鲁棒性和稳定性五个关键轴（axes）综合量化性能。

Result: 在 1170 次标准化算法-任务评估中，扩散模型整体表现最强；变分自编码器（Variational Autoencoder, VAE）和遗传算法（Genetic Algorithm, GA）在特定场景下展现出独特优势。

Conclusion: MatFormBench 为目标驱动材料配方建立了统一的评价标准，实现了可复现的基准测试（reproducible benchmarking）、有原则的算法比较（principled algorithm comparison）以及逆设计策略的诊断分析（diagnostic analysis），为推进材料逆设计提供了基础性工具。

Abstract: Inverse design of materials has significantly advanced target-driven formulation optimization, yet existing materials machine learning benchmarks remain limited to forward property prediction, failing to systematically evaluate inverse optimization and generation algorithms, a critical gap that hinders the progress of target-driven materials design. To address this limitation, we propose MatFormBench, a novel benchmarking ecosystem tailored to evaluate and guide generative strategies for target-driven formulation. MatFormBench integrates a physics-driven formulation generation scheme to generate synthetic samples that faithfully emulate realistic materials structure-property response relationships, complemented by five escalating difficulty levels to quantify the complexity of these relationships. To rigorously assess algorithm performance, we further propose MatFormScore, a multi-dimensional metric that comprehensively quantifies performance across five critical axes: target success, search efficiency, exploratory capacity, robustness, and stability. We validate MatFormBench by evaluating 39 diverse inverse design algorithms, covering classical surrogate-assisted black-box search, state-of-the-art deep generative models, and increasingly popular Large Language Model (LLM)-based recommendation strategies. Across 1170 standardized algorithm-task evaluations, diffusion-based models demonstrate the strongest overall performance, while Variational Autoencoder (VAE)-based and Genetic Algorithm (GA)-based methods exhibit distinct advantages in specific scenarios. By establishing a unified evaluation standard for target-driven materials formulation, MatFormBench enables reproducible benchmarking, principled algorithm comparison, and diagnostic analysis of inverse design strategies, providing a foundational tool for advancing materials inverse design.

### [109] [Tunable competing optical excitation pathways in the topological surface states of Bi$_2$Te$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26799)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用角度分辨双光子光电子能谱（angle-resolved two-photon photoemission spectroscopy）技术，对Bi₂Te₃的拓扑表面态进行测量，分析其激发路径与光谱调制行为。

Conclusion: 这些结果为TSSs的光激发机制提供了微观层面的理解，并突显了调控其光学响应的潜力，对未来自旋电子学（spintronic）器件的应用具有参考价值。

Abstract: Understanding coherent optical responses of topological surface states (TSSs) requires disentangling excitation pathways from the electronic band structure. Here, using angle-resolved two-photon photoemission spectroscopy, we identify two distinct excitation pathways in the TSSs of Bi$_2$Te$_3$: an off-resonant transition via virtual states and a resonant transition via unoccupied intermediate states. A pronounced modulation of the spectral response is observed, revealing a competition between the two coherent pathways. This competition is tunable via temperature-induced shifts of the chemical potential, which selectively modify the resonant channel. These results provide microscopic insight into the optical excitation mechanisms of TSSs and highlight the potential for controlling their optical responses, relevant for future spintronic devices.

### [110] [Defect engineering of ultrathin gallium nitride via electric fields for advanced electronic, magnetic, and gas sensing applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26817)

Using nitrogen monoxide (NO) adsorption as a prototype, we find that the interaction is defect-modulated and potentially tunable by electric fields. By systematically examining the geometry, energetics, band structure, density of states, magnetic response, and charge transfer, this study clarifies the interplay between defects and external electric fields, providing insights into theoretical upper bounds for property tuning and semiconductor device engineering.

### [111] [Radiative electronic bound states in the continuum from defects in semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26841)
*Seong Yun Hong,Liang Z. Tan,Ki Hoon Lee,Youngho Kang,Yeonghun Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以硅G中心为原型，通过含Hubbard $U$修正的混合泛函第一性原理计算，揭示了原本埋藏于价带顶（VBM）之下的局域缺陷态在光激发下发生交换驱动的能级重排，跃升至VBM之上，从而形成辐射性电子束缚态（electronic BICs）。该机制抑制了非辐射衰减，实现了稳定的辐射发光，并通过计算温度依赖的非辐射寿命与实验光致发光（PL）寿命定量吻合，为连续谱埋藏缺陷态的光学活性提供了新的范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合泛函（hybrid-functional）第一性原理计算，并加入Hubbard $U$修正，以硅G中心（silicon G-center）作为原型体系，分析局域缺陷态在基态与激发态下的能级位置变化，同时计算温度依赖的非辐射寿命并与实验光致发光（PL）寿命进行比较。

Result: 在基态下，局域缺陷态埋藏于价带顶（VBM）之下；光激发后，交换作用驱动能级重排（exchange-driven energy-level reordering），使该态跃升至VBM之上，形成辐射性电子束缚态（electronic BICs）。该机制有效抑制了非辐射衰减，计算得到的温度依赖非辐射寿命与实验PL寿命定量一致。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一种连续谱埋藏缺陷态的稳定化机制，并将电子束缚态（electronic BICs）确立为设计缺陷基光学系统（包括量子发射器和量子比特）的通用范式。

Abstract: Continuum-buried defect states in semiconductors are generally expected to be optically inactive due to their strong coupling to continuum bands. Here, we show that such defects can instead host radiative electronic bound states in the continuum (BICs), using the silicon G-center as a prototypical example. Hybrid-functional first-principles calculations with a Hubbard $U$ correction reveal that a localized defect state, initially buried below the valence band maximum (VBM) in the ground state, undergoes exchange-driven energy-level reordering under optical excitation and shifts above the VBM. This exchange-induced transition suppresses nonradiative decay and enables robust radiative emission. By computing temperature-dependent nonradiative lifetimes and comparing them with experimental photoluminescence (PL) lifetimes, we quantitatively reproduce the observed temperature dependence of the emission. These results uncover a stabilization mechanism for continuum-embedded defect states and establish electronic BICs as a general paradigm for designing defect-based optical systems, including quantum emitters and qubits.

### [112] [Electronic properties governing the phase stability and elastic anisotropy of C14 and C15 Cr-Hf-Nb Laves phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26868)
*M. Díaz-Choque,C. F. Schuch,L. T. F. Eleno*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用密度泛函理论（DFT）分析了Cr-Hf-Nb体系中C14和C15 Laves相的热力学稳定性、弹性各向异性及电子性质，确认了两种相的稳定性和弹性各向异性排序，并揭示费米能级附近的强反键行为是主要失稳机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）进行计算，结合生成焓（formation enthalpy）和全面弹性性质分析评估热力学与力学稳定性；通过弹性参数评价弹性各向异性（elastic anisotropy）；利用电子结构和晶体轨道哈密顿布居（COHP）分析探明原子间成键行为。

Result: C14相（HfNb₂, HfCr₂, NbCr₂）和C15相（HfCr₂, NbCr₂）均具有能量与力学稳定性；C14相弹性各向异性顺序为HfCr₂ > NbCr₂ > HfNb₂，C15相则为NbCr₂ > HfNb₂ > HfCr₂；费米能级附近XM₂ M–M键的强反键行为是两类Laves相的主要失稳机制。

Conclusion: DFT计算证实了所研究的C14与C15 Laves相在热力学和力学上均稳定，并明确了弹性各向异性的组成依赖关系；电子结构分析揭示了反键态对相稳定性的关键影响。

Abstract: This study utilizes Density Functional Theory (DFT) to investigate the thermodynamic stability, elastic anisotropy, and electronic properties of C14 and C15 Laves phases within the Cr--Hf--Nb system. Both formation enthalpies and comprehensive elastic property analyses confirm the energetic and mechanical stability of the C14 (HfNb$_2$, HfCr$_2$, NbCr$_2$) and C15 (HfCr$_2$, NbCr$_2$) phases. Furthermore, the evaluation of elastic anisotropy reveals a descending order of HfCr$_2$ > NbCr$_2$ > HfNb$_2$ for the C14 phase, contrasting with NbCr$_2$ > HfNb$_2$ > HfCr$_2$ for the C15 phase. Finally, electronic structure and COHP analyses indicate that strong anti-bonding behavior near the Fermi level within the XM$_2$ M--M bonds acts as a primary destabilization mechanism for both of these Laves phases.

Abstract: Hybridization of highly itinerant Dirac electrons with localized flat-band states is predicted to yield emergent phenomena such as exotic heavy-fermion behaviour. Epitaxial graphene on two-dimensional adsorbate structures on SiC(0001), which host flat bands, offers a promising platform to explore these effects. However, direct experimental evidence of interlayer hybridization in such systems has so far been lacking. Here, we address this gap using time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (trARPES) where interlayer hybridization manifests in three key observations: (1) accelerated Dirac-carrier relaxation arising from additional electronic and phononic decay channels provided by the flat-band subsystem, (2) transient charging of the Dirac cone enabled by direct optical excitation from the flat bands, and (3) ultrafast back-transfer of charge into the flat bands on timescales governed by the interlayer coupling strength. Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulation）研究缺陷迁移；迁移势垒通过微动弹性带方法（Nudged Elastic Band, NEB）计算；有限温度下的扩散率分别通过均方位移方法（mean square displacement, MSD）和跳频方法（jump frequency approach）进行评估。

Abstract: The migration of point defects and formation of spin defects in 3C-SiC were investigated using molecular dynamics simulations, with migration barriers obtained from Nudged Elastic Band (NEB) calculations and finite temperature diffusivities evaluated using both mean square displacement (MSD) and jump frequency approaches. While both methods reproduce Arrhenius behavior, the jump frequency formulation exhibits improved statistical stability. Activation energies of 2.12~eV for carbon vacancies and 0.88~eV for carbon interstitials are obtained, consistent with literature. The resulting mobility hierarchy governs defect evolution and complex formations. Interstitial vacancy recombination competes with vacancy aggregation into divacancies, influencing the stabilization of spin active defect centers. ### [118] [Electron Polaron at Neutral 180$^\circ$ Domain Wall in PbTiO$_3$: Stability, Trapping Energies, and Transverse Polarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27077)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用含哈伯德修正的密度泛函理论（DFT+U）方法，通过有限尺寸修正的极化子能级对齐程序确定Ti 3d态的哈伯德参数（Hubbard parameter），构建体相和畴壁超胞模型进行计算。

Result: 体相中极化子捕获能（trapping energy）为−0.06 eV；畴壁超胞中过量电子局域在Ti上形成Ti³⁺中心，出现占据的d_xy轨道带隙态（in-gap state）。体相类与畴壁附近Ti位点的捕获能差异仅约0.01 eV。极化子诱发垂直于畴壁的横向极化分量，增强局域类奈尔（Néel-like）畸变。

Conclusion: 中性180°畴壁不会显著改变Ti中心电子极化子的稳定性，但极化子可通过局域横向极化响应与畴壁耦合，诱导局域结构畸变。

Abstract: We use density-functional theory with a Hubbard correction to investigate Ti-centered electron polarons at neutral PbO-centered $180^\circ$ domain walls in tetragonal PbTiO$_{3}$. The Hubbard parameter for Ti $3d$ states is determined using the finite-size-corrected polaronic energy-level alignment procedure, yielding stable electron-polaron formation in bulk PbTiO$_3$ with a trapping energy of $-$0.06 eV. In the domain-wall supercell, the excess electron localizes on Ti and forms a Ti$^{3+}$ center with an occupied $d_{xy}$ orbital in-gap state. Comparison of bulk-like and near-wall Ti sites shows that their trapping energies differ by only about 0.01 eV, indicating that this neutral domain wall does not provide a significant thermodynamic driving force for electron-polaron segregation. While the Ising-like reversal of the out-of-plane polarization is preserved, the localized electron induces a finite transverse polarization component normal to the wall, enhancing a local Néel-like distortion that is strongest when the polaron is located at the wall. These results show that neutral $180^\circ$ domain walls in PbTiO$_3$ do not substantially alter the stability of Ti-centered electron polarons, but they can couple to the polaron-induced lattice distortion through a localized transverse polarization response.

### [119] [Origin of the Temperature-Induced Gap Bowing of Formamidinium-Methylammonium Lead Iodide Perovskites: Role of Cationic Rattlers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27104)
*Kai Xu,Adrián Francisco-López,Bethan L. Charles,M. Isabel Alonso,Miquel Garriga,Mark T. Weller,Alejandro R. Goñi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过结合变温与变压光致发光测量，揭示了FA-MA混合阳离子铅卤钙钛矿单晶在低温相中带隙弯曲（gap bowing）现象的起源：热膨胀与电子-声子相互作用均有贡献，但后者为主导因素，由混合振动模式激活的反常电子-声子耦合机制驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体带隙的温度依赖性对优化光电器件至关重要，然而FA-MA铅碘钙钛矿低温相中显著的温致带隙弯曲（gap bowing）的起源此前尚不明确。

Method: 对一系列FA<sub>x</sub>MA<sub>1-x</sub>PbI<sub>3</sub>混合阳离子单晶（x∈[0,1]）开展温度与压力依赖的光致发光（photoluminescence）测量。

Result: 带隙弯曲由热膨胀（thermal expansion）与电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interaction）共同引起，其中后者是主导项；该效应源于一种反常电子-声子耦合（anomalous electron-phonon coupling）机制，涉及无机笼八面体倾斜声子与低频FA摆动模式（rattler modes）的混合振动模式，并在正交相和（赝）四方相低温相中发生，FA浓度在20%–90%区间时可能呈现条纹畴结构（stripe domains）。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了铅卤钙钛矿中一种直接影响其光电器件性能的奇特行为，即混合振动模式驱动的反常电子-声子耦合是低温相带隙弯曲的主要起源。

Abstract: A thorough understanding of the temperature dependence of semiconductor band gaps is essential for optimizing optoelectronic devices. In this respect, the origin of the pronounced temperature-induced gap bowing observed in low-temperature phases of formamidinium-methylammonium (FA-MA) lead iodide perovskites has remained elusive until now. By combining temperature and pressure-dependent photoluminescence measurements on a series of FA$_x$MA$_{1-x}$PbI$_3$ mixed-cation single crystals with $x\in[0,1]$, we unravel the origin of this bowing. Both thermal expansion as well as electron-phonon interaction effects are responsible. However, the latter is the leading term, driven by the activation of an anomalous electron-phonon coupling mechanism linked to mixed vibrational modes, which combine inorganic-cage phonons involving octahedral tilting with low-frequency FA librations, i.e., FA rattler modes. This occurs in the orthorhombic and (pseudo)tetragonal low-temperature phases, presumably featuring stripe domains with alternating octahedral tilt-axis patterns for FA concentrations between 20\% and 90\%. In this way, we have shed light on an intriguing behavior of lead halide perovskites that directly affects their optoelectronic properties.

### [120] [Light-induced Faraday effect from dynamical breakdown of Kleinman symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27127)
*Niccolò Sellati,Jacopo Fiore,Lara Benfatto*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明，在圆偏振光泵浦-探测实验中观测到的异常大的偏振旋转并非源于逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）产生的宏观磁化，而是完全由三阶光学磁化率（third-order optical susceptibility）的反对称分量引起。这一光致法拉第效应（light-induced Faraday effect）本质上是动力学的，在克莱因曼对称性（Kleinman symmetry）被破坏时出现。通过一个方格上的最小sp紧束缚模型，研究显示该效应即使在远离耗散共振时也能达到可观大小，且与声子的共振耦合可显著增强响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期圆偏振光泵浦-探测实验观测到异常大的偏振旋转，其幅度远超逆法拉第效应的理论预期，暗示产生了数量级上更大的有效磁场。这挑战了光致时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking）的既有理解，亟需新的理论解释。

Method: 研究通过理论推导证明静态偏振旋转完全源自三阶光学磁化率的反对称分量，而非宏观磁化。采用方格上的最小sp紧束缚模型（minimal sp tight-binding model）进行数值演示，并分析了克莱因曼对称性破坏的条件以及声子共振耦合的影响。

Result: 光致法拉第效应是动力学效应，在克莱因曼对称性被破坏时出现；即使在远离耗散共振的区域，该响应仍可达到显著大小；该效应在纯电子层面即可产生，但通过与声子的共振耦合可得到显著增强。

Conclusion: 观测到的异常偏振旋转来源于三阶光学磁化率的反对称分量，无需材料的宏观磁化即可解释，这修正了传统上对逆法拉第效应的理解。

Abstract: The observation of anomalously large polarization rotations in pump-probe experiments with circularly polarized light has recently challenged the conventional understanding of the inverse Faraday effect. The striking magnitude of these responses implies the generation of effective magnetic fields orders of magnitude larger than theoretical expectations, raising fundamental questions about the nature of light-induced time-reversal symmetry breaking. In this work we demonstrate that a static polarization rotation can originate entirely from the antisymmetric component of the third-order optical susceptibility, without generating a macroscopic magnetization of the material. We show that this light-induced Faraday effect is inherently dynamical, emerging when Kleinman symmetry breaks down. Using a minimal sp tight-binding model on a square lattice, we demonstrate that the light-induced Faraday response can be sizable even far from dissipative resonances. While the effect emerges at a purely electronic level, we show that resonant coupling with phonons can significantly enhance the pump-probe response.

</details>


### [121] [Identifying and designing altermagnetic crystals in real space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27151)
*Ying Chen,Qiushi Huang,Yu Wu,Xiaolan Yan,Su-Huai Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于实空间对称性的简单判据来识别交变磁性（altermagnetism）晶态：在III型磁性空间群描述的共线补偿反铁磁体中，若反演操作不交换两个自旋相反的亚晶格，则通常允许交变磁自旋劈裂。该判据将交变磁体的识别简化为透明直观的实空间对称性检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交变磁体识别方法通常需要完整的磁性空间群（magnetic space group）或自旋群（spin group）分析，过程繁琐且不够直观。作者希望提出一种更简单、直接的实空间判据，从而方便地判断共线反铁磁体中是否存在交变磁自旋劈裂。

Method: 文章聚焦于由III型磁性空间群描述的共线补偿反铁磁体，其磁原胞与非磁晶体原胞一致。作者基于晶体学操作如何置换两个自旋相反的亚晶格（sublattice），提出实空间判据：若反演（inversion）操作不在这两个亚晶格之间传递，则通常允许交变磁自旋劈裂。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对代表性非中心和中心对称材料进行验证。

Result: 所提出的实空间判据在非中心对称和中心对称的代表性材料中均得到第一性原理计算的验证。该判据还可推广至低维晶体或赝晶体（pseudocrystals）。

Conclusion: 该工作将交变磁性的识别简化为一个透明直观的实空间对称性检验，为发现交变磁晶体提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Altermagnetism is a compensated magnetic phase characterized by zero net magnetization and exchange-driven spin splitting. However, identifying altermagnets among collinear antiferromagnets usually requires full magnetic-space-group or spin-group analysis, which is not intuitive. Here we formulate a simple real-space criterion based on how the crystallographic operations of the host nonmagnetic structure permute the two opposite-spin sublattices. For simplicity, we focus on collinear compensated antiferromagnets commonly described by type-III magnetic space groups, whose magnetic primitive cell coincides with the host nonmagnetic crystallographic primitive cell. In this class, altermagnetic spin splitting is generally allowed unless inversion operation exists which transfer between the two opposite-spin sublattices. First-principles calculations on representative noncentrosymmetric and centrosymmetric materials demonstrate these criterions. Similar rules can also be applied to low-dimensional crystals or pseudocrystals. Our work reduces the identification of altermagnetism to a transparent real-space symmetry test and provides a practical route for discovering altermagnetic crystals.

</details>


### [122] [Rapid estimation of synthesizability windows of inorganic materials from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27162)
*Finja Tadge,Javier Sanz Rodrigo,Andrea Crovetto*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种高通量生成材料相占优图（phase predominance diagram）的方法，通过结合元素相参考能拟合、机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials）来快速预测材料的合成条件，大幅降低了计算成本，并成功应用于氧化物、氮化物、硫化物、磷化物及三元金属磷硫化物体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在热力学平衡假设下，快速预测材料合成条件仍具挑战：仅基于凸稳定壳（convex stability hull）的方法忽略了有限温度效应，而基于声子（phonon）的相图计算又过于昂贵。现有方法难以在计算效率与准确性之间取得平衡。

Method: 通过对零温总能拟合元素相参考能（elemental phase reference energies）以改进生成焓（formation enthalpy）计算；利用机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials）快速获取振动熵（vibrational entropy）和热容（heat capacity）；进而高通量生成作为温度和气体反应物分压函数的相占优图（phase predominance diagram）。

Result: 在氧化物、氮化物、硫化物、磷化物及48个更复杂的三元金属磷硫化物体系中生成了相占优图；与实验合成文献总体吻合良好；计算成本相比传统基于DFT声子计算的方法大幅降低；识别出多个在零温稳定壳下表现为亚稳态（metastable）、但在特定热力学窗口下可稳定存在的化合物。

Conclusion: 该方法能够将“高于稳定壳的能量”（energies above stability hull）转化为直观的合成条件，弥合计算预测与实验合成之间的鸿沟，并可推广至任何无机材料的合成条件快速估算。

Abstract: Fast prediction of the synthesizability conditions of materials remains challenging, even assuming synthesis under thermodynamic equilibrium. Approaches solely based on convex stability hulls neglect finite-temperature effects, while phonon-based phase diagram calculations are computationally demanding. Here, we demonstrate high-throughput generation of phase predominance diagrams as a function of temperature and partial pressures of gaseous reactants, helping bridge the gap between computational predictions and experimental synthesis. We employ fitting of elemental phase reference energies to zero-temperature total energies for improved calculation of formation enthalpies, along with machine-learned interatomic potentials for rapid determination of vibrational entropy and heat capacity. The resulting predominance diagrams can be intuitively understood by experimentalists and can be used to translate energies above stability hulls into synthesis conditions. Predominance diagrams are generated for selected oxide, nitride, sulfide, and phosphide systems, as well as for 48 more complex ternary metal phosphosulfide systems. The calculated predominance diagrams generally show good agreement with the experimental synthesis literature, with a drastic reduction in computational cost compared to a conventional approach relying on DFT-based phonon calculations. We identify several compounds predicted to be stable under well-defined thermodynamic windows, even though they appear as metastable in a zero-temperature stability hull picture. The method can be applied to rapidly estimate synthesis conditions for any inorganic material.

</details>


### [123] [Amorphous vs. Short-Range-Ordered Complexions: Consequences for Grain-Boundary-Mediated Plasticity in Nanocrystalline Al-Ni Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27218)
*Frederic Sansoz,Eve-Audrey Picard*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模蒙提卡罗（Monte Carlo）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究了纳米晶Al-Ni合金中非晶态晶界（grain-boundary, GB）复合相（complexions）的短程有序（short-range ordering, SRO）对塑性机制的影响，发现非晶复合相通过剪切转变区（shear transformation zone）促进均匀塑性但强度较低，而含SRO的复合相虽强度更高但导致应力集中与强烈剪切局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热稳定纳米晶合金中的非晶晶界复合相通常被视为结构均匀的，但其无序本质易产生局域短程有序（SRO），而SRO对晶界介导的塑性机制的影响尚不明确，因此本文旨在填补这一认知空白。

Method: 采用大规模蒙提卡罗（Monte Carlo）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，对两种Ni浓度（2 at.%和4 at.%）的纳米晶Al-Ni合金进行退火处理：913 K退火产生厚均匀非晶间薄膜复合相，378 K退火产生含FCC型和BCC型短程有序（SRO）的半非晶复合相。

Result: 非晶复合相作为位错陷阱（dislocation sinks），抑制剪切局域化并通过剪切转变区（shear transformation zone）促进均匀塑性，但强度较低；含SRO的复合相产生更高强度，但在晶界网络（GB network）上引发异质性应力集中，导致强烈剪切局域化，且与Ni浓度无关。

Conclusion: 两种复合相状态的力学响应差异反映了从非晶复合相合金中剪切转变区控制的塑性行为，到SRO复合相合金中晶界应力异质性控制的行为这一根本性机制转变，突显了复合相工程（complexion engineering）调控纳米晶材料力学性能的潜力。

Abstract: Amorphous grain-boundary (GB) complexions in thermally stable nanocrystalline alloys are commonly assumed to be structurally homogeneous, yet their disordered nature makes them susceptible to local short-range ordering (SRO). The influence of local SRO on GB-mediated plasticity mechanisms in such complexions remains poorly understood. This article employs large-scale Monte Carlo and molecular dynamics simulation to address this gap through simulations of nanocrystalline Al-Ni alloys at two Ni concentrations, 2 at.% and 4 at.%. Annealing at 913 K produces thick uniform amorphous intergranular film complexions, while annealing at 378 K produces semi-amorphous complexions containing FCC-type and BCC-type SRO. These two complexion states produce fundamentally different mechanical responses. Amorphous complexions act as dislocation sinks, suppressing shear localization and promoting homogeneous plasticity through shear transformation zones, but at the cost of lower strength. SRO complexions generate higher strength but also promote heterogeneous stress concentrations across the GB network, leading to intense shear localization regardless of Ni concentration. This contrast reflects a fundamental shift in governing mechanism, from shear-transformation-zone-controlled behavior in amorphous complexion alloys to GB-stress-heterogeneity-controlled behavior in SRO complexion alloys. These findings highlight the potential of complexion engineering to tailor the mechanical properties of nanocrystalline materials.

</details>


### [124] [At-Scale Data-Driven Exploration of High-Voltage Cathode-Active Materials for Sodium Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27229)
*Suchona Akter,Mohammad R. Momeni*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究构建了一个面向钠离子电池（SIBs）正极活性材料（CAMs）发现的大规模稳定材料数据库，并开发了基于描述符的机器学习（ML）模型，用于预测平均电压和比容量。通过前四名模型的委员会预测与高通量第一性原理验证相结合，筛选出高性能候选材料，建立了一套可扩展且可迁移的加速SIBs高压正极材料发现框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钠离子电池（SIBs）具有资源丰富、成本低廉及钠离子迁移率高于锂离子等优势，其高压正极活性材料（CAMs）的发现依赖于新型全无机材料。然而，全无机材料家族化学空间极为庞大且多样，亟需高效的数据驱动筛选方法以加速探索稳定且高性能的候选材料。

Method: 首先，从Materials Project、AFLOW、OQMD和GNoME四个大型数据库中筛选并构建了经化学验证的稳定材料数据库。其次，基于仅充电态结构（charged-only structures）的数据集，开发了具有泛化性和可迁移性的基于描述符的机器学习（ML）模型。采用前四个训练好的ML模型组成委员会（committee），预测平均电压（average voltage）和比容量（specific capacity）作为目标性质。最后，对排名靠前的候选CAMs进行高通量第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证，评估其电压曲线、相稳定性、钠化/脱钠过程的结构鲁棒性及电子性质。

Result: 成功建立了大规模、经化学验证的SIB正极材料数据库，开发了基于描述符的ML模型，并利用委员会模型实现了平均电压和比容量的有效预测。通过高通量第一性原理计算对排名靠前的候选材料进行了验证。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的数据整合、机器学习排序预测与第一性原理验证相结合的策略，建立了一个可扩展且可迁移的框架，能够加速发现用于钠离子电池（SIBs）及其他电池体系的稳定、高压正极活性材料（CAMs）。

Abstract: Sodium-ion batteries (SIBs) share similar electrochemistry with Li but offer several advantages, including high abundance in nature and low cost, as well as suitability for fast charging due to a Na-ion mobility higher than that of Li. The development of high-voltage SIBs heavily relies on the discovery of novel, robust cathode-active materials (CAMs). All-inorganic materials represent the most mature and practical choice as CAMs for next-generation SIBs; however, their family spans a vast and chemically diverse space. In this work, we present a large-scale, chemically validated database of stable materials for SIB cathode discovery, curated from four major databases: Materials Project, AFLOW, OQMD, and GNoME. Generalizable and transferable descriptor-based machine learning (ML) models are developed based on a dataset of charged-only structures rather than charged/discharged pairs. Using a committee of the top four trained ML models, average voltage and specific capacity are predicted as target properties. Finally, a subset of top-ranked candidate CAMs is validated through explicit, high-throughput first-principles calculations of voltage profiles, phase stability, structural robustness upon sodiation/desodiation, and electronic properties. Together, this integrated data curation, ML ranking and predictions, and first-principles validation strategy establishes a scalable and transferable framework for accelerating the discovery of stable, high-voltage CAMs for SIBs and beyond.

Conclusion: 受控机械合成捐赠（mechanosynthetic donation）被确立为可编程原子精确制造（programmable atomically precise fabrication）的一项基础能力，为未来实现更复杂的原子级精准结构构筑提供了可行路径。

We demonstrate single-site C$_2$ donation, spatially patterned multi-site C$_2$ donation, and the stepwise assembly of polyyne structures through successive C-C bond formation. Together, these results establish controlled mechanosynthetic donation as a foundational capability for programmable atomically precise fabrication.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: MISTnetX有效解决了含能材料多尺度模拟中尺度分离缺失的难题，为冲击转爆轰过程提供了一种无参数的预测方法。

Abstract: The shock-to-detonation transition in energetic materials is governed by coupled processes spanning Angstroms to millimeters and femtoseconds to microseconds, where traditional multiscale models fail due to the lack of scale separation. We address this grand challenge by directly bridging large-scale molecular dynamics (MD) simulations with continuum finite-element (FE) models using MISTnetX, a convolutional deep neural network. Trained on MD simulations of shock propagation through complex microstructures, MISTnetX captures shock-microstructure interactions, hotspot formation, and the transition to deflagration, supplying critical sub-grid information to FE simulations of mechanics, shocks, thermal transport, and chemistry. ### [127] [A gentle introduction to the cosmological multiverse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27107)
*Oliver Janssen*

Main category: physics.pop-ph

TL;DR: 本文面向艺术家读者，科普性地介绍了宇宙学多重宇宙（cosmological multiverse）概念。文章从广义相对论（general relativity）和宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）出发，阐述了宇宙学常数带来的重大疑难，以及多重宇宙如何可能解决这一疑难，同时指出多重宇宙会变得任意巨大和古老，并引出了永恒暴胀（eternal inflation）中的测量问题（measure problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向艺术家等非专业受众，以通俗易懂的方式介绍宇宙学多重宇宙的概念及其背后的核心物理问题，特别是宇宙学常数疑难及其潜在解决方案。

Method: 采取科普性论述方式，从广义相对论和宇宙学常数出发，逐步引入宇宙学常数疑难，进而讨论多重宇宙作为可能的解决方案，最后指出该方案带来的新问题（测量问题）。

Result: 指出多重宇宙可以变得任意巨大和古老，且存在一个尚未解决的核心难题——如何在永恒加速膨胀的宇宙中对观测做出明确无歧义的预测，即永恒暴胀的测量问题。

Conclusion: 多重宇宙虽有可能解决宇宙学常数疑难，但它本身并非免费的午餐，会带来任意大规模和年龄的问题，以及目前尚未解决的测量问题。

Abstract: We give an introduction to the cosmological multiverse, aimed at an audience of artists. We discuss general relativity -- our modern theory of gravity -- and the cosmological constant, which is widely believed to be responsible for the observed accelerated expansion of the universe. We then turn to a big puzzle that the cosmological constant poses, and, eventually, how the multiverse could solve this puzzle. There's no such thing as a free lunch, however: the multiverse can become arbitrarily large and old. The unsolved problem of making unambiguous predictions for observations in eternally accelerating universes is known as the measure problem of eternal inflation.

<div id='physics.optics'></div>
