### [128] [Programming nanomechanical computation with light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26319)
*Xiaofei Guo,Jonne Drost,Fons van der Laan,Jesse J. Slim,Marc Serra-Garcia,Ewold Verhagen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过腔光力学（cavity optomechanics）相互作用，利用强非线性效应实现了由激光控制的纳米机械自由度计算，展示了具备电平恢复功能的基本数字逻辑门，并指出该系统可在接近热振幅的热力学随机性主导区域运行，为受控非线性谐振器（controlled nonlinear resonators）的物理计算（physical computing）开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将物理系统视为计算机，可将热噪声、对称性或拓扑等物理性质视为非常规计算资源。然而，利用这些资源需要在系统中通过强可控的非线性来实现可编程的计算功能。当前缺乏有效的途径以受控方式实现此类物理计算。

Method: 利用腔光力学相互作用实现激光控制的纳米机械自由度计算；通过强光学-力学非线性和精确读出，构建具备电平恢复（level restoration）功能的基本数字逻辑门，并实现受控机械耦合（controlled mechanical couplings）。

Result: 成功展示了一组具有电平恢复功能的基本数字逻辑门；系统在接近热振幅（thermal amplitudes）的区域运行，该区域由热力学随机性（thermodynamic stochasticity）主导。

Conclusion: 该系统为实现受控非线性谐振器的物理计算开辟了一条新路径，表明强光力学非线性和精确读出能力使得在热噪声主导的环境中仍可实现计算功能。

Abstract: Looking at physical systems as computers allows us to regard physical properties, such as thermal noise, symmetry or topology, as unconventional resources for computation. However, harnessing these resources requires programming computational functionality through strong, controllable nonlinearities in the system. Here, we show that cavity optomechanical interactions allow laser-controlled computation with nanomechanical degrees of freedom. We demonstrate a set of basic digital logic gates with level restoration and controlled mechanical couplings as essential ingredients for arbitrary computing networks. Owing to the strong optomechanical nonlinearity and precise readout, the system operates close to thermal amplitudes, in the regime where thermodynamic stochasticity governs its behavior. This opens a new path for the realization of physical computing with controlled nonlinear resonators.

### [129] [Axion-like particles solve the $B\to Kν\barν$ and $B\to πK$ puzzles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24713)
*Bhubanjyoti Bhattacharya,Alakabha Datta,Girish Kumar,Danny Marfatia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对Belle~II合作组观测到的$B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$分支比相对于标准模型（Standard Model）预期存在2.7σ增强，以及$B \to \pi K$衰变中的分支比和CP不对称性测量遗留的异常，提出用质量接近$\pi^0$的短寿命类轴子粒子（axion-like particle, ALP）来解释这两个味改变中性流（flavor-changing neutral current, FCNC）B衰变中的反常现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Belle~II合作组新近测得的$B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$分支比与标准模型预期存在2.7σ的偏差，同时$B \to \pi K$衰变中的分支比和CP不对称性测量长期存在未解异常。这两个反常现象暗示可能存在超越标准模型的新物理，亟需一个统一的理论框架予以解释。

Method: 构建一个最小模型，引入一个质量接近$\pi^0$的短寿命类轴子粒子（ALP），该ALP与光子、顶夸克（top quark）及一个重惰性中微子（heavy sterile neutrino $\nu_N$）耦合。ALP通过与$\pi^0$混合贡献于$B \to \pi^0 K$衰变，并通过离壳（off-shell）耦合到惰性中微子对贡献于$B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$过程。

Result: 该模型对所有$B \to K^{(*)} + \mathrm{inv}$衰变模式以及稀有Kaon衰变$K^+ \to \pi^+ + \mathrm{inv}$和$K_L \to \pi^0 + \mathrm{inv}$给出了具体预言。模型对缪子磁矩（magnetic moment of the muon）有显著贡献，而对电子磁矩和$b \to s e^+ e^-$过程的贡献可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 所提出的ALP最小模型能够同时解释Belle~II的$B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$反常和$B \to \pi K$衰变中的长期异常，并为相关稀有衰变过程和缪子反常磁矩提供可检验的理论预言。

Abstract: The recent measurement of the branching ratio of $B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$ (where "inv" denotes invisible states) by the Belle~II collaboration is enhanced relative to the standard model expectation by 2.7$σ$. An older puzzle persists in measurements of the branching ratios and CP asymmetries of $B \to πK $ decays. We address these two anomalies in flavor-changing neutral current $B$ decays, with a short-lived axion-like particle (ALP) with mass close to that of the $π^0$. In the minimal model, the ALP has couplings to the photon, top quark and a heavy sterile neutrino $ν_N$. The ALP contributes to the $B \to π^0 K$ decays by mixing with the $π^0$. It contributes to $B^+ \to K^+ + \mathrm{inv}$ by its off-shell coupling to sterile neutrino pairs. We make predictions for all $B \to K^{(*)} + \mathrm{inv}$ modes and for the rare kaon decays $K^+ \to π^+ + \mathrm{inv}$ and $K_L \to π^0 + \mathrm{inv}$. We find an appreciable contribution to the magnetic moment of the muon, and negligible contributions to the magnetic moment of the electron and $b \to s e^+ e^-$.

</details>


### [130] [Particle-Lund Multimodality in Jet Taggers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26821)
*Loukas Gouskos,Benedikt Maier*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出PLuM，一种多模态架构，将粒子成分和Lund平面分裂投影到共享潜在空间并用统一transformer联合处理。通过交叉注意力机制发现，显式的层次化QCD结构信息在b-jet标记等任务中仍能提供超越原始粒子表示的辨别能力，尤其在HH(4b)末态下背景抑制提升25%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究基于transformer的喷注标记器（jet tagger）是否已从粒子成分输入中隐式捕获了层次化的QCD结构信息，抑或显式的物理表示仍具有互补价值。

Method: 引入PLuM多模态架构，将粒子成分（particle constituents）和Lund平面分裂（Lund plane splittings）投影到共享潜在空间（shared latent space），通过统一transformer联合处理，并利用交叉注意力（cross-attention）机制检验结构化QCD信息是否提供额外判别能力。

Result: 在top夸克和H→bb标记任务中观察到系统性增益；H→cc和H→4q拓扑未见类似提升。在LHC HH(4b)分析场景下，25%双希格斯效率工作点处，PLuM的背景抑制（background rejection）比基线提高25%。

Conclusion: 显式的层次化QCD辐射结构信息在transformer时代仍保留判别价值，b-jet形成相关的层次信息对原始粒子表示具有互补性，不同喷注动力学方面被深度学习算法编码的方式值得进一步研究。

Abstract: The Lund plane offers a physics-motivated, hierarchical representation of QCD radiation within jets, while transformer-based taggers have reached state-of-the-art performance by learning directly from raw particle constituents and their pairwise relations. We investigate whether transformers implicitly capture hierarchical QCD structure from constituent-level inputs, or whether explicit physics representations remain complementary. To test this, we introduce PLuM, a multimodal architecture that projects particle constituents and Lund plane splittings into a shared latent space, processing both jointly with a unified transformer. Cross-attention allows the model to probe whether structured QCD information provides discriminating power beyond what particles alone encode. We observe systematic gains for top-quark and $\mathrm{H}\to\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$ tagging, while finding no comparable improvement for $\mathrm{H}\to\mathrm{c}\bar{\mathrm{c}}$ or $\mathrm{H}\to 4\mathrm{q}$ topologies. This selective enhancement suggests that explicit hierarchical information about b-jet formation remains complementary to raw particle representations even in highly expressive architectures, while other topologies are already well-captured at constituent level. For high-impact LHC analyses such as Lorentz-boosted di-Higgs searches in the four $\mathrm{b}$ quark final state ($\mathrm{H}\mathrm{H}(4\mathrm{b})$), the gains are substantial: at a $25\%$ di-Higgs efficiency working point, PLuM achieves $25\%$ higher background rejection than the baseline. Our results indicate that physically structured representations of QCD radiation retain discriminating value in the transformer era, motivating further study into how different aspects of jet dynamics are encoded by deep learning algorithms.

</details>


### [131] [Family-separated seesaw relations of Majorana neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27049)
*Zhi-zhong Xing*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在规范跷跷板机制（canonical seesaw mechanism）框架下，针对轻中微子和重马约拉纳中微子（Majorana neutrinos）的质量与味混合矩阵元，发现了一个全新且特殊的精确跷跷板方程解，并由此建立了一个家族分离的跷跷板场景（family-separated seesaw scenario），该场景提供了可检验的预言，包括轻中微子味振荡与重中微子衰变中CP破坏效应的直接关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规范跷跷板机制是中微子扇区最自然的标准模型扩展，但在精确求解跷跷板方程方面仍存在未解决的问题，需要找到更简洁、具有可检验预言能力的解析解。

Method: 通过解析求解精确跷跷板方程（exact seesaw equation），发现了一个特殊解 $m^{}_i/M^{}_i = - R^2_{αi}/U^2_{αi}$，其中 $i$ 表示家族指标，$α$ 表示味指标，从而建立了家族分离的跷跷板场景。

Result: 得到了一个家族分离的跷跷板场景，该场景在原始跷跷板参数与活跃自由度之间建立了简单关系，并给出了可检验的预言，即轻中微子味振荡中的CP破坏效应与重马约拉纳中微子衰变中的CP破坏效应之间存在直接关联。

Conclusion: 所提出的家族分离跷跷板场景为理解中微子质量与混合提供了一种全新的解析路径，并且其预言的CP破坏关联性有望被未来的实验所检验。

Abstract: Given the canonical seesaw mechanism as a most natural extension of the standard model in its neutrino sector, we find out a special but brand new solution to the exact seesaw equation: $m^{}_i/M^{}_i = - R^2_{αi}/U^2_{αi}$ for the masses and flavor mixing matrix elements of light and heavy Majorana neutrinos of the $i$-th family (for $i = 1, 2, 3$ and $α= e, μ, τ$). This family-separated seesaw scenario allows us to establish simple relations between the original seesaw parameters and the active degrees of freedom, and thus offers some testable predictions such as a direct correlation between the CP-violating effects in light neutrino flavor oscillations and heavy Majorana neutrino decays.

</details>


### [132] [Polarization dependence of the $φ$ meson mass from finite-temperature QCD sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27347)
*Hidefumi Matsuda,Philipp Gubler,Koichi Hattori*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文利用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rules）研究了有限温度和有限动量下φ介子的性质，发现横模和纵模的质量随动量增加而上升，且横纵分裂（transverse-longitudinal splitting）随温度和自旋相关热凝聚（spin-dependent thermal condensates）增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究介质效应对φ介子性质的影响，特别是有限温度与有限动量下洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）的破缺如何引发横模与纵模的不同修正。

Method: 采用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rules）在有限温度和有限动量框架下分析φ介子，并纳入维数四的自旋相关热凝聚（spin-dependent thermal condensates）贡献。

Result: 随着动量增加，横模与纵模的质量均上升，并出现明显的横纵分裂（transverse-longitudinal splitting）；该分裂随温度升高而增大，且主要源于维数四的自旋相关热凝聚。

Conclusion: 介质中洛伦兹不变性破缺导致φ介子横模与纵模在有限动量下产生不同的质量修正，其中自旋相关的维数四热凝聚是横纵分裂的主要来源。

Abstract: We study the $φ$ meson at finite temperature and finite momentum using QCD sum rules. The presence of medium breaks the Lorentz invariance, and induces distinct in-medium modifications of the transverse and longitudinal modes at finite momentum. We find that, with increasing momentum, the masses of both modes increase and a clear transverse--longitudinal splitting develops. The splitting is found to grow with temperature and to be mainly generated by the dimension-four spin-dependent thermal condensates.

</details>


### [133] [Looking for Condensed Gluons: A Cross-Scale Journey from the Deep Structure of Protons to High-Energy Cosmic Rays -- A Mini-Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27018)
*Wei Zhu,Yu-Chen Tang,Ye-Yin Zhao,Bo Yang,Yu-Chen Xiong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了质子内部夸克-胶子动力学与宇宙高能辐射现象可通过胶子凝聚（gluon condensation, GC）直接关联。论文系统回顾了GC研究的三个关键方面：基于结构对称性的Zhu-Shen-Ruan (ZSR)非线性演化方程及其与DGLAP、BFKL、GLR-MQ-ZRS方程的自洽联系；方程中的混沌解与遮蔽-反遮蔽协同效应驱动胶子在临界动量附近聚集形成新型高密度强相互作用物质；微观结构的这种变化在高能宇宙伽马射线谱中表现为破缺幂律特征，为天体物理源的强子机制提供新见解。GC不仅涉及极端条件下量子色动力学的新奇行为，还可能成为利用宇宙射线信号探测质子深层结构的重要窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在弥合质子内部夸克-胶子动力学与宇宙高能辐射现象这两个传统上被视为完全独立的领域之间的鸿沟，证明胶子凝聚（GC）可作为连接二者的直接桥梁。

Method: 论文采用综述方法，聚焦GC研究的三个关键方面：首先介绍基于结构对称性导出的ZSR非线性演化方程，及其与DGLAP、BFKL、GLR-MQ-ZRS等方程的关联；其次分析该方程的混沌解与遮蔽-反遮蔽协同效应；最后探讨微观结构变化在高能宇宙伽马射线谱中的可观测表现。

Result: ZSR方程与已有量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）演化方程自洽关联；混沌解与遮蔽-反遮蔽协同效应可驱动胶子在临界动量附近聚集，形成新型高密度强相互作用物质；微观结构变化在高能宇宙伽马射线谱中表现为破缺幂律（broken-power-law）特征。

Conclusion: GC不仅涉及极端条件下的QCD新奇行为，还可能是利用宇宙射线信号探测质子深层结构的关键窗口。若该图像得到更高精度伽马射线观测、强子碰撞实验及相关理论研究的验证，高能伽马射线谱的某些特征需在强子动力学更深背景下重新审视；同时GC也可能为核物理中的π介子凝聚（pion condensation）乃至凝聚态物理研究提供新的切入点。

Abstract: Quark-gluon dynamics within protons and high-energy radiation phenomena in the universe are typically regarded as two entirely distinct fields. This paper aims to demonstrate that gluon condensation (GC) may serve as a direct bridge between these two fields. We review three key aspects of GC research: first, the Zhu-Shen-Ruan (ZSR) equation, as a nonlinear evolution equation based on structural symmetry, exhibits self-consistent connections with the DGLAP, BFKL and GLR-MQ-ZRS equations, providing a theoretical foundation for the generation of GC; second, the chaotic solutions and the shadowing-antishadowing synergy inherent in this equation can drive gluons to aggregate near the critical momentum, thereby forming a novel type of high-density, strongly interacting matter; third, these changes in microstructure manifest themselves as a broken-power-law feature in high-energy cosmic gamma-ray spectra, thereby offering new insights into the hadronic scenarios underlying certain astrophysical sources. Consequently, GC not only concerns the novel behaviour of quantum chromodynamics under extreme conditions but may also serve as a vital window for probing the deep structure of protons using cosmic-ray signals. With the advancement of higher-precision gamma-ray observations, hadron collision experiments and related theoretical research, the physical picture of GC and its observational criteria are expected to undergo more rigorous testing. Should this picture be confirmed, certain features in the high-energy gamma-ray spectrum will need to be re-examined within the deeper context of hadronic dynamics; simultaneously, GC may also provide a new entry point for research into pion condensation in nuclear physics and even condensed matter physics. Consequently, the significance of the search for GC extends beyond the model itself, reaching into multiple fields of natural science.

</details>

### [134] [On radiation from hyperbolic motion, behavior of electromagnetic fields, and coordinate transformations at infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26139)
*E. T. Akhmedov,M. N. Milovanova*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该论文明确指出，均匀加速电荷的辐射逃逸出林德勒楔（Rindler wedge），而在林德勒楔内部，无论是在闵可夫斯基坐标系（Minkowski frame）还是林德勒坐标系（Rindler frame）中，都没有通量到达无穷远。尽管这两个坐标系之间的变换在无穷远处并不平凡，这一结论仍然成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清均匀加速电荷的辐射是否存在于林德勒楔内部这一长期争议，并解决两种坐标系（闵可夫斯基与林德勒）在无穷远处对辐射通量描述的不一致问题。

Method: 通过显式计算，分别在闵可夫斯基坐标系和林德勒坐标系下分析均匀加速电荷产生的辐射通量（flux）在无穷远处的行为，并考察两种坐标系之间的坐标变换在无穷远处的非平凡性质。

Result: 辐射仅出现在林德勒楔外部；在林德勒楔内部，两种坐标系下均不存在到达无穷远的辐射通量。坐标变换在无穷远处的非平凡性并不影响这一物理结论。

Conclusion: 均匀加速电荷的辐射被限制在林德勒楔之外，林德勒楔内部的观测者无法接收到该辐射，且这一结论在两个不同坐标系下是一致的。

Abstract: We show explicitly that radiation from a uniformly accelerating charge escapes outside Rindler wedge, while within Rindler wedge there is no flux through infinity, neither in the Minkowski frame nor in the Rindler frame. This remains true despite the fact that the coordinate transformation between the Rindler and Minkowski frames is not trivial at infinity.

</details>

### [135] [x-periodic Quasi One Dimensional Anomalous (Rogue) Waves in Multidimensional Nonlinear Schrödinger Equations: Fission, Fusion, and Recurrence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26961)
*Francesco Coppini,Paolo Maria Santini*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本论文研究了多维聚焦非线性薛定谔（MNLS）方程在准一维（Q1D）区域中异常波（AWs）的调制不稳定性（MI）的首次非线性阶段及其回复动力学。研究表明，首次非线性阶段具有普适性，由Akhmediev呼吸子的绝热形变描述；而回复动力学在不同模型间存在显著差异，并可通过有限间隙微扰理论进行解析描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作中已证明Q1D区域中MNLS方程调制不稳定的首次非线性阶段具有普适性，本文进一步关注x周期异常波（AWs）的回复（recurrence）动力学，探究其在不同多维非线性薛定谔模型中的行为差异。

Method: 利用近期发展的异常波有限间隙微扰理论（finite gap perturbation theory of NLS AWs）对Q1D区域中的AWs回复动力学进行解析和定量描述，并将解析结果与数值模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 尽管MI首次非线性阶段对所有MNLS方程本质上是普适的，但回复动力学在不同模型间表现出显著的O(1)差异；后续非线性阶段则展现出愈发复杂的裂变与聚变过程组合，形成日益丰富的动力学编排。

Conclusion: 鉴于所研究MNLS方程的物理相关性以及所讨论过程的普适性，这些现象有望在水波、非线性光学、等离子体物理、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚等多个物理领域中被观测到。

Abstract: In a recent work we studied the first nonlinear stage of modulation instability (NLSMI) of x-periodic anomalous (rogue, freak, extreme) waves (AWs) of physically relevant multidimensional (generalizations of the focusing) nonlinear Schrödinger (MNLS) equation, like the non integrable elliptic and hyperbolic nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS) equations in d+1 dimensions, d = 2, 3, in the quasi one dimensional (Q1D) regime in which the wavelength in the direction of propagation x is small with respect to the wavelengths in the transversal directions. We showed that, at leading order, the first NLSMI is universal, independent of the particular MNLS model, and described by suitable adiabatic deformations of the quasi-homoclinic Akhmediev breather solution of NLS, in excellent agreement with numerical simulations. In the present work we focus on the recurrence of x-periodic AWs in the Q1D regime. We show that, although the first nonlinear stage of MI is essentially universal for all MNLS equations, the recurrence dynamics exhibit significant O(1) differences among different models. Moreover, successive nonlinear stages generally display increasingly complex combinations of fission and fusion processes, leading to progressively richer dynamical choreographies. Since MNLS equations in the Q1D regime can be viewed as multidimensional perturbations of the integrable NLS equation, we use the recently developed finite gap perturbation theory of NLS AWs to give an analytic and quantitative description of the recurrence of Q1D AWs, in excellent agreement with numerical simulations. Due to the physical relevance of the MNLS equations considered in this work, and due to the universality of the processes discussed in this paper, it is plausible that they be observable in many fields of physics, like water waves, nonlinear optics, plasma physics, Bose-Einstein condensates, etc . . .

</details>

# astro-ph.GA [[Back]](#toc)

### [136] [For modified gravity, it's the LITTLE THINGS that matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27217)
*Geoff Beck*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用LITTLE THINGS和SPARC两个矮星系样本，通过哈密顿蒙特卡洛采样和ELPD模型比较，发现晕核模型以>4σ置信度优于MOND，但大多证据来自少数星系，不能最终否定MOND。MOND的外部场效应证据较弱，多数SPARC星系仍与通用MOND标度兼容。MOG的通用旋转曲线模型被强烈否定（>8σ）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矮星系长期以来被视为暗物质模型的重要检验场所，例如尖点-核问题（cusp-core problem）在此最为显著。本文旨在检验MOND（Modified Newtonian Dynamics）与暗物质晕模型在矮星系中的偏好程度，并评估MOND的“外部场效应”（external field effect）及MOG（Modified Gravity）通用旋转曲线模型的适用性。

Method: 选取两个矮星系样本：LITTLE THINGS和SPARC中的矮星系。采用哈密顿蒙特卡洛（Hamiltonian Monte Carlo）采样方法进行参数推断，并通过ELPD（expected log pointwise predictive density）差异进行稳健的模型比较。

Result: 晕核模型（cored halo model）以>4σ置信度优于MOND，但这一偏好主要来自19个SPARC星系中的7个和18个LITTLE THINGS星系中的11个，且少数偏好极为显著。仅有一个星系偏好MOND而非晕核模型。MOND外部场效应的存在证据较弱。多数SPARC星系仍与通用MOND标度兼容。LITTLE THINGS中自由MOND模型相对于通用值有~8σ偏好，但物理意义存疑。MOG的通用旋转曲线模型在两个样本的所有星系中以>8σ置信度被否定。

Conclusion: 矮星系数据对晕核模型存在显著统计偏好，但对MOND的否定并非结论性；MOND的外部场效应未获有力支持；而MOG的通用旋转曲线模型被强烈排除。

Abstract: Dwarf galaxies have long been recognised as important testing grounds for models of dark matter. For instance, it is here where the cusp-core problem is most apparent. In this work we select two dwarf galaxy samples: LITTLE THINGS and dwarf galaxies in SPARC. We use these to examine whether there are preferences for MOND or dark matter halos in these objects. Notably, our analysis employs the latest developments in Hamiltonian Monte Carlo sampling methodology and robust model comparison via ELPD differences. Our findings suggest a $>4σ$ preference for cored halo models over MOND. However, this relies on significant preferences from 7 out of 19 SPARC galaxies and 11 of 18 from LITTLE THINGS (few of which are overwhelming). It is notable that only a single galaxy prefers MOND over a cored halo. Thus, this evidence is suggestive, but does not conclusively decide against MOND. We also test for evidence of a MOND external field effect, and find weak evidence against its presence. Despite these statistical preferences, most SPARC galaxies remain compatible with a universal MOND scale. In LITTLE THINGS, a free MOND model is preferred to a universal value at $\sim 8σ$, but this is of doubtful physical significance. For MOG, the story is different, here we find $\gtrsim 8σ$ preferences for all halos (or MOND) against universal MOG models with significant exclusions in individual galaxies across both samples. Thus, a proposed universal rotation curve model derived from MOG is quite strongly disfavoured.

</details>

### [137] [Generalized Minkowski Theorem for Tetrahedra in ${\rm dS}^3$ and ${\rm AdS}^3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26410)
*Hongguang Liu,Qiaoyin Pan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在常曲率洛伦兹空间 dS³ 和 AdS³ 中，针对广义四面体证明了闵可夫斯基定理（Minkowski theorem）的霍尔诺米取值（holonomy-valued）类洛伦兹类比，通过四个非平凡的 SO⁺(1,2) 霍尔诺米（等价于 SL(2,ℝ) 自旋提升）确定内蕴面法向量、二面角 Gram 矩阵 G 及定向三重积，在闭包、非退化及外凸分支条件下重建唯一的严格凸四面体，并讨论了极性对偶投影四面体及不同扇区与欧几里得情况的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典闵可夫斯基定理（关于凸多面体由其面面积和外法向量唯一确定）推广到常曲率洛伦兹空间（de Sitter 空间 dS³ 和反 de Sitter 空间 AdS³）中，建立基于霍尔诺米取值的重建定理。

Method: 利用四个基于点的 SO⁺(1,2) 霍尔诺米（holonomy）或其 SL(2,ℝ) 自旋提升（spin lift）作为输入数据，定义内蕴面法向量（intrinsic face normals）、二面角 Gram 矩阵 G（dihedral Gram matrix）及内蕴面法向量的定向三重积（oriented triple products）；在闭包（closure）、非退化（nondegeneracy）和外凸分支条件（outward convex branch condition）下，通过 det G 的符号区分 dS 或 AdS 模型，重建唯一的严格凸四面体（strictly convex tetrahedron）（至多相差一个整体等距）。

Result: 重建的四面体的基于点列维-奇维塔面霍尔诺米（based Levi-Civita face holonomy）正好等于预设的霍尔诺米；外蕴面法向量（extrinsic face normals）定义了极性对偶投影四面体（polar-dual projective tetrahedron）；在全零类 AdS 扇区（all-null AdS sector）中得到理想对偶四面体（ideal dual tetrahedra），在全类时 AdS 扇区（all-timelike AdS sector）中得到超理想对偶四面体（hyperideal dual tetrahedra）；在全类空扇区（all-spacelike sector）中，更换为 SU(2) 实形式可恢复欧几里得球面与双曲四面体的重建定理。

Conclusion: 成功建立了常曲率洛伦兹空间中四面体的闵可夫斯基定理的霍尔诺米形式，统一了洛伦兹几何与欧几里得几何中四面体重建问题的框架，并揭示了不同因果扇区（causal sector）与对偶四面体几何之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We formulate and prove a constant-curvature, holonomy-valued Lorentzian analogue of Minkowski theorem for generalized tetrahedra in the constant-curvature Lorentzian spaces ${\rm dS}^3$ and ${\rm AdS}^3$. Four non-trivial based ${\rm SO}^+(1,2)$ holonomies, or equivalently ${\rm SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$ spin lifts, determine intrinsic face normals, a dihedral Gram matrix $G$, and oriented triple products of intrinsic face normals. Under closure, nondegeneracy, and the outward convex branch condition, these data reconstruct a unique strictly convex tetrahedron up to ambient isometry. The sign of $\det G$ selects the de Sitter or anti-de Sitter model, and the prescribed holonomies are exactly the based Levi-Civita face holonomies of the reconstructed tetrahedron. The extrinsic face normals also define a polar-dual projective tetrahedron. In particular, the all-null AdS sector gives ideal dual tetrahedra, and the all-timelike AdS sector gives hyperideal dual tetrahedra. In the all-spacelike sector, changing to ${\rm SU}(2)$ real form recovers the reconstruction theorem for Euclidean spherical and hyperbolic tetrahedra.

</details>


### [138] [Laplace's law for sharp and diffuse interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26773)
*Sergey L. Gavrilyuk,Henri Gouin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过虚功原理（principle of virtual work）推导包含界面的流体平衡方程，对比了扩散界面（diffuse interface）与尖锐界面（sharp interface）两种模型，并建立了表面张力系数（surface tension coefficient）与模型参数之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液体-蒸汽界面（liquid-vapor interface）的建模在物理和工程中具有重要意义，但扩散界面与尖锐界面两种方法在数学表示和物理假设上存在差异，需要系统比较以明确二者的联系。

Method: 基于虚功原理（principle of virtual work）在包含界面的域中推导流体平衡方程；扩散界面模型中的表面张力系数依赖于跨界面的密度分布（density profile），而尖锐界面模型将液-蒸汽层表示为几何曲面，其比能（specific energy）为曲面上的狄拉克δ函数（Dirac delta function）。

Result: 给出了扩散界面与尖锐界面两种方法之间的定量关系，具体关联了表面张力系数与模型参数。

Conclusion: 扩散界面与尖锐界面模型在描述液-蒸汽界面时可通过确定的参数关系相互连接，为跨尺度界面建模提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study both diffuse and sharp liquid-vapor interfaces. The equilibrium equation of fluids is derived by using the principle of virtual work in a domain including the interfaces. For diffuse interfaces, the surface tension coefficient depends on the density profile across the interface. For sharp interfaces, the liquid-vapor layer is mathematically represented by a geometric surface and its specific energy is a Dirac delta function at the surface. We compare the both approaches and find relations between the surface tension coefficient and parameters of the models.

</details>


### [139] [Partial theta-series and branching rules for the $\sl(3)$ parabolic Verma modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26946)
*Dotsenko Egor*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究 $\sl(3)$ Casimir 平坦联络（flat connection）在根超平面（root hyperplane）周围的单值性（monodromy），通过推导关于根 $\sl(2)$ 子代数的分支规则（branching rules）计算根单值算子在抛物线 Verma 模（parabolic Verma modules）上的迹（traces），并证明这些迹是特殊类型的部分 theta 函数（partial theta functions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在计算 $\sl(3)$ Casimir 平坦联络的根单值算子（root monodromy operators）在抛物线 Verma 模上的迹，从而揭示该联络在根超平面附近的单值性结构。

Method: 推导关于相应根 $\sl(2)$ 子代数（root $\sl(2)$ subalgebras）的分支规则，并利用这些规则计算作用于抛物线 Verma 模的根单值算子的迹。

Result: 证明了根单值算子的迹是特殊类型的部分 theta 函数。

Conclusion: 根单值算子的迹可以表示为特殊的部分 theta 函数，这为 $\sl(3)$ Casimir 平坦联络的单值性提供了显式描述。

Abstract: The monodromy of the $\sl(3)$ Casimir flat connection around root hyperplanes is studied. For the computation of the traces of the root monodromy operators, acting on the parabolic Verma modules, we deduce branching rules w.r.t. the corresponding root $\sl(2)$ subalgebras. We show that the traces of the monodromy operators are partial theta functions of special type.

</details>


### [140] [Bounds on relative modular Hamiltonians in general QFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27198)
*Adriano Chialastri,Christoph Minz,Ko Sanders*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用代数量子场论（algebraic QFT）的局域性（locality）性质，通过参考态的模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian）来估计两量子态之间的相对模哈密顿量（relative modular Hamiltonian）和相对熵（relative entropy），并对CCR系统的相干态（coherent states）进行了验证，证明该方法在无法精确计算相对模哈密顿量的情况下仍能给出有效估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对熵是量子信息论和量子场论中的核心概念，但其计算需要处理相对模哈密顿量，而后者通常极难显式计算。本文旨在发展一种无需精确计算即可估计相对模哈密顿量和相对熵的方法。

Method: 利用一般代数量子场论的局域性性质，以上界或下界形式，将区域$V_2$的代数的相对模哈密顿量用参考态$\hatω$在更大区域$V_3$或更小区域$V_1$上的模哈密顿量来估计。估计方案的可适用性与Sorkin悖论意义上的超光速信号传递（superluminal signalling）相关联。

Result: 对于CCR系统的相干态（特别关注自由标量场），该估计方法即使在相对模哈密顿量无法精确计算时仍然适用。对于足够规则的激发，通过压缩（squeezing）可恢复精确结果。对于无质量场，双锥区域（double cone regions）也建立了类似结果。

Conclusion: 该方法为无法精确计算相对模哈密顿量的情形提供了相对熵公式的独立证明，且结果表明该估计并未丢失过多信息。

Abstract: The relative entropy between two states is a key concept in quantum information theory and quantum field theory. In the setting of quantum field theory, its computation requires the handling of relative modular Hamiltonians, which are typically very difficult to compute explicitly. In this paper, we exploit locality properties of general algebraic QFTs to estimate relative modular Hamiltonians between two states, $ω$ and $\tildeω$, and hence also their relative entropy, in terms of the modular Hamiltonian of a reference state $\hatω$, which might be better understood. For suitable pairs of states we can estimate the relative modular Hamiltonian for the algebra of a region $V_2$ from above, resp. from below, in terms of the modular Hamiltonian of $\hatω$ on a larger region $V_3$, resp. a smaller region $V_1$.
  Pairs of states and choices of regions which are susceptible to our scheme are related to the presence of superluminal signalling in the sense of Sorkin's paradox. If $ω=\hatω$, then there exists a unitary that maps $ω$ to $\tildeω$ on $V_3$ and that does not allow superluminal signalling from the spacelike complement $V_3'$ to $V_2$, resp. from $V_1$ to $V_2'$, if our upper, resp. lower, bound applies.
  To investigate the strength of our estimates we consider coherent states for CCR systems, focussing particularly on free scalar fields. Our estimates apply even if the relative modular Hamiltonian cannot be computed exactly. For sufficiently regular excitations we recover an exact result by squeezing. Our method thus yields an independent proof for the relative entropy formula in cases where the relative modular Hamiltonian cannot be computed exactly. For massless fields we establish the analogous result also for double cone regions. These results indicate that our estimates do not lose too much information.

</details>

### [141] [Practical tensor calculus on embedded submanifolds of arbitrary codimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27260)
*Vladimir Yushutin*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种完全外蕴（extrinsic）、无需参数化的张量微积分（tensor calculus）框架，适用于任意维度和余维数（codimension）的、带边界的嵌入子流形（embedded submanifolds），并展示了其在不可压缩欧拉流、柯西应力（Cauchy stress）分析以及演化子流形上张量场的物质导数（material derivative）等方面的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有张量微积分在嵌入子流形上的处理通常依赖局部参数化，缺乏一种完全外蕴、分量自由（component-free）且具有算法递归性的统一框架，不利于计算和理论分析。

Method: 采用完全外蕴且免参数化的方法，通过张量的特殊行表示（row representation）实现算法递归性，该表示类似于完全树（complete trees）的递归数据结构；覆盖了切向投影（tangential projection）、外蕴导数（extrinsic derivative）、协变导数（covariant derivative）、外蕴斯托克斯公式（extrinsic Stokes' formula）以及拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子（Laplace-Beltrami operator）等核心概念。

Result: 推导了黎曼流形上不可压缩欧拉流的新外蕴守恒律——零外蕴动量原理（principle of vanishing extrinsic momentum）；论证了角动量守恒（conservation of angular momentum）仅在应力张量被限制作用于切向取向时才蕴含其切向性与对称性；针对演化子流形给出了任意阶张量场的外蕴物质导数表达式以及张量狄利克雷能量（tensorial Dirichlet energy）的变化率。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一套可直接用于数学建模、几何感知偏微分方程（geometry-aware PDE）分析以及嵌入子流形上数值方法的实用记号和工具。

Abstract: We present a fully extrinsic, parametrization-free variant of tensor calculus on embedded, possibly evolving, submanifolds with boundary in arbitrary dimension and codimension. The proposed approach is component-free and, for general rank tensors, covers fundamental concepts such as tangential projection, extrinsic and covariant derivatives, the extrinsic Stokes' formula, and the Laplace-Beltrami operator. The distinctive features of the developed framework are its algorithmic recursivity and the transparency provided by the special row representation of tensors reminiscent of the recursive data structure of complete trees. Consequently, the suggested tensor calculus is amenable to computations and theoretical analysis, and the latter is demonstrated for general dimension and codimension through three standalone applications. First, we derive a new extrinsic conservation law, namely the principle of vanishing extrinsic momentum, for incompressible Euler flows on Riemannian manifolds. Second, we revisit the concept of Cauchy stress on embedded submanifolds with positive codimension and argue that the conservation of angular momentum implies tangentiality and symmetry of the stress tensors only when they are restricted to act on tangential orientations. Third, for evolving submanifolds, we introduce the material derivative of tensor fields of general rank in an extrinsic manner and derive an expression for the rate of change of the associated tensorial Dirichlet energy. The paper provides a practical notation and tools that are immediately usable in mathematical modeling, analysis of geometry-aware PDEs and in numerical methods on embedded submanifolds.

</details>


### [142] [The $σ$-inverse mean curvature flow and the generalized Penrose conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26504)
*Conghan Dong*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在初始数据集满足主能量条件且外曲率与度量成比例的特殊情形下，证明了广义彭罗斯猜想：最外层广义表观视界的每个连通分量的面积不超过16πm²。该方法基于一种称为σ-逆平均曲率流的新几何流及一个可能具有独立意义的新单调性公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义彭罗斯猜想（generalized Penrose conjecture）断言，在满足主能量条件（dominant energy condition）的完全渐近平坦初始数据集$(M^3, g, \mathbf{k})$中，最外层广义表观视界（outermost generalized apparent horizon）$N$的面积$|N|$受限于$16\pi m^2$，其中$m$为ADM质量（ADM mass）。该猜想是广义相对论中质量与黑洞面积关系的重要几何不等式，本文旨在证明该不等式在$\mathbf{k}$与$g$成比例这一特殊情形下对每个连通分量成立。

Method: 本文提出了一种新的几何流——σ-逆平均曲率流（σ-inverse mean curvature flow），并结合一个全新的单调性公式（monotonicity formula）来建立所需的不等式。该方法针对外曲率（extrinsic curvature）$\mathbf{k}$与度量$g$成比例的特殊情形进行构造和分析。

Result: 在$\mathbf{k}$与$g$成比例的特殊情况下，本文为最外层广义表观视界$N$的每个连通分量建立了面积不等式$|N| \leq 16\pi m^2$，从而验证了广义彭罗斯猜想在该情形下的成立。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入σ-逆平均曲率流及相关单调性公式，在特殊情形下证明了广义彭罗斯猜想。该单调性公式可能具有独立的研究价值，为后续在更一般条件下研究该猜想提供了潜在工具。

Abstract: Let $(M^3, g, \mathbf{k})$ be a complete asymptotically flat initial data set satisfying the dominant energy condition, and let $m$ denote its ADM mass. The generalized Penrose conjecture asserts that the area of an outermost generalized apparent horizon $N\subset M$ satisfies $|N| \leq 16 πm^2$. In this paper, we establish this inequality for each connected component of $N$ in the special case where $\mathbf{k}$ is proportional to the metric $g$. Our approach is based on a new geometric evolution, which we call the $σ$-inverse mean curvature flow, together with a novel monotonicity formula that may be of independent interest.

</details>

### [143] [Spectral property for the 2D Zakharov-Kuznetsov equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27341)
*Justin Holmer,Svetlana Roudenko*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文分析了二维Zakharov-Kuznetsov（ZK）方程中virial算子的谱性质，这是建立孤立波爆破或渐近稳定性的关键要素，并将该问题简化为仅需数值验证内积符号和特定特征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ZK方程是等离子体物理中三维模型的简化，也是著名Korteweg-de Vries（KdV）方程的高维推广。孤立波在ZK方程中的稳定性或修正ZK（KdV型）方程中的稳定爆破问题具有重要物理意义，而virial算子及其谱性质是分析这些问题的核心要素。

Method: 本文采用解析方法研究了virial算子的谱性质，将原本复杂的分析问题简化为仅需数值验证一些内积（inner product）的符号和某些特征值（eigenvalue）的问题。

Result: 找到了二维ZK方程中virial算子的一种谱性质，该性质是建立高维问题中孤立波爆破或渐近稳定性的关键要素。

Conclusion: 通过将稳定性和爆破分析归结为数值可验证的条件（内积符号和特征值），为后续高维ZK型方程中孤立波的爆破与稳定性研究提供了简化且可行的分析框架。

Abstract: We discuss a spectral property for the virial operator of the 2D Zakharov-Kuznetsov (ZK) equation. This is a crucial ingredient to establish blow-up or asymptotic stability of solitary waves in higher-dimensional problems.
  This model in 3D setting was originally introduced by Zakharov and Kuznetsov in plasma physics, and is also a higher-dimensional generalization of the well-known Korteweg-de Vries (KdV) equation. The problem of stability of solitary waves in ZK equation or stable blow-up in modified ZK (or KdV-type) equation is an important physical question, for which virial operators and their spectral properties are the essential elements of the analysis. In this paper we investigate this problem analytically and reduce it to verifying numerically only some signs of inner products and certain eigenvalues.

</details>

### [144] [Antisymmetric spontaneous resistivity anisotropy due to hard-axis collapse in polycrystalline Co thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27099)
*Y. Fernandes,J. Geshev,A. M. H. de Andrade,A. D. C. Viegas*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文研究了多晶钴（Co）薄膜中与磁化难轴坍缩（magnetization hard-axis collapse）相关的磁电阻（magnetoresistance）现象，发现平面霍尔电阻（planar Hall resistance）在室温下存在多个稳定且可重复的剩余态（remanent states），并提出基于剩余平面霍尔效应（remanent planar Hall effect）的低成本自旋电子学（spintronic）存储与传感平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该现象（磁化难轴坍缩导致的剩余电阻态）在现有文献中尚未被充分探索，因此作者从应用物理学（applied-physics）角度对其潜在意义进行了初步研究。

Method: 在生长于硅（Si）衬底上的多晶钴（Co）薄膜中进行输运（transport）测量，通过施加特定取向的外磁场并观察面内纵向（in-plane longitudinal）和横向（transverse）电压响应，分析难轴区域磁场撤去后稳定的非均匀磁构型（non-uniform magnetic configurations）所产生的电阻态。

Result: 在特定外磁场取向下，系统展现出不同的剩余电阻（remanent resistance）水平；平面霍尔电阻在室温下表现出至少三个可区分且可重现的剩余态，可用于信息存储。

Conclusion: 在多晶钴薄膜中观察到的剩余平面霍尔效应（remanent planar Hall effect）为实现简单、低成本的自旋电子学存储与传感器件提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate magnetoresistance phenomena associated with the magnetization hard-axis collapse in polycrystalline Co thin films. Transport measurements reveal that, for specific orientations of the applied magnetic field, the system exhibits distinct remanent resistance levels in both the in-plane longitudinal and transverse voltage responses. In particular, the planar Hall resistance shows multiple stable and reproducible levels at room temperature, enabling the identification of at least three remanent states that can be distinguished and used for information storage. These resistance levels originate from non-uniform magnetic configurations stabilized after the application and removal of the external magnetic field in the hard-axis region. Since this phenomenon remains largely unexplored, we present an incipient study addressing its potential implications from an applied-physics perspective. The observation of such behavior in polycrystalline Co thin films grown on Si substrates suggests a simple and low-cost platform for spintronic memory and sensing devices based on the remanent planar Hall effect.

</details>


### [145] [Phase-Topology Classification of Memristor Hysteresis Loops via Self-Crossings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27342)
*Ovidiu-Zeno Lipan,Eric Neuhaus,Rafael Schio Wengenroth Silva,Soumen Pradhan,Fabian Hartmann,Leonardo K. Castelano,Ana Luiza Costa Silva,Sven Höfling,Victor Lopez-Richard*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一个拓扑与代数框架，将忆阻器（memristor）迟滞回线（hysteresis loop）的横向自交点数（transverse self-intersection number）视为一个受拓扑保护的整数不变量（integer-valued invariant），并利用微分拓扑、奇点理论（singularity theory）和尖点突变（cusp catastrophe）方法对六维参数空间进行分层，从而完整分类了多瓣迟滞行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管忆阻器件已在非易失性存储（non-volatile memory）和神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）中取得突破，但其迟滞回线的几何结构——特别是多个自交点的出现与鲁棒性——尚缺乏深入理解。

Method: 采用微分拓扑（differential topology）、奇点理论（singularity theory）和尖点突变（cusp catastrophe）工具，利用判别式（discriminant）和结式（resultant）对六维参数空间进行分层，将参数空间划分为由可显式计算的花苞面（catastrophe surfaces）分隔的结构稳定区域。

Result: 证明了交叉数（crossing number）在连续形变下保持严格不变，仅在自切点（self-tangencies）或尖点奇异性（cusp singularities）处发生变化，从而提供了对所有多瓣迟滞行为的完整分类。

Conclusion: 该研究将器件物理学（device physics）与现代奇点理论（singularity theory）联系起来，为在下一代电子器件和类脑硬件（brain-inspired hardware）中利用高阶记忆效应提供了清晰的路线图。

Abstract: Memristive devices have revolutionized non-volatile memory and neuromorphic computing, yet the geometry of their hysteresis loops -- in particular, the occurrence and robustness of multiple self-crossings -- remains poorly understood. Here we introduce a topological and algebraic framework that treats the number of transverse self-intersections of a memristor hysteresis loop as a robust integer-valued invariant. Drawing on differential topology, singularity theory, and cusp catastrophe, we employ discriminants and resultants to stratify the six-dimensional parameter space. This approach partitions the parameter space into structurally stable regions separated by explicitly computable catastrophe surfaces. We demonstrate that the crossing number remains strictly invariant under continuous deformations and changes only at self-tangencies or cusp singularities, thereby providing a complete classification of all multi-lobed hysteresis behaviors. These insights bridge device physics with modern singularity theory and suggest a clear roadmap for exploiting higher-order memory effects in next-generation electronics and brain-inspired hardware.

### [146] [Sampling Data with Chains of Forward-Backward Diffusion Steps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27006)
*Hyunmo Kang,Noam Itzhak Levi,Corinna Elena Wegner,Daniel J. Korchinski,Matthieu Wyart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出U-turn链——一种通过迭代扩散模型的前向-后向步骤构建的马尔可夫链，结合Metropolis-Hastings校正从能量修正目标中采样。研究表明，最小U-turn动力学在合成语言中经历了一个由数据流形碎片化驱动的遍历性破缺相变，并在自然语言和自然图像上验证了相关预测，揭示了高层特征弛豫缓慢及层序反转等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从学习到的高维分布中采样是一个基础性计算问题。现有扩散模型采样方法在保持数据流形结构方面存在局限，亟需一种既能保留流形约束又能保证采样正确性的方法。

Method: 提出U-turn链（U-turn chains）方法：通过迭代扩散模型的短前向-后向步骤构建马尔可夫链（Markov chain），每一步提出的移动保持在学到的数据流形（data manifold）上，并配合Metropolis-Hastings校正（Metropolis-Hastings correction）从能量修正目标（energy-modified targets）中采样。

Result: 对于合成语言，最小U-turn动力学（minimal U-turn dynamics）发生了由数据流形碎片化（fragmentation）驱动的遍历性破缺相变（ergodicity-breaking phase transition），在足够大的U-turn幅度下恢复遍历性。在非遍历区域，低层特征弛豫速度快于高层特征；该层序仅在足够大的U-turn幅度下发生反转。在自然语言和自然图像上，最小U-turn弛豫缓慢，尤其对于CNN或LLM深层表示近似的高层特征。层序反转仅在大噪声、混合效率高时出现，表现出强烈约束、弱混合局部动力学的特征。

Conclusion: 讨论了对扩散模型（diffusion models）采样的启示：在高度约束的数据流形中，局部动力学可能难以实现高效混合，需要足够大的扰动幅度才能恢复遍历性并加速高层特征弛豫。

Abstract: Sampling from learned high-dimensional distributions is a foundational computational problem. We introduce U-turn chains: Markov chains obtained by iterating short forward-backward steps of a diffusion model, in which each step proposes a move that remains on the learned data manifold and, paired with a Metropolis-Hastings correction, samples from energy-modified targets. For synthetic languages, we show that minimal U-turn dynamics undergoes an ergodicity-breaking phase transition driven by fragmentation of the data manifold; ergodicity is restored at larger U-turn magnitude. In the non-ergodic regime, low-level features relax faster than high-level ones, an ordering that inverts only at sufficiently large U-turn magnitude. We test these predictions on natural language and natural images. In both modalities, minimal U-turns relax slowly, especially for high-level features approximated by deep representations in CNNs or LLMs. The layer-ordering inversion appears only at large noise when mixing is efficient -- signatures consistent with strongly constrained, weakly mixing local dynamics. We discuss the implications of these results for sampling with diffusion models.

</details>

Method: 采用数值计算方法，基于最大匹配模型（Nussinov算法）生成具有最大碱基对数的RNA二级结构集合；使用18种天然小核RNA（small nuclear RNAs）作为实例；通过序列置换实验研究核苷酸组成固定下超度量程度的变化。

Conclusion: 核苷酸顺序（而非仅核苷酸组成）在塑造RNA二级结构的层级（超度量）性质中起关键作用。

Abstract: We present a numerical study of the ultrametric properties of the set of RNA secondary structures with the maximum number of base pairs (energetically degenerate minima) within the maximum matching model (Nussinov algorithm). Using 18 natural small nuclear RNAs as examples, we show that the degree of nontrivial ultrametricity varies widely. We consider the optimization problem for the degree of nontrivial ultrametricity of RNA secondary structures with the maximum number of base pairs under a fixed nucleotide composition. It is found that permuting the nucleotide sequence can strongly change the degree of ultrametricity, indicating the key role of nucleotide order in shaping the hierarchical properties of RNA secondary structures.

### [148] [Relationship between heat effects and shear modulus relaxation during structural relaxation of a telluride glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26767)
*G. V. Afonin,R. A. Konchakov,D. A. Chareev,S. A. Badmaeva,R. S. Khmyrov,A. N. Vasiliev,N. P. Kobelev,V. A. Khonik*

Result: 加热过程中的热效应与玻璃态和晶态的剪切模量及其温度导数之间存在定量关联，Eq.(1) 能够良好描述基于剪切模量弛豫数据输入的放热（exothermal）与吸热（endothermal）反应。

Conclusion: 该定量关系首次被应用于具有方向性原子键（directional interatomic bonding）的非金属玻璃，结果表明弛豫现象由弹性偶极子（elastic dipoles）——即对称性低于周围基质的原子构型——所主导。

Abstract: We performed parallel measurements of heat effects and shear modulus relaxation for glassy Te$_{75}$Ge$_{15}$Ga$_{10}$ taken as a representative of practically important non-metallic glasses with covalent bonding. It is shown that the heat effects occurring upon heating are quantitatively linked to the shear moduli in the glassy and crystalline states and their temperature derivatives as implied by Eq.(1), which was originally derived for metallic glasses. This relationship provides a good description of exo- and endothermal reactions using shear modulus relaxation data as an input. This is the first application of this approach to a non-metallic glass with directional interatomic bonding. The obtained results suggest that relaxation phenomena are governed by elastic dipoles -- atomic configurations with the symmetry lower than that of surrounding matrix.

### [149] [Locally resolved electronic textures of reconstruction domains in marginally twisted monolayer-bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26393)

TL;DR: 本研究利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy, STM）和扫描隧道谱（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy, STS），揭示单层-双层石墨烯界面在极小扭转角下会弛豫为三种不同堆叠（stacking）畴的网络，并观测到畴壁在不利堆叠节点周围的“旋绕”（twirling）现象，阐明了结构-性能关系对莫尔（moiré）现象的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验采用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）和扫描隧道谱（STS）技术，对极低旋转角度下的单层-双层石墨烯体系进行空间分辨的光谱映射，并将实验结果与计算得到的局域态密度（local density of states, LDOS）进行对比验证。

Result: 发现体系弛豫为三种不同堆叠畴的网络，每种畴具有独特的电子纹理（electronic texture）；观测到Bernal堆叠与菱面体（rhombohedral）堆叠畴之间隧穿特性的偏压依赖切换；测量到的光谱图显示出畴壁围绕能量上不利的AAB堆叠节点发生“旋绕”，且这一现象由面外变形（out-of-plane deformations）所促进。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了支撑莫尔驱动现象的基本结构-性能关系（structure-property relationships），为在范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures）中利用结构自由度开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Controlling the stacking and rotational registry of graphene layers provides a powerful handle on atomic-scale structural reconstructions that alter the electronic landscape at the nanoscale. In particular, this governs how massless and massive Dirac fermions coexist and interact at the monolayer-bilayer graphene interface. In the limit of marginal twist, the system reconstructs into domains of distinct vertical stacking order, introducing characteristic electronic properties and new electronic length scales, a regime that, despite its structural richness, remains largely unexplored. Here, using scanning tunnelling microscopy and spectroscopy, we demonstrate that at very low rotation angles the monolayer-bilayer graphene system relaxes into a network of three distinct stacking domains with individual electronic textures revealed through spatially resolved spectroscopic mapping and corroborated by computed local density of states. We report switching of the hierarchy of the tunnelling characteristics between Bernal and rhombohedral domains as a function of bias voltage. Furthermore, the measured spectroscopic maps exhibit theoretically anticipated domain wall 'twirling' around energetically unfavorable AAB stacking nodes, promoted by out-of-plane deformations. Our results shed light on fundamental structure-property relationships underpinning moiré-driven phenomena, opening new avenues for harnessing structural degrees of freedom in van der Waals heterostructures.

### [150] [Anharmonic Quantum Transport Analysis of Thermal Transport Anomalies in Ultrathin Silicon Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26529)
*Lokanath Patra,Mayur Pratap Singh,Satish Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过非平衡格林函数（NEGF）模拟结合密度泛函理论训练的神经演化势，揭示了超薄硅纳米线中热导率（k）随直径（d）先减后增的非单调依赖关系，并指出该行为在室温下源于Poiseuille-like流体动力学声子流，在低温下则源于声子谱的量子化受限效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维半导体中的热输运对纳米电子学、量子器件和热电器件的热管理至关重要。经典分子动力学（MD）方法在低温及强受限条件下存在局限性，无法准确描述超薄硅纳米线中热导率随直径的非单调变化。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's function, NEGF）模拟，并融合密度泛函理论（DFT）训练的神经演化势（neuroevolution potentials），实现全量子力学视角下的热输运计算。

Result: 对于[001]和[110]取向的硅纳米线，热导率（k）随直径（d）减小至临界值d_c（分别为6.24 nm和5.50 nm）后，再随d增大；该行为在10–300 K范围内均成立。室温下，受限区域中动量守恒的正常散射主导，引发Poiseuille-like流体动力学声子流；低温下，径向受限使声子谱量子化，仅低频声子（<2 THz）通过准弹道传播贡献热输运。

Conclusion: 与经典MD相比，NEGF框架在低温下（如10 K）具有定量准确性，克服了经典MD因波尔兹曼统计过激发高频振动、忽略量子抑制以及高估强受限纳米线热导率等问题。

Abstract: Thermal transport in low-dimensional semiconductors is crucial for advancing thermal management in nanoelectronics, quantum devices, and thermoelectric devices. Recent molecular dynamics (MD) studies have identified a nonmonotonic dependence of thermal conductivity (k) on diameter in ultrathin silicon nanowires (NWs). However, classical MD methods are limited at low temperatures and in strongly confined regimes. This work introduces a fully quantum-mechanical perspective on this anomaly by employing anharmonic non-equilibrium Green's function (NEGF) simulations combined with density-functional-theory-trained neuroevolution potentials. For [001]- and [110]-oriented NWs, k decreases with diameter d to a minimum at d_c = 6.24 nm and 5.50 nm, respectively, then rises with d, for a temperature range of 10-300 K. At room temperature, this behavior arises from dominant momentum-conserving normal scattering relative to Umklapp processes in confined regimes, thereby enabling Poiseuille-like hydrodynamic phonon flow that competes with boundary scattering. At cryogenic temperatures, strong radial confinement quantizes the phonon spectrum, and only low-frequency phonons (< 2 THz) significantly contribute to heat transport through quasi-ballistic propagation of long-wavelength modes, as demonstrated by the spectral thermal conductance. In contrast to classical MD, which is inaccurate at low temperatures due to overexcitation of high-frequency vibrations by Boltzmann statistics, neglect of quantum suppression, and overestimation of thermal conductivity in thinner NWs with stronger quantum confinement, the NEGF framework provides quantitative accuracy even at low temperatures, such as 10 K.

</details>


### [151] [Geometric Protection of Bipartite Entanglement in Hopf-Linked Quantum Rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26622)
*V. Yogesh,Prosenjit Maity*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深锁互连Hopf量子环（Hopf-linked quantum rings）中两相互作用电子的二分纠缠（bipartite entanglement）边界，揭示几何保护机制的局限性及其在介观半导体架构中的标度限制。

Method: 采用未展开的三维库仑相互作用（3D Coulomb interaction）的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，结合高阶Schrieffer-Wolff变换分析非共面几何倾斜对交换简并（exchange degeneracy）和宇称混合（parity mixing）的影响。

Result: 发现了精确连续空间对称性，该对称性可几何隔离正宇称Bell态（positive-parity Bell state），防止经典相互作用驱动的局域化；非共面几何倾斜（α>0）可提升交换简并并维持最大纠缠流形；但高阶变换揭示未抵消的轨道间动量跃迁（inter-orbital momentum transitions）会引发动态宇称混合，定义出纠缠不可逆坍缩的临界相互作用阈值（λ_crit）。

Conclusion: 几何保护在介观半导体架构中存在根本性标度限制，需借助合成宏观平台（synthetic macroscopic platforms）才能实现稳健的拓扑保护（topological protection）。

Abstract: We determine the bipartite entanglement bounds of two interacting electrons in deeply interlocked Hopf-linked quantum rings via exact diagonalization of the unexpanded 3D Coulomb interaction. This identifies an exact continuous spatial symmetry that geometrically isolates the positive-parity Bell state, preventing classical interaction-driven localization. A non-coplanar geometric tilt ($α> 0$) is essential to lift the exchange degeneracy and maintain this maximally entangled manifold as a state of frozen entanglement. However, a higher-order Schrieffer-Wolff transformation demonstrates this geometric protection is fundamentally bounded; uncancelled inter-orbital momentum transitions inevitably induce dynamical parity mixing. This defines a critical interaction threshold ($λ_{crit}$) for irreversible entanglement collapse. Our analysis shows that the resulting bounding conditions reveal scaling limitations in mesoscopic semiconductor architectures, dictating the necessity of synthetic macroscopic platforms to achieve robust topological protection.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋输运穿过界面（interface）是自旋电子学（spintronic）器件的关键，但在超快时间尺度上对其进行探测仍然困难。现有方法难以在保持其他生长参数不变的条件下，独立调控界面粗糙度并定量评估其对超快自旋输运的影响。

Method: 实验采用太赫兹发射光谱测量Co|Pt异质结构（heterostructure），通过改变底层Au缓冲层（Au buffer layer）的厚度来系统调控界面粗糙度，同时保持其他生长参数不变。从测得的太赫兹电场中，在修正样品阻抗（impedance）和光学吸收（optical absorption）变化后，提取出界面自旋流透明度（interface spin-current transparency）ts。

Result: 当界面均方根粗糙度（root-mean-square roughness）和横向晶粒尺寸（lateral grain size）均增大三倍时，界面自旋流透明度ts仅下降约30%，且太赫兹频谱未观察到可测量的变化。

Conclusion: 超快时间尺度上的界面自旋输运对界面形貌（morphological）变化相对鲁棒（robust），太赫兹发射光谱可作为探测不完美界面处自旋动力学的可靠手段。

Abstract: Spin transport across interfaces is critical for spintronic devices, yet remains difficult to probe on ultrafast timescales. We use terahertz emission spectroscopy on Co|Pt heterostructures whose interface roughness is tuned through the thickness of an underlying Au buffer layer, while leaving other growth parameters unchanged. From the measured THz electric field, we extract the interface spin-current transparency ts after correcting for the changes in sample impedance and optical absorption of the stack. Surprisingly, we find that ts decreases by only approximately 30% as the interface root-mean-square roughness and the lateral grain size both increase by a factor of three, with no measurable change in the THz spectrum. These results demonstrate that interfacial spin transport is relatively robust against morphological variations on ultrafast timescales, establishing terahertz emission spectroscopy as a reliable probe of spin dynamics across imperfect interfaces.

</details>


### [153] [Orbital Magnetization from Uniform and Periodic Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26889)
*Chunli Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过量子霍尔铁磁体（quantum Hall ferromagnet）的解析计算，证明在周期磁场（零净通量）下通过局域哈特里-福克投影子响应（local Hartree-Fock projector response）计算的轨道磁化强度（orbital magnetization），与沿斯特热达线（Středa line）通过对均匀磁场求导巨势（grand potential）得到的结果一致，从而揭示轨道磁化强度应被视为与产生斯特热达公式（Středa formula）的谱流（spectral flow）相关的能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均匀磁场（uniform magnetic field）会改变电子的动量空间结构，导致朗道量子化（Landau quantization），进而引发一个基础性问题：在零场动量空间中进行的线性响应计算，如何复现系统对均匀磁场的热力学响应？本文旨在从解析角度回答这一矛盾。

Method: 本文以量子霍尔铁磁体为模型系统，采用两种独立路径计算轨道磁化强度 $M$：其一，在零净通量的周期性磁场下，通过局域哈特里-福克投影子响应计算 $M$；其二，沿斯特热达线对均匀磁场求巨势导数计算 $M$。两种方法分别保持或改变希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的朗道能级简并度（Landau-level degeneracy）。

Result: 两种计算方法得到的轨道磁化强度 $M$ 结果完全一致，尽管第一种方法保持希尔伯特空间固定，第二种方法改变了朗道能级简并度。这一一致性表明轨道磁化强度并非仅依赖单一的计算途径。

Conclusion: 两者的吻合暗示应将轨道磁化强度理解为与产生斯特热达公式的谱流相关联的能量。本文同时为轨道磁化强度及其与斯特热达公式的关系提供了教程性介绍。

Abstract: Magnetization is thermodynamically defined as the derivative of the grand potential with respect to a uniform magnetic field. However, a uniform magnetic field makes the kinetic momentum operators noncommuting and Landau-quantizes the electron motion. This changes the zero-field momentum-space to Landau-levels and raises a fundamental question: how can the thermodynamic response to a uniform field be reproduced by a linear-response calculation carried out in the momentum space of the zero-field problem? We address this question analytically in a quantum Hall ferromagnet that allows the orbital magnetization $M$ to be computed in a closed form. We first compute $M$ from the local Hartree--Fock projector response to a periodic magnetic field with zero net flux. We then compute $M$ from the derivative of the grand potential with respect to a uniform magnetic field along the Středa line. The two approaches give the same result, even though the first keeps the Hilbert space fixed while the second changes the Landau-level degeneracy. Their agreement suggests that we should view orbital magnetization as the energy associated with the spectral flow that gives rise to the Středa formula. Our work provides a tutorial introduction to orbital magnetization and its relation to the Středa formula.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析，考虑手征反常引起的手征磁电流沿传播方向的分量，研究谷不平衡振荡（valley imbalance oscillations）与等离体子电荷振荡（plasmonic charge oscillations）之间的杂化效应。

Result: 预言了一种线性色散（linearly dispersing）混合模式，该模式与体等离体子（bulk plasmon）发生避免交叉（avoided crossing），形成在普通金属中不存在的混合体激发（hybrid bulk excitation）。

Abstract: Collective modes provide direct fingerprints of quantum matter. We predict a previously unidentified hybrid bulk electromagnetic mode in Weyl semimetals arising from the interplay between the chiral anomaly and the orientation of its associated chiral magnetic response relative to the direction of the wave-vector. When the anomaly-induced chiral magnetic current has a component along the propagation direction, oscillations of valley imbalance hybridize with plasmonic charge oscillations, producing a linearly dispersing mode that undergoes avoided crossing with the bulk plasmon, producing a hybrid bulk excitation absent in ordinary metals. The hybrid mode provides a direct signature of Weyl semimetals and a probe of the chiral anomaly and its associated chiral magnetic effect, with observable features in electron energy-loss spectroscopy. Studying this interplay can uncover various optical and electronic properties of Weyl semimetals.

### [155] [Quantum Geometric Origin of Hall Viscosity and Nonlocal Hall Conductivity in Lattice Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27059)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示晶格能带中霍尔黏度与量子几何（quantum geometry）之间的内在联系，并将这种几何效应与非局域霍尔电导（nonlocal Hall conductivity）的可观测电学响应关联起来，从而为霍尔黏度提供电学探测手段。

Method: 理论推导了能带投影电四极矩（band-projected electric quadrupole）与贝里曲率（Berry curvature）及量子度量（quantum metric）的关系，分析了投影坐标代数与非局域霍尔电导二次波矢系数的对应结构，并对比了理想能带与朗道能级（Landau level）形式的偏差。

Result: 霍尔黏度由贝里曲率决定的投影坐标代数量子度量决定的波包四极展宽共同控制；推导出晶格黏度-电导率关系（lattice viscosity-conductivity relation）；理想能带中偏离朗道能级形式的程度由贝里曲率涨落（Berry curvature fluctuations）量化。

Conclusion: 非局域霍尔响应可作为霍尔黏度底层量子几何的电学表征，以及能带几何理想性（geometric idealness）的输运诊断工具。

Abstract: We show that Hall viscosity in lattice bands is governed by a band-projected electric quadrupole encoded within the quantum geometry: Berry curvature sets the projected-coordinate algebra, while the quantum metric determines the quadrupolar spread of a wave packet. The same structure enters the quadratic wave-vector coefficient of the nonlocal Hall conductivity, yielding a lattice viscosity-conductivity relation. In ideal bands, the deviation from the Landau-level form is quantified by Berry curvature fluctuations. Our results establish the nonlocal Hall response as an electrical signature of the quantum geometry underlying Hall viscosity and as a transport diagnostic of geometric idealness.

### [156] [Microwave-driven Floquet-Fano interference in a ring-chord quantum dot structure for enhanced spin-caloritronic performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27181)
*Parbati Senapati,Kalpataru Pradhan*

TL;DR: 研究微波辐照下四量子点环—弦纳米结构中的光子辅助热电输运。通过非平衡格林函数结合Floquet理论与自洽Hartree处理，揭示了Floquet边带与几何驱动Fano干涉的协同效应。在中间温度下，环—弦几何结构达到ZT≈12，自旋热电优值达Z_sT≈18，输出功率达6.24 fW，效率接近卡诺效率的62%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数形式（nonequilibrium Green's function formalism）结合Floquet理论（Floquet theory）和自洽Hartree处理（self-consistent Hartree treatment），在线性响应区域（linear response regime）内对电子-电子相互作用进行描述。

Result: 在中间温度T=0.3Γ_0下，环—弦几何结构的热电优值ZT≈12，效率接近卡诺效率的62%，输出功率为6.24 fW；引入自旋极化注入后，自旋热电优值Z_sT≈18。

Abstract: We investigate photon-assisted thermoelectric transport in four--quantum-dot nanostructures featuring ring and ring--chord geometries coupled to ferromagnetic leads. Focusing on the interplay between microwave-induced Floquet sidebands and geometry-driven Fano interference, we employ the nonequilibrium Green's function formalism combined with Floquet theory and a self-consistent Hartree treatment of electron-electron interactions within the linear response regime. The inclusion of a longitudinal interdot chord bridging the lead-coupled dots introduces a discrete interference pathway that competes with the continuum of ring-mediated states, giving rise to pronounced Fano resonances. Microwave irradiation dynamically reshapes these resonances through photon absorption and emission processes, enabling tunable control of electrical conductance, thermopower, and electronic thermal conductance. Quantitatively, at an intermediate temperature of $T=0.3Γ_0$ (where $Γ_0$ denotes the dot-lead coupling strength), the microwave-driven ring-chord geometry exhibits an exceptional thermoelectric figure of merit of ZT $\approx$ 12 and an optimal efficiency--power trade-off, reaching nearly $62\%$ of the Carnot efficiency with an output power of $6.24~\mathrm{fW}$. Crucially, the combination of spin-polarized injection from the leads and Zeeman splitting within the dots induces a robust spin-dependence within this Floquet--Fano interference. This cooperative interplay results in an enhanced spin Seebeck response and a maximum spin thermoelectric figure of merit of nearly $Z_sT \approx 18$. Our findings establish microwave-driven engineering of Fano interference as an effective strategy for modulating spin-caloritronic behavior in multi-quantum-dot devices.

By showing the contrast between electrical transport of mono- and multilayer MoS2 exfoliated on Au under ultra-high vacuum (UHV) and ambient conditions, we experimentally prove that, contrary to the prevailing view in the literature, the intrinsic MoS2/Au junction is highly conductive and exhibits ohmic behaviour. Our results indicate that interfacial contamination is responsible for the high contact resistances reported to date and affects the thickness dependence of electrical transport, explaining the discrepancies observed in the literature.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非中心对称金属（noncentrosymmetric metals）中，点群对称性（point-group symmetry）可禁止线性和二次电场诱导的轨道磁化，使得三次响应成为主导信号，但相关的微观机制尚不清晰，亟需理论解析。

Method: 作者使用了一个Ward完备的有限动量三次Kubo核（Ward-complete finite-momentum cubic Kubo kernel），并结合反对称线性动量投影（antisymmetric linear-in-$q$ projection），推导了直流响应的表达式。

Result: 直流响应（dc response）被分解为三个量子几何通道（quantum-geometric channels）：混合电磁位置位移四极矩（mixed electric-magnetic positional-shift quadrupole）、量子度量漂移项（quantum-metric drift term）和轨道矩八极矩（orbital-moment octupole）。三者共享相同点群对称性，但在寿命（lifetime）、频率（frequency）和栅压（gate）指纹上存在差异。对于翘曲的$C_{3v}$表面，度量通道满足截断无关的标度律$\barχ_G \propto μ^{-2}$。

Conclusion: 作者提出三次谐波磁光克尔谱可作为实验探测该量子几何响应的可行手段，为非中心对称材料中的非线性磁光效应提供了理论框架和实验指引。

Abstract: In noncentrosymmetric metals such as $C_{3v}$ topological-insulator surfaces, moiré heterobilayers, and zincblende crystals, point-group symmetry can forbid the linear and quadratic electric-field-induced orbital magnetization, leaving the cubic response as the leading signal. Using a Ward-complete finite-momentum cubic Kubo kernel with an antisymmetric linear-in-$q$ projection, we show that the dc response separates into three quantum-geometric channels. These are a mixed electric-magnetic positional-shift quadrupole, a quantum-metric drift term, and an orbital-moment octupole. The three contributions share the same point-group symmetry but differ in their lifetime, frequency, and gate fingerprints. For a warped $C_{3v}$ surface the metric channel obeys the cutoff-independent law $\barχ_G \propto μ^{-2}$. We propose third-harmonic magneto-optical Kerr spectroscopy as an experimental route.

</details>


### [161] [Absence of a Superradiant Phase Transition in Dirac Landau Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27319)
*Elsa Jöchl,Felix Helmrich,Frieder Lindel,Lucy Hale,Lorenzo Graziotto,Mona Jarrahi,Tobia F. Nova,Jérôme Faist,Giacomo Scalari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过太赫兹光谱实验测量了石墨烯与太赫兹腔的超强耦合体系，发现即使在耦合强度达到Ω_R/ω_cav≈0.4的情况下，仍未观察到超辐射相变（SRPT）的软化下极化激元支，表明石墨烯朗道极化激元中不存在规避No-Go定理的超辐射相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光子凝聚为宏观占据基态的超辐射相变（superradiant phase transition, SRPT）是腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics, cQED）的核心预言之一，但五十年来在平衡态实验中始终未能实现；是否存在此类相变在光-物质耦合系统中仍存争议，广泛建立的No-Go定理在多模型中都排除了其可能性。石墨烯的线性狄拉克色散在领头阶不产生抗磁性的$\vec{A}^2$项（diamagnetic term），使其成为可能规避No-Go定理的最干净候选体系，因此需通过实验验证其是否能实现SRPT。

Method: 本文首次对封装单层石墨烯薄片与单个互补开口谐振环（complementary split-ring resonator）构成的超强耦合系统进行了太赫兹光谱测量。通过调控载流子密度，系统从弱耦合扫描至超强耦合区域，达到归一化耦合强度Ω_R/ω_cav≈0.4。实验测量了完整的极化激元色散，并与基于近场模型从头推导的Hopfifield哈密顿量进行定量比较。

Result: 在达到Ω_R/ω_cav≈0.4的超强耦合条件下，未观察到二级SRPT应表现出的下极化激元支软化现象。完整的极化激元色散被一个基于近场模型的Hopfifield哈密顿量定量重现。

Conclusion: 实验结果表明，在目前可达到的最强耦合条件下，石墨烯朗道极化激元中不存在规避No-Go定理的SRPT。该结果为腔驱动相变在二维狄拉克系统中的预言建立了实验基线，并对固态cQED中利用真空诱导有序（vacuum-induced order）的理论方案具有直接影响。

Abstract: The condensation of photons into a macroscopically populated ground state, a superradiant phase transition (SRPT), is one of the most striking predictions of cavity quantum electrodynamics (cQED), yet has resisted experimental realization in equilibrium for over fifty years. Whether such a transition can survive at all in light-matter coupled systems is still debated, with a widely established \textit{No-Go} theorem ruling it out across several models. Graphene cyclotron transitions ultrastrongly coupled to terahertz (THz) cavities have been at the heart of this debate. At leading order, the linear Dirac dispersion of electrons does not generate the diamagnetic $\vec{A}^2$ term that enforces the theorem, making graphene the cleanest candidate for a No-Go-evading phase transition.
  Here, we present the first THz spectroscopic measurements of an encapsulated monolayer graphene flake ultrastrongly coupled to a single complementary split-ring resonator. By tuning the carrier density we sweep the system from weak coupling into the ultrastrong regime, reaching a normalized coupling $Ω_\text{R}/ω_\text{cav} \approx 0.4$. This is well into the range where a second order SRPT would manifest by a softening of the lower polariton branch, which we do not observe. The full polariton dispersion is instead quantitatively reproduced by a Hopfield Hamiltonian derived from first principles using a near-field model that accounts for the sub-wavelength character of the cavity.
  Our results establish an experimental baseline for predictions of cavity-driven phase transitions in two-dimensional Dirac systems, and rule out a No-Go-evading SRPT in graphene Landau polaritons up to the strongest couplings accessible today, with direct implications for proposals invoking vacuum-induced order in solid-state cQED.

</details>


### [162] [Spontaneous persistent currents and time-reversal symmetry breaking in thick-walled Weyl semimetal cylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27368)
*J. C. Pérez-Pedraza,Juan A. Cañas,Daniel A. Bonilla,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了厚壁外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）圆柱体在外加轴向磁场中的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应（Aharonov-Bohm effect），发现Weyl节点的空间分离可作为内禀手征规范场（chiral gauge field），自发破坏时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），并导致持续电流和传导通道展开等新奇量子现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究厚壁外尔半金属圆柱几何体在外加轴向磁场中的Aharonov-Bohm效应，以揭示Weyl节点空间分离所扮演的内在规范场角色及其对时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）破坏的贡献。

Method: 采用低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian），对无限长和有限长两种圆柱几何分别解析求解本征值问题；在径向壁施加无穷大质量边界条件（infinite-mass boundary conditions），在圆柱端盖施加MIT袋边界条件（MIT bag boundary conditions），分别处理节点内束缚（intra-node confinement）和谷间散射（inter-valley scattering）。

Result: 数值结果表明，Weyl节点的空间分离作为内禀手征规范场（chiral gauge field），即使在零外磁通下也会内在破坏时间反演对称性（TR symmetry），解除手征简并（chiral degeneracy）。该对称性破坏表现为自发持续电流（persistent currents）和传导通道的展开。此外，纵向束缚（longitudinal confinement）导致传播方向依赖的能量分裂，改变部分态密度（partial density of states），并引发空间-手征电流不平衡（spatio-chiral current imbalances）。

Conclusion: 外尔半金属圆柱的几何和拓扑特性可产生内禀手征规范场效应，导致时间反演对称性自发破坏及相关的量子输运现象，为理解拓扑半金属中的手征量子现象提供新视角。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the Aharonov-Bohm effect in a thick-walled Weyl semimetal (WSM) cylinder subject to an external axial magnetic field. By employing a low-energy effective Hamiltonian, we analytically solve the eigenvalue problem for both infinite and finite-length cylindrical geometries. We apply infinite-mass boundary conditions at the radial walls and MIT bag boundary conditions at the cylinder caps to properly account for intra-node confinement and inter-valley scattering, respectively. Our numerical results demonstrate that the spatial separation of the Weyl nodes acts as an internal chiral gauge field. This geometric field intrinsically breaks time-reversal (TR) symmetry, lifting the chiral degeneracy even at zero external flux. This symmetry breaking manifests as spontaneous persistent currents and the unfolding of conductance channels. Furthermore, longitudinal confinement induces propagation-direction-dependent energy splitting, altering the partial density of states and causing spatio-chiral current imbalances.

### [163] [Signal-to-Noise Ratio and Sample Size Govern Representational Alignment in Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26973)
*Ali Hussaini Umar,Alessandro Laio*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文通过回归与分类任务实验，系统研究了神经网络中潜表示对齐（alignment）现象与信噪比（SNR）及训练样本量的关系，发现对齐随SNR单调变化、随样本量非单调变化，且对齐程度与泛化误差并不直接相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络在不同架构、训练协议或数据集下训练的潜表示会表现出结构相似性（对齐现象），但对其与数据质量（信噪比）和数量（样本量）之间的定量关系尚缺乏深入理解。

Method: 分别对真实数据集和合成数据上的回归与分类任务进行集成训练（ensemble training），使用独立噪声扰动训练集；同时构建一个单隐层线性网络（linear network），使得对齐程度可解析计算，用于与非线性网络对比。

Result: 对齐程度随信噪比（SNR）单调变化，但随训练样本量呈现非单调变化；对齐在插值阈值（interpolation threshold）附近达到最小值；更强的对齐并不必然对应更低的泛化误差。

Conclusion: 对齐程度与数据质量和数量之间存在非平凡依赖关系，且该关系与泛化性能解耦，提示对齐不应简单视为泛化能力的代理指标。

Abstract: Neural networks are known to develop latent representations that are $aligned$, namely structurally similar across networks trained with different architectures, training protocols, or training datasets. We study this phenomenon in a controlled setting, where we train an ensemble of networks on regression and classification tasks using training sets perturbed by independent realizations of a noise process. We show that the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) and the training sample size influence the alignment in qualitatively similar ways in networks trained on real-world datasets and in an extremely simple $linear$ network with a single hidden layer, for which the alignment can be estimated analytically. Across linear and nonlinear networks, regression and classification tasks, and both synthetic and real-world data, we consistently observe that alignment varies monotonically with SNR but non-monotonically with training sample size. In particular, the alignment is minimized near the interpolation threshold, and a stronger alignment does not necessarily correspond to better generalization error. These findings reveal a non-trivial dependence of alignment on data quality and quantity, decoupled from generalization performance.

</details>

### [164] [Search for a new heavy scalar resonance decaying to a pair of Z bosons in the four-lepton final state in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26462)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于CMS实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb$^{-1}$的质子-质子对撞数据，搜索通过双Z玻色子衰变的重标量共振态（heavy scalar resonance），未发现超出标准模型预期的显著信号，并在95%置信水平上给出了产生截面与分支比乘积的上限（0.05–0.1 pb至0.001 pb）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找超出标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的新物理信号，尤其是通过双Z玻色子（$ZZ$）衰变道探测重标量共振态，以检验是否存在新的重希格斯粒子或其他标量粒子。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb$^{-1}$），在共振质量130 GeV至3 TeV范围内进行搜索。考虑了窄宽度（narrow-width）和宽宽度（broad-width）两种宽度场景，以及胶子聚变（gluon fusion）和矢量玻色子聚变（vector boson fusion）两种产生过程。对于宽宽度场景，还考虑了新共振态、125 GeV希格斯玻色子产生以及连续本底之间的干涉效应。

Result: 在所检验的相空间内未观察到显著超出标准模型本底预期的信号。在95%置信水平上，给出了重标量共振态产生截面与双Z玻色子衰变分支比乘积的上限：低质量区约0.05–0.1 pb，高质量区降至约0.001 pb。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现新重标量共振态的证据，排除了在双Z玻色子衰变道中一定质量和耦合强度范围内的新物理信号，为后续理论模型和更高灵敏度实验提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for a new heavy scalar resonance decaying to two Z bosons, each subsequently decaying to a pair of electrons or muons, is presented. The results are based on a proton-proton collision data set collected by the CMS experiment at the LHC at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The search is performed over a wide range of resonance masses from 130 GeV to 3 TeV, considering both narrow- and broad-width scenarios, and considering the gluon fusion and vector boson fusion production processes. For the broad-width scenario, the interference between the new resonance, the 125 GeV Higgs boson production, and the continuum background is taken into account. No significant excess with respect to the standard model background expectation is observed in the examined phase space. Upper limits at the 95% confidence level are set on the product of the heavy scalar resonance production cross section and the branching fraction for its decay into two Z bosons. The exclusion limits range from 0.05$-$0.1 pb in the low-mass region to 0.00 pb in the high-mass region.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器采集的约100亿J/ψ事例，本文在J/ψ→γK⁰_S K⁰_S π⁰和J/ψ→γπ⁰π⁰η过程中观测到X(2370)粒子，并联合此前报道的J/ψ→γK⁰_S K⁰_S η′过程，精确测定其质量与宽度分别为2359 MeV/c²和170 MeV；同时首次以超过9σ显著性观测到X(2370)→a₀(980)⁰π⁰衰变，其衰变模式与赝标量胶球（pseudoscalar glueball）的特征相符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用大统计量的J/ψ衰变数据，通过多种末态道确认X(2370)的存在，并精确测定其质量与宽度；通过分析其衰变模式与η_c的相似性，检验X(2370)作为赝标量胶球（pseudoscalar glueball）候选者的理论预言。

Method: 从BESIII探测器采集的(10087±44)×10⁶个J/ψ事例出发，分析J/ψ→γK⁰_S K⁰_S π⁰和J/ψ→γπ⁰π⁰η两个过程，在K⁰_S K⁰_S π⁰和π⁰π⁰η不变质量谱（invariant mass spectra）中寻找X(2370)的信号，并结合此前J/ψ→γK⁰_S K⁰_S η′的结果进行联合拟合。

Result: X(2370)在两个过程中分别以超过14σ和20σ的统计显著性（statistical significance）被观测到。联合测量给出其质量m=2359⁺¹³₋₁₄ MeV/c²、宽度Γ=170⁺⁴⁴₋₂₉ MeV。首次以超过9σ的显著性观测到X(2370)→a₀(980)⁰π⁰衰变链（其中a₀(980)⁰→π⁰η）。

Conclusion: X(2370)的衰变模式与η_c存在相似性，这一特征与赝标量胶球的理论预期一致，支持X(2370)是赝标量胶球候选者的论断。

Abstract: Based on $(10087\pm44)\times10^{6}$ $J/ψ$ events collected with the BESIII detector, the $J/ψ\rightarrowγK^{0}_{S}K^{0}_{S}π^{0}$ and $J/ψ\rightarrowγπ^{0}π^{0}η$ processes are studied. The $X(2370)$ is observed in both the $K^{0}_{S}K^{0}_{S}π^{0}$ and $π^{0}π^{0}η$ invariant mass spectra, with statistical significances greater than $14σ$ and $20σ$, respectively. Combining measurements from these processes with measurements from the previously reported $J/ψ\rightarrowγK^{0}_{S}K^{0}_{S}η^{\prime}$ process, the mass and width of the $X(2370)$ are determined to be $2359^{+13}_{-14}~\text{MeV}/c^{2}$ and $170^{+44}_{-29}~\text{MeV}$, respectively. In addition, the decay $X(2370)\to a_{0}(980)^{0}π^{0}$ with $a_{0}(980)^{0}\to π^{0}η$ is observed with a statistical significance exceeding $9σ$. The similarities in decay modes between the $X(2370)$ and $η_{c}$ are consistent with the features of a pseudoscalar glueball.

</details>

### [166] [Local network evolution rules drive shortest path multiplicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25237)
*Alexei Vazquez*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 通过数值模拟证明，局部网络演化（local network evolution）自然会导致高最短路径多重性（shortest path multiplicity），而真实网络中的高最短路径多重性及其与社区结构（community structure）的关联正是局部演化规则的必然结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实网络（real networks）具有高最短路径多重性，且该特征与网络的社区结构存在相关性。由于局部网络演化能够诱导社区的形成，因此有必要探究高最短路径多重性是否为局部演化规则的天然产物。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）的方法，对局部网络演化规则下的最短路径多重性特征进行验证。

Result: 数值模拟结果表明，局部演化规则确实会导致网络产生高最短路径多重性。

Conclusion: 真实网络的高最短路径多重性是局部演化规则的自然预期结果，这从演化机制角度解释了该统计特征的存在。

Abstract: The shortest path multiplicity is an important metric of complex networks. The shortest path multiplicity of real networks is high and it correlates with their community structure. Since local network evolution induces network communities, it is possible that a high shortest path multiplicity is the natural expectation of local evolution rules. Here I demonstrate, by means of numerical simulations, that this is indeed the case.

### [167] [Sobolev convergence of log-determinants for smooth Wigner matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27222)
*Giorgio Cipolloni,Patrick Lopatto*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究表明，光滑Wigner矩阵的对数行列式（log-determinant）和特征值计数函数（eigenvalue counting function）所导出的场（fields），在任意负Sobolev空间（negative Sobolev space）$H^{-s}$中，依分布收敛（converge in law）到中心化的高斯（centered Gaussian）对数相关（logarithmically correlated）随机元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解随机矩阵（random matrix）谱统计中泛函（如对数行列式和特征值计数函数）在大矩阵极限下的随机场行为，特别是其在分布意义下是否收敛到某种高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）类型的对数相关结构。

Method: 通过分析光滑Wigner矩阵的对数行列式和特征值计数函数在负Sobolev空间中的极限分布性质，建立其与中心化高斯对数相关随机元的分布收敛关系。

Result: 这两类函数所定义的场在任意负Sobolev空间$H^{-s}$中均依分布收敛到中心化高斯对数相关随机元。

Conclusion: 光滑Wigner矩阵的对数行列式和特征值计数函数在负正则性空间中呈现出对数相关高斯场的极限结构，为随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中的泛函收敛提供了新的分布结果。

Abstract: We show that the fields emerging from the log-determinant and the eigenvalue counting function of smooth Winger matrices converge in law to centered Gaussian, logarithmically correlated, random elements in every negative Sobolev space $H^{-s}$.

### [168] [Taming non-equilibrium thermal fluctuations in subthreshold CMOS circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26267)
*Nahuel Freitas,Geremia Massarelli,Jeremy Rothschild,Dylan Keane,Ethan Dawe,Sewook Hwang,Akhil Garlapati,Trevor McCourt*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文展示了一个完全基于CMOS的实验平台，该平台能够直接控制其内在热涨落，作为可编程多变量高斯采样器（multivariate Gaussian sampler），为概率计算（probabilistic computing）、随机计算（stochastic computing）及随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）研究提供硬件基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着CMOS技术尺寸缩小，热涨落（thermal fluctuation）对电路行为的影响日益显著，给传统电路设计带来挑战；然而，热噪声（thermal noise）固有的随机性在新兴的概率计算（probabilistic computing）领域正被视为潜在资源。

Method: 该工作构建了一个完全CMOS的实验平台，能够直接控制其本征热涨落，实现可编程多变量高斯采样器（programmable multivariate Gaussian sampler）功能。

Result: 所得器件可作为节能随机计算（energy-efficient stochastic computing）的硬件原语（hardware primitive），并为电子噪声（electronic noise）与随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）研究提供实验平台。

Conclusion: 该CMOS平台通过利用而非抑制热噪声，为概率计算和随机系统中的基础研究提供了一种新的硬件途径。

Abstract: As CMOS technology scales down, thermal fluctuations increasingly impact circuit behavior, posing challenges to conventional circuit design. However, the inherent stochasticity introduced by thermal noise is now being explored as a potential resource in the emerging field of probabilistic computing. This work presents a fully CMOS experimental platform that enables direct control over its intrinsic thermal fluctuations. These devices function as programmable multivariate Gaussian samplers, offering a hardware primitive for energy-efficient stochastic computing and serving as an experimental platform for studies in electronic noise and stochastic thermodynamics.
