### [169] [Multi-Scale Coherence of Represented Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26412)
*Amir Jafari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文引入一种依赖表示（representation-dependent）的诊断方法，用于检验有限间距流几何（finite-separation flow geometry）在不同观测分辨率下是否保持稳定。该方法通过比较向量场在不同平滑分辨率下的增量方向，计算相干矩阵（coherence matrix），并在合成无散场、Lorenz相空间以及三维O(1)标量场泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）流中展示了其应用，揭示了二阶统计量无法捕捉交叉分辨率几何信息，以及表示、模型和截断对有限间距流几何的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性与统计物理中的许多问题通过表示流（represented flows）进行建模，包括物理空间向量场、相空间漂移场以及截断的重整化群β函数。现有诊断手段（如局部、谱或不动点诊断）不足以检验表示、模型或截断是否改变了有限间距流几何在不同分辨率下的一致性，因此需要一种互补的场级（field-level）一致性检测工具。

Method: 对于两个分离点（或状态、理论），该方法将向量场在两个不同平滑分辨率下进行粗粒化（coarse graining），然后比较对应向量场增量的方向。归一化后的比较结果在采样间距上取平均，生成一个依赖于所选变量、粗粒化方式、度量和采样协议的相干矩阵（coherence matrix）。该诊断是表示依赖的（representation-dependent），不构成坐标不变的（coordinate-invariant）量。

Result: 在合成无散场（divergence-free fields）中，即使傅立叶振幅、谱和标量两点关联函数相同，不同场仍产生不同的相干矩阵，表明二阶统计量无法决定交叉分辨率的增量几何。Lorenz相空间测试显示，平滑坐标褶皱（coordinate wrinkling）在不改变底层动力学的情况下改变了表示漂移几何，而弱模型扰动在局部拉伸代理（local stretching proxies）保持接近时仍降低了有限间距相干性。三维O(1)标量场的泛函重整化群流中，M=4,5,6的LPA β场内部相干，但交叉截断相干性随高阶耦合方向激活而下降。

Conclusion: 该诊断提供了一种实用的场级检测手段，用于检验表示、模型和截断如何保持有限间距流几何，是对标准局部、谱或不动点诊断的补充而非替代。

Abstract: Many problems in nonlinear and statistical physics are formulated through represented flows, including physical-space vector fields, phase-space drift fields, and truncated renormalization-group beta functions. We introduce a complementary representation-dependent diagnostic for testing whether finite-separation flow geometry is stable across observational resolution. For two separated points, states, or theories, the method compares the direction of the corresponding vector-field increment after the field has been smoothed at two resolutions. Averaging this normalized comparison over sampled separations gives a coherence matrix tied to the chosen variables, coarse graining, metric, and sampling protocol; it is a consistency test, not a coordinate-invariant quantity. We demonstrate the diagnostic in three settings. Synthetic divergence-free fields with identical Fourier amplitudes, spectra, and scalar two-point correlations nevertheless produce distinct coherence matrices, showing that second-order statistics do not determine cross-resolution increment geometry. Lorenz phase-space tests show that a smooth coordinate wrinkling changes represented drift geometry without changing the underlying dynamics, and that a weak model perturbation lowers finite-separation coherence even when local stretching proxies remain closely matched. Finally, for functional renormalization-group flows of the three-dimensional \(O(1)\) scalar theory, projected \(M=4,5,6\) LPA beta fields remain internally coherent, while cross-truncation coherence decreases as higher-order coupling directions are activated. The diagnostic provides a practical field-level check of how representations, models, and truncations preserve finite-separation flow geometry, complementing rather than replacing standard local, spectral, or fixed-point diagnostics.

</details>


### [170] [A tridiagonal matrix-valued process with stochastic resetting for arbitrary Dyson index $β>0$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26945)
*Gernot Akemann,Satya N. Majumdar,Patricia Päßler*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个对称三对角矩阵值过程 β-TMP，其对角元和非对角元分别由 Ornstein-Uhlenbeck 过程和 Cox-Ingersoll-Ross 过程驱动，并研究了其在两种随机重置（stochastic resetting）机制下的特征值联合分布，以及该过程在无序量子紧束缚哈密顿量退火配分函数计算中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于构造一类可精确求解特征值联合分布的时变随机矩阵过程，并考察随机重置（stochastic resetting）对该过程统计性质的影响，从而为无序量子系统等物理问题提供分析工具。

Method: 定义 β-TMP 过程，其中对角元服从独立 Ornstein-Uhlenbeck 过程，非对角元服从依赖行索引参数的独立 Cox-Ingersoll-Ross 过程；引入两种重置机制：同步重置（β-SRTMP）与独立重置（β-IRTMP），并分别分析其特征值联合分布。

Result: β-TMP 过程的矩阵元联合分布及其 N 个实特征值的联合分布可在任意时刻精确计算。β-SRTMP 过程在长时间下的特征值联合分布可解析计算，且与任意 β>0 下重置 Dyson 布朗运动（resetting Dyson Brownian motion）稳态的联合分布相同。β-IRTMP 稳态的解析求解困难，但数值模拟显示其平均特征值密度与 β-SRTMP 有明显差异。

Conclusion: 该三对角矩阵值过程为研究随机重置对随机矩阵系综的影响提供了可解析处理的框架，并可应用于一维无序量子紧束缚哈密顿量的退火配分函数计算。

Abstract: We introduce a symmetric tridiagonal matrix-valued process ($β$-TMP) $H(t)$ whose diagonal entries $H_{k,k}(t)$ evolve independently via an Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process starting at the origin and the off-diagonal entries $H_{k,k+1}(t)$ evolve independently via the Cox-Ingersoll-Ross process, starting at the origin and with parameters that depend on the row index $k$. We show that the joint distribution of the entries of the matrix can be computed exactly at all times and moreover, the joint distribution of its $N$ real eigenvalues can be computed exactly at all times too. We then subject this time-evolving matrix-valued process to stochastic resetting with rate $r$ in two different settings: (i) simultaneous resetting of the matrix entries to the origin with rate $r$ ($β$-SRTMP process) and (ii) independent resetting of the matrix entries to the origin with rate $r$ ($β$-IRTMP process). We show that the joint distribution of the eigenvalues of the $β$-SRTMP process at long times can be computed analytically and it coincides with the joint distribution of the positions of the resetting Dyson Brownian motion in its stationary state for arbitrary $β>0$. For the $β$-IRTMP stationary ensemble, computing analytically the joint distribution of eigenvalues or even the average density of eigenvalues is difficult. However, generating the stationary $β$-IRTMP ensemble numerically is relatively straightforward and we compare its numerical average eigenvalue density to the corresponding analytical results for the $β$-SRTMP stationary ensemble with same parameter values, showing that they are quite different from each other. Finally, we provide a simple and concrete application of this tridiagonal matrix-valued process in computing the annealed partition function of a disordered quantum tight-binding Hamiltonian on a one-dimensional lattice.

</details>


### [171] [Long-range deformations in Gaussian States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26932)
*Francisco Pereira,Nandagopal Manoj,Sara Murciano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究由局域哈密顿量（local Hamiltonian）驱动的虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution）在一维系统中能否诱导相变，重点分析了 Kitaev Majorana 链基态经幂律耦合二次哈密顿量虚时演化后的行为，发现衰减指数 α 控制三种红外区（infrared regime），且即使在长程相互作用下，系统在非零变形强度处也不出现尖锐相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域哈密顿量的虚时演化在一维系统中无法诱导相变，但更长程的相互作用可能突破这一限制。本文旨在检验这一可能性，并探究长程相互作用的虚时演化能否产生明确的量子相变（quantum phase transition）。

Method: 从 Kitaev Majorana 链的基态出发，利用具有幂律耦合（power-law couplings）的二次哈密顿量进行虚时演化，耦合形式为 $1/r^α$，其中 $r$ 为格点间距。由于演化后的态仍保持高斯态（Gaussian state），纠缠和关联函数可解析计算。

Result: 发现衰减指数 α 控制三种红外区：α>1 时仅出现平滑交叉（smooth crossover），拓扑区（topological regime）仅在变形强度趋于无穷时渐近达到；α=1 时变形立即驱动系统流向拓扑相，且存在一个特殊情况，涌现的 Kramers-Wannier 对称性强制长距离呈现 Ising 型标度行为；α<1 时所有非零变形强度下均表现出临界类似行为。即使在任意长程耦合下，模型在非零变形强度处也不出现尖锐相变。

Conclusion: 长程相互作用虽能改变虚时演化的红外行为，但不足以在非零变形强度处产生清晰的相变点，仅能诱导平滑交叉或临界类似行为。

Abstract: Imaginary-time evolution by a local Hamiltonian cannot induce a phase transition in one dimension, but longer-range interactions may subvert such constraints. Starting from the ground state of the Kitaev Majorana chain, we modify the wave function by an imaginary-time evolution generated by a quadratic Hamiltonian with power-law couplings that enhance pairing correlations, typically of the form $1/r^α$, where $r$ is the distance between two sites. As the state remains Gaussian, entanglement and correlation functions can be computed analytically. We find that the decay exponent $α$ controls three distinct infrared regimes: for $α>1$, the deformation produces only smooth crossovers at finite deformation strength, while the topological regime is reached only asymptotically as the deformation strength tends to infinity. At $α=1$, the deformation induces an immediate flow to the topological phase: an infinitesimal deformation strength drives the system to a topological regime, and in a particular case, an emergent Kramers-Wannier symmetry enforces Ising-like scaling at long distances. For $α<1$, the deformed state shows the same critical-like behavior for all non-zero deformation strength. We observe that even with arbitrarily long-range interactions, these models do not display a sharp phase transition at non-zero deformation strength.

</details>


### [172] [Quantum statistical mechanics: Gauge invariance, operator shifting, hyperdensity functionals, and nonequilibrium sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26650)
*Johanna Müller,Matthias Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对量子多体系统中针对算符平移（operator shifting）的规范不变性（gauge invariance）的统计力学理论进行了扩展阐述。平移超算符（shifting superoperator）实现规范变换，保持可观测量平均值的统计力学不变性，并导出了一系列精确求和规则（sum rules），涵盖单体力、超力（hyperforce）、乘积及二体力情形。论文还推广了量子平移至多组分系统，证明了与交换对称性的兼容性，建立了量子超密度泛函理论（hyperdensity functional theory），并论证了非平衡态下的动力学求和规则及其与经典对应量之间的异同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子多体系统中，算符平移导致的规范变换对统计力学的可观测效应尚缺乏系统理解。该工作旨在建立一种基于统计力学的规范不变性理论，以揭示平移变换下平均物理量保持不变的深层结构，并推导相关的精确求和规则。

Method: 引入平移超算符作为规范变换的实现工具，该超算符作用于位置和动量自由度，具备李代数（Lie algebra）对易子结构。通过该超算符建立希尔伯特空间算符之间的映射，并基于此推导热平衡、非平衡及基态下的平均量的不变性。进一步将理论推广至多组分系统，证明与费米子和玻色子交换对称性的兼容性，并建立量子超密度泛函理论以形式化地获取超力和一般量子可观测量。

Result: 得到了单体力、超力、乘积及二体力求和规则等精确求和规则；证明了平移超算符与之前提出的量子正则变换之间的联系；建立了量子平移的多组分推广；证明了算符平移与费米子/玻色子交换对称性兼容；提出了量子版本的超密度泛函理论；在含时哈密顿量驱动的非平衡情形下证明了精确的动力学求和规则。

Conclusion: 该规范不变性理论具有基础性地位，其底层几何结构与狄拉克对应原理（Dirac's correspondence principle）下的正则量子化相容。量子求和规则与其经典对应物之间的异同反映了各自描述层次的特征差异。

Abstract: We provide an extended acount of the recent statistical mechanical theory of gauge invariance against operator shifting in quantum many-body systems (arXiv:2509.20494). The gauge transformation is enacted by a shifting superoperator that displaces the fundamental position and momentum degrees of freedom. The shifting superoperator constitutes a map between Hilbert space operators and it features Lie algebra commutator structure. Averages of general observables remain invariant under the shifting both in and out of thermal equilibrium, as well as in groundstates. The gauge invariance induces exact sum rules that interconnect global observables and associated locally resolved correlation functions. In particular we describe the resulting one-body force, hyperforce, product, and two-body sum rules. We relate the shifting superoperator to a previously formulated quantum canonical transformation and present the generalization of quantum shifting to multi-component systems. The gauge theory respects fundamental fermionic and bosonic particle properties, as we demonstrate by proving the compatibility of operator shifting and exchange symmetry. We formulate the quantum version of hyperdensity functional theory to provide formal access to hyperforces as well as to general averaged quantum observables via universal density functionals. For time-dependent situations, we describe quantum dynamical gauge invariance and prove exact dynamical sum rules for nonequilibrium situations, as generated by Hamiltonian time dependence. We argue for the fundamental status of statistical mechanical gauge invariance based on the compliance of the underlying geometry with canonical quantization according to Dirac's correspondence principle. Analogies and differences of the quantum mechanical sum rules with their classical counterparts remain indicative of the respective levels of description.

</details>


### [173] [Spatiotemporal Structures of Parametrically Driven Nonlinear Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26668)
*Yu Funami,Kazushi Aoyama*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了参量驱动（parametric driving）对一维Frenkel-Kontorova模型（一种非线性多体晶格系统）的影响。数值结果表明，参量振动（parametric vibration）可诱导出时空有序结构（spatiotemporal ordering），其特征为次谐波频率（subharmonic frequency）ω_ex/2和波数k。随驱动强度P_ac增加，k逐渐增大并发生不连续跳变至k=π。线性稳定性分析表明，k共振对应不稳定模，π共振对应稳定模，而k共振由参量放大（parametric amplification）与非线性效应引发的集体涨落（collective fluctuation）协同作用实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究参量驱动对一维Frenkel-Kontorova模型中时空有序行为的影响机制，理解非线性多体晶格系统中由外场驱动诱导的有序相变及其背后的动力学原理。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究参量驱动下Frenkel-Kontorova模型的动力学行为，并结合扩展线性稳定性分析（extended linear stability analysis）对观测到的时空有序模的稳定性进行理论解释。

Result: 数值发现参量振动可诱导出以次谐波频率ω_ex/2和波数k为特征的时空有序结构；波数k随驱动强度P_ac逐渐增大，并在某临界点发生不连续跳变至k=π；线性稳定性分析揭示，k共振对应不稳定模，π共振对应稳定模；k共振的起源在于参量放大与非线性效应驱动的集体涨落之间的协同作用。

Conclusion: 参量驱动能够在一维Frenkel-Kontorova模型中诱导丰富的时空有序现象，其波数选择机制由参量放大与非线性集体涨落的耦合决定，揭示了驱动非线性晶格系统中的有序形成机制。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the effects of parametric driving on the one-dimensional Frenkel-Kontorova model, a nonlinear many-body lattice system. It is numerically found that a parametric vibration induces spatiotemporal ordering characterized by the subharmonic frequency $ω_{\mathrm{ex}}/2$ and wavenumber $k$ which takes nontrivial values depending on the vibration strength $P_{\mathrm{ac}}$ and frequency $ω_{\mathrm{ex}}$. With increasing $P_{\mathrm{ac}}$, $k$ gradually increases and discontinuously jumps up to $k=π$. Based on an extended linear stability analysis, we show that the former $k$ resonance (the latter $π$ resonance) corresponds to the unstable (stable) mode and that the $k$ resonance is made possible by the interplay between the parametric amplification and the collective fluctuation developing through the nonlinear effect.

### [174] [Subdiffusion equation with Cattaneo effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27145)
*Tadeusz Kosztołowicz,Aldona Dutkiewicz,Katarzyna D. Lewandowska*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对普通次扩散方程中传播速度无限大的非物理问题，通过引入由随机时间延迟控制的Cattaneo效应，推导出一种Cattaneo型次扩散方程（CTSE）；该方程包含一个与次扩散指数独立的分数阶时间导数项。研究表明，尽管在短时间极限下均方位移（mean square displacement）表现出超扩散（superdiffusion）特征，但CTSE描述的整个过程仍为次扩散（subdiffusion）。此外，论文还分析了Cattaneo效应在部分吸收边界条件下的影响，并提出了实验识别该效应的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 普通的次扩散方程（ordinary subdiffusion equation）含有一阶或更低阶的分数阶时间导数，但会导致扩散分子的传播速度无限大，这不符合物理现实。为解决这一非物理性质，已有多种形式的Cattaneo次扩散方程被提出，但需要更系统的理论定义与分析。

Method: 将Cattaneo效应定义为普通次扩散通量激活过程中的随机时间延迟，并将该效应纳入通量方程，从而推导出Cattaneo型次扩散方程（CTSE）。假设时间延迟的概率分布由Mittag-Leffler函数（Mittag-Leffler function）控制，使得CTSE在普通次扩散方程基础上增加一个独立的分数阶时间导数项。在此基础上，结合部分吸收壁的Robin边界条件（Robin boundary condition）进行求解，并提出了实验识别Cattaneo效应的方案。

Result: CTSE描述的整个过程在整个时间域内仍为次扩散，但扩散粒子的均方位移（mean square displacement）在短时间极限下的时间演化表现出典型的超扩散（superdiffusion）特征。这一结果表明Cattaneo效应在短时尺度上改变了扩散行为的表观特征。

Conclusion: 在次扩散方程中引入通量激活延迟的Cattaneo效应，可构建更符合物理实际的CTSE模型；该模型在短时表现出超扩散特征，但整体仍为次扩散。Cattaneo效应也会影响边界条件中的通量延迟，需在部分吸收壁的Robin边界条件中加以考虑。文中还提供了实验上识别该效应的可行方法。

Abstract: The ordinary subdiffusion equation, with a fractional time derivative of at most first order, describes a process in which the propagation velocity of diffusing molecules is unlimited. To avoid this non-physical property different forms of the Cattaneo subdiffusion equation have been proposed. We define the Cattaneo effect as a delay of the ordinary subdiffusion flux activation by a random time. By incorporating this effect into the flux equation we get a Cattaneo--type subdiffusion equation (CTSE). We consider a subdiffusion process in which the Cattaneo effect is generated by the time-delay probability distribution controlled by the Mittag-Leffler function. Then, CTSE differs from the ordinary subdiffusion equation by a term with a fractional time derivative, whose order can be independent of the subdiffusion exponent. The influence of the Cattaneo effect on the solutions to the CTSE is discussed. We show that the process described by CTSE is subdiffusion in the entire time domain even though the temporal evolution of the mean square displacement of diffusing particle in the short-time limit is typical for superdiffusion. The delay in the flux activation in the subdiffusion equation should also cause a flux delay in a boundary condition. As an example, we study subdiffusion with the Cattaneo effect in a system with a partially absorbing wall at which the Robin boundary condition is assumed. We also propose a method for experimentally identifying the Cattaneo effect in a subdiffusive system.

</details>


### [175] [Quantum fluctuations and chaos in fully connected spin models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27199)

Abstract: We investigate beyond-mean-field dynamics in a fully connected $\mathrm{SU}(3)$ spin-exchange model, focusing on the interplay between chaotic dynamics and quantum fluctuations. Using the two-particle irreducible (2PI) effective action formalism, we derive equations of motion that systematically account for higher-order correlations generated by interactions, and demonstrate how quantum fluctuations can regularize chaotic dynamics displayed by macroscopic observables. Our results show that an accurate treatment of fluctuations is essential for describing macroscopic dynamics in quantum many-body systems and promote 2PI as a robust framework for connecting microscopic correlations to macroscopic nonequilibrium phenomena.

### [176] [Non-stationary current fluctuations in 1D boundary-driven diffusive systems via Macroscopic Fluctuation Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27275)
*Daisuke Suzuki,Tomohiro Sasamoto*

Method: 对两端连接粒子库（particle reservoirs）的一维边界驱动扩散系统，在恒定扩散系数（diffusion coefficient）与任意迁移率（mobility）条件下，精确推导了弛豫过程中的流方差（current variance）；针对反射布朗运动（Reflective Brownian Motion, RBM），进一步推导了累积量生成函数（cumulant generating function）。

Result: 得到了恒定扩散系数与任意迁移率下弛豫过程流方差的精确解析表达式，以及RBM情形下的累积量生成函数。结果表明，在趋近稳态过程中的非稳态流涨落（non-steady current fluctuations）可被MFT框架定量描述。

Conclusion: MFT的应用范围可以从非平衡稳态成功扩展至弛豫过程等非稳态过程，为定量描述非稳态流涨落提供了有效理论工具。

Abstract: While Macroscopic Fluctuation Theory (MFT) has been highly successful in analyzing non-equilibrium steady states, its application to non-steady-state processes remains limited. In this study, we apply MFT to the relaxation process of one-dimensional boundary-driven diffusive systems coupled to particle reservoirs at both ends. We exactly derive the current variance for systems with a constant diffusion coefficient and arbitrary mobility, as well as the cumulant generating function for the current in Reflective Brownian Motion (RBM). Our results demonstrate that non-steady current fluctuations during the approach to a steady state can be quantitatively described within the MFT framework.

### [177] [Cumulants of mean transverse momentum and elliptic flow in the hydrodynamic model of heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26737)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已观察到平均横向动量与椭圆流之间存在关联，但其集体起源的严格检验尚缺乏定量理论预测。本文旨在通过流体动力学模型推导出可实验检验的定量关系，以验证这些观测关联是否确实源于系统的集体演化。

Method: 采用相对论性粘滞流体动力学模型（relativistic viscous hydrodynamic model）模拟相对论性重离子碰撞，计算平均横向动量与椭圆流的高阶累积量（higher order cumulants）；同时使用基于初始状态熵分布（entropy distribution）构建的逐事件预测器（event-by-event predictors）进行计算，并推导平均横向动量累积量与谐波流（harmonic flow）不同矩之间的定量关系。

Result: 基于初始熵分布的预测器能够定量描述论文所考虑的高阶累积量的中心度依赖性（centrality dependence）。流体动力学模拟结果很好地满足所推导的平均横向动量累积量与谐波流矩之间的定量关系。

Conclusion: 所推导的定量关系可用于在实验上检验平均横向动量与谐波流之间观测关联的集体起源（collective origin），为区分集体动力学与其它机制提供了理论判据。

Abstract: Higher order cumulants between the mean transverse momentum and elliptic flow are calculated in a relativistic viscous hydrodynamic model of relativistic heavy-ion collisions. The results of the hydrodynamic simulations are compared with calculations using event-by-event predictors of the final collective observables constructed from the initial state entropy distribution. The predictors describes quantitatively centrality dependence of the higher cumulants considered in the paper. We derive a quantitative relations between the cumulants of the mean transverse momentum and different moments of the harmonic flow. The hydrodynamic simulations satisfy those relation very well. Those relations could be used to test experimentally the collective origin of the observed correlations between the mean transverse momentum and harmonic flow.

### [178] [Sensitivity of Heavy-Quark Dipolar Flow to its Initial Spatial Distributions in Cu+Au Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26766)
*Ankit Kumar Panda,Tribhuban Parida*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 通过朗之万（Langevin）方法结合流体动力学背景，研究不对称Cu+Au碰撞中粲夸克动力学，发现粲夸克的定向流（$v_1$）比带电强子大约一个量级，且对初始空间分布和温度依赖的拖曳系数（drag coefficient）高度敏感，表明精确测量重味定向流可约束重夸克输运系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在不对称核-核碰撞（Cu+Au）的几何条件下，粲夸克（charm quark）的动力学行为及其产生的定向流（directed flow, $v_1$），并评估其作为约束重夸克输运系数（transport coefficients）的探针潜力。

Method: 采用嵌入于真实流体动力学背景（hydrodynamic background）的朗之万方法（Langevin approach）模拟粲夸克在Cu+Au碰撞中的演化，分析其定向流信号。

Result: 不对称碰撞导致初始能量密度呈空间偏斜（lopsided）分布，在横平面产生偶极流（dipolar flow）结构。粲夸克的$p_T$积分$v_1$比带电强子大约一个量级；$p_T$微分$v_1$对重夸克初始空间分布高度敏感，且显著依赖于温度依赖的拖曳系数。

Conclusion: 重味定向流（heavy-flavor directed flow）的精确测量可有效约束重夸克输运系数，改进基于朗之万方法的描述能力，提升对重离子碰撞中重味观测量的预测可靠性。

Abstract: We investigate charm-quark dynamics in asymmetric Cu+Au collisions at top RHIC energy using a Langevin approach embedded in a realistic hydrodynamic background. The intrinsic asymmetry of the colliding nuclei leads to a spatially lopsided initial energy-density profile, which generates a dipolar flow structure in the transverse plane even at midrapidity. As charm quarks propagate through this medium, they acquire a finite directed flow, $v_1$. We find that the $p_T$-integrated heavy-quark $v_1$ is approximately an order of magnitude larger than that of charged hadrons. In addition, the $p_T$-differential $v_1$ exhibits strong sensitivity to the initial spatial distribution of heavy quarks, emphasizing the importance of pre-equilibrium dynamics in determining final-state anisotropies. Beyond geometric effects, $v_1$ also provides direct sensitivity to medium interactions through the temperature-dependent drag coefficient. Its pronounced dependence on this transport input indicates that precision measurements of heavy-flavor directed flow could place meaningful constraints on heavy-quark transport coefficients, thereby improving Langevin-based descriptions and predictive power for heavy-flavor observables in heavy-ion collisions.

### [179] [Conserving relaxation-time approximation for electron-electron collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26207)
*Sayak Bhattacharjee,Tatia Kiliptari,Dmitrii L. Maslov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种守恒弛豫时间近似（cRTA），通过显式守恒粒子数、能量和动量，并采用能量分辨投影到所有碰撞不变量空间，使得该近似适用于费米面附近非平衡准粒子分布能量依赖敏感的输运量。通过与多个精确和渐近精确结果的对比验证，cRTA在多种费米液体（Fermi liquid）输运场景中达到了百分量级的定量吻合，证明了其作为超越费米面投影近似的简单且准确的输运框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统弛豫时间近似（relaxation-time approximation, RTA）在描述超越费米面投影近似（Fermi surface projection approximation）的输运现象时存在局限性，尤其无法准确处理能量依赖的准粒子分布以及粒子数、能量、动量的守恒律。本文旨在发展一种能够显式满足这些守恒律且适用于更广泛输运场景的改进方案。

Method: cRTA通过将弛豫项投影到完整的碰撞不变量（collision invariants）空间，并引入能量分辨投影，显式地强制执行粒子数、能量和动量的守恒。该方法通过对比多种精确或渐近精确的解析解进行基准检验（benchmark），包括无序非伽利略不变费米液体（non-Galilean-invariant Fermi liquid, FL）的直流电导率（dc conductivity）的低温与高温极限、干净伽利略不变费米液体（Galilean-invariant FL）的有限波矢纵电导率（longitudinal conductivity）的流体力学与无碰撞极限，以及干净非伽利略不变费米液体在超越半经典极限（semiclassical limit）下的光学电导率（optical conductivity）的渐近标度形式。

Result: 基准检验结果显示，cRTA在无序非伽利略不变FL的直流电导率、干净伽利略不变FL的有限波矢纵电导率以及干净非伽利略不变FL的光学电导率等多个观测量上，均与精确解达到百分量级（percent level）的定量吻合。

Conclusion: cRTA提供了一个简单且准确的输运理论框架，能够有效处理超越费米面投影近似的输运问题，在保持计算简便性的同时满足守恒律约束，并在多个典型输运场景中验证了其定量精度。

Abstract: We develop a conserving relaxation-time approximation (cRTA), which explicitly enforces conservation of particle number, energy, and momentum and employs an energy-resolved projection onto the full space of collision invariants. This makes the cRTA applicable to transport quantities sensitive to the energy dependence of the nonequilibrium quasiparticle distribution near the Fermi surface. We benchmark the cRTA against several exact and asymptotically exact results. In particular, it reproduces the low- and high-temperature limits of the dc conductivity of a non-Galilean-invariant Fermi liquid (FL) with disorder, the hydrodynamic and collisionless limits of the finite wavevector longitudinal conductivity of a clean Galilean-invariant FL, and the asymptotic scaling forms of the optical conductivity of a clean non-Galilean-invariant FL beyond the semiclassical limit. For several observables, the agreement with exact solutions is quantitative at the percent level. These results demonstrate that the cRTA provides a simple and accurate framework for transport beyond the Fermi surface projection approximation.

</details>


### [180] [Quantum Interference Corrections in Electron Hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26223)
*Alberto Cortijo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文发现电子流体中的量子干涉修正受到流体动力学Ward恒等式的严格约束，电荷与动量守恒保护了m=0,±1模式，导致首要修正出现在自旋-2的m=±2应力扇区。由此产生的流体动力学Cooperon（库珀子）具有鲁棒的红外结构，能重整化应力弛豫进而影响粘滞度，在通道流中降低粘性电阻率，产生与普通弱局域化符号相反的流体动力学干涉特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究电子流体中量子干涉修正（quantum-interference corrections）如何受流体动力学Ward恒等式（hydrodynamic Ward identities）约束，并分析其对粘滞度（viscosity）及宏观流动行为的影响。

Method: 通过流体动力学Ward恒等式分析电子流体中量子干涉修正的模式结构，识别电荷与动量守恒所保护的扇区（m=0,±1）以及导致首要修正的自旋-2应力扇区（m=±2），进而推导出流体动力学Cooperon（Cooperon）的红外结构及其对粘滞度的重整化效应。

Result: 首要量子干涉修正出现在自旋-2的m=±2应力扇区；流体动力学Cooperon具有鲁棒的红外结构，能重整化应力弛豫（stress relaxation）从而影响粘滞度；在通道流（channel flow）中该效应降低粘性电阻率（viscous resistivity），产生与普通弱局域化（weak localization）符号相反的干涉特征。

Conclusion: 电子流体中的量子干涉修正受流体动力学守恒律严格约束，导致其宏观干涉信号与固体中普遍存在的弱局域化效应符号相反，为电子流体动力学中的量子输运现象提供了新的理论预测。

Abstract: We show that quantum-interference corrections in an electron fluid are tightly constrained by hydrodynamic Ward identities: charge and momentum conservation protect the $m=0,\pm1$ sectors, so the leading correction first appears in the spin-two $m=\pm2$ stress sector. The resulting hydrodynamic Cooperon has a robust infrared structure that renormalizes stress relaxation, and hence the viscosity. In channel flow this lowers the viscous resistivity, producing a hydrodynamic interference signature with the opposite sign to ordinary weak localization.

</details>


### [181] [Hydrodynamic Cooperons in Electron Fluids: Schwinger--Keldysh Derivation and Quantum Corrections to Magnetoresistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26226)
*Alberto Cortijo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在流体力学（hydrodynamic）区域内的二维电子系统中，发展了用于量子干涉修正的 Schwinger–Keldysh 有效理论，发现领先的量子相干修正进入自旋-2 应力扇区，并重整化剪切粘度，影响 Gurzhi 响应及其低场磁流体力学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在流体力学区域，二维电子系统中的量子干涉效应尚未被系统有效地描述。现有理论缺乏一个自洽的框架来同时处理无序平均、量子相干修正以及集体模式的修正，这促使作者从清洁流体力学不动点出发，构建一个包含随机摩擦无序模型的有效理论。

Method: 以清洁流体力学不动点（clean hydrodynamic fixed point）为起点，引入最小随机摩擦无序模型（random-friction disorder model），在自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）下获得有限动量弛豫时间。通过对无序平均后的理论构造流体力学 Cooperon，并计算其相关的自能修正对集体模式的影响。

Result: 守恒律保护了密度和动量扇区，使得领先的量子相干修正被迫进入自旋-2 应力扇区。该应力自能修正重整化了剪切粘度，并同时改变 Gurzhi 响应及其低场磁流体力学（magnetohydrodynamic）信号。

Conclusion: 基于 Schwinger–Keldysh 有效理论，本文建立了一套描述流体力学区域二维电子系统中量子干涉修正的框架，指出应力扇区是量子相干修正的主要载体，且这些修正通过重整化粘性响应直接影响可观测的输运行为。

Abstract: We develop a Schwinger--Keldysh effective theory for quantum-interference corrections in a two-dimensional electron system in the hydrodynamic regime. Starting from the clean hydrodynamic fixed point, we introduce a minimal random-friction disorder model that generates a finite momentum-relaxation time within the self-consistent Born approximation. The disorder-averaged theory then allows us to construct a hydrodynamic Cooperon and to compute the associated self-energy corrections to the collective modes. Conservation laws protect the density and momentum sectors, so that the leading quantum-coherence correction is forced into the spin-two stress sector. The associated stress self-energy renormalizes the shear viscosity and modifies both the Gurzhi response and its low-field magnetohydrodynamic signatures.

</details>


### [182] [GPU-accelerated finite-temperature Lanczos method for spin Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26261)
*Shadan Ghassemi Tabrizi,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在GPU上实现了面向Heisenberg自旋哈密顿量的有限温度Lanczos方法（FTLM），提出了两种状态到索引的映射策略，验证了FP32精度的可行性，并在单GPU上实现了相比多核CPU约一个数量级的加速，支持维度约10^8的希尔伯特空间扇区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现有限温度Lanczos方法（FTLM）在GPU上的高效部署，使其能在单机工作站而非分布式内存集群上运行，并克服传统查表法在GPU上内存开销过大的问题。

Method: 采用无矩阵（matrix-free）的逐行收集（row-wise gather）公式计算哈密顿量作用；引入并比较了两种状态到索引（state-to-index）策略：压缩查找表（compressed lookup table, CLT）和GPU适配的组合排序方案（combinatorial-ranking scheme）。

Result: FP32 GPU计算的热容和磁化率误差远低于FTLM迹估计器（trace estimator）的随机不确定度；在单工作站GPU上实现约一个数量级的加速，并支持维度约10^8的希尔伯特空间扇区。

Conclusion: 该方法可在单GPU工作站上高效、高精度地模拟大型自旋系统，且代码已作为开源工具公开发布。

Abstract: We present a GPU implementation of the finite-temperature Lanczos method (FTLM) for Heisenberg spin Hamiltonians that targets workstation hardware rather than distributed-memory clusters. The Hamiltonian action is evaluated matrix-free in a row-wise gather formulation. We introduce and compare two state-to-index strategies: a compressed lookup table (CLT), which reduces lookup memory by a factor of 16 relative to a full table while retaining a fixed, branch-light access pattern, and a GPU-adapted combinatorial-ranking scheme that removes the lookup table altogether. Numerical tests against FP64 CPU references show that FP32 GPU arithmetic changes heat capacities and magnetic susceptibilities by amounts several orders of magnitude below the stochastic uncertainty of the FTLM trace estimator at typical sample sizes. Benchmarks show speedups of up to about one order of magnitude over optimized multicore CPU calculations and enable Hilbert-space sectors of dimension ~10^8 on a single workstation GPU. The MATLAB/CUDA implementation, including example input files and benchmark scripts, is openly available at https://github.com/ghasdeke/ftlm-gpu (archived at DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.20378647) under the Apache-2.0 license.

</details>


### [183] [Nematic Phase Transitions in Multilayer Graphene Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26270)
*R. David Mayrhofer,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于自洽哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）框架，结合含三角翘曲（trigonal warping）的真实能带结构与双栅屏蔽库仑相互作用，研究了伯纳尔双层石墨烯（Bernal bilayer graphene）中向列相（nematic order）的出现。通过计算载流子密度和位移场变化下的相图，发现了一系列与实验一致的同位旋（isospin）极化态，并识别出少数载流子费米口袋数量变化导致的C₃对称性自发破缺，即向列序。进一步通过解析判据验证了向列序出现在完全极化与部分极化相边界附近，且受屏蔽相互作用强度调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验在石墨烯多层体系中发现了多种电子有序相，包括谷极化/自旋极化相和非常规超导相，同时在伯纳尔双层石墨烯和菱面三层石墨烯中观察到电子向列态（electronic nematic states）。本文旨在从理论上研究这些体系中向列序的产生机制，并以伯纳尔双层石墨烯为重点。

Method: 采用自洽哈特里-福克（self-consistent Hartree-Fock）框架，使用包含三角翘曲（trigonal warping）的真实能带结构以及双栅屏蔽库仑相互作用（dual-gate screened Coulomb interaction），计算随载流子密度和位移场变化的相图。

Result: 发现一系列与实验一致的同位旋极化态，包括部分极化态，其中多数载流子具有大费米口袋，少数载流子具有小费米口袋。在部分同位旋极化态中，观察到少数载流子呈现三个C₃对称口袋、或仅有一个/两个口袋的区域，表明系统出现自发向列序（spontaneous nematic order），破坏了C₃对称性。数值结果表明，向列性出现在完全极化与部分极化相边界附近，受屏蔽相互作用强度调控。

Conclusion: 作者解析推导了向列序的判据，该判据与数值结果一致。因此，该研究为石墨烯多层体系中向列相的出现提供了理论解释和定量判据。

Abstract: Recent experiments on graphene multilayers under displacement field have demonstrated a wide variety of electronically ordered phases, including valley and/or spin polarized phases as well as potentially unconventional superconducting phases. In addition, quantum oscillation measurements in Bernal bilayer graphene and rhombohedral trilayer graphene showed the presence of electronic nematic states. Here, we investigate the emergence of nematic order in these systems, with emphasis on Bernal bilayer graphene, within a self-consistent Hartree--Fock framework, using a realistic band structure with trigonal warping and a dual-gate screened Coulomb interaction. We compute the phase diagram as carrier density and displacement field are varied, and find a sequence of isospin (spin and valley) polarized states consistent with experiment, including partially polarized phases with a large Fermi pockets for isospin-majority carriers and smaller Fermi pockets for isospin-minority carriers. Within these partially isospin polarized states, we identify regions with three $C_3$-symmetric pockets for the minority carriers and regions with only one or two such pockets, implying that the system develops a spontaneous nematic order that breaks $C_3$ symmetry. We find numerically that nematicity emerges near the boundary between fully and partially polarized phases and is controlled by the strength of the screened interaction. We analytically derive a criterion for the nematic order, which agrees with our numerical results.

### [184] [Algebras of order parameters in one-dimensional spin systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27193)
*Ameya Chavda,Clement Delcamp,Alex Turzillo,Minyoung You*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维量子晶格模型中具有有限可逆或非可逆对称性的序参量（order parameters），揭示了弦序参量（string order parameters）的多重态在对称性的Drinfel'd中心（Drinfel'd centre）中组织成拉格朗日代数（Lagrangian algebra），并通过张量网络（tensor network）方法证明了弦算符（string operator）的期望值依赖于与拉格朗日代数相关的管代数模（tube algebra module）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在一维量子晶格模型中，具有有限可逆或非可逆对称性的系统中，弦算符需满足何种条件才能在给定能隙相（gapped phase）中获得非零期望值。该问题与对称性破缺模式以及拓扑序的分类密切相关。

Method: 采用张量网络（tensor network）方法对能隙相进行分类，并将其重构为对称范畴上的模范畴（module categories）。利用管代数模与拉格朗日代数（Lagrangian algebra）之间的关系，推导弦算符期望值的显式表达式。

Result: 弦序参量的多重态在对称范畴的Drinfel'd中心中组织成拉格朗日代数；弦算符的期望值明确依赖于与拉格朗日代数相关的管代数模，该模对应于相应模范畴的全中心（full centre）。此外，这些技术可推广至对称混合态（symmetric mixed states）的相。

Conclusion: 乘法规则（multiplication rule）在红外极限下控制着构成弦算符的扭曲区局域算符（twisted sector local operators）的融合（fusion）。能隙相对应一种自发对称性破缺模式，其中拓扑线的莫里塔类（Morita class of algebras of topological lines）保留在基态子空间中。

Abstract: We study order parameters in one-dimensional quantum lattice models with finite invertible or non-invertible symmetry. We investigate what properties a string operator must satisfy in order to acquire a non-vanishing expectation value in a given gapped phase. We deduce that multiplets of string order parameters organise into a Lagrangian algebra in the Drinfel'd centre of the symmetry category. In particular, we highlight the role of the multiplication rule as governing the fusion of the twisted sector local operators that constitute the string operator in the infrared limit. Our derivations exploit the tensor network approach to the classification of gapped phases and its reformulation in terms of module categories over the symmetry category. Within this framework, a gapped phase is associated with a pattern of spontaneous symmetry breaking wherein a Morita class of algebras of topological lines is preserved in the ground state subspace. The crux of the proof is to show that the expectation value of any string operator explicitly depends on the tube algebra module associated with the Lagrangian algebra, which is realised as the full centre of the corresponding module category. Finally, we demonstrate that these techniques extend to phases of symmetric mixed states.

Abstract: Structural and dynamic correlations in the ground state of the one-dimensional Fermi one-component plasma are studied by Quantum Monte Carlo simulations. Evidence is reported of density correlations slowly decaying with distance, with the concurrent emergence of quasi-crystalline order even in the weakly correlated regime. Effects of quantum statistics in the momentum distribution are discussed.

### [186] [Surface d-orbital order in intermetallic compound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26426)
*Zhanyang Hao,Haohao Sheng,Wanru Ma,Wengen Zheng,Yongqing Cai,Zijuan Xie,Wanlin Cheng,Zuowei Liang,Wu Xie,Wenjuan Zhao,Chen Liu,Zhibin Su,Junhao Lin,Liusuo Wu,Zhengtai Liu,Mao Ye,Ji Dai,Massimo Tallarida,Shengtao Cui,Yogendra Kumar,Kenya Shimada,Kenichi Ozawa,Shuki Torii,Kazuhiro Mori,Yue Xie,Junze Deng,Jiaou Wang,Xuetao Zhu,Jiandong Guo,Jiawei Mei,Zhenyu Wang,Xianhui Chen,Ping Miao,Zhijun Wang,Chaoyu Chen*

TL;DR: 本文报道了在金属间化合物Tb2CoAl4Ge2的表面态中发现了稀土5d轨道序（orbital order），并通过角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）观测到费米面形变和能带分裂等向列相（nematic）特征，结合中子衍射和扫描隧道显微镜排除结构与磁性起源，为纯表面轨道序的存在提供了有力证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道序（orbital order）在强关联电子体系（strongly correlated electron systems）中扮演基础性角色，但其存在性及能带结构指纹（band structure fingerprint）长期未解，亟需实验证据予以阐明。

Method: 利用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）观测表面电子结构；采用高分辨率中子粉末衍射（high-resolution neutron powder diffraction）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy, STM）排除结构与磁性的干扰；通过平均场哈密顿量（mean-field Hamiltonian）中的铁轨序项（ferro-orbital order term）描述实验结果。

Result: ARPES揭示了费米面形变（Fermi surface deformation）和能带分裂（band split）等特征性向列相（nematic）特征；中子衍射和STM测量排除了该轨道序的结构与磁性起源。

Conclusion: Tb2CoAl4Ge2的表面态中存在纯表面轨道序（pure surface orbital order），这一发现避免了庞磁电阻锰氧化物中的结构畸变、铁基超导体中的磁序以及铜氧化物中的电荷转移p轨道序等复杂因素的干扰。

Abstract: Orbital order describes a quantum state where occupied orbitals line up in a periodic pattern. While orbital physics plays a fundamental and universal role in strongly correlated electron systems, the existence and particularly the band structure fingerprint of orbital order remain a long-standing mystery. Here, we report the discovery of rare earth 5d-orbital order developed by the surface states of intermetallic compound Tb2CoAl4Ge2. Angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy reveals characteristic nematic features like Fermi surface deformation and band split. These experimental observations can be described by a ferro-orbital order term in the mean-field Hamiltonian. The structural and magnetic origin of such order is excluded by systematic high-resolution neutron powder diffraction and scanning tunnelling microscopy measurements. Our results provide strong evidence for a pure surface orbital order scenario avoiding complications from structural distortion as in colossal magnetoresistance manganites, magnetic order as in iron-based superconductors, and charge transfer p-orbital order in cuprates.

</details>


### [187] [Designing Quantum Matter in Pyrochlore Iridates: A Perspective on Recent Thin-Film Advances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26603)
*Xiaoran Liu,Michael Terilli,Ana-Marija Nedic,Jiandong Guo,Jak Chakhalian*

Method: 该评述基于近年实验进展，聚焦于三项主要调控手段：维度约束（dimensional confinement）、外延应变（epitaxial strain）以及界面耦合（interfacial coupling）。通过这些方法，研究人员在(111)取向薄膜、准二维极限以及与其他量子材料（如自旋冰烧绿石）的界面中实现了对竞争相互作用的精细操控。

Result: 主要发现包括：(111)取向薄膜中磁性外尔半金属相（magnetic Weyl semimetal phase）的实现；应变调控的磁多极序（strain-engineered magnetic multipolar orders）；准二维极限中手性自旋液体（chiral spin liquid-like state）的出现；以及烧绿石铱氧化物与自旋冰烧绿石等材料界面上新型电子各向异性态（electronically anisotropic states）的发现。

Conclusion: 低维烧绿石铱氧化物为理论与实验提供了充足机遇，以实现对新颖量子物态的揭示、控制与设计。未来方向包括：合成新型异质结构、应用先进探测手段以及探索非平衡现象（non-equilibrium phenomena）。

Abstract: The pyrochlore iridates R2Ir2O7 have emerged as a unique playground for exploring exotic quantum phenomena arising from the intricate interplay of strong spin-orbit coupling, electron correlations, and geometric frustration. While bulk crystals of these materials have revealed a rich landscape of correlated and topological states, recent breakthroughs in epitaxial thin-film synthesis and heterostructure engineering unlocked an entirely new dimension of discovery. This brief Perspective reviews recent advancements highlighting how new tuning knobs such as dimensional confinement, epitaxial strain, and interfacial coupling can be used to manipulate the delicate balance of competing interactions. We discuss several key discoveries enabled by this approach including the realization of the magnetic Weyl semimetal phase in (111) oriented films, strain-engineered magnetic multipolar orders, the emergence of a chiral spin liquid-like state in the quasi-2D limit, and the discovery of novel electronically anisotropic states at interfaces between pyrochlore iridates and other quantum materials, such as spin ice pyrochlores. These findings showcase that low-dimensional pyrochlore iridates provide ample opportunities for both theory and experiment to unravel, control and ultimately design novel quantum states of matter. We conclude by outlining key open questions and future directions ranging from the synthesis of new heterostructures to the application of advanced probes and the exploration of non-equilibrium phenomena.

### [188] [Weak first-order phase transition out of the classical kagome spin liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26779)
*Cecilie Glittum,Olav F. Syljuåsen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋分量展开方法，证明经典kagome海森堡反铁磁体中的自旋液体在低温下会经历一阶相变进入√3×√3相，而非此前蒙特卡洛模拟所认为的持续无序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典kagome海森堡反铁磁体（classical kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet）中自旋液体（spin liquid）在低温下的终态问题已争论超过三十年，此前蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟结果存在不确定性，需要更精确的理论方法予以澄清。

Method: 采用自旋分量展开（expansion in the number of spin components）方法进行分析，并引入次近邻相互作用（second-neighbor interactions）以考察相变行为的一般性。

Result: 自旋液体在低温下通过弱一级相变（weak first-order phase transition）进入√3×√3相，该相的有序矩（ordered moment）在零温下达到饱和；加入次近邻相互作用后，该相变属于一阶相变线，终止于一个临界点（critical point）；相比之下，烧绿石反铁磁体（pyrochlore antiferromagnet）在所有温度下均保持无序。

Conclusion: 经典kagome海森堡反铁磁体中的自旋液体并非在所有温度下稳定，其在低温下会通过一级相变转变为长程有序态，纠正了此前蒙特卡洛模拟的结论。

Abstract: The low-temperature fate of the spin-liquid regime in the classical kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet has been debated for over three decades. Using an expansion in the number of spin components, we show that, contrary to earlier Monte Carlo simulations, the spin liquid terminates at a weak first-order phase transition into the $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ phase which ordered moment saturates at zero temperature. Adding second-neighbor interactions, this transition belongs to a line of first-order phase transitions that ends at a critical point. For comparison, the pyrochlore antiferromagnet remains disordered at all temperatures.

### [189] [Neural Autoregressive Control Variates for the Quantum Monte Carlo Sign Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26814)
*Bei Qiao,Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文训练一对自回归（autoregressive）模型构造零均值控制变量（control variates），在量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟中缓解符号问题（sign problem）。该方法在三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体的小N极限下进行基准测试，可将平均符号的标准误差降低一个数量级，能量估计器的标准误差降低三到五倍，即使在平均符号降至10⁻³以下时仍然有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子蒙特卡洛模拟中的符号问题严重限制了其在 frustrated 晶格等非二分格点系统上的应用，亟需一种能够有效降低方差、缓解符号问题的通用方法。

Method: 训练两个自回归模型，分别约束在正负符号扇区（positive- and negative-sign sectors）内，具有严格不交叠的支持集（disjoint support），每个模型在其扇区内精确归一化；两者的差值结构上具有零均值，提供无偏辅助可观测量（unbiased auxiliary observable），其与符号估计器的相关性控制方差缩减。在随机级数展开（stochastic series expansion, SSE）框架内实现，通过增量环拓扑更新（incremental loop-topology update）扩展到 frustrated 晶格；通过 twist 通道实现符号遍历采样（sign-ergodic sampling）。控制变量采用自回归 transformer 实现，通过序列结束奇偶掩码（end-of-sequence parity mask）强制精确的符号扇区分辨率，并将增量环计数的变化和累积 frustration 奇偶性作为拓扑特征（topological features）嵌入。

Result: 在三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体的小N极限下进行基准测试：控制变量将平均符号的标准误差降低一个数量级，能量估计器的标准误差降低三到五倍；即使在平均符号降至10⁻³以下时仍然有效。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了框架并提供了原理验证（proof-of-principle）演示，表明自回归控制变量可以有效缓解符号问题；未来工作将利用物理启发的架构（physics-informed architectures）扩展到更大系统。

Abstract: We train a pair of autoregressive models to construct zero-mean control variates to mitigate the sign problem in quantum Monte Carlo simulations. The two autoregressive networks are confined to the positive- and negative-sign sectors with strictly disjoint support, and each is exactly normalized over its sector. Their difference is therefore structurally zero-mean, providing an unbiased auxiliary observable whose correlation with the sign estimator controls the variance reduction. We implement the method within the stochastic series expansion framework, which we extend to frustrated lattices by developing an incremental loop-topology update. Sign-ergodic sampling is achieved through a twist channel, which is the unique sign-changing mechanism on non-bipartite lattices. We implement the control variates as autoregressive transformers with an end-of-sequence parity mask that enforces exact sign-sector resolution, while the incremental loop-count change and cumulative frustration parity are incorporated as topological features. On the triangular-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet, we benchmark the method in the small-$N$ limit. The control variate reduces the standard error of the average sign by up to an order of magnitude and that of the energy estimator by a factor of three to five, remaining effective even when the average sign drops below $10^{-3}$. This work lays out the framework and provides a proof-of-principle demonstration that autoregressive control variates can effectively mitigate the sign problem. Scaling to larger systems with physics-informed architectures is the subject of future work.

</details>


### [190] [Self-Consistent Spectral Quadrature Approach to Many-Body Green Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26887)
*Stanislav Yu. Kruchinin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自洽谱求积（self-consistent spectral quadrature, sc-SQ）框架，用于计算多体格林函数（many-body Green functions）。该方法通过高斯-克里斯托费尔（Gauss–Christoffel）求积近似Källén–Lehmann谱测度，得到具有保证谱正定性的有理格林函数表示，并通过奇异值分解（SVD）的秩选择准则自动确定数值可分辨的极点阶数。自洽性通过要求计算期望值所用的谱函数与求积重构生成的谱函数一致来实现。在安德森杂质模型（Anderson impurity model）上的基准测试表明该方法与数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group, NRG）结果定性一致，并在Bethe格点哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）的动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）框架中成功捕捉了三峰安德森杂质谱以及Mott能隙形成等非微扰特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体格林函数的计算是凝聚态物理和量子化学的核心问题，但现有方法在高精度与计算效率之间往往难以兼顾。该方法旨在提供一种系统性的、非微扰的数值方案，能够自动识别谱函数的数值可分辨结构，同时确保谱正定性。

Method: 方法的核心包括三个环节：首先，利用高斯-克里斯托费尔（Gauss–Christoffel, GC）求积近似Källén–Lehmann谱测度，得到有理格林函数表示，该表示在极点阶数N下精确再现前2N个谱矩（spectral moments），并保证谱正定性。其次，对Hankel矩阵施加基于奇异值分解（SVD）的秩选择准则，通过奇异值间隙（singular-value gap）自动识别数值可分辨的极点阶数N*，作为相关复杂性（correlation complexity）的精度引导诊断。最后，通过固定点（fixed-point）迭代实现自洽性：用于计算期望值的谱函数必须与求积重构生成的谱函数一致；该固定点层级可系统性地连接至Hartree–Fock和Hubbard-I等已知近似。

Result: 在安德森杂质模型上，sc-SQ方法准确捕捉了三峰谱结构，与NRG基准结果定性一致。在Bethe格点哈伯德模型的DMFT计算中，方法成功再现了半满填充下准粒子权重（quasiparticle weight）的抑制行为，并在N≥5时于绝缘分支上观察到Mott能隙（Mott gap）的形成，与NRG参考结果定性吻合。

Conclusion: sc-SQ框架为多体格林函数的数值计算提供了一种自洽、非微扰且具有谱正定性保证的新途径。该方法能够自动识别谱结构复杂度，并系统地将Hartree–Fock和Hubbard-I等近似纳入统一框架，在强关联电子体系的定性描述中表现出与NRG一致的有效性。

Abstract: We develop a self-consistent spectral quadrature (sc-SQ) framework for the calculation of many-body Green functions. The method approximates the Källén--Lehmann spectral measure by Gauss--Christoffel (GC) quadrature, yielding a rational Green function representation with guaranteed spectral positivity that exactly reproduces the first $2N$ spectral moments at pole order $N$. A key component is an SVD-based rank-selection criterion on the Hankel matrix, which identifies the numerically resolvable pole rank $N^*$ from the singular-value gap and acts as a precision-guided diagnostic of correlation complexity. The scheme is made self-consistent by requiring that the spectral function used to evaluate expectation values coincides with the spectral function generated by the quadrature reconstruction. This defines a fixed-point hierarchy that connects systematically to established approximations, including Hartree--Fock and Hubbard-I, and incorporates non-perturbative features such as multi-peak spectral structure. We benchmark the approach for the Anderson impurity model against numerical renormalization group (NRG) results and apply it within dynamical mean-field theory for the Hubbard model on the Bethe lattice. The method captures the three-peak Anderson impurity spectrum and the suppression of quasiparticle weight in the half-filled Hubbard model on the Bethe lattice, including Mott-gap formation on the insulating branch for $N\geqslant 5$, in qualitative agreement with NRG references.

</details>


### [191] [Inter-Landau-Level Pair Tunneling Rigidifies the Long-Wavelength Structure Factor of the ν=1/3 Laughlin State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26957)
*Hongyi Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文检验了关于朗道能级混合（Landau-level mixing）在ν=1/3分数量子霍尔态中会使长波结构因子软化的经典理论链条。在哈尔丹球面上对N=6, 2Q=15系统进行的微扰计算（Schrieffer-Wolff方法）支持经典预期（S(1)增加约21%），但非微扰的全双朗道能级精确对角化（exact diagonalization）结果显示相反趋势：S(1)刚性化，从0.118单调下降至0.080（抑制约32%）。两种方法的结果符号相反，差距约53个百分点。通道掩膜消融定位该反转主要源于DD↔UU对隧穿通道（占98%）。四路分解表明三体相干成分的强度约为微扰混合成分的2.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验由Girvin、MacDonald和Platzman提出的经典推理链条：在ν=1/3的分数量子霍尔效应中，朗道能级混合（LLM）应导致长波结构因子S(L)软化，其机制涉及有效赝势V₁的抑制、磁振子能隙（magnetoroton gap）闭合以及单模近似（single-mode approximation）的连锁效应。

Method: 在哈尔丹球面（Haldane sphere）上对ν=1/3、N=6、2Q=15系统进行研究。(i) 微扰方法：采用一阶Schrieffer-Wolff变换对LLL Laughlin态进行缀饰，结合Löwdin重整化赝势（Löwdin-renormalised pseudopotentials）。(ii) 非微扰方法：使用修复后的DiagHam 2LL模块进行严格的双朗道能级（LLL+SLL）精确对角化（exact diagonalization），首次在球面上保留完整的层间散射通道（inter-LL scattering channels）。进一步通过通道掩膜消融（channel-mask ablation）和四路分解（four-way decomposition）进行归因分析。

Result: 微扰计算得到S(1)在κ=10时增加约+21%，与GMP预测（V₁ᵉᶠᶠ软化约19%）一致。非微扰精确对角化结果则显示S(1)从κ→0时的0.118单调下降至κ=10时的0.080，抑制约32%，符号与微扰结果相反，二者差距约53个百分点。通道掩膜消融表明反转主要由DD↔UU对隧穿通道贡献（占98%）。四路分解显示三体相干成分（three-body coherent content）的强度约为微扰混合成分的2.5倍。

Conclusion: 在ν=1/3分数量子霍尔态中，微扰与非微扰方法对朗道能级混合效应的预测存在定性分歧：微扰方法支持结构因子软化，而非微扰精确对角化显示结构因子刚性化。该反转主要源于DD↔UU对隧穿通道，且三体相干效应显著压制了微扰混合效应。这挑战了经典推理链条的普适性，提示需要重新审视朗道能级混合在分数量子霍尔系统中的物理效应。

Abstract: A textbook chain of reasoning, originating with Girvin, MacDonald, and Platzman, predicts that Landau-level mixing (LLM) at nu=1/3 should soften the long-wavelength structure factor S(L): virtual excitations suppress V_1, the magnetoroton gap closes, and the single-mode approximation then forces S(L) to increase. We test this chain on the Haldane sphere at nu=1/3, N=6, 2Q=15. (i) Perturbatively, via first-order Schrieffer-Wolff dressing of the LLL Laughlin state, fed Lowdin-renormalised pseudopotentials: the dressed state gives Delta S(1) at kappa=10 of approximately +21%, consistent with the GMP prediction (~19% softening of V_1^eff). (ii) Non-perturbatively, via rigorous two-Landau-level (LLL+SLL) exact diagonalisation using a repaired DiagHam 2LL module that retains, for the first time on the sphere, the full inter-LL scattering channels. The response reverses sign: S(1) rigidifies monotonically from 0.118 at kappa->0 to 0.080 at kappa=10, a 32% suppression. Perturbative and non-perturbative results thus disagree in sign, with a gap of ~53 percentage points between +21% (SW) and -32% (full ED). Channel-mask ablation localises the reversal to the DD<->UU pair-tunneling channel (98% of the shift). A four-way decomposition shows the three-body coherent content overpowers the perturbative admixture by ~2.5x. Repaired code: https://github.com/Cannan-1/DiagHamOnSphereOpenSource (v2.0).

</details>


### [192] [Quantum criticality and factorization in a constrained Rydberg spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27166)
*Yuan Jiang,Wen-Long You,Liangsheng Li,Maoxin Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过精确对角化、密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）及变分均匀矩阵乘积态（variational uniform matrix-product state）方法，系统研究了一维约束量子自旋链的零温相图，揭示了Luttinger液体、反铁磁有序相和极化顺磁相，并发现反铁磁序的两种破坏机制及一条精确基态因子化线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上，相干驱动的里德伯原子阵列（Rydberg-atom arrays）中同时存在局域拉比驱动（local Rabi driving）和偶极-偶极交换相互作用（dipole-dipole exchange interactions），但该系统的零温量子相图尚不清楚。本文旨在系统刻画这一约束量子自旋链中的竞争序和相变机制。

Method: 首先将系统投影到阻塞约束（blockade-constrained）希尔伯特空间，得到局域与非局域量子涨落平等竞争的有效模型。然后综合运用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）、密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）和变分均匀矩阵乘积态（variational uniform matrix-product state, VUMPS）计算方法。

Result: 建立了完整的零温相图，包含Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquid）、反铁磁有序相（antiferromagnetic ordered phase）和极化顺磁相（polarized paramagnet）。识别了反铁磁序的两种破坏机制：强驱动下的传统Ising相变（Ising transition）和弱驱动下连续量子熔化（continuous quantum melting）为Luttinger液体——后者通过纠缠诊断（entanglement-based diagnostics）和有限纠缠标度（finite-entanglement scaling）表征。此外，在有序相内部发现了一条精确基态因子化线（exact ground-state factorization line）。

Conclusion: 该因子化线为零纠缠的解析可解参考点，为可编程里德伯量子模拟器（programmable Rydberg quantum simulators）的实验研究提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We investigate the zero-temperature phase diagram of a one-dimensional constrained quantum spin chain realized in coherently driven Rydberg-atom arrays with competing local Rabi driving and dipole-dipole exchange interactions. Projecting onto the blockade-constrained Hilbert space yields an effective model in which local and nonlocal quantum fluctuations compete on equal footing. Combining exact diagonalization, the density-matrix renormalization group, and variational uniform matrix-product-state calculations, we establish a complete phase diagram comprising a Luttinger liquid, an antiferromagnetic ordered phase, and a polarized paramagnet. We identify two distinct mechanisms for the destruction of antiferromagnetic order: a conventional Ising transition at strong driving and a continuous quantum melting into the Luttinger liquid at weak driving, characterized using entanglement-based diagnostics and finite-entanglement scaling. In addition, we uncover an exact ground-state factorization line embedded within the ordered phase, providing an analytically tractable zero-entanglement reference point for experiments with programmable Rydberg quantum simulators.

</details>
